#/ /shiShyabhAsanasyasUbhAnukUlashtsamaNDalasarbasyaprabhubadzradhAradhIkAshasarakirtidhAdzashrIbhadratobimokShanAmabiharatasma// / /rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag
rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa slob bshad bstan pa'i nyi 'od ces bya ba bzhugs so// //

/ /na maHpra dhu badzra dha rA ya/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje 'chang chen po snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i bstan pa'i srog gi zungs su bslab gsum
ngur smrig 'chang ba'i zlos gar mkhan tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa slob bshad bstan pa'i nyi 'od
ces bya ba dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i zhabs rdul bung ba snying pad ke sa rar 'god na smin grol lam gyi 'bras mchog mngon du gyur min de srid thugs rje'i mthu dpung lhag
par bskyed nas dngos grub rgya mtsho'i gru char stsal du gsol/ /gzod ma nyid nas yongs su brnyes pa bla med ye shes bdud rtsi'i bcud/ /sems can kun gyi thar pa'i srog song
gsang gsum rgyan gyi 'khor lo'i mdzod/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang mi yi gzugs kyis blo gsal skal bzang rgya mtsho'i mgon/ /grags pa'i rgyal mtshan srid rtser bsgreng zhabs
pad

dkar chun po thod du 'ching / /mtha' klas mkhyen pa'i nam mkhar thugs rje'i nyi/ /'char nub spangs pa'i rnal dpyod tsha zer gyis/ /chos phung bye ba'i 'dab stong yongs grol
ba'i/ /mkhas grub skyes rabs tshangs pa'i blo las brgal/ /khyad par rgyal kun mgrin gcig legs so'i tshig /brjod yul 'dren pa bzhi pa'i bstan 'di la/ /mtha' klas byon pa
dam pa'i zlos gar gyi/ /grangs tshad gzhal 'dod byis pa'i sems de ngal/ /bye brag grub pa'i 'khor sgyur bi rU pa/ /sa skya'i 'jam mgon rim byon thugs kyi bcud/ /snyan brgyud
bstan pa'i shing rta chen po'i srol/ /phye ba'i rtogs brjod cha tsam gleng bar spro/ /chu 'dzin stug po'i phang nas dbyar gyi rnga/ /rab snyan glu dbyangs sgrog tshe
mdongs mtha' can/ /dga' ba'i zlos gar bsgyur na shes ldan rnams/ /ngo mtshar dad pa'i spu long cis mi g.yo/ /rlung gis sbur ma mthon por bteg pa ltar/ /med bzhin sgro

btags rdzun gyi rnam par thar/ /mthong na dam pa'i spyod tshul lhug pa ru/ /smra ba sngon bsags legs byas bye bas nyos/ /ku sha'i rtse mos 'thor te rgya mtsho'i mtha'/ /'dzad
byed dka' thub bsten pa'i rjes 'gro ba/ /phra mo'i blo gros khab kyi mig bu ru/ /khyod yon lhun po 'dzud pa'i go skabs ci/ /'on te rin chen gling nas nor bu'i tshogs/
/ded dpon gcig gis 'dren par mi bzod kyang / /rang gis ji tsam 'khur nus bdog pa yis/ /dbul ba'i gdung sel 'dod 'jo dngos po'i gshis/ /'khyog tshig chags pa'i gdong pa rig
byed sgor/ /sprul pa'i zol sbyor rgan po ma yin pa'i/ /mkhas grub ngang tshul gser sgong yongs smin pa/ /sngon med tshangs par lta la lha rnams brel/ /phyogs 'dzin gdon
gyis phrag dog sbyin skyes mgor/ /mthu stobs rdo rje rtse brgya rab bsnun kyang / /ris med 'gro la brtse ba'i spyan stong dkyus / /ring por skyong ba'i bshes gnyen 'chi
med gtso/ /rlabs chen mdzad pa sos kyi dga' ston dus/ /'dren byed tshig sbyor dpyid kyi lang tsho ma/ /spel legs zlos gar 'phreng mdzes gsong po'i glu/ /gzur gnas gzhan gsos
mgrin nas len 'di nyon/ /de yang slob dpon daNDis/ shis brjod phyag bya dngos po ni/ /nges par bstan pa'ang de yi sgo/ /zhes thog mar shis brjod/ phyag bya/ dngos po
nges bstan rnams sum ldan/ gnyis ldan sogs ci rigs pa bshad pa'i da lam phyi ma'i sgo nas tshigs su bcad pa sngon du song bas skabs su gleng bar bya ba ni/ ji skad du/ mchog
gi khyad par nyid la reg na de yi yon tan cha shas kyis/ /

dman pa dag kyang bsngags 'os la 'god mthu chen rnams kyi byed pa'i phul/ /ma la yar nye phal gyi shing yang rkang 'thung bzang po'i dri bsung ngad / /'chang bar byed pa'i
nus pa rab mtho tsandan de dag rgyal gyur cig /ces lho phyogs ma la ya'i nags klung du skyes pa'i shing phal pa dag kyang 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi tas/ ma la ya las 'ongs
pa yi/ /sdong dum phal la rin thang brtsi/ /zhes tsandan gyi dri bsung lan cig ma yin par sim pa'i nus pas ljon pa phal pa la'ang tsandan dang phyogs 'dra'i dri nus 'byung
ba ltar mkhas dang grub pa'i yon tan yang nas yang du brjod cing bsams na rang cag blo dang spyod tshul ches cher dman pa rnams kyang bya ba ngan pa las ldog cing skyed
thon nas dam pa'i rnam thar la rim gyis 'jug pa sogs dgos pa lhag par che zhing rang gi legs byas kyi phung po bla nas blar 'phel ba'i tshogs rgya cher gsog pa'i phyir dus
gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa ma lus pa'i gsang ba rab 'byams mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo'i bang mdzod gdan gsum tshang ba'i khyab bdag dgyes mdzad rdo rje bshes gnyen dam
pa'i sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rol pa tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam par thar pa'i rim pa la/ mdo sde rgyan las/ skye ba skyed mos tshal 'gro ltar rtogs nas/ /spro ba'i
sems drangs dga' zhing de la 'jug /ces rgyal sras 'phags pa sems can gyi don du bsams bzhin srid par skye ba len pa la ngang pa pad mtshor 'jug pa ltar spro zhing sprul
pa bye ba ther 'bum dus gcig tu ston pas 'di lta bu'o zhes lce brgyas bskal par brjod kyang zad pa'i mtha' ga la zhig /'on te thun mong gi gdul bya

rnams la grags pa'i yang srid dang thugs rgyud gcig pa rags rim brjod na/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i bstod pa bkra shis mtshan bzang mar/
mgon khyod gdod ma'i dbyings su sangs rgyas kyang / /grangs med gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa bzhin/ /ngo mtshar skye ba'i zlos gar bcu gsum gyis/ /phan bde'i dga' ston
spel la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes dang / 'dar pa rin cen dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i tshigs bcad mar/ bde chen 'khor lo'i mgon po he ru kaH /blo 'das 'od gsal dga' mas 'khyud pa'i
dpal/ /dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i rigs bdag rdo rje 'dzin/ /khyab bdag bla ma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /mgon khyod 'og min chen po'i zhing khams su/ /sku gsum yan lag bdun
ldan mngon gyur kyang / /zhing 'dir skal bzang 'gro rnams bsgral ba'i slad/ /bgrang yas rnam 'phrul bstan la gsol ba 'debs/ /'phags yul auDDi ya na'i nor 'dzin mar/ /mkha'
spyod dbang mos rjes bzung stha wi ra/ /brtul zhugs spyod pas gdug can kun sgrol ba'i/ /rnal 'byor dbang por bstan la gsol ba 'debs/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sangs rgyas
ston pa dang / /chos sku 'od zer mtshungs med bu ston rje/ /yar klungs pa dang dge slong dbang mo sogs/ /mkhas grub brgyud mar bltams la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa 'di'i
dngos bstan la bdun las ma byung yang bkra shis mtshan bzang mar bcu gsum byung ba smos na dpal ldan rgyud kyi ye shes le'ur/ dbyibs kyi rlung ni chen po thams cad dag gis
sangs rgyas zhing rnams mtha' dag rnam par 'god par byed/ /

'jig rten khams 'di so so dag la slar yang khor yug ri bo chen po dag ni kun nas so/ /de yi dbus su las kyi sa ni chen po dag gi rang bzhin 'jig rten khams su rab tu 'gyur/
/lhag ma longs spyod rang bzhin yul gyi bde ba byed pa rin cen kun gyis rab tu gang ba rnams/ /zhes phyi nang sbyar ba'i phyi rol gyi 'gro ba'i las snang gis ri rab dbyibs
tshul mngon pa dang dus kyi 'khor lo tha dad pa'i lugs phyi ma ltar rdo rje'i rwa'i 'og na yod pa'i gling drug ni longs spyod kyi sa dang de'i phyi rol gling bzhi gling
phran brgyad la bdun pa las kyi sa zhes bshad cing / dza na skye ba la'o zhes pa'i byings bzhag /na'i a brjod don yin pas phyis/ buka? rkyen du byin/ ka la yan bzhin yang
ste ya la brjod pa bor ba'o zhes ka phyis/ rnam dbye dang po'i gcig tshig si byin/ mi zad pa la si dbyi'o zhes si phyis/ de'i sde pa la sde pa'i mtha' 'os/ na ma ru bsgyur/
gsal byed dbyangs med pa pha rol gyi yi ger drang ngo / /zhes bsgrubs pas dzambu ni lus can skye ba'i gnas yin la/ bye brag 'dzam gling chung ngu ni bde mchog mkha'
'gro rgya mtsho'i rgyud kyi le'u dang po las/ 'dzam bu gling ni chen po yi/ /dum bu bcu gnyis kyi ni dbus/ /zhes pa'i lho phyogs dzambu tri shas mtshan pa'i gling 'di nyid
kyi lte ba ma dhya ga ta dha ra/ tsandra par pr-i Sho dha ra la sogs pa rnams sos/ bsdu ba byas pas ma ga dha ste dbus 'gyur 'chang zhes dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa
rnams mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i rten yin pas bskal mtha'i dus kyang gzhom gzhig mi nus pa rdo rje gdan

lte bar byas pa'i phyi rol tu/ lung las/ mnyan yod gnas bcas tsam pa ka /wa ra NA si yangs pa can/ /rgyal po'i khab dang drug po ni/ /de dag grong khyer chen por grags/ /zhes
'phags yul na yongs su grags pa'i grong khyer chen po drug dang gzhan yang shar phyogs rgya nag po'i rgyal khams na 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis rtsis kyi sgo mo brgyad khri
bzhi stong gsungs pa'i gnas ri bo rtse lnga/ lho phyogs su dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten na dus kyi 'khor lo'i ye shes sems dpa' ma bsdus par dngos su bzhugs pa
sku gsung thugs kyi dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs/ de'i lho phyogs rgya mtsho'i 'gram na ri bo po ta la zhes thugs rje chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi gnas/ nub phyogs na ayon mkha'
'gro'i gsang mdzod he ru kaHrang byung gi gtsug lag khang / byang phyogs na chos rgyal rigs ldan rim par byon nas 'gro ba rnams phyi nang gzhan gsum gyi sgo nas bkri
bar mdzad pa'i gnas shambha la/ der ma zad kye rdor bde mchog sampu Ti mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho sogs las 'dzam bu gling dbus ma 'di nyid rang na yul nyer bzhi dang dur khrod
brgyad sogs gnas sum cu rtsa gnyis yod par bshad cing / rma bya chen mo las/ yul 'khor lnga brgya/ ljongs chen po bcu drug /yul phran stong / gzhan yang mi rigs mi gcig
pa sum brgya dang drug cu skad rigs bdun brgya nyi shu sogs mtha' klas pa'i nang tshan rgya bod gnyis su sku'i sprul pa rags pa tsam bshad pa bcu gsum las// ! dang po rnal
'byor dbang phyug ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyi gsang ba'i rnam thar las/ nub

cig dpal phug tu bzhugs khri'i steng na bla ma bzhugs gsung ngag bskyar nas gnang rgyu yin zer zhu mkhan mang po tshogs 'dug pa la bslab gsum pa gsal po 'dug gzhan ngo shes
pa mi 'dug /khog phug yin snyam pa'i dpe cha zhig gi lung mdzad byung ba na/ thod phu'i blo gsal rgya mtsho de birWa pa lags sam zer ba zhig 'dug pa la don 'di ga yin te
tshig 'di cung zad sdeb ma shes 'dug gsung / bdag gi thod phu'i rnal 'byor dbang phyug de/ da lta'i blo gsal rgya mtsho yin zhes byas na bde ba 'dra zhus pas de ga bris
pas yong gsung / de nas gzhung bshad cig kyang 'go tshugs snang gsum yang tshugs byung nas na ning gi zin bris la zhus dag byed dgos snyam pa dang gnyid sad/ bsams pas thod
phur byon pa'i rje gha ya dha ra rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi thugs kyi sprul par mnal lam bka' rgya ma las bshad/ de dang pha bla ma thugs rgyud gcig pa'i brda ru 'dug snyam
pa byung gsungs pa khungs shin tu che bas slob dpon 'di rdo rje gdan gyi shar phyogs bi Sha na sman gyi dbang po'i grong khyer na rgyal po gser gyi 'khor lo'i sras su
sku bltams par mtshan mkhan gyis mthu stobs kyi sgo nas bstan pa gsal bar 'gyur zhes lung bstan nas mtshan dngul gyi 'khor lor gsol/ so ma pU rir mkhan po dul ba'i lha
la rab tu byung rig pa'i gnas lnga la sbyangs/ nA landar mkhan po chos kyi bshes gnyen la bsnyen par rdzogs shing theg pa che chung gi chos mtha' klas pa dang khyad par rnal
'byor gsang mtha' 'khor lo sdom pa gsan/ gnas brtan dpal ldan chos skyong

zhes grags te nA lenda'i mkhan por gyur/ nyin mo sde snod gsum la 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum dang mtshan mo bde mchog gi rnal 'byor lhur blangs nas dgung lo bdun cu tsam slebs
kyang rtags bzang ba med pa'i khar mi sdug pa'i mtshan ma mang du byung ba slob dpon 'dis sbyor lam phal cher bgrod nas lte 'og gi kSha ma la sogs par rlung sems 'dus te
mthong lam thob par nye ba bla ma'i gdams pa'i phu thag ma chod pa'i skyon yin pa ma mkhyen par kho bo gsang sngags dang las 'brel med pa 'dug dgongs 'phreng ba chab khang
du bskyur te rgyu'i theg pa la gzhol bar brtson pa na tho rengs mnal lam du bdag med ma bud med tha mal pa'i gzugs kyis lung bstan pa ltar mdzad pas nyer gsum gyi srod
la bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dngos su dbang thob ste mthong lam rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes rgyud la 'khrungs/ khams 'dus pa dang po gtum mo drod rtags
kyi lam 'khrid pa'i dus zug rngu dang gcan gzan gdug pa can sogs shar/ khams 'dus pa bar ma thig le bde stong gi lam 'khrid pa'i dus me chu 'khrug pa/ khams 'dus pa tha ma
skyon med gnyug ma ye shes kyi lam 'khrid pa'i dus bla ma yid dam gyi zhal ral ba sogs skyon du bzung ba nye lam rdo rje btsun mo'i gdams pas ting nge 'dzin du ngo shes
nas nyams su bzhes pas zhag re la sa re thob nas zhag drug song ba na sa drug pa mngon du gyur/ lam gyi bogs 'byin sha chang bsten pa la ma dad pa bzlog pa dang bstan pa
la mi gnod pa'i ched du rab byung gi rtags bor te ngan par zhal gyis bzhes nas wa ra NA sir byon pa chu bo ganggA'i 'gram du nga

ngan pa yin pas lam thong gsungs pas chu bo gyen du bzlog /wA ra NA sir dge 'dun rnams kyi grub thob tu shes te sngar rnga kha gnyis pa brdungs nas gnas dbyung gi bya ba byas
pa la bzod par gsol/ wA ra NA si'i nags khrod du bzhugs pa rgyal po gho nanta tsakras pho brang du gdan drangs pa nang pa'i rnal 'byor par shes nas yan lag rnams lcags
kyis bcings te chur bskyur ba sa 'og tu 'dzud pa sogs byas kyang gnod par ma nus pas rgyal po sogs yul 'khor ba thams cad rdo rje theg pa'i bstan par bkod/ lho phyogs su
byon pa'i lam du gru gla la brten nas chu bo bzlog pa dang phyir 'bab pa'i rdzu 'phrul mdzad/ mnyan pa'ang slob dpon gyi rjes su 'brangs pas skal ldan cig car ba'i lam gyis
bkri bar 'os pa'i DoM bhi he ru kar grags/ de nas chang 'tshong ma kA ma ru siddhi la chang nyo ba'i rin med par brten nyi ma bzung ba na rgyal pos gsol ba btab pa ltar
btang bas zhag gsum gyi mtshan phyed tsam song bas rdo rje gdan pa'i bstod par/ chu bo chen po gyen du bzlog /chang la nyi ma gte mar bcug /birWa pa zhes bya ba yi/ /bla
ma de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes bsngags/ rim bzhin lho phyogs bhi me sa ra'i rgyal po nA tha pa tas rang gi mchod gnas ral pa can lnga brgya'i slob dpon du bskos/ ra dang
ma he khri phrag bsad pa'i khrag mchod byed pa'i dbang phyug gi rten la slob dpon 'dis phyag mdzad pa na de phyed tsam gas pas rgyal po 'khor bcas skrag par gyur/ ral
pa can gcig las sad nas rjes su 'brangs pa sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la ma zhugs pa 'jug 'dod

yod pa'i mtshan gzhi shar phyogs nag po par grags/ de nas taM bra pra ti ma'i rgyal po dzim gim zhes bya bas 'jon dmar las grub pa'i dbang phyug gi sku zhal gsum phyag drug
pa khru brgyad cu yod pa zhabs rdos bsnun te gnas khang nas bskrad pa kha bub tu 'gyel bar mu stegs pa rnams kyis gsol ba btab pas 'bras chan tsam gyis mchod pa'i dam bca'
'dzin du bcug ste gyen du bslang ba sogs mu stegs grangs med btul/ lha mo tsaNDi ka'i rdo sku rang byon zhig gnas sar mi byung tshad rang byung gi tri shu las bsad pa'i
ro la tshogs 'khor byed pa'i rnal 'byor ma rnams nang pa'i bstan pa la bkod/ de wI ko Ti'i ri sul gyi thugs rje chen po'i rdo sku'i drung du phebs pa'i tshe thugs rje chen
pos khyod kyi nus pas ri rab brlag par nus kyang sems can gyi las zad pa med pas mu stegs rnams la gnod pa ma byed ces gsungs pa so ba nA tha btul nas bka' bzhin sgrub
par dam bcas/ so ba nA tha'i mu stegs pa rnams btul nas nang pa'i sde btsugs/ slob dpon nag po pa shar phyogs kyi phyi pa'i rgyal po gdug pa can 'dul ba/ DA ma ru pa rjes
su 'dzin pa/ ayon nas rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi rgyab brten du gyur pa'i lung skor sde lnga spyan 'dren pa'i don gsum la brdzangs/ slob dpon nyid thugs rje chen po'i bka'
bzhin re zhig brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa'i 'phro bshol nas rdo skur thim mam zer/ la la sku dngos rdo'i rnam par song ba glengs/ de yang 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud las/ yi ge
dha zhes sdom brtson nyid/ /lho yi phyogs su rnam par grags/ /pha rol rgol ba bzlog nas kyang / /de

bzhin sdom brtson sngags kyang 'grub/ /ces pa chos 'byung mang por slob dpon chos grags la 'chad pa chos kyi skad dod dharma'i zur ni gnyis kar tshang ba dang bstan pa la rab
tu byung ba'i sdom brtson yin par mtshungs na'ang chos grags kyis tshad ma rigs pas rgol ba tshar bcad pa de 'dra ba'i paNDi ta ni ches mang la/ brtul zhugs spyod pa'i
rdzu 'phrul gyis log lta bcoms pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdzad pa dang sku tshe de la mchog gi dngos grub brnyes pa dpal ldan chos grags la ma byung bas 'khrul pa 'ong
don med cing / grub thob thams cad kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba ni slob dpon 'di nyid do// ! gnyis pa stha bi ra ni shing sbrul 'dar du zhal gyi gtor chen skabs tshar chen rang
gi mnal lam du gsal ba bzhin rdo rje gdan gyi nub phyogs na nges gsang rdo rje theg pa'i chos kyi 'byung gnas auDDi ya na zhes yul de'i skye bo rnams 'phur nas 'gro ba'i
ma dang mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i yul khyad par can der sku bltams pa na 'tshod gzhon nu'i dus rje btsun rdo rje btsun mo mkha' la spyod pa'i dbang mos rjes su bzung ste lung bstan
nas gzengs bstod/ mdo rgyud kyi gzhung la skyes thob kyi shes rab dang sbyor byung gi brtson 'grus kyis gnas lnga mkhyen pa'i paNDi ta'i rtser son bstan pa'i rtsa ba
so so thar pa'i bslab pa la gtso bor mdzad pas mtshan stha wi ra ste gnas brtan du grags/ rgya gar rdo rje gdan gyi mkhan por gyur te rgyal ba'i bstan pa chos spyod rnam
bcu'i sgo nas nyams pa gso ba dang sngar yod rnams dar rgyas su mdzad par brten paN grub kun gyi gtsug tor gyi rtse mor 'dzegs

shing brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mthar phyin pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyis nag phyogs la dga' ba'i 'byung po gdug pa can gyi nus stobs phral nas yang dag pa'i lam la bkod pa sogs mdzad
pa mtha' yas/ rdo ring rin po che'i skye brgyud grub chen lwa ba pa dang 'di nyid dus mtshungs pa yin nam snyam mo// ! gsum pa paN chen dharma pA la ni/ zur thams cad
mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang grol gyi gsal snang la shar bar som nyi mi mnga' bas/ rgya gar shar phyogs su sku 'khrungs pa'i slob dpon dharma pA la zhes gnas lnga rig pa mthar
phyin zhing rlung sems la rang dbang du gyur pas sku tshe la mnga' brnyes pa zhig byon pa'i tshe/ rdo rje gdan gyi ka ba nas mgon po'i sgrub skor slob dpon padma badzra
gyis spyan drangs pa rgya gar du bka' gter gnyis su grags pa'i gter ma de yin zhing / man ngag rnams slob dpon klu sgrub la gsan/ bka' mi nub par bya ba'i phyir du paN
grub dha rma pA la la gnang 'di nyid kyis bal po'i rten khyad par can rnams mjal bar byon pa'i tshe tshad pa'i snyun gyis zin par gangs ri mthong sar phebs na phan zer
bar brten ha nu manthas 'phangs pa'i kha ba'i dum bu la gangs can du grags pa'i mnga' ris smad kyi gangs ri dang / mtsho ma pham pa gzigs su byon pa na lha btsad pos chos
la gus pa'i bkur sti cher mdzad/ khyad par skad gnyis smra ba rin cen bzang pos yo ga'i skor mang du gsan/ mgon po'i sgrub thabs rgya gar gyi gter ma rnams gsan pas lo chen
nas brgyud pa la'ang bka' gter zung du 'jug cing / las mgon gyi skor lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi gter ma

gsan tshe gnyis po zhu dag pher ba byung skad/ lo chen gyis gser snyim pas bcus nas phul ba ma bzhes nan tar gsol bas khyed mi dga' na ngas 'di khyer gsungs nas rdog po gcig
bsnams 'tsho bas phongs na nor dgos kyang nged de 'dra'i tshan min gsungs/ phar gshegs dus dharma pA la yin par shes pa tsam gyis 'do le la spyan drangs rnyed bkur bsam
gyis mi khyab pa byung zhing rgya gar du 'phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam skad/ lhag bsam rab dkar las/ me 'bar ma yi dkar chag phal cher du/ /kha chen dharma pA la zhes
gsungs pa/ /yo ga stod lugs brgyud pa'i de nyid dang / /gcig gam gcig na shar phyogs par bshad cing / /zhes pa'i dgongs pa gsal byed mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi
dri lan du/ me 'bar ma yi dkar chag phal cher dang yang dgon pa'i zin bris las/ kha che dharma pA la zhes bshad pa ni yi ge pa'i skyon cung zad dam gsung bgros ma zin par
snang ste/ bod du byon nas lo chen gyi bla ma mdzad pa'i dharma pA la 'di nyid ni/ rgya gar shar phyogs pa yin par yo ga dang mgon po'i lo rgyus yi ge rnams las gsal ba'i
phyir ro zhes gsungs pas shes nus so// ! bzhi pa paN grub gha ya dha ra ni/'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsang ba'i rtogs brjod nas gong du drangs pa bzhin rgya gar shar
phyogs bhangga la'i rgyal po tsaNDa ru pa akShi'i yig mkhan gyi rigs yin pas ka phastha zhes grags shing / mtshan dngos gha ya dha ra ste bod skad du sprin 'dzin zer rig
pa'i gnas lnga la shin tu mkhas shing slob dpon gnyis spangs zhabs kyis rjes su bzung nas gsung

ngag gi bka' babs/ zab chos 'di nyid bod du dar ba'i rten 'brel 'grig tshul ni 'brog mi'i mnal lam bka' rgya mar/ lho nas mi nag po ri bo tsam pa 'phur byung ba'i kha nas dung
gi seng ge skyugs/ de'i kha nas gser gyi rdo rje byung ba'i lte ba nas bum pa chus gang ba thugs kar thim pa'i mnal lam byung ba'i sang nyin sgor A tsarYas rwa dung bus
byung ba na ltar btang bas lwa ba dmar po gyon pa zhig gis khyed la bstad nas 'ongs zer ba nang du bos nas gsung gleng mdzad par rgyud sde rgya mtshor mkhas shing khyad
par rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi gdams pa yod pa mkhyen nas thog mar tshar gsum khug pa'i chos 'brel sogs gsan/ lo gsum nas tshur bod du yong / de dus chos yon gser srang
lnga brgya grabs kyis gsung ba bzhin zhal dan mdzad/ lha rtse brag tu bzhugs pa'i tshe zhal dan bzhin paN chen gha ya dha ra phebs/ paNDi ta'i zhal nas gsung ngag 'dzugs
pa la gnas khyad par can dgos gsung ba chu la mu gu zhes pa'i sgra byung ba gar song rtsad bcad pa mthar mu gu lung du thim pas rnam par grol ba'i sgra rten 'brel legs par
dgongs nas der gnas mdzad/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa lo gsum la rdzogs par gnang / paNDi ta 'byon par brtsams pa la sngar zhal dan bzhin
lo lnga bzhugs par gsol bas chos tshar nas bsdad par dgos pa med gser phri nas phul chog gsung yang rten 'brel mi legs dgongs te gser srang la bteg pa cung zad ma longs
par lha rje zur phu che la gdams pa yod bas gser khur shog gsungs pa bzhin phul/ paNDi tar gser

srang lnga brgya/ gla rtsi stong / rnga dkar nyis brgya dang rnga nag stong / gos dar sogs chos yon bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul bas paNDi ta'i thugs la gser mang drags pas sgyu
ma yin nam dgongs mang mkhar gril chen gyi mi mang sar cir 'dug dris pas gser shin tu bzang zer bar brten mnyes te da khyod la ci dgos gsungs par chos 'phro 'dra yod
na zhu gsungs pas/ sku rgyab tu mgon thang bzhes 'phreng ba mgul la bcug gtor ma dbu thog tu bsnams nas lhag ma med pa'i dbu snying mdzad/ slar ci dgos gsung bar chos 'di
bdag min pa bod du gzhan la mi gnang ba zhu zhus pas paNDi ta mnyes kyang zer/ la la zhu lugs de cung zad ma byung bas gdung brgyud kyis mi phan pa'i rten 'brel 'phyugs
par glengs skad/ 'on kyang mnal lam gyi lung bstan bzhin chos brgyud kyi bstan pa bod dang bod chen po'i rgyal khams yongs su khyab pa'i 'phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam/
'gos lhas btsas bla chen la chags sdang gi rnam pas khyad du thon pa zhig bzhed nas mai tri pa gdan 'dren du byon pa lam du gha ya dha ra dang mjal bar su yin dris pas mai
tri pa yin gsungs par brten gsang 'dus sogs kyi chos zhu bsgyur du ma mdzad/ rjes su rtsad chod kyang chos zhus zin pa dang shin tu mkhas par 'dug pas zhabs tog bstar/
phebs res 'di la sprin gyi shugs can du grags pas/ grub brgya'i bstod par/ rgyal rigs rig pa'i gnas lngar mkhas/ /nam mkha'i lha la the tshom gcad/ /sprin gyi shugs can zhes
pa yi/ /bla ma de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes 'byung /

bla chen gshegs nas gyi jo lo tsA bas gdan drangs khong la gsung ngag kyang gnang / gnyos yon tan grags kyis gdan drangs der paNDi ta la 'chi ltas byung bas mkha' reg thod
phur 'brog mi'i slob ma se rog gnyis yod sar phebs/ gshegs pa'i tshe dbu gtsug nas 'od dkar po rdza ma tsam gyi nang nas rnam shes kye rdor zhal brgyad pa rkang gang tsam
zhig sgra 'od me tog gi char dang bcas nub phyogs su song ba'i ngo mtshar ba de 'dra bod du su la'ang ma byung zhing / mkhas grub kyi yon tan ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//
! lnga pa mkhas grub khyung po ni/ 'gro mgon sangs rgyas ston pa yin par tshar chen nyid kyis zhal gyis bzhes shing sangs rgyas ston pa ni khyung po'i skye bar grags pas/
rje btsun bod mkhar ba chen po'i rnam thar du/ sngon gyi dus na mkhas grub khyung po de/ /bdag sogs dmu rgod 'gro la brtser dgongs nas/ /dus 'dir tshar chen rdo rje 'chang
du grags/ /bdag sogs gdul bya'i re ba skong der 'dud/ /ces pa yid brtan gyi gnas kho nar nges pa'i phyir/ khyung po nyid kyi gsung las/ ban chung bdag gi skyes sa gangs
dkar mda'/ /snye mo ra mang rje rigs khyung po yin/ /pha ru smos pa khyung rgyal stag skyes dang / /ma ru smos pa mgo bza' bkra shis skyid/ /de nyid rum du bdag nyid zhugs
pa'i tshe/ /pha ma yul mi bde skyid ldan par gyur/ /stag gi lo la ma yi rum nas btsas/ /zhes pa ltar yul snye mo ra mang du yab khyung po'i rigs stag skyes/ yum bkra
shis skyid kyi sras su sku bltams/ lo bcu lon nas yig rtsis mkhas par shes/ bcu gnyis lo

la pha mes bag chags kyi/ /sems phyogs bon bslabs rdzogs chen phyag chen bslabs/ /zhes dgung lo bcu nas 'dri klog rtsis sogs la mkhas par sbyangs/ bcu gsum nas bla ma g.yung
drung rgyal po la bon gyi skor gsan mkhas par gyur te ka pa li 'dren pa bdun brgya tsam gyi tshogs pa bskyangs nas bon gyi 'chad nyan dang bstan bcos mang du mdzad pas
dbus gtsang kun tu dar rgyas su gyur na'ang bon 'di gsha' ma rang zhig min pa 'dra snyam rgya gar du 'byon par brtsams tshe yab yum gnyis kyi ring mi 'byon par bshol btab
la brten/ sngags rnying ma ba bla ma 'byung gnas seng ge la sems klong man ngag gi sde rnams gsan zhing slob ma sum brgya tsam bskyangs kyang spyod pa la ma mgu bar lhas
bskor ba dang sbrags bla ma ni ru par phyag chen/ mtshan brjod/ do ha/ dgra 'jigs kyi skor sogs gsan na'ang thun mong gi dngos grub tsam la ma rangs pas/ de tshe rgya gar
grub thob a mo ghas/ /'di ni sprul pa'i sku ste rgya gar 'gro/ /paNDi ta dang grub thob thams cad kyi/ /thugs bcud bsdus nas 'gro rnams smin grol mdzad/ /sna tshogs sprul
pas gdul bya 'dul bar 'gyur/ /theg chen snying po mtha' bral chos sgra sgrog /mthar thug gsang sngags bde stong dbyer med kyi/ /seng ge'i nga ro phyogs bcur sgrog par
'gyur/ /zhes lung bstan dang mthun par zhing btsongs pa dang sru mo'i g.yu sogs la brten pa'i gser mang po bsnams nas byon tshul/ de nas rin cen gser phye 'phongs med khyer/
/gces pa'i srog la ma bltas dka' spyad nas/ /rgya dang bal po'i yul du lan

bdun phyin/ /rgya gar mkhas pa brgya dang lnga bcu bsten/ /khyad par mkhas shing grub thob lnga bcu dang / /rtsa ba'i bla ma khyad 'phags rnam bzhi bsten/ /longs sku drug pa
rdo rje 'chang chen la/ /dngos su chos gsan ye shes mkha' 'gro gnyis/ /mnyes par byas nas mthar thug gdams ngag zhus/ /zhes bal por paNDi ta bha su na ma ti la bitpA ta
sbyangs shing bya rgyud kyi skor gsan bla ma rdo rje gdan pa la dge tshul sgrub pa sogs bla ma brgya lnga bcu la rgyu 'bras kyi theg pa'i chos mtha' klas pa gsan/ paN grub
thams cad zhal mthun par nA ro pa'i lcam ne gu zhes rdo rje 'chang la chos dngos su gsan pa zhig dur khrod so sa gling na yod pa thos pas der byon pa na shing tA la bdun
srid tsam gyi mkha' la bud med smug nag rus rgyan sprad pa zhig 'dug par gser phul zhing gsol ba btab pas tshes bco lnga'i srod la sgyu lus dbang mo che'i dbang gnang
ba sogs chos drug gi gdams pa rnams gsan/ gzhan yang mai tri pa dang rA hu la sogs la myur mdzad mgon po'i chos skor zhus nas bod du byon/ ljongs 'dir chig chos rdo rje'i
rgyas btab kyi brgyud pa bdun ldan sogs dpal ldan shangs pa bka' brgyud kyi bstan pa phyogs kun tu khyab par gyur/ zhing 'dir mdzad pa rdzogs nas/ bla ma yi dam lung bstan
pa'i/ /mthar thug gsum gyi dus la babs/ /da ni zhing khams mthar thug pa'i/ /bde ba can gyi zhing du 'gro/ /zhes dus la babs pas 'pho ba ye shes skar khung ma la brten
te dbu thod lag mthil tsam zhig mkha' la 'phar nas sgra 'od dang bcas te gshegs/ khams pa'i gra

pa rnams kyi dbang du song nas pur sbyangs pas/ 'di yi lus ni bde mchog 'khor lo ste/ /gsung ni ma hA mA ya'i bdag nyid 'gyur/ /thugs ni dpal ldan dgyes pa rdo rje ste/ /sprul
pa'i gnas mchog gsang ba 'dus pa la/ /gsang gnas bde skyong gshin rje gshed du 'gyur/ /zhes pa dang mtshungs par/ lha sku dang ring bsrel gyi phung por song / deng sang
yang shangs chos khungs btsun gyi rgyun ma chad pa tshar chen gyi thugs rje kho nar mngon no// !drug pa paN chen bsod snyoms pa chen po ni/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer
gyis paN chen gyi sngon gnas dran zhing chos 'od yin pa rje mkhyen brtse'i mnal lam gyis shes nus pas/ rgya gar nub phyogs kha che khri brtan du yab tshong dpon srid brtan
yum dge ba ma gnyis kyi sras su me mo lug gi lo la sku bltams/ spyir ma byon sangs rgyas gsum pa rab gsal gyi rnam par sprul pa yin pas 'phags pa'i gang zag gi yon tan
dpag par dka' zhing thun mong ba'i snang ngor yang chung ngu'i dus nas yig rtsis sgra snyan/ sdeb sbyor/ mngon brjod/ zlos gar dang gzhan yang rig pa'i gnas bco brgyad la
mkhas pa'i rtser son/ mkhan po chen po A kA ra gupta la bsnyen par rdzogs te tshul khrims rnam par dag pas gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur/ thun
mong ba nang rig pa sde snod gsum dang thun mong min pa gsang chen rdo rje theg pa la sbyangs pas mkhas grub kyi snyan pas sa steng khyab/ khro phu ba gnubs byams pa'i
dpal lo tsA mdzad bzhed kyis mang yul skyid grong du bzhugs dus

rgyal tsha'i slob ma don zhags par brtag pa zhus par 'phags pa wa ti la gsol ba thob ces gsungs pa ltar btab pas lo tsA ba'i mnal lam du A tsarYa dung so yod pa zhig gis dung
seng / byang chub shing gi lo ma la paNDi ta bya'i gdong pa can dang shel gyi me long la paNDi ta shin tu mdzes pa'i gzugs/ mi gzugs dkar po rnams gtad byung ba so so'i
rgyab tu rgya yig yod pa de skabs ma mkhyen kyang seng ge lo tsA ba/ mi dkar mi tra dzo ki /me long buddha shrI/ shing lo kha che paN chen du 'dug pa bzhin bal yul dang
rgya gar rnams su byon nas paN grub sngon ma gnyis spyan drangs pa'i rjes su/ rgya rtsis pa'i shing pho byi ba mchu zla ba'i tshes bdun la gdan 'dren pa'i ched lam du zhugs/
rgyang ro gong chung gi dge bshes rgya bla ma na re paN chen spyan 'dren pa la cum cum dang zhum zhum byas pas mi yong 'ud thag gis song gsung ba bzhin gro mor byon
paN chen phebs lam nor ba'i chom rkun dug sbrul gcan gzan sogs kyi 'jigs pa yod pa'i lam du byon kyang ci yang ma nyes par bai DUrYa'i tshong 'dus su byon/ lo tsA bas rgya
yig bris pa'i zhu yig gser gyi sher snying dang gser srang lnga sogs kyi rten bzang po dang bcas paNDi ta dza ya shrI dang wA ra NA si gnyis/ jo sras nyi ma dang khams
pa byang grags gnyis pho nyar btang / gdan 'dren pa 'ong bar mkhyen nas la drung byon kyang ma byung bas phyir ldog par brtsams pa na bang chen rnams slebs/ paN chung rnams
la ji ltar byed dri ba mdzad pas nged kyis mi shes chos rje nyid kyis mkhyen gsol ba la brten mtshams mdzad nas sgrol ma la gsol ba btab/ de'i dus rgya gar shar

phyogs kyi gnas brtan mang pos slob dpon klu sgrub kyis rab gnas mdzad pa'i sgrol ma ngo chen du spyan drangs nas gdan 'dren la byung bar/ bod kyi pho nya bas dkon gnyer kha
che bar rngan pa byin te rten gnyis zhal tshur bsgyur lo tsA ba byon pa na paN chen gyis gzhon nu 'di 'dras lo tsA ba e yong mi shes pas sems bskyed dang sgrub thabs 'ga'
zhig byin nas phyir bzlog dgongs pa la dza ya shrIs bslabs nas lo tsA bas paN chung dgu la dri ba mi 'dra ba gnyis gnyis dris pas phyi dro nas nam phyed kyi bar du song
/ chos rje'i thugs dam nar ma mang po chag kyang thugs dgyes te bod na 'di 'dra ba'i chos smra ba 'ong ba ngo mtshar che gsungs/ rim gyis phag rir phebs phyogs 'dus kyi
skya ser grangs med pa la man ngag kha 'thor mang du gsungs tshong 'dus nas chu mig gi bar du dge 'dun shin tu mang pos bskor bas khyim pa rnams kyis zhal yang lta dka'
bar gyur/ khro phur dbyar gnas mdzad pa'i tshul shing len mi brgyad brgya lhag tsam byung / brgyad stong pa dang so thar gyi lung mang du gsungs/ rtag tu ngu'i le'u la babs
pa'i tshe mchod pa'i maNDal ri mo can gyi steng du po ti bzhugs pa la mchod pa mang po byed bzhin par nub phyogs la song bas rgas khar kha cher 'gro bar 'dug gsungs/ snar
gyi glas mo cher byon nyis 'grol du gsungs pa la de bzhin nyid kyi le'u la slebs pa'i tshe chos rje'i phyag dpe brgyad stong pa'i po ti sgrol ma'i pang du byas der mchod
pa mang po byas nas shar phyogs su song bas dbus su 'gro dgos pa 'dug gsungs shing

der yang dbyar gnas mdzad/ lha sar shAkya mu ni sogs rten rnams mjal/ srin po rir dbyar gnas mdzad/ rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang dang byams chos sde lnga/ dbu ma rigs tshogs
drug sogs chos mang du gsungs/ bsam yas su lha btsun zhi ba 'od phyi mas gdan drangs mchims phu sogs gnas rnams gzigs/ srin po rir bzhugs thog rgya 'bri mtshur gsum gyi gdan
'dren byung / byams pa'i cha rkyen gyi ched du gnyal lo ro sogs yul gru mang por phebs/ chu sprel khro phu'i byams chen la rab gnas mdzad pas ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam
gyis mi khyab pa byung / sngon bla chen po'i sdom rgyun dang stod 'dul ba sogs byung na'ang bsod snyoms pa chen po 'di nyid kyis mkhan po mdzad nas byang rdor rnam gnyis
sogs bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i paN chen brgyud pa zhes 'phags yul la 'gran bzod pa'i bstan pa rma med pa'i bka' drin rgya cher mdzad jo bo stan gcig pa'i sde btsugs/ dpal
ldan sa skyar phebs dus rje btsun chen pos rdor dril nam mkha' la 'jog pa/ cang te'u sogs kyi sgra rang sgrar 'khrol ba/ rgya khab phye ltar gsol te phyir 'don pa/ dhU tI'i
rgyu ba bkag pas gza' 'dzin mi 'byung ba sogs la rgya gar na'ang 'di lta bu'i grub thob dkon zhes 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang gsan/ nyang smad rgyan gong gi gtsug lag khang
du rje btsun sa paNDi ta bsnyen par rdzogs/ bod rnams kyis bzhugs par gsol yang ma bzhed par 'bul ba'i dngos po rnams yul so so'i dge 'dun la bkye/ lo tsA bas glo bo'i
bar gdan 'dren du byon par phyag gis mi theg

pa'i gser gyi gnang sbyin mdzad/ kha cher lo bcu gnyis bzhugs nas rgyal po mu stegs par song ba nang pa'i bstan pa la bkod yul der rab byung gi sde mang du btsugs/ sngar bod
du slob ma rnams kyis dus mchod 'dzin pa'i dus mi shes pa 'dug gsol bas nam 'das pa'i dus na rdza sku rnams gas 'ong gsungs/ shing mo bya'i lo dgung lo dgu bcu rtsa dgur
phebs pa na ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te dga' ldan du gshegs so// ! bdun pa chos rje sangs rgyas ston pa ni/ rnam thar gsol 'debs tshigs bcad mar gsal zhing rje nyid
kyis zhal gyis bzhes pa bzhin yul dbus kyi sa'i cha khyung btsun rdo rje dpal yum gyi pho brang gangs kyi ri bo'i 'dabs zhol rtsa'i bsil ma zhes bya ba'i grong khyer du
ya ngal dkar po'i rus las chad pa'i g.yung drung gi ston pa sa la dbang ba gsal ba'i khri zhes bya ba nas brgyud pa rim par bon gyi ring lugs la brten nas grub pa brnyes
pa mang du byung ba'i mthar dam pa 'di nyid 'khrungs la/ 'on kyang bon la mi dgyes par chos 'ba' zhig don du gnyer bas yab mes kyi sgrub thabs gsum tsam las cher ma gsan/
dgung lo brgyad dgu lon pa'i dus 'dri klog sbyangs/ dgung lo bcu'i dus su ma gcig sprul sku la gcod dbang dang zhal gdams chig brgyud zhus/ bcu gcig dang bcu gnyis kyi
dus su 'khor ba mtha' dag sdug bsngal gyi rang bzhin can du dgongs pa'i nges 'byung gi bsam pa brtan pos dgung lo bcu gsum par bla ma rtso ri ras par rab tu byung mtshan
brtson 'grus seng ger btags/ slob

dpon sregs dum pa ras pa/ bzang yul ba/ khro phu ba/ sa skya pa/ slob dpon jo stan mkhar skya ba sogs yongs 'dzin bcu lhag gi zhabs pad nye bar bsnyen te theg pa che chung
gi zab chos mang du gsan/ bcu dgu par mkhan po chos rgyal gyi drung du bsnyen par rdzogs/ khyad par bla ma rngog ston zhes sa lo dang khro lo la dag pa mi ster ba skad byed
pa de la kun las btus pa sogs zhus/ khong mos pa'i bla ma sangs rgyas gnyan ston gyi drung du byon pa'i tshe bla ma'i zhal nas de ring rab grong nas sgom chen pa zhig
'ong bar gda' bas ayon dang dza landha ra tshun chod nas phyi'i rgya mtsho'i mtha' tshun 'geng pa'i chos bdag cig yin pas phyag bdar gyis gsungs/ mjal ba'i tshe khyod nga'i
rtsar lo gsum gyi ring ma thon pa'i gong la lung bstan byed pa'i bla ma rngog ston grong ang gsungs pas mngon mkhyen thogs med du dgongs/ khyod 'dir 'ong ba'i rgyu ci
yin gsungs par khyed sgyu lus rmi lam 'byongs shing 'od gsal mngon du gyur pa'i yi dam gyi zhal gzigs chos skyong bran du 'khol zer bas 'ongs lags pas bla ma shangs pa'i
gdams pa rnams gnang 'tshal zhus pas rje btsun ne gu ma'i thugs kyi nying khu chos drug gi dbang byin rlabs man ngag lung rgyab rten mtha' dag rdzogs par gnang nas brgyud
pa rin chen sna bdun gyi tha ma yin no zhes ngos 'dzin mdzad/ 'gro don 'phrin las kyang rgya cher bskyangs pas shangs pa bka' brgyud kyi bstan pa'i sgron me'o// !brgyad
pa kun mkhyen chos 'od ni/ bo dong du tshar chen phebs rgyu'i do nub rje mkhyen brtse'i mnal lam du kun

mkhyen chos sku 'od zer yin zer ba'i bla ma bgres po sku sha 'byor ba'i sku chas na bza' zhabs phyags sogs sang nyin rje nyid la ji lta ba bzhin 'dug gsungs pa kun mkhyen chos
'od kyi sku'i skye bar nges shes rnyed pas/ yul nyang stod gser sdings su gdung gsum pa yab kun mkhyen gzhon nu 'od/ yum mgar btsun ma shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi sras
su g.ya' ma ri'i gtsug lag khang gi 'dabs su shing khyi ston 'bring nyi ma sgra gcan gyis zin pa'i dus sku bltams mtshan bdag med rdo rjer btags/ yum gyi lad mo mdzad pas
yi ge'i 'dri klog dang kha ton rnams tshegs chung ngus mkhyen/ zhang po dang mnyam du gser sdings su chos zhu ba la byon pa'i tshe rtsed mor g.yengs pas nga'i chos 'go dang
khyod kyi rtsad 'go tshugs pa chos la mi gus sam zhes bka' bkyon pas chos rna bas nyan pa dang yan lag gis rtse ba mi 'gal zhes chos rnams shar gyis bskyar bas kun ya
mtshan zhing sngon gnas gsungs pas kha che paN chen gyi sprul par grags/ bla mas kyang yab tu zhal gyis bzhes nas de phyin chad bstan bcos kyi mdzad byang la rnal 'byor
gyi dbang phyug ces gsungs skad/ bcu gsum pa la gnas rnying du mkhan po rin chen pa la rab tu byung ba'i mtshan chos sku 'od zer du btags shing nyer lnga la bsnyen par rdzogs/
dgung lo lnga nas bcu'i bar yab kyi drung du gsang 'dus dang bde mchog sogs zab chos mtha' dag bum pa gang byor gsan/ chos rje 'jam gsar pa la gshed dmar dus 'khor
phar tshad/ 'jam rgyal la smyung gnas/ bzad ring las

mngon pa/ sa lo la sgra tshad snyan ngag sdeb sbyor bde dgyes/ bi bhU ti la 'phreng ba skor gsum/ sanggha shrI la ka tsan/ dpyal chos bzang la dpyal lugs/ lce mdo sde seng
ge la yo ga /'phags pa rin po che/ mchims chen po/ rdza chung ma sogs mkhas grub mang po bsten nas mdo rgyud kyi chos la mkhas par gyur pas kun mkhyen du grags/ lha sar jo
shAka gi drung du byon nas bshad sgom gang byas na bzang zhes gsol ba btab pas ston pa dngos su gyur te/ khyod kyis dang por brtsams pa nas zhes sogs kyis dbugs dbyung
/ hor dmag gi gnod pa byung ba'i tshe mang po'i srog bskyabs/ 'dol chung chos 'khor gyi dus mkhas pa'i snyan grags kyis khyab/ gser sdings su bzhugs nas dbang lung 'khrid
byin rlabs rgyud bshad man ngag mdo phyogs kyi gzhung bshad sogs gdul bya'i re ba yongs su bkang / sa skam po las chu 'byin pa dang mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med mnga'/
'od gsal khor yug tu 'byongs pa sogs rdo rje'i rnal 'byor mchog las nam yang mi g.yo ba'i ngang nas gdan sa slob dpon 'od zer mgon la gtad de dben gnas bya btang du don dgu
pa chu 'brug hor zla gsum pa'i nyer dgu la nam mkha' zla ba lta bu la tshom bu so gnyis 'od lngas bskor ba thal byung du gyen la 'gro ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma
dang bcas te dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so// !dgu pa kun mkhyen bu ni/ dpe khang na rgya dpe 'di 'dra yod ces dri tshad mdzad pa rnams phal cher 'grig cing / zha lu'i gdan
sar phebs dus dbu zhwa ser po bzhes dgos zhus pas 'di sngar khri 'di'i steng nas mang po zhig gyon yod

da res sa zhu rang byed gsungs kun mkhyen bu'i dus bzhes pa la dgongs shing phyis kyi mkhan po la dngos brgyud gang gi sgo nas bu'i bstan pa la 'di nyid las lhag pa ma byung
ba sogs kyis shes nus pas yul nyang ro sna bzhi zhes par gdung rabs bcu bdun par sngags rnying ma'i grub thob rim par byon pa'i brag gi gdung las yab bla ma brag ston rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang dang yum slob dpon bsod nams 'bum gyi sras su shab smad sgom gnas dgon gsar du lcags stag dpyid zla 'bring po nag pas nya ba'i nyer bzhi la sku 'khrungs/
chung ngu'i dus yum gyis shes rab bskyed pa'i thabs mang du mdzad cing 'jam dbyangs zhal gzigs/ thog mar 'da' ka ye shes la 'byor klog mdzad pa sogs 'dri klog la thogs
pa mi mnga'/ mes tshul khrims bzang po'i drung du dgung lo drug tsam nas chos rnam dag yin min gyi shan 'byed mdzad/ bdun la khro phu ba chen por sems bskyed zhus pas
byang chub kyi sems thugs rgyud la 'khrungs/ dgung lo brgyad nas rin po che khro phu bar bde mchog /mes tshul khrims bzang po la rnying ma bka' gter/ dgung lo bco brgyad
par mkhan po rin cen seng ge dpal dang slob dpon tshad ma'i skyes bu la rab tu byung / mkhan slob gnyis sogs mkhas pa du ma bsten nas phar phyin gtso bor gyur pa'i mdo
phyogs kyi gzhung 'grel mtha' dag la sbyangs pas mkhas pa'i grags pa thob/ dgung lo nyer gsum pa la gtsang tshong 'dus mgur mo'i bla brang du mkhan chen grags pa gzhon nu
dpal bzang dang slob dpon bsod nams grags pa'i drung du

bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan slob gnyis la 'dul ba'i chos du ma gsan/ chos dbar la 'phreng brag lung sogs su phar phyin dang mngon pa kun las btus sogs kyi bshad pa dang / bsgrub
bya khri phrag tu longs pa'i mkhan slob mdzad/ thar lo la sgra ka tsan/ dus 'khor/ kye rdor/ bde mchog /gshed skor/ tha snyad rig pa sogs/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge la
sa lugs nas brgyud pa'i gsang sngags kyi chos skor shin tu rgya che ba/ pha rgod pa la gsang 'dus/ rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan la dus 'khor slob dpon 'phags pa la gsang
'dus rim lnga sogs/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan la kye rdor gtso bor gyur pa'i mdo sngags kyi chos du ma gsan zhing 'chad nyan mdzad bzhin pa'i mur lcags pho spre'u'i
lo dpal zha lu gser bkang du phebs nas sde dgon mtha' dag gi gtsug gi nor bur bkur zhing mdo phyogs kyi 'chad nyan rgya che ba dang sngags chos kyang gsungs shing /
grub thob ze dmar bar bde mchog dang gshed skor sogs gsan/ jo bo rje'i phyag tsha bzhugs pa'i spel chung zhig yod pa la gzhi byas ri phug gi gtsug lag khang 'dus sde dang
bcas pa btab/ gsang sngags kyi dbang lung rgyud bshad gtso bor gyur pa'i 'chad nyan dang mdo sngags kyi bstan bcos po ti sum cur nye ba'i thugs rtsom mdzad/ sa ga zla ba'i
dus chen la rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor zhe lnga tsam zhal 'byed pa/ khyad par rnal 'byor rgyud la khro spro sgo bzhi'i gsol 'debs/ sa gar mchod gar sogs shin tu zhib
pas rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa'i srog 'thud pa ltar gyur/ bla ma chen po

bsod nams blo gros dang thugs sras sems dpa' chen po sogs che btsun mkhas grub kyi slob ma nam mkha'i skar tshogs ltar grangs yas/ sgra tshad pa sogs zhal slob rnams la rgyal
ba gnyis pa gtsong kha pa chen pos rgyud sde bzhi phal cher gsan nas dar bas mnyam med ri bo dga' ldan pa zhes shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i mtha'i bar du khyab pa'ang 'phrin
las kyi cha shas su sems/ rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi lam la brten nas spangs rtogs kyi yon tan ni bsam pa'i ra ba las brgal zhing bstan 'gro'i don rlabs po che mdzad bzhin
pa'i ngang nas shing 'brug hor zla drug pa'i nyer gcig la dga' ldan gyi gnas su byams pa'i thugs kar sku'i bkod pa bsdus so// !bcu pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs
pa chen po ni/ 'dar du zhal gyi gtor chen dus tshar chen gyi mnal lam du 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa'i lo rgyus kyis nges par nus pas bod 'dir mi'u gdung drug tu grags pa'i
nang tshan ldong gi rigs las rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen rim par byon nas dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rnams dang bla res
slob res su gyur pa'i dpon brgyud du shing pho spre'u'i lo la sku bltams/chung ngu'i dus nas sngon gyi bag chags bzang po'i mthu brtas pas yi ge 'dri klog sogs tshegs
med par mkhyen/ khu ston seng ge bzang po'i drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa nos mtshan seng ge rgyal mtshan du gsol/ kye rdor gyi dkyil 'khor du smin par mdzad/ sku na gzhon
dus gzhung lugs la sbyangs te

dgung lo bcu'i thog bsam yas su phar phyin gyi gra skor mdzad/ Teachersbco brgyad pa la dwags po'i mkhar klu bzang du dpal ldan bla ma dam pa dang mjal nas mi phyed pa'i dad
pa thob/bcu dgu pa la bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa zhus/ 'di nas bzung phal cher drung du nye bar bcar nas gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa gser chos bcu gsum
chos skyong che chung gi skor sogs dpal ldan sa skya pa'i zab chos mtha' dag bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan/ gsung ngag gi dus nyams skyon med 'ba' zhig skyes pas bla
ma dang chos la thugs nges gting nas 'khrungs pas snyan brgyud bzhi pa mos gus gzhon nu'i bde ba lta bu der snang / bla ma'i phyag dpe 'bri'dri ba sogs dang chabs cig par
gsung rgyun zin bris su mdzad pa'ang pod longs 'ga' zhig mchis/ mgon po'i thun mong min pa'i bka' babs gsum la gdung brgyud rim byon/ yar klungs pa/ bar sdings pa gsum
du mdzad pa'i klung khu dbon rnams sa lo 'jam rdor man chad kyi gdung brgyud las sa skya pa'i don gyi bstan pa 'dzin par gzur gnas shig gis ltas na 'gangs nges par che/ der
ma zad mdo rgyud kyi chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu la gsan pa mdzad/ gzhan yang kun mkhyen bu/ sems dpa' chen po thogs med pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ bla ma chen po
bsod blo ba sogs yongs 'dzin bcu phrag gsum tsam bsten nas thos bsam rgya cher mdzad/ nang bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor la brtan pa thob pas yi dam gyi lha mang po'i zhal
gzigs shing byin gyis brlabs/ dam can srung ma rnams

bran du 'khol bas mthu stobs nus pa phul du phyin/ sku'i dog cha sel ba la mgon po zhal gyi rjes gnang zhus shig pa'i brdar chos skyong A tsarYa thod 'phreng bzung bar sprul
nas khyod mi rus kyi 'phreng ba 'di bzung na khe che ste mi 'dzin pa 'dug zer/ zham ring par gtogs pa zhig gis ka ca mang po khyer ba na gzhan zhig la mon pu tra babs te
nga mnga' ris na la rtse nas 'ongs pa'i 'ba' ra yin/ pu ra yin/ rkun ma bsam yas 'ja' dkar na yod pa la khyed tsho mgo gtums nas sdod dam zer ba'i khungs ston pa sogs srung
ma rnams kyis 'phrin las mtha' dag g.yel med du bsgrub/Disciplesthugs dam zab mo'i khor yug la bzhugs pa'i thun mtshams tshor 'phags pa rin po che'i dbon brgyud slob
dpon blo gros rgyal mtshan/ gsang phu'i gdan sa pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ khyad par yab 'jam dbyangs chen po'i rtsa ba'i bla ma dbon rgyal mchog pa sogs la gser chos snyan
brgyud kyi zab chos rgya cher stsal bas deng sang gi bar du rje btsun gong ma'i bstan pa'i srog tu song / gzhan yang gdul bya so so'i blo dang 'tsham pa'i chos 'khor rgya
cher bskor/ brtag gnyis kyi TI ka dang kun rig gi dkyil 'khor sogs thugs rtsom mang du mdzad/ skabs shig mar ngo'i tshes bcu la drung chos rje pa'i dus dran gyi sgrub mchod
mdzad pa'i tshe tho rengs bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gnyis bsgoms nas cung zad 'od gsal du song ba'i ngang du srid gsum 'gran zla bral ba'i chos rje de nyid byon te 'o
'di yin te zhes pa gsung byon pas dngos su mjal ba las brgya 'gyur gyis lhag pa'i

dag snang dang / nyams sad pa na dad gdung gi yus kyis brnangs byin rlabs kyi gzi byin 'bar ba'i rkyen gyis sngar las lhag pa'i bde gsal mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin khyad par
can thugs la 'khrungs shing rim gyis rtogs pa'i yon tan gong nas gong du 'phel bar gyur/ gsang ba'i bdag po mi'i gzugs can grub chen las kyi rdo rjes sku tshe 'di'i rjes
ma bde ba can gyi zhing du 'khrungs par lung bstan pa bzhin snang ba mtha' yas kyi nyal sgom dang bde ba can gyi smon lam gyis mtshams sbyar nas dgung lo re dgu pa lcags
pho 'brug gi lo dbo zla ba'i gnam gang la 'od dpag med kyi thugs kar gshegs so// !bcu gcig pa pha rgod bsod nams bzang po ni/ tshar chen shangs zur khang du phebs dus
bris thang dang gzims khang sogs sngon gnas rjes dran gyi ngos 'dzin mdzad par snang / bla ma 'di nyid sku 'khrungs nas chung ngu'i dus tha mal pa'i spyod tshul ye mi mdzad
par 'dri klog bslab sbyangs sogs la brtson par mdzad/ yongs 'dzin mang du bsten te bstan pa'i sgor 'jug pa nas mdo rgyud kyi chos tshul du ma gsan/ khyad par sngon gyi
bag chags sad pas dpal ldan shangs pa bka' brgyud kyi bstan pa la thugs mos par byung nas 'jag chen kun dga' dpal bzang la ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu'i thugs kyi nying
khu chos drug gi smin byed spyi bka' zur bka' byin rlabs/ rtsa ba chos drug /sdong po phyag chen/ yal ga lam 'khyer/ me tog mkha' spyod/ 'bras bu 'chi med rang grol gyi
'khrid/ rgyab rten gyi lung sogs chos drug 'jag lugs la thos bsam sgom gsum

smin par mdzad/ sgyu lus 'byongs shing rmi lam la rang dbang thob pas dag pa'i zhing khams mang por bgrod cing der bzhugs pa'i 'dren pa rnams la chos zhu ba sogs lam rtags
ngo mtshar ba mang du byung / shangs zur khang du bzhugs pas zur khang pa bsod nams bzang por grags/ mchog sred rnam sprul rje btsun kun spangs chen por 'jag lugs shangs
chos stsal ba sogs mkhas grub kyi slob ma mang du byung zhing thos bsam sgom gsum gyis nyin mtshan dus 'da' ba zhig go/ !bcu gnyis pa rnal 'byor dbang mo ni/stag tshang lo
tsA ba dang dpon slob tu 'brel ba'i bag chags kyis tshar chen rin po ches sgra pa sku skye la 'jam dkar zhal gzigs ma'i rjes gnang gsan pa gnang zhing / rje btsun ma 'di
ni g.yas ru'i sa'i cha bza' shing gi ra ba sogs kyis khor yug tu bskor ba'i yul ljongs yid du 'ong ba'i khang par rje 'di nyid kyi sku zhang gi rigs su bltams nas chung
ngu'i dus gtsug lag gi yon tan 'ga' la bslab sbyangs mdzad/ srid pa'i bde ba mtha' dag me 'bar ba'i klong ltar gzigs pas bcos ma ma yin pa'i nges 'byung gi bsam pas khyim
thabs kyi bya ba dug can gyi zas bzhin spangs te shes bya thams cad mkhyen pa 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu stag tshang lo tsA ba shes rab rin cen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i
drung du rab tu byung nas tshul khrims mig gi 'bras bu ltar bsrung pas dge slong dbang mo zhes snyan pa'i grags pa phyogs kun tu khyab/dam pa de nyid gtso bor gyur pa'i
mkhas grub du ma bsten nas dbang 'khrid man ngag gi zab chos rgya cher gsan/

nang rang byung rdo rje lus kyi dkyil 'khor du rtsa khams rlung gsum thams cad dag pa ye shes kyi lha bde stong gi rol par 'char ba sogs yon tan phun sum tshogs pas ma dang
mkha' 'gro'i gtso mo mdzad pa zhig go /zhi bde'i pad 'dab 'jam mnyen mal stan las/ /sred bral sna tshogs 'gro khams tsher dong du/ /nyer 'jug snying rje'i cha gang chu shel
dbang / /lhag bsam rlung gis gdul bya'i mkha' la drangs/ /thugs bskyed nam yang mi yol rlabs 'phreng gis/ /gzhan phan gru gzings dal med rtag g.yeng bar/ /rang bder gcig
tu gzhol ba'i chu lha mo/ /khrel rgod so yi lbu ba 'khrigs pa bzhin/ /'dus gsum bgrod dka'i 'phrang las sgrol ba'i sa/ /drug mnan ring min zung 'jug phyag rgya che/ /brnyes
kyang da dung bslab pa'i zol sbyor gyis/ /gzhan 'drid sgyu thabs 'di 'dra rigs sam ci/ /sna tshogs sprul pa'i gser zhun nyag thag la/ /mkhas btsun bzang grub rin cen
brgyus pa'i rgyan/ /lung rtogs gom stabs lhod po'i sa srungs lus/ /mngon par spud las glang po phal gyi min/ /kun dga'i bde ba bskyed nus dri zhim dang / /bzhon pa'i bser
bu lho phyogs nags kyi klung / /lan brgyar myul ba'i reg byas bsnun pa'i mod/ /gyen du ldang ba'i ba spu'i rtse mo rtsub// !bcu gsum pa sku tshe 'di'i rtogs pa brjod
pa la gang du byon pa'i yul ni/ kye rdor bshad rgyud r-i ki a ra li'i rgyud las/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po 'grub byed sa bcu gsum pa mngon du byed pa la 'dzam gling chung
ngu 'di sa bcu gsum pa thob byed kyi skabs su gsungs pas gling gzhan las ngo mtshar

bar bdag med bstod par/ sbas pa'i rtsa lnga bdud bral cha dang bcas/ /snying gi dbus zhugs gtsug tor mchog tu thim/ /'phags pa'i lam lnga drug pa cha yi dngos/ /rdo rje 'dzin
pa bcu gsum sar phyag 'tshal/ /zhes byung zhing mtsho ma dros pa'i 'gram du shing dzambu tri sha'i 'bras bu rdza ma tsam pa chur lhungs pa'i sgra las dza~M zhes byung
bas gling dang shing gnyis ka la ming der chags pa'i gling 'di la shar du rgya nag dang khri brtan/ lhor rgya gar dang kha che/ nub tu stag sde dang gzig yan/ byang du khrom
dang ge sar/ dbus su bod yul gangs kyi ra ba dang dgu'o/ /zhes pa'i bod kha ba can gyi ljongs 'di/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud las/ bod kyi yul dang de bzhin du/ /mA la wa dang
pU li sogs/ /nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i yul yin no/ /zhes bde mchog tu bod 'di srung 'khor gyi gnas brgyad kyi zla tshad dang / kye rdor du gnas dang sa sbyor ba'i sa bcu gnyis
par bshad cing / bal po'i rgyal po de wa lhas khri btsun la gdams par/ nga yi snying dang 'dra ba'i bu mo khyod/ /bod ces bya ba khyad par 'phags pa'i yul/ /ri mtho sa
gtsang gangs ri gnyan gyi mgul/ /bsil la mdzes pa lha gnas gzhal yas khang / /ngo mtshar rmad byung phan bde 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /chu bo bzhi 'bab rtsi shing nags kyis mdzes/
/'bru sna lnga 'khrungs rin cen sna tshogs 'byung / /zhes phun sum tshogs pa'i yon tan khyad par du 'phags par bstan zhing / zhing sa dang khang sa gnyis te sa'i dge
/khang rdo dang chus bskor gyi rdo ste rdo'i dge /zhing chu dang 'thung chu ste chu'i dge /khang shing dang 'bud shing ste shing gi dge /gam

'brog dang rgyang 'brog ste 'brog gi dge zhes dge bcu'i yon tan yongs su tshang ba'i yul chen po 'di nyid la bod skyong ba'i rgyal po mes dbon gyi dus dbu ru dang g.yo ru/
g.yas ru dang ru lag ces ru bzhir bshad cing / tshal pa si tu'i deb dmar du sa hor mchod yon gyi dus gong ma'i lung gis phyed gsal chen mo byas skabs chu mig khri skor gyi
sa'i char gtogs pas/ gsol 'debs las/ dus 'dir mtho ris phun tshogs rgyas pa'i grong / /dpal ldan rmu zhes rab grags bsti gnas su/ /rigs rus mngon mtho'i skal bzang yab
yum gyi/ /sras su dge bar 'khrungs la gsol ba 'debs/ /rje btsun yum gyi ye shes gsal snang du/ /dpal gyi 'dab rgyas gtor ma'i 'dzum dkar las/ /ayon sku brnyan thugs kar thim
pa dang / /rgyal ba'i mchod rten gzigs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa'i bye brag yul ni rdo rje gdan nas dpag tshad brgya bgrod pa na grum stod dpal ldan sa skya/ de las
ha cang gis mi ring ba mu ku ta zhes bod skad du rnam par grol ba ste tshe gcig la grol lam rnyed pa'i gdams pa gsung ngag rin po che bod 'dir thog mar byung ba'i gnas dang
'dabs chags pa/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i sku rang byon bzhugs pa'i sa'i cha/ ba da ra'i gling bgrod kyi rtogs pa brjod pa'i yal 'dab tu/ rtse mo shin tu mtho ba yi/
/shel gyi sa gzhi mdun du mthong / /bya rnams kyis kyang bgrod dka' ba/ /'jam pa'i brag ni gcig pu der/ /zhes shin tu mtho ba'i brag ri dang spang ljongs gangs kyi rdul
mang yongs su brtsegs pa las snyan pa'i sgra lhung lhung du sgrog pa'i chu'i lha mo dbu ba'i do shal dkar po ring du 'phyang

ba'i rgyun mi chad par 'bab pa/ ne'u gsing gi ngos su bya sna tshogs skad snyan sgrog cing ri dgas rnams bag phebs par rgyu ba/ 'khrungs rabs so bzhi pa las/ de nas anda rnyil
gyi 'od ltar sngo/ /nyi ma'i 'od kyis gnam sngon bzhu ba bzhin/ /kho ra khor yug mtsho 'gram ltar mi mngon/ /gting dpag dka' ba'i mtsho 'jing nang du zhugs/ /zhes gnam
sngon zhun ma lta bu'i lcags kyi chu klung chen po 'bab pa'i 'gram dang nye ba/ rab gsal gyi rtogs brjod las/ gser gyi ba gam gzhal yas khang / /khang pas bskor ba'i grong
khyer ni/ /'od ldan zhes bya bsod nams nas/ /'od ldan mtho ris lta bu yod/ /ces 'chi med kyi gnas sa la 'phos pa lta bu'i grong khyer gyi kho ra khor yug yid du 'ong
ba'i mtha' skor kun tu sprin bzhon gyi rtogs brjod las/ bung ba'i na chung rnam sprul longs spyod ldan/ /sbrang rtsis myos shing rnam par 'byams dus der/ /me tog rab rgyas
'khri shing tshal gyi gzhir/ /rig 'dzin rgyal po'i sras ni rnam par rgyu/ /zhes kha dog sna tshogs mngon par bkra zhing dri ngad bzang po 'thul ba'i ze'u 'bru la bung ba
rnams chags pa'i glu len cing 'bras bu can sogs yal ga lo ma me tog kun nas dud pa'i ljon shing gi 'phreng ba tshar du dngar ba/ spang ljongs mar gad zhun ma brdal ba lta
bu dud 'gro rnams dal bur rgyu bas 'tsho zhing / 'bru sna tshogs yongs su smin pa'i snye ma'i tshogs mgo bo cung zad dud pa/ klu kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar du/ ha ri tsan
dan gyis byugs lus can lha yi me tog 'phreng ba rab tu 'dzin/ /nor bu'i rgyan gyi 'od dag reg pas dngas shing bkra bar bya ba'i gos dang ldan/

/grub pa'i skye bo dag dang lhan cig spel bar gyur pa'i rig 'dzin 'di dag rnams/ /tsan dan grib bsil dag la dga' ma'i 'thung lhag tu gyur chang dag 'thung bar byed/ /ces skye
bo rnams gos rgyan bzang po dang chang gis myos pas glu gar rtsed 'jo ji snyed byed la/ de yang mdo rgya cher rol pa las/ dge slong de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan
gyi gnas dam pa na 'dug pa ni rnam par lta ba chen po bzhi la rnam par blta ste/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dus la rnam par lta ba dang / gling la rnam par lta ba
dang / yul la rnam par lta ba dang / rigs la rnam par lta ba'o zhes pa'i rigs la lta tshul/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho las/ 'dzam bu'i gling ni chung ngu 'dir/ /bdag ni shAkya'i
rigs rjes 'gro/ /zhes nyi ma'i gnyen gyi brgyud rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i rig phun sum tshogs pa la gzigs pa ltar dam pa 'di nyid kyi rigs ni bod 'dir rus chen bzhir gyes
pa'i nang tshan rmu ldong stod mi nyag ste bzhi las ldong gi rigs su gtogs pa/ de yang yig tshang mkhas pa dga' byed las/ /'gro ba'i gtsug rgyan dpal ldan sa skya pas/
/chol kha gsum la kha lo sgyur ba'i dus/ /de yi 'phrin las sgrub pa'i dpon chen dang / /slob dpon dge bshes blon chen rim pa rnams/ /mkhas mchog stobs ldan grangs las 'das
mod kyi/ /thog mar lus po che yi mi gsum po/ /grum pa sa skya'i dpon chen shAka bzang dang / /shar smad btsong kha'i dge bshes rin brtson dang / /mdo stod gon gyo'i hor
che ston tshul yin/ /de gsum nang nas rigs mtho blo gtsang ba/ /dge bshes chen po nas brgyud deng

sang bar/ /bla ma'i zhabs tog dbus gtsang bya ba dang / /bkur skyong phyogs la blo gros spyan ldan zhing / /mi mthun dpung 'joms ma sangs bka' babs zhes/ /snyan pa'i grags
pa phyogs su kun khyab pas/ /blon chen 'di pa'i byon tshul 'di ltar ro/ /de'ang 'di ltar thos te/ sngon bod du chos skyong ba'i rgyal po khri srong lde btsan dang / de'i
sras bzhi pa khri lde srong btsan rgyal po'i sku ring la mtha' dmag 'gags pa'i bod yul gyi phyogs bzhir sgo bsrung ma bskos/ khyad par bod dmag khri dmag mang po khyer nas
bha ta hor gyi sgom gra bcom/ g.yul rgyal snang spyad nas phyir byon dus de phyogs kyi sgo srung ba la bod dmag slebs nas rkyen btus pa'i dpa' bo mi dgu/ dmag brgya phrag
dgu dang bcas pa hor bod kyi so mtshams su bzhag /de dus khong rnams kyis nged rnams ji tsam la log yong rgyu yin zer ba zhus pas rgyal po'i lung gis nged kyi bka' ma
byung bar ldog tu med gsungs pas/ de phyin nas dpa' bo mi dgu po'i rus ming bka' ma log zer bar chags te/ der yunaring pas bka' ma log gi bod 'brog sde tshan mang po yod
do/ /se chen rgyal po'i blon chen saM gha ching sang zer ba de yang rus pa bka' ma log tshang yin zer bar 'dug /de rnams kyi che brgyud las chad pa shar btsong kha mtsho
sngon gyi mthil na skad gsar pa bya ba dang / jag rong pas/ ku ku med bya ba yul khams chen po gsum gyi bdag po ye bzang ring mo'i sras che ba skya ming dbon po rin chen
rgyal mtshan bya ba blo gsal zhing skye mched dngas pa zhig byung ba de nyid gzhon

nu nas dkar po'i chos la mos pa zhig yod pas/ yul khams rnams mched zla kun 'dzin du bcug nas/ gtsang sa skya bla ma'i snyan grags tshor/ mos gus chug ste zhabs la gtug par
'dod nas yar byon pas mdo stod kyi hor tshe ston tshul yang chos don du gnyer ba la der ma brten sa skyar chas pa dang khong rnam gnyis bya ba lung par mjal/ mdo stod smad
kyi phyogs sred dang sku tshe sngon ma'i 'brel shugs kyi spun phu nu ltar thugs shin tu mthun par byung nas de'i dbyar gya ma 'brong du dgon par bsdad/ ston de 'gro mgon
chos rgyal 'phags pa gong nas yar phebs dus 'brong ngu dgon pa bas gdan drangs bsnyen bkur zhus/ de thog tu khong rnam gnyis pas kyang rab byung zhus dbon po'i mtshan
rin cen brtson 'grus bya bar btags/ bdag bslab gnyer mthar phyin pa zhig byed 'dod pas rjes su bzung du gsol zhus pas/ de bzhin legs/ slob dpon shar pa ye shes kyis bslab
gnyer gyi mgon gyis la dge bshes chen po zhig mgyogs par yong bar byed do gsungs pas dge bshes la snga ba rin cen brtson 'grus bya ba'ang de dus nas byung bar gda'o/ /der
gnyis kas phyags phyir byon sa skyar phebs bslab gnyer mdzad pas shes rab dang thugs rus che ba'i tshad thub par byung / ring por ma lon par sa skya'i dge bshes rnams kyi
nang nas mkhas grags thon par byung / bar skabs nas bla ma 'phags pa'i phyags phyi zhabs tog mthil bzhugs yun ring mdzad bya ba'i ljid khur chen po mang du bkal/ de mtshams
sa 'bri 'khrug pa'i 'go tshugs gong du khrims kyi gtug bsher la phyogs phyogs nas mi drag pa 'gro dgos pa byung dus dpon

chen shAkya bzang po dang / dge bshes rin cen brtson 'grus/ rin po che ston tshul gsum pos bla ma dang bstan pa gdan sa chen mo'i phyis la bsams te blos blangs nas byon/ khrims
lugs su song bas tshal gung thang nas pho brang shangs mtho'i bar la an khur nas rkang thang la byon/ gong du thug bsher legs/ sa skya pa'i bya ba rnams gang 'dod legs
par grub nas yar 'khor ba'i dus khong rnams sa skya pa la yus che ba'i mi gsum du grags pa byung zhing chen por gyur/ spyi sgos su bla ma'i gnang sbyin/ brgya stong so
sos bya dga' chen po byas/ khyad par dge bshes chen po la ja rin du sa skya'i drug phya ma'i 'dab sgo dang tshong 'dus khang leb kyi mgo byas grang khang gar/ phul gyog
gzhis ka rnams gtsang mar gnang / skya btsun thams cad kyis bkur sti zhabs tog che bar byung / de skabs su mched grogs ston tshul ba'i gros la bslab gnyer gyis dka' spyad
bshes gnyen gyi snyan grags thob/ sa skya pa gsang sngags zab mo'i bdag po yin pas da yang gsang sngags dang mthun par mdzad na sku khams kyi 'tsho skyong du'ang 'gyur/
ma 'ongs pa'i dus su'ang bu slob rjes 'dzin sogs khyad che bar yong zer ba la gsan nas/ nyang stod bye mda' ba'i ma gcig mkha' 'gro 'bum mngon chung ngu'i gyog gzhis kar
bzhag phyag rgyar bsten pa la sras gsum byung ba'i che ba ban rgan blo gros rin cen/ bar pa dharma dkon cog /chung ba dbon kun dga' rdo rje rnams byung / bar pa 'di 'gro
mgon phyag na'i sras dharma pA la rakShi ta dang lo zla zhag

dus mnyam du 'khrungs pa nas mtshan 'di chos rgyal 'phags pas btags par yang byed do/ /de'i dus na hor rgyal bu chos dpal bod 'chos la byon pa'i bsu skyel zhabs tog la dge
bshes chen po de pas 'bad rtsol bskyed pas nyi ma nub phyogs kyi bya ba rnams legs par grub nas phyir 'byon dus sog pa mdo bar skyel thung la byon par rgyal po mnyes nas
byang re thag phyir 'then gang 'dug /rin cen brtson 'grus mi brgyud dang bcas pa shes su chug cing / khyod kyis she mong 'dabs pa bzhin bu tsha bo rnams kyis kyang gong ma
yon mchod la she mong 'dabs chug zer ba'i li ji bzang po gnang / de nas dge bshes chen po sa skya'i tshong 'dus khang leb tu bde bar gshegs rting sras che ba ban rgan la
yab kyi rjes su zhugs nas khrims gnyis kyi bya ba dang sa skya'i zhabs tog /nang so'i mthil len/ dngos su bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i zhabs la gtugs she mong 'dabs par ta'i
tu'i pho brang du byon nas bla ma'i sku drin la ol jo thu rgyal pos lha rgod mdung rtse yan dang ra g.yu mtsho man 'di blo gros rin cen mi brgyud dang bcas pa shes su
chug gsung ba'i 'ja' sa gtsang ma gnang / gcung gnyis po nye ring med par bskyangs/ gcen la byang gi khri dpon dang gcung la du dben sha'i las ka zhus nas bskos/ dharma
dkon cog gi gzhi ba la ma gcig mkha' 'gro 'bum gyi zhal ta ma gcig dang / dpon kun rdor la ma gcig 'od 'bum gyi tsha mo zhig blangs pa gnyis ka la sras ma byung / ban rgan
pas zhal ta mdzad zhal ta ba re re 'og tu bzhag pa la khri dpon dharma dkon cog la sras khri dpon chos rgyal

dang dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po byung / du dben sha kun dga' rdo rje la sras khri dpon dkon cog rgyal mtshan byung / khri dpon rgyal gyis yab kyi shul du bya ru'i khri dpon
thog gcig byas sku gshegs/ sras med pas dkon cog rgyal mtshan khri dpon la bskos/ bla chen kun blo'i phyags phyir gong ma byon yan phebs jo mo sreg shing dpon mo blangs
nas mthong smon sa cha/ lha khang / spang grong gi kha 'dzin byed dus sras bzhi byung ba'i che ba dbon po dkon cog 'od zer dang dkon cog rin cen/ mkhan po bsod nams blo
gros/ chung ba rgod po rin chen rnams byung ngo / /gcung po 'di ma sangs kyi sprul pa yin pa'i rgyu mtshan ni/ 'di'i skabs su dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po pa de nyid 'brog
khri skor gyi ru thog mtsho mo ru khyung gis bskor ba sgar chen bzhugs dus chibs gar ba ston chen bya ba zhig bor nas lha 'dre mi gsum la bca' hu bkram rtsad gcod pa phyogs
bzhir btang bas/ shar phyogs pa'i mi gnyis kyis kha ba skya sib babs pa'i steng la rta rjes 'dug pa mthar ded pas shar sog la skya mo'i zhol na sgar chen zhig 'dug pa
de khrod na chibs pa yang 'dug nas mgron gnyer la rgyu mtshan bsnyad sgar 'di su'i yin dris pas sgar 'di ma sangs kyi sgar yin/ ge sar dang sgu ldi la sogs yod zer gur nang
du khrid sgu ldi yin zer ba de na re/ nged kyis kha sing nas byang stong sa la yongs dpon chen pa dang mjal rtsis la ma phrad/ da bzod khyed kyi dpon po zhig yod pa de
dang yang yang phrad zer ba gyis la/ rta dang mda' rgod sgro ma 'di phul zer nas khyer yongs/ dbon

chen pa la phul de rting dpon po rgod po rin cen pa 'khrungs so/ /dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po pa de nyid ti shrI kun rgyal ba'i zhabs la gtugs gong la phyags phyir byon/ bla
ma'i sku drin dang khrims kyi bya ba la mkhas pas sngon ma dpon chen shrI ming dang de rting dbus gtsang dpon chen sngon ma thog mar phebs dus ban rgan pas zhal ta mdzad/
jo mor bla ma mus chen pa'i dpon mo dang / dpon mo jo mo rim par blangs na'ang sras ma byung ba zhal ta ma 'bum rgyan bya ba la sras grags pa rgyal mtshan pa byung zhing
/ rting ma zur sras dpon po hor tsha ba bya ba zhig kyang byung / dpon chen pas dbon po dkon cog 'od zer byang khrid dpon la bskos/ sras po grags pa rgyal mtshan pa sa
skya nang sor bzhag /dbus gtsang sde la bkod nas dpon po dkon cog rin chen phyags phyir khrid yongs gong ma mchod yon gyi drung du byon snga rting dril bas lo bco brgyad
tsam gong du bzhugs/ swon jing dben gyi rtsa ba'i dpon chen mi shangs len gsum mdzad/ lung gu ta hu'i zon gnang / yar 'byon khar nga'i sgra ber khyung gsum gyi tshong ba
bod la lo re bzhin yong ba'i 'bab sa'i gnas gzhi zhig brtsig dgos zhus pas gang 'os tshol gsungs par shangs nang g.ye dmar sgang brgyud nas sa che bar 'dug pas 'di dgos
zhus pas gye re bab lha gdong yan/ thag ma ngal gdong / dang ra shing gcig man gyi sa cha/ rgyal ba bzang po'i rta sga 'bogs la byin zhing / de khongs gang 'os su gnas gzhi
brtsig tu chug gsungs pa'i lung bzang po gnang bas yar phebs nas shangs mthong smon gyi sa 'di na chu

gnas pa'i rdzing zhig 'dug pas ming dang gang sa nas rten 'brel legs pas 'di khongs su chug pa gyis gsungs/ lcags ri spel lcog rnams dkyil du khang leb chen po dang bcas pa
btab/ de rting gong ma yon mchod kyi sku rim smon lam 'debs shing spos sreg pa'i lha khang zhig bzhengs su 'jug pa dgos zer ba'i zhu ba gong du btang bas/ de bzhin yin chug
gsung ba'i lung phebs nas myug rgyal khang rgyal po'i pho brang la dpe blangs pa bzhengs/ chos sde 'di sngon bod rgyal blon dus kyi ka ca rnying pa dang / ri rting ma
ma'i dgon lag rnying pa dar cha med pa zhig 'dug pa'ang dpon chen pas rgyal khang bzhengs pa dang mnyam du/ so paNDi ta 'jigs med grags pa chos dpon la gdan drangs sgos
kyi mnga' zhabs la btsun khral thengs gnyis brgyab nas bshad grwa btsugs chos sde'i she mong bskyed/ chos khrims dar bar mdzad/ yab yum gyi phyi rten la g.ye dmar sgang stod
du sku 'bum chen mo bzhengs zha lu bu ston rin po che gdan drangs nas rab gnas dbus gtsang du rgyas pa'i dpe thub pa mdzad de/ lung gis bskos pa'i dpon chen gnyis byang
ba'i phyag tsha ba gcig dang bcas pas gong dang dbus gtsang du dpon chen thengs gsum mdzad pa de bar la/ gdan sa chen po'i zhabs tog /bla ma la bkur sti/ mnga' zhabs kyi
skyong dar/ phag gru khri dpon dang mkhas pa la sogs khrims 'gal mu med byed mkhan rnams la drag las kyis 'jun 'dur/ gzhan yang rgyal khrims chen po'i bya ba gang la'ang
nye ring med cing blang dor ma 'dzol bar

byung bas kun gyis byang chub sems dpa'i dpon chen du grags shing / gong nas rting la phebs rjes la sras blo gros rgyal mtshan pa byung ba/ gcen dpon grags rgyal ba dang dgung
lo bcu bdun bco brgyad kyi khyad yod pas na grags rgyal ba'i sras yin par byed pa'ang yod la/ khong rnam gnyis kyi bar du dbon po hor tshas dpon thog tu lo gcig gnyis
bzhugs zer ba'ang gleng / dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po pas khrims las kyi bya ba dpon chen dbang brtson la 'phrod pa'i skabs su lha rtse'i gzims khang lho mar bde bar gshegs
so/ /pur bzhu dus thugs thugs thag dang bcas te byon pa de gzims khang gung ldebs ris la chos rgyal 'phags pa'i sku 'dra bzhugs pa de'i thugs kar thim pa kun gyi mthun
du grub bo/ /phyi skor gyi dpon chen la 'di nyid bla ma la gus shing khrims gnyis kyi bya ba mkhas par byed do/ /dpon chen pa'i sras po grags pa rgyal mtshan pa snga sor
sa skya nang chen bzung rting la dpon chen gyi ming thob shangs mthong smon bzung ba'i skabs der sku gshegs so/ /gcung po dpon po hor tsha'i sras sna dkar ba dpon kun dga'
rgyal po brgyud chad/ blo gros rgyal mtshan pas si tu'i ming dang las ka thob/ dpon chen pas dbon po 'di dang mthong smon sbrags nas ta'i si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan
la sprad/ gtsang phyogs kyi sde pa dar lcogs dkar po 'dzugs pa'i sngon ma byas zer ba'ang 'dug /'di'i ring la mthong smon spel chen bzhengs/ sgo spe zur cog rnams kyi kha
sgron 'obs lcags chung ba bzos so/ /de'i sras bzhi'i che ba du dben

sha byang chub rgyal ba dpal bzang po ba lhog thung du grags pa thugs rgod cing rtsom rkyen pas de'i ring la rdzong shangs dang phyi nang gi sde 'khrug mang / de 'og mkhan
po kun dga' blo gros pas myug chos sde'i mkhan po mdzad/ de 'og tu dben sha kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas rgyal mthong bzung kun dang mthun pa'i lugs shes che bar byung / gcung
po chung ba dbon po kun rdor ba'o/ /du dben sha kun rgyal bas gdung brgyud lcam blangs pa la sras gcig byung ba du dben sha rin cen rgyal po ba sku brtan par bzhugs pa'o/
/khri dpon dkon cog 'od zer bas byang ru thog gi khri dpon mdzad cing / dpon po dkon cog rin cen dang rgod po rin cen pas myug rgyal khang gi 'go byas dre sgal sogs 'dzin/
mkhan po bsod nams blo gros pas zhang po'i gdan sa sreg shing mkhan po mdzad pa'i skabs su mthong smon na dpon chen grags rgyal ba yod pa/ dpon skya g.yog ris kyi dbang
du song nas shangs pa nang ma bde/ dpon po sku mched che ba gnyis sku gshegs rting dbon po rgod po rin cen pas stag tshang rdzong khar bla chen bsod blo sku mched pa'i
zhabs la gtugs/ rgyab bcol nas rdzong shangs bde gzar yun ring / dgung lo bco brgyad pa la bla chen pa'i phyags phyir las chen g.yas ru byang nas gong la byon/ bla ma'i
sku drin la tho gan the mur rgyal pos phing gcig pa'i mi dpon/ hwing swon jing dben gyi hu shrI'i mtshan dang dam rtags/ ban rgan blo gros rin cen pa'i dus ji ltar gnang
ba bzhin gyi bod 'brog dbang

ris rnams rgod po rin cen hu shrI mi brgyud dang bcas pa la 'jags su chug gsung pa'i lung bzang po dang bcas gnang / yar phebs bla ma sku mched pa'i zhabs tog sde pa stag tshang
rdzong pa'i phyi'i dgra bzhi la dmag dpon gyi bya ba gang la'ang sde pa'i mtshan jus gtso bor bton nas/ dpon sa nas kyang thag rta nag gi gnyer kha gnang / sna dmar
rdzong brtsigs/ shangs pa nang ltar gyi bde gzar 'pho 'phyugs mang na'ang phyi nang sus kyang rgol bar ma nus pas rgod pa'i snyan grags shin tu che zhing pho stag lo la
rdzong stag sna don grub rtse bzung ste de'i char gtogs pa'i mnga' zhabs bod 'brog mang du chod nas da lta'i bar la brtan zhing 'phel ba dang bcas pa yin no/ /de la yum mi
gcig pa'i sras po gsum byung ba'i che ba rta nag pa dpon po shAkya rin cen/ bar ba byang ngam ring pa rgyal ba rin cen/ chung ba skyor mo ba sog po rin cen rnams te/ shAkya
rin cen pas yab kyi gnyer las kyi rjes rta nag bzung / de la sras dug tsher rin cen dang / nam mkha' rin cen/ dge sbyong dkar por grags pa rnams so/ /rgyal ba rin cen
pa la sras rnam rgyal rin cen pa dang dpal ldan rin cen byung ba gnyis ka yab kyi sngon la 'das so/ /sog po rin cen pas lha bu khong lam rdzong gsar brtsigs/ sras rgyal
po rin cen pa dang dge sbyong bsod nams rin cen pa/ grags pa rin cen pa rnams byung ngo / khri dpon dkon cog 'od zer ba sku mched phyogs gcig pa'i dus kyi sras po gcig byung
ba drung chen glang po rin cen pa/ de nyid yab

grongs pa'i rjes la stag tshang rdzong khar 'khrungs/ dpon sa bla brang du khu bo rgod po rin cen pa 'tsho skyong mgo 'don yang dag mdzad/ cher skyes nas dbang grags pa rgyal
mtshan pa'i zhal mthong / dbang rnam sras pa'i zhabs la gtugs gzims dpon mdzad/ khu dbon phyogs gcig tu dril nas dgra 'dul gnyen skyong dpon sa'i zhabs tog bur rta'i gsog
rum skyong dar 'jig rten gyi bya ba gang la'ang shin tu mkhas shing thugs rtsol che bas grags pa phyogs kun khyab bo/ /khyad par dbus pa bdag po grags pa rgyal mtshan
pas phag mo gru pa srid la gtogs pa'i dbus gtsang gi dmag dpung stobs che ba bsdus nas me pho khyi lo ston stag sna rdzong la skor rgyag yun ring byas/ nang yan 'tshag skyel
bred sdigs ji snyed cig byung nas yab sras dpon g.yog rnams kyis legs par sra bcas phur btsugs 'thab srol sprad pas dbus gtsang du mkhregs pa'i tshad thub pa byung rting
stan shar gtsang srid du grags pa'i 'go de nas btsugs pas sa skya pa'i bstan jus yar 'phel du byung ba blon chen de nyid kyi thugs bzhed dang 'phrin las brten pa'o/
/de'i sras lnga'i che ba drung chen nam mkha' rin cen pa ni sku gzhon nu nas klog yig sogs bslab shes kyi yon tan mtha' dag mngon du phyogs nas mi dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan
pa dang / mes po hu shrI chen po'i zhabs la gtugs gsol ja bzung / pho rtsal sna dgu bkur skyong 'grogs lam sde srid 'dzin pa'i bya ba la yon tan sgor mor 'dzom pas
kun gyis ma sangs sprul par 'dzin cing

khyad par khyi lo dmag chen gyi dus rdzong gi rtse zhol srung ba gang khag pa thams cad du phebs nas sgyogs mda' rdos nang sprad pas gshin rje ngo dmar du grags shing phyi
nas gdong len mi su yang med pa byung ngo / /gzhan yang dmag che chung 'thab srol snga phyi mang po'i 'go la byon nas dus nam yang gdong 'bud ngo lang kho na mdzad cing phyis
skor bya ba gang la'ang gtan brling gtso bor bton pas phyi nang kun gyis 'di ni dpa' mdzangs 'dzom pa'i skyes bu chen po yin zhes grags so/ /de'i gcung po rgyal bzang
rin cen/ rgya mtsho rin cen/ nor bu rin cen/ grub pa rin cen rnams yin la/ gcung 'dis rdzong rab 'byor rtse bzung tshar shwon bod 'brog gsar du chod/ gcen gyi khab tu gdung
brgyud lam mo byang sems nam mkha' rgyal mo ba byon sras che ba chos rgyal rin cen pa mched gsum ste/ sku mched khu dbon zhal ngo yang mang la rags pa sku brtan par
bzhugs par lags pa/ blon chen che brgyud ma sangs sprul pa'i rigs/ /kha drag mi dpung 'dzom pa 'khor bcas 'di/ /phas rgol mi mthun phyogs las rgyal ba dang / /dpal 'byor
yar ngo'i zla ltar rgyas gyur cig /ces byung ba'i mes drung chen nam mkha' rin cen yan chad shangs pa yin na'ang / de nas la stod du gzhis bzung ba yin cing / de yang chos
rgyal rin cen dpal bzang zhes yi dam gyi lhas rjes su bzung zhing dpal mgon stag zhon bran du 'khol ba'i mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug de'i jo mor mkha' 'gro'i rigs can/ bon
po dben rtsa kha pa'i sras mo bkra shis a mtsho zhes pa sngon gyi las 'phros chos

la mos pa dkon cog la bla mar 'dzin cing dge 'dun la rnyed bkur dang ngan long la sbyin gtong brtson pa/ byams pa dang snying rjes rgyud dul ba/ khyad par stag tshang lo tsA
bar shin tu dad cing / de nas brgyud pa'i chos nyams su len par gzhol ba de gnyis dam pa 'di dang lcam sring lnga tsam gyi yab yum yin cing / tshes bcu'i dus chen zhig
la sangs rgyas kun 'dus rdo rje drag po rtsal gyi 'phrin las gyer ba'i nub yum gyis dpal gtor phyogs la dbu sngas bstad de gzims pa na mnal lam du dpal gtor gyi pad 'dab
gcig chad pa'i rnam pas sgo dbye ba lta bu byas/ de'i nang nas gu ru rin po che'i sku yid du 'ong ba 'od zer dang bcas pa zhig seng ge la bcibs te thal mar byung nas thugs
kar thim pa dang / yang nub cig stag tshang lo tsA ba dpon slob nas nged tshor do nub gnas tshang dgos 'dug pas nang sor zhus pa'i sdod yul g.yor gsung pa ltar sta gon
mdzad pa'i tshe bla ma de 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rnam par gyur pa thugs kar thim pa'i snang ba byung / mnal sad tsa na lus shin sbyangs kyi bde ba lta bur yug cig lus
pas zhal ta ma zhig gis da bzhengs/ las thebs 'chag zer bas nyams de sad kyang de nyin gyi phyag las mtha' dag sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i bde ba de ka'i ngang du 'gro ba zhig
byung / gnas pa de nam byung ba'i dus dngos su me tog gi char/ 'ja' dkar po/ sngar tshor ma myong ba'i dri bzang po 'thul ba yong zhing / yang mnal lam du mi zhig gis g.yu
ster ba/ gser gyi mchod

rten 'od zer 'phro bar khrus gsol zhing skor ba mdzad pa sogs dam pa 'di lhums su 'jug pa'i ltas ngo mtshar ba mang du byung / 'khrungs lo ni 'o skol gyi ston pa drag po zhes
pa lcags sprel la sku bltams nas lo nyis stong lnga brgya bcu bdun 'das pa 'phags pa'i yul du stod 'grel pa'i lugs kyi rjes su 'brangs te dundu bhi zhes pa rnga chen du
grags shing shar phyogs rgyal po'i khab tu zhin zu'i zhes chu pho khyi lor 'jig rten yongs grags dang bstun na 'thad cing gtsug lag dang bstun na khrag skyug ces pa chu
mo phag gi lo'i dus kyang mdzod rang 'grel du/ sangs rgyas pa rnams kyi dus kyi dang po ni dgun no/ /gnyis pa ni dpyid do/ /gsum pa ni dbyar ro/ /zhes 'dul mngon pa rnams

grogs/ /sbrang rtsi 'thung ba rnams kyi gnyen/ /skal bzang 'khri shing 'khyud byed pa/ /legs ldan dpyid ni mthong bar gyur/ /ces dpyid zla 'bring po nya ro hI ta'i khyim

gyi/ /grags pas rgyu skar tshogs rnams blta ba bzhin/ /'jam dpal rdo rje 'phags pa'i zhabs pad rdul/ /dmar 'od gtsug tu lhungs pa'i yus po che/ /bstan srid bla nas blar

rnams la bar chad sel ba'i bka' bsgo 'phrin bcol la brten nub cig mnal lam du sku smad la sgra tshal g.yogs 'dug pa'i ngang la g.yag khyu chen po byung bar ya nga ba'i
snang ba shar ba'i tshe de khrod nas g.yag chen po zhig gis nged tsho khyed la gnod pa skyel du 'ongs pa min zer nas rwa rtses sbra tshal blangs nas phyir bsal song ba dang
/ yang skabs shig bud med cig gis sa la ri mo 'ga' zhig bris pa'i grangs brtsis nas lo 'di'i bar zhabs kyi snyun ro cung zad langs yong de nas gzhi med du 'gro zer ba
kho na ltar byung ba g.yag rnams dregs pa pho brgyud dang bud med de mo brgyud kyi rnam 'phrul te bstan

srung rnams kyis 'phrin las bsgrubs par snang / slar bkra shis lhun por skor tsam phebs nas mdo phyogs kyi thugs gnyer 'phro 'thud/ tshad ma'i bshad pa dang zhal blangs kyi
skabs rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras 'di ltar bzhed ces grub mtha' zur khyad yang yang gsungs pas der tshogs rnams kyis chos rje tshar pa 'di rang re'i chos grwar 'grims
pa tsam ma gtogs don la sa skya pa yin 'dug ces ma rangs pa byas skad/ snga dro zhig bkra shis lhun po'i khron pa chen po'i thad der phebs pas bud med lang tsho dar la babs
pa sma ra dang smin ma se khyug ge ba byas pas khyed la rje rdo ring pa'i gsung las kha'ur myur du byon gsung gi gda'/ de'i lag rtags 'di yin zhes glegs bam chung ngu
zhig gtad nas gar song cha med du yal song ba dpe de mkha' spyod skor gsum gyi be'u bum yin 'dug mi 'gyangs par rdo rje theg pa'i smin grol gyi gdams pa rnams nyan pa legs
pas 'dir byon zhes kha'u skyes lhas nas rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po'i phyag tham byung ba na rje btsun mi la rje mar pa'i drung du byon pa lta bu'i dga' spro bsam gyis
mi khyab pa dang bcas grum stod kha'u brag rdzong du sang phebs rgyu'i do nub nam phyed tsam la mgon khang gi sgo brdungs nas sang chos skyong sogs man ngag rnams kyi snod
tshar pa yong ba yod zer ba gsan pas sang nang par rdo ring rin po ches mdang 'di bzhin byung bas de ring khong 'byor pa 'dra gsungs/ sku 'khor ba zhig gis byung tshul
snyan du gsol bas khong yul mnyan pas stan legs pa zhig thing gsungs 'phral du

sku zhabs su btang ba'i tshe ras yug dkar po sne tshang ba'i mjal dar phul/ chos rje'i drung phebs lam la 'o mi brgyal zhing bde bar byon pa bka' drin che gsungs/ sngon nas
zhal mjal zhing thugs mos che ba'i steng bshes springs las/ rdo thal gyis byugs dgung zla'i 'od kyis ni/ /ches dkar nyid du ci ste mi bgyid lags/ /zhes snga rabs kyang ches
cher lhag pa'i thugs mos 'khrungs bkra shis lhun po'i khron pa kha'i gnas tshul zhus nas dpe de gzigs phul bas bzhad mo mdzad pa dang sbrags pa~X'i mkha' spyod mas gdan
'dren la phyin gda' ba glegs bam 'di'ang de'i chos skor yin/ da re zhig dpe khrod du skyol mdzod gsungs pa bzhin phyag dpe'i khrod du skyel bar phebs pas dpe rags brtsigs
pa'i gseb nas dpe de gton shul har re 'dug pa der bcug pas khrig 'grig song bas dad pa dang ngo mtshar dpe gang gis kyang mtshon du med pa thob pa'i gsung sgros gnang
ba lam yig tu lar 'di skor gyi gtam mang po zhig yod kyang gsang ba'i don du mngon/ phyi ltar du zhing skyong dbang po mngon sum du bzhugs pa'i dben gnas kha'u brag rdzong
gi rnal 'byor spyod pa'i 'dus sde rnams mdzes pa'i rgyan/ nang ltar du lha sngags ye shes kyi nus pas rdo rje'i chos skyong mtha' dag bran du 'khol ba'i mthu stobs kyi
gad brgyangs srid rtse'i bar du sgrog pa'i dpa' bo/ /gsang ba ltar na bde stong zung du 'jug pa'i sgyu ma'i gar gyis dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho spro ba dang bsdu ba'i byed po
khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' dngos dpal ldan bla

ma dam pa 'di'i zhabs pad yun du bsnyen pa'i ched du don med kyi g.yeng ba'i 'du 'dzi thams cad rgyang du bsrings/ bgrang bya du mar bag phab ste bzhugs nas dam pa'i chos kyi
bka' drin nod pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu 'brog mis 'phags pa'i yul du paN grub shrI lendra ru tsi'am slob dpon mi thub zla bar grags pa la rtsa ba med pa'i lam 'bras

phal cher gyi mig dang rna ba'i spyod yul du ma gyur pa gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis yab 'jam dbyangs chen po dang / rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang pos 'khor lo sdom pa dkon cog rgyal mtshan kho nar stsal ba chu bo gnyis 'dres kyi tshul du thugs kyi bum pa gtams pa las nye bar 'ongs pa snyan brgyud slob bshad
kyi nyams 'khrid zab mo lan grangs gsum gyi bar du smin rgyas su gsan pa'i cha lag dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyu dus kyi dbang / bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang / de'i sindhU
