phyug gi thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i

byin rlabs/ bla ma rin 'byung dang tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ brda chig brgyud/ gsang bcu'i rgyas btab/ sgrub pa lung sbyin sogs lam 'bras la brten pa'i dbang byin rlabs
nyi shu/ de dag gi rgyab chos su gsung ngag bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar/ gsung ngag gi glegs bam gnyis/ gzhan yang dbang gi chu bo chen po sogs rje btsun gong ma'i gsung
mang po dang rje rdo rje 'chang chen po yab sras gnyis dang bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i yi ge sogs rje nyid la gang bzhugs pa thams cad bum pa gang
byo'i tshul du gsan pa yang / deng sang khyi dang glo ba lta bur thug phrad byed pa'i lugs dang ye mi 'dra bar bla ma la yun ring po nas gsol ba btab/ gser gyi maNDal dang
mkha' 'gro lnga mnyes par byed pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgya cher bskor ba snyan brgyud dang po'i rten 'brel/ so so'i thad du nges par dgos pa'i dbang byin rlabs lung rnams
tshang bar gnang ba snyan brgyud gnyis pa'i rten 'brel/ snang gsum nas bzung dbang bzhi pa'i bar gyi 'khrid rnams bla mas kyang dmar 'khrid du bstan slob mas kyang rgyud
la myong thon ma byung gi bar bsgoms pa snyan brgyud gsum pa'i rten 'brel/ de la brten nas snyan brgyud bzhi pa'i rten 'brel bla ma la rdo rje 'chang dngos kyi mos gus
skyes shing sgro 'dogs thams cad cig car du chod/ /nyams dang rtogs pa'i mtsho rdol rten 'brel thams cad rang 'grig tu gyur pas mos gus gzhon nu'i bde ba lta bus thugs
rgyud tshim pas tshad ma bzhi dang snyan brgyud bzhi'i bdag

por gyur to/ /deng sang tshogs bshad pa rnams bar do sogs kyi 'khrid glegs bam dngos bstan la med ces blor mi shong yang 'jam mgon sa paN gyis/ 'on kyang rten 'brel zab mo'i
gnad/ /da dung kun gyis rtogs par dka'/ /glegs bam tsam la brten pa yi/ /lam 'bras pas kyang 'di mi shes/ /zhes glegs bam la ma brten pa'i snyan brgyud yod pa ma go ba'i
skyon yin la/ gal te tshe 'dir ma grol zhing 'da' kha ma yang gnad du ma song ba'i rigs la bar dor 'o brgyal nges par 'byung bas/ dbang po rab la'ang ltos sa ltos 'jog
gi rab 'bring tha gsum 'byung bas rtsi lugs shes dgos shing 'khor 'das dbyer med la bshad lung yam me ba las ma byung bas sa skya pa'i dge bshes chen por rloms te sems ngo

pa de 'di yin pa 'dug /

su blangs tsam nyid nas mtshan rtog gi dri ma bral ba'i phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes myur du 'char la/ dam chos kun gdul bya'i blo khrid las/ /phyogs 'dzin gyi grub mtha'

la 'gram chu mi ldang ba zhig yod pas/ lam glur/ rje rdo ring pa dang mjal nas bla ma dang chos gzhan la brten nas sangs rgyas sgrub bsam pa med gsung ba'ang don 'di

po/ 'dod

rgyal ste dmar chen skor gsum gyi thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs rjes gnang lung man ngag /snying gi gser thag /ti nu/ nor rgyun ma ste dmar chung skor gsum/
dzam dmar srog sgrub/ 'dzam nag /seng ge sgra/ 'chi med rdo rje'i lha mo/ seng gdong ma/ tshe dpag med dkar po yum bcas sogs gser chos skor/ bstan srung rgya mtsho'i sde
dpon rdo rje nag po chen po la bka' babs bzhir bzhugs pa'i skor nas gsang 'khrid dang bran bdud kyi rjes gnang thun mong min pa dkyil 'khor gyi dbang rnams ma gtogs lha

brten nas sgrub pa/ nang rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga la brten nas sgrub pa/ gsang ba yang gsang sems nyid la brten nas sgrub pa'i snying por gyur pa nang 'khrid yar klungs
pa dang / gsang 'khrid gnyis/ rdo rje brag rdzong ma phyi nang gsang gsum gyi 'khrid/ rgyab rten gyi yi ge mgon pod me 'bar ma/ der ma 'dus pa'i rgwa a rnyan dam pa yar klungs
pa bar sdings pa gsum gyi yi ge sogs shin tu zab pa'i yig sna dang / yi ger ma 'khod pa zhal nas zhal snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa'i gdams pa mtha' klas pa dang thun

thugs sras kun spangs rje/ /kho bos gtsug gi

rgyan du bsten/ /ci gsung bka' rnams 'bad pas bsgrubs/ /skyabs gzhan spangs nas gcig tu dril/ /de yi mthu las thugs rje'i rgyun/ /bka' drin bdud rtsis snying myos pa'i/ /tshul
bzhin shes pa kho bor gda'/ /zhes gsungs/ gsang 'khrid kyi rjes gnang dang gsang 'khrid dngos gzhi/ las bzhi'i mgon po'i rjes gnang sogs kha shas ma gtogs dpal mgon stobs
'phrog dbang po gdong bzhi pa'i rjes gnang spu gri so rdeb dang tshe sgrub srung 'khor gyi 'khrid las tshogs yig chung shog dril/ der ma 'khod pa snyan nas snyan du
brgyud pa'i gdams pa sogs tshang bar gsan/ zhal gyi rjes gnang skabs rje nyid kyi sku'i mdangs na bza'i kha dog sogs mthing khar gzigs shing khyad par ye shes dbab pa'i bar
la bar snang nas mi rkang gi sgra shin tu gsal ba dang phun sum tshogs pa mnga' ba gser gyi ri bo 'dra zhes sogs bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad dbyangs dang bcas nas sgrog
pa gsal bar gsan/ khyad par mgon po gdong brnyan can gyi rjes gnang gsan pa'i tshe phyag mdzad pa nas bzung 'jigs pas sku lus kyi tsho mi thub pa lta bu dang ye shes dbab
dus mgon khang rdib pa 'dra ba dang kha'u'i ri thams cad nyil ba bzhin gyi tshag sgra 'ur sgras khyab pas re zhig thugs dran med du song / thugs dran rnyed tshe gnas lugs
don gyi mgon po rang rgyud la shar ba'i bde ba chen po byin rlabs kyi chu bo ma nub pa yin gsung byung ba na bla ma'i zhal la gzigs par mi bzod pa 'jigs su rung ba

zhig tu shar zhing snyun ro sogs bgegs kyi rnam pa 'dra ba'ang sangs/ man ngag g.yul las rnam rgyal gyi las sbyor mdzad pas zhag 'ga' nas bsgral bya de pu tras dngos su khrid/

po/ dkar bdud sogs sa skya pa'i zab chos su grags pa'i dbang lung du ma/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang byin rlabs spros med kyi 'khrid/ 'jigs byed rwa lugs/ nag po mtsho

yig skor gyi lung tshang la ma nor bar gsan/ su kha siddhi'i dbang dang de dag dang 'brel ba'i yig sna/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa rgya gzhung dang bcas pa sogs mdor na rje btsun

mchog thun gyi dngos grub sna tshogs pa 'bad med du rnyed pa'o/ /gsol 'debs las/ slar yang grum stod kha'u'i lam bgrod tshe/ /bstan srung rnams gnyis dzo ka'i zol gyis 'ongs/
/pho nya'i tshul du mkha' la zhabs bskyod de/ /gegs med 'phrin las bsgrub la gsol ba 'debs/ /nam yang 'bral med ltos par bcas pa kun/ /rje btsun bla mas skyong bar zhal
bzhes shing / /chos kyi 'phrin las 'khor lo sgyur ba yi/ /rgyal tshab mchog tu bsngags la gsol ba 'debs/ /'chi med bdud rtsi bsgrub pa'i bka' gnang zhing / /dbang bskur
dam tshig rdo rje dril bu gtad/ /gzhal med sku gdung yid bzhin dbang po las/ byin rlabs bdud rtsi bzhes la gsol ba 'debs/ /'od gsal dbyings las bzhengs pa'i mdzes sku yi/
/ngo mtshar gsung gi snang bas lung bstan cing / /sngon nas 'brel ba'i mkha' spyod dga' ma des/ /dgyes pa'i 'dzum zhal bstan la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa/ de nas rmu gshong
du yab yum mjal ba sogs la phebs/ ring por ma lon par rdo rje 'chang kun spangs chos rje'i drung du phebs rtsis kyis gzhis nas chibs thog tu khyon pa nas bzung kha'ur
ma byon par A tsarYa gzi brjid can gnyis kyis gar bsgyur zhing sku'i g.yas g.yon skyor ba'i tshul gsal bar gzigs pa mgon po che chung gnyis sku lus dang grib ma bzhin 'bral
med du bsrung skyob mdzad cing 'phrin las bsgrub pa'i mtshan mar gsal/ dgung lo bcu bdun nas zhabs pad bsten pa'i dbang

du byas na lo ngo bdun tsam dam bcar bzhugs lo drug gi ring mdzad par kun spangs chen po'ang de bar zab chos rnams 'phrod pa gnang nas mkha' spyod du gshegs par bzhed pa'i

lo nyer gsum du phebs pa shing pho sprel lo skye 'chi la rang dbang 'dus pa'i dbang gis rje btsun rdo ring chen po de nyid zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i gsung 'ga' shas phebs
pa'i tshe/ bka' las bdag gis sbyir bstan pa dang sems can gyi don dang lhag par bdag cag mgon skyabs gzhan med pa'i 'gro ba rnams la thugs brtse ba chen pos dgongs nas

med du bsgoms na bla ma 'bral med du

yong ba yin gsung ba dang / nged bka' gdams pa'i jo bo rje'i gsung las/ sbrul gyi pags pa brjes kyang sbrul mi 'chi/ /kho bo 'chi tshul bstan kyang a ti sha /gsungs pa bdog
pas de dang 'dra/ khyed dad pa yod pa rnams la ni nga dang 'du 'bral med pa yin/ khyed tsho rkyang par ma zad khyod tsho la blo bstad pa tsho'ang ngas skyong ba yin/ ha
cang chos rje'i dgongs pa la bla ma'i stong 'ur la dgongs pa yong ste/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba'i gsung sgros bris pa las/ bla ma de mnar med na bzhugs kyang rang gis sangs rgyas

tshul ni seng

ge rtse ba'i mnga' thang myur du 'jig pa/ rje nyid kyi sku tshe'i tshad/ snod ldan gyi slob ma rags rim yong ba dang chos ston pa'i dus tshod/ sku tshe phyi ma'i skor sogs
kyi lung bstan shin tu rgyas pa yod 'dug kyang deng sang zin bris sogs gsal bar mi snang / rdo rje dril bu sngar thugs bed spyad pa'i legs pa zhig gnang ste chos rje rang
'di dkrol nas dbang bskur gzhan don rgya chen po mdzod cig gsungs/ gzhan dngos po'i gnang sbyin gyi rigs zhu yi med 'dug kyang da lam sku khams hreb pas rten 'brel 'phyugs
dogs zhu ba mdzad/ nyin gcig sku srung khrod nas 'phags pa dang bdag chen rin po che gnyis kyi bdud rtsi ril bu dang sgrub yig bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa gnang
/ rje btsun rin po che'i bdud rtsi'i phabs rgyun dang sgrub snod rnams bla brang shar par yod pas sku nye yin gshis g.yar po mdzad na yong / bdag chen rin po che'i bdud
rtsi ril bu 'di khar song na skye ba bcu gnyis tshun la sangs rgyas thob pa'i lung bstan thengs gsum byung / bdag la sgrubs shig par bka' stsal kyang ma grub khyed kyis
sgrubs shig ces sku dpung steng du phyag gis cab cab mdzad byung bar/ sngar sems dpa' chen po la'ang thog mar mdzad dka' byung ba'i 'phros 'dug pas bdag gis mi 'ong ngam
zhu ba gnang bar yig cha 'di gsal po yin pas 'di steng nas mdzad na 'grub gsungs/ hor zla bcu pa'i tshes bco lnga la kun spangs chen po dag pa'i zhing du gshegs pa'i tshul
bstan pa'i bzhugs gdan gyi khar byang sems dkar po

mtheb kor gyi rgya tsam zhig byung ba de zhal du lhag ma ma lus par gsol bas brgyud pa zin pa'i rten 'brel 'grig /mchod 'bul dang dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa rgya cher spel ba'i
khur bzhes mdzad/ nyin gcig sprin dkar gyi phung po'i gseb na seng ge gnyis kyis bteg pa'i rin po che'i khri'i steng na rdo ring rin po che sku'i dbyibs dang cha byad
ji lta ba bzhin gsal bar gzigs te dbugs dbyung gzengs bstod byin rlabs mdzad/ tshar chen nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gsol 'debs las/ slar yang 'od gsal ngang las sku bzhengs te/
/seng ge'i khri la zhabs sen padma bkod/ /'dzum zhal bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyis skal ldan gyi/ /snying gi gdung ba bsal la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so/ /de'i tshe rje btsun rdo
rje rnal 'byor ma mngon sum du zhal bstan pa'i ngo mtshar gyi snang ba ci yang shar zhing / rdo ring rin po cher byin rlabs gsan pa'i dus bar snang gi sprin gseb nas rje
btsun ma'i sku gzigs par brten chos rje la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs byas res kyis rtags khyad par can re yong gi 'dug gsung ba'ang 'di rigs la dgongs so/ /dbyangs can
bzhad pa'i sgrib bral mkhyen mtsho'i nang / /mchog sred sprul pa'i gar dang las smon gyis/ /'brel ba'i gzugs brnyan shar nas lung ston pa/ /rnam gsum dam pa'i yon tan dngom
pa bzhin/ /mi bzad dug gi rlangs 'khrigs sa bdag gdon/ /srog rtsa drag sngags ma gi tas bcad dang / /lhan cig chos srung rwa rtses klu gnyan byad/ /nyer bkrol

bgrang bya'i lung bstan rna bar snyan/ /tshad ma bzhi ldan 'khor los thub bstan lus/ /kun tshang gling bzhir dbang sgyur yab rje'i khrir/ /mnga' gsol cod pan 'ching la gdan
gsum lha/ /mkha' khyab me tog glu gar rol mor brel/ /yi dam chos srung dgyes pa'i dpyid kyi ma/ /'bod byed sos kyis khu byug 'dren pa'i glus/ /mchog thun dngos grub 'dab
brgya grol ba'i sbubs/ /phan bde'i sbrang rtsi mngar po ci yang 'dzag /snyan brgyud chos kyi brda sprod ma lus pa/ /rang rigs dbang por gtad pas sarba dznyaH /chos dbyings
zag bcas bde ba'i mal nyal kyang / /dag sku'i gdong bzhi sprul de su yis 'gog /byu ru'i 'khri shing bzhin du dmar ba'i gzugs/ /mnyes lcugs 'khril ldem rtse 'jo'i yid 'ong
ma/ /dar babs lang tsho'i utpal dmar po'i sgros/ /'dzum pa'i bdud rtsi 'dren byed gzigs mor dngar/ /gsol 'debs las/ dpal ldan nA lendra yi chos grwa cher/ /bdag chen
rje yi zhabs zung gus bsten cing / /rdo rje 'chang dbang rje btsun sgo rum pas/ /zab lam gdams pa stsal la gsol ba 'debs/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i yongs 'dzin dbang po mchog
/drug cu rtsa gsum gus pas nyer bsten nas/ /rgya chen gsar snying rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i tshogs/ /ma lus thugs su chud la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes par tshig gi zin so yod med
sna tshogs kyang / de nas kha'u skyes lhas kyi sum cu rtsa gsum zer ba'i brang khang du sku mtshams shin tu dam par bcad nas lam dus thun bzhi ma dang gtso bor lam zab
kyi rnal

'byor lhur blangs pa'i tshe dgyes mdzad rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor dang gsang 'khrid kyi nyams len gnang ba'i dus mgon po lha brgyad 'khor dregs pa brgyad dang bcas pa gsal
bar gzigs/ yang nub cig mnal lam du ma jo'i rnam pa can zhig gis ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma mjal na 'di na yod ces zer bar dgyes bzhin du bud med des lam sna byas te phebs
pas dur khrod chen po bsil ba'i tshal yin rgyu ba'i shing tho re yod pa'i dbus na rdo phung zhig gi gseb tu gnam sgo 'dug pa phye ste 'di na yod zer ba gzigs pas zhal
bram gzugs dkar po ral pa'i thor tshugs can ras dkar po gyon pa phyed krung du bzhugs pa phyag g.yas na thod khrag dang g.yon na mi rkang gi gling bu dang shing gi bum pa
'dzin pa/ 'od zer du ma 'phro ba zhig gzigs/ de nas kyang 'bral med lta bur dngos su yang yang 'byon zhing las thams cad bsgrubs par mchis/ gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa
skyar phebs nas rten brten pa thams cad zhib mor mjal ba gnang zhing khyad par mgon po dngos su gzigs/ dge 'phel du rten bzhengs kyi tshe sku 'bag gi zhal rdul 'phyi ba
mdzad pas pu tras dngos su 'ongs te 'phyi lugs 'di bzhin byed dgos zhus/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi tsam la babs pa'i tshe gdan sa 'og nas bdag chen rin po che ngag gi dbang
phyug gi zhabs phyi mdzad nas dbus phyogs su phebs/ gsung ngag lam 'bras/ gshed dmar gyi dbang byin rlabs spros med kyi 'khrid/ rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang sogs bka' chos
mang du gsan/ gal

che dus mchod dpon dang dbang 'khrid kyi skor la thugs dogs sel gyi rigs nang bcar du 'bul ba sogs bdag chen rin po che'i phyag g.yog nang skor gyi rnam pa'ang yun ring tsam
mdzad/ bdag chen rjes chos kyi 'khor lo skor zhig pa'i gnang ba stsal ba la brten nas rong ston shes bya kun rig gi gdan sa nA lendra'i tshogs chen la gsung ngag rin po
che tshogs bshad yongs rdzogs shig gnang / thams cad dad pa'i sa la bkod de bdag chen rin po che las kyang 'ur ba tsam byung bar drung 'khor nas phrag dog gi rnam pa ci
rigs byung / lhun grub sdings pas sbyin bdag byas 'phan yul bya bzang gi chos khri'i gdong gi sa stong der spyil bu zhig yod par bcad rgya mdzad de dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed
kyi bsnyen pa zla ba lnga tsam song ba'i snga dro nyi ma rtse shar la 'od dmar pos lho'i phyogs rnams gang 'dug pa nyi zer yin nam dgongs/ gzigs pa na me dpung chen po
'ur sgra dang bcas pa blos mi 'khyud pa'i dbus na 'jigs byed yongs rdzogs 'khor bcu gcig zhabs g.yas brgyad kyi thad du las gshin rwa rtse shin tu rno ba g.yas gri gug g.yon
pas mi dar ma zhig gi ske zhags pas bcings pa de la zhal nas 'phros pa'i me 'phog pa na bug pa dgu nas khrag 'dzag pa zhig gzigs/ kha skong gi sbyin sreg kyang mdzad/
lam yig tu rje ngag dbang grags pa'i zhabs phyir lo brgyad tsam bsdad gsung pa'ang 'di'i skabs su yin par mchis/ chu 'brug lo zla ba dang po'i nang du gtsang la phebs/ 'di
res bsnyen par rdzogs kyang gsol 'debs la rtsa ba bcol bas 'og

tu 'byung / ston bo dong du rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bdag po chen po'i bar gyi dbang yongs su rdzogs pa dang gur mgon gyi man ngag sogs chos
bka'i rigs rgya cher gsan/ sngon yar klungs pa dang 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa dpon slob tu gyur pa'i rten 'brel dus 'dir 'grig tshul kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i rnam thar du/ bdag
gis bla ma dam pa'i drung na mjal zhing gsung chos 'dra'ang gsan gyi 'dug pa mthong bas sngar ye ma mjal na'ang 'dris 'dris 'thad 'thad 'dra mo zhig gis sems la dga' tshor
dang bla ma'i dga' ba la bsam pa dung dung pa byung / rje 'dar phyogs la phebs khar bdag yod sar thol gyis byon byung nas gos chen lcags nag kha do pa zhig dang stong
skud dmar po mang po zhig gnang / 'di la phyag 'phreng thag pa bzhin mdzod gos chen 'di la bris sku lta bu mdzad dam gang na'ang mi la ma gnang bar phyag tshags mdzod/
rten 'brel zhig yod do gsungs shing zhal 'dzum mang po mdzad kyin 'dug pa de dus ni dga' ba la bsam pa las ma byung / da bsams na mgon po che chung 'di rnams thob pa'i rten
'brel sgrig pa gnang bar 'dug go /rgyal ba'i dgongs pa zab gsal mkha' dbyings las/ /tshur mthong byis pas spar tshod ci zhig things/ /dus gsum gsal bar mkhyen des bdag
lta bu'ang / /snyan brgyud gdams pa'i snod du rung bar dgongs/ /dam pa'i zhal bzhes rdo yi ri mo bzhin/ /'gyur med bden pas thugs la btags na yang / /

rang gis gsol ba btab pa mi dran pa/ /a ho las nyon dbang gis skyes pas lan/ /zhes so/ /slar rang gi bsti gnas su chos sgo ba 'khrul zhig byams pa shes rab bzang po'i drung
du dpal rnal 'byor gsang mtha' 'khor lo sdom pa'i skor gyi bka' babs te lam rdzogs par gsan/ mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa 'jigs med dpa' bo'i lugs 'dzin
pa 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis la rje btsun gong ma'i yab mes 'khon rigs sngags 'chang rnams kyi yi dam kyi lha mchog gi dngos grub 'bad med du stsol ba dpal chen
po khrag 'thung he ru ka yang dag lha lnga bcu rtsa brgyad kyi dbang dang yig sna/ bar chad bdud sde'i g.yul las rgyal ba bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje gzhon nu lha khra
stong las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang bzhi dang smad las gdug pa sgrol ba'i rjes gnang / man ngag yig skor/ chos skyong dkar bdud kyi rjes gnang las tshogs/ rnam 'joms
bir lugs lha don lnga'i dbang lung / gur gyi mgon po gri gug lha lnga'i rgyud lugs kyi dbang / sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i man ngag lugs kyi dbang bzhi/ lha brgyad/
lha bcu gnyis ma/ gyi ljang lugs kyi lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang / de dang 'brel ba'i sgrub skor sogs mkhas grub kun dga' rnam rgyal gyi thugs dam mgon pod yongs rdzogs/
klu sgrub lugs kyi mgon po gdong brnyan can phyag drug pa dang las bzhi'i mgon po'i rjes gnang / par bu'i cho ga sogs las tshogs kha shas/ sman bla sprul sku'i rjes

gnang / rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras ser chen rta bdag brgyad kyis bskor ba/ ljang gu klu brgyad kyis bskor ba/ mthing kha lha mo brgyad kyis bskor ba/ slob dpon padma saM
bha wa lugs kyi sprin gseb ma rta bdag brgyad/ yang gsang drag po mdung dmar can rta bdag brgyad dang bcas pa rnams kyi rjes gnang dang rnam sras skor gyi yig sna kha
shas/ dmar po skor gsum gyi rgyun gang yod/ dpal tshogs kyi bdag po jo bo rje'i ga ga ma dkar po phyag bzhi pa/ chags pa'i rdo rje sogs kyi rjes gnang dang yig skor rnams
gsan/ kha skong dkar chags las/ 'on kyang 'cham dang 'gros kyi spros pa ni/ /'dod na rdo rje gdan pa las gzhan pa'i/ /tshad ldan med phyir de yi lugs bzhin ston/ /ces pa'i
don ltar mgon po che chung gnyis kyi 'cham dbyangs sogs kyi phyag len dpyis phyin par sbyong bdar mdzad/ dpon slob gnyis chos skyong skor la go bsdur gnang nas deng sang
bod na sa skya pa'i chos skyong la nged rang gnyis las mkhas pa med pa 'dra zhes kyal ka gsungs skad/ zhabs cher bsnyun yang gtsang chur 'jug pa sogs las gzhan ma'i 'phrod
bsten gyi spros pa dor te thos bsam lhur mdzad pas kun ha las te chos sde'i grwa rigs rnams yon tan gyi sbyong bdar dran bskul la de las lhag pa ma byung zer/ rdzong
lugs kyi bstan pa'i srol 'byed chen po rtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dngos slob rgyud gsum smra ba shes rab rin chen gyi drung du gur gyi mgon po lcam dral lha
gsum/ lha brgyad mkha' 'gro sbags sgrub rnams kyi

rjes gnang / gzhan las ches zab pa rtsa ba'i man ngag gnyis/ rnam par dbye ba bcu gnyis/ yan lag gi man ngag bcu drug /cho ga'i lag len nyi shu/ de dag gi yig cha'i gtso bo
mang po'i lung sogs sa skya rdzong chung par grags pa'i man ngag mtha' dag gi zab chos mang po gsan cing / bla ma 'di dag gis gtso byas gur gyi mgon po'i skor kho na la
bla ma bcu bsten lugs srol ma 'dres pa yongs su rdzogs par gsan pa/ ji skad du/ khyad par nag po chen po'i man ngag ni/ /brgyud ldan bla ma bcu phrag gcig la zhus/ /'gran
zla kun bral drin can rdo ring pa'i/ /snyan brgyud zab mo bum pa gang byor thob/ /ces dang / e waM pa ni bsdus la spros pa chung / /mus srad pa ni dkar chag khrims chags
can/ /rdo rje gdan pa 'cham dang nus pa'i bdag /kho bos thob pa'i thun mong brgyud pa gsum/ /zhes byung la/ gnod sbyin beg tse lcam dral gyi rjes gnang lung man ngag rnams
gsan/ gzhan yang snga phyi bsdoms par bla ma bsten pa'i skor la lo zla'i dus nges can ma rnyed pas phyogs mtshungs su bkod par/ dwags po paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal
lam rje btsun 'phrin las zhabs la sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo sogs kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal nas brgyud pa'i zab chos du ma dang kar lugs sogs kyi chos bka' kha
yar/ gzhung du rngog ston chen po bsod nams bstan 'dzin la rngog lugs kyi dkyil 'khor bdun gyi dbang dang rgyud bshad/ chos skyong dud sol lha mo'i skor rnams dang /

mi tra brgya rtsa ni dbang dang rjes gnang gang yin la dpyad gzhi 'dug kyang gsan/ bla chen mdo khams pa yon tan rgya mtsho la sa dge zhal gsum gyi 'jigs byed mkhan por grags
pa rnams kyi rna ba'i spyod yul du ma gyur pa'i rdzogs rim ye shes mkha' 'gro'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang la brten pa'i rwa 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud sogs zab chos du
ma/ 'gos rdo rje seng ge la gshin rje gshed dmar po lha bcu gsum gyi rnal 'byor bzhi'i 'khrid/ rnal 'byor bzhi/ bdud rtsi'i lha mo nor 'dzin ma dkar mo/ 'khrul 'khor/ phyi'i
byad rdzas/ rnam rtog 'od gsal 'pho ba rnams kyi byin rlabs/ de dag gi yig cha mang po'i lung / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang lung / rdo rje 'phreng
ba sogs kyi dbang lung / chos rje nyan chen par kye rdor bka' babs bzhi/ gsang 'dus lugs gsum sogs/ grub mchog sbyin pa rgya mtsho la skyes lhas pa'i zab chos sngar
gsan bldabs pa dang phran bu lus pa'i rigs rnams zhu ba mdzad cing dag pa'i snang bar yang yang mjal ba yod 'dug /mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug drang srong dka' bzhi par gtso
bor dpal rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa'i dbang lung man ngag thams cad gsan zhing dbang mdzad pa'i skabs khrag 'thung lha dgu'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor dngos su bstan
ging lnga gza' gdong / gnod sbyin beg gdong lcam sring gi chos skor rnams kyang gsan/ chos skyong rnams kyi phyag nas bzung ste mi la mi sprod pa'i tshul du bran dang 'bangs
su dngos

su gtad/ byang gter gyis thog drangs pa'i gsang sngags rnying ma'i chos skor ches mang ba gsan/ dpon slob gnyis car phan tshun thugs nang shin tu dag cing 'dar phyogs su'ang
spyan 'dren ched bstad gnang nas zhabs tog chen po mdzad/ rjes su'ang shar phyogs la phebs res kyis mjal tsam re mdzad cing bka' chos gang 'os re yang nges par gsan/ ldong
gi sngags 'chang chen po chos skyong bsod nams bkra shis par gter kha mi 'dra ba nyi shu tsam gyi dbang lung gsan par phebs pa'i tshe sngags 'chang rin po ches khyed
dpon slob rnams ma byon pa'i zhag gsum tsam gyi nub sngags gzhon dkar po zhig byung nas khyod la nga'i chos skor rnams zhu ba la mi zhig 'ong bar yod pas de la rdzogs par
gshod de ngas byin gyis brlabs pa yin gsung ba byung gsungs/ drin can sangs rgyas rnam rgyal la shangs pa bka' brgyud kyi lam yongs rdzogs gsan cing yab mes brgyud pa'i
bla brgyud yin ces shin tu gus par mdzad/ brag dkar sems dpa' chen po bsod nams rgyal mtshan la phyag rdor 'khor chen lam yongs rdzogs sogs chos mang du gsan/ bzad g.yu gong
par ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i zab chos gzhan nas ma rnyed pa du ma/ byang stag lung sbas don pa la phag gru lugs kyi phyag bzhi pa'i lam yongs rdzogs bsam sdings
mkhan chen sangs rgyas ye shes la mgon po lha chen dpal 'bar gyi rjes gnang / rwa sgreng mkhan po dpal 'byor bsam grub la mi'u thung gsod byed kyi rjes gnang / jo stan
rong shAka pa bkra shis rin cen la a ti lam yongs rdzogs

dang 'dod rgyal nor bu gsal 'bar gyi lung gsan de skabs rdzogs chen gyi rtogs pa phul bas nged rang la nyams myong dga' mo yod pa'i lugs yin kyang 'di 'dra skyes ma myong gsungs
pas tshogs pa rnams dad nas gsung chos mang du zhus/ nya mgo gru khar mnyan pa dus la ma 'byor bas nga chu la 'ding ba bting nas 'gro gsungs pas mdun gyi nam mkhar
dpal phag mo grub pa byon nas snyigs ma'i sems can nyon mongs can la gsang ba'i spyod pa ma byed gsung ba zhig byung bas gru la phebs/ gdan sa thel gyi gnas rnams zhib par
mjal/ 'jag spyil sku 'dra rin po che phag mo gru pa dngos su gzigs spyan nam mkha'i mthongs su zhal 'dzum mdangs dang bcas pas lta stangs su bzhugs song ba brda ston khyad
par can du dgongs/ khams lcags mo ba mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug bkra shis seng ge la gur mgon khro bcu'i rjes gnang / zhal gyi gsang 'khrid rjes gnang dang / rtsa gsum
'khor lo bzhi la brten pa'i 'khrid zab mo lo chen gnyan gyi thugs bcud ches dkon pa gsan/ bla ma 'dis stan thog gcig tu zhal gyi bsnyen pa 'bum phrag drug cu tsam song
ba'i nus pa bsam gyis mi khyab/ gsang 'khrid brgyud 'debs su/ skyes mchog chos rje'i sras kyi thu bo pa/ /zhing skyong bran du 'khol ba'i rdo rje 'dzin/ /rtsa ba'i bla ma
drin can mdo khams pa/ /zhes byung la/ rtag brtan sprul skus 'khrid brdzus ma yin zhes smra ba ni sprang pos thang ston par 'phya ba'i dper snang / shambhar

chos rje kun dga' sangs rgyas la gnubs lugs kyi stag zhon lha mang gi dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen pas e waM chos ldan gyi mkhan po kun spangs
pa mdzad nas thar rtser bzhugs dus rdo ring rin po ches khong sems dpa' chen po'i dbon yin cing rang re'i brgyud pa'ang chos rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras gnyis la thug gi
yod gshis da lam 'dir brel ba langs pa'i chos kyi gseng zhig kyang 'dug pas khyed rang ngor du lam 'bras gsan par byon zhes phyag tham dang bcas thar rtser phebs par lam
'bras yongs su rdzogs pa/ mgon po'i nang 'khrid kyi man ngag chos rje dpal ldan rgyal po nas brgyud pa sogs dang gzhan dbang rjes gnang du ma gsan cing gsung ngag la bogs
'byin lta bu'i thugs bskyed kyang thon pas thugs mos shin tu che ba byung / mnal lam du rje rdo rje 'chang yin zer ba zhig dang mjal bas rkyen byas thugs rgyud la nyams
rtogs khyad par can 'khrungs/ yab chos rgyal rin cen rgyal mtshan la yab chos du ma gsan cing bla ma 'di nyid kyis mgon po stag zhon dngos su bran gyi tshul du gtad pas
las sgrub kyin 'dug pa'i rgyu mtshan lam yig na'ang gsal/ 'di yan la bka' drin che ba'i bla ma nyer bdun du mdzad cing gzhan yang bya 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge la bya rgyud
sgo drug sogs/ spyan snga shAkya rgyal mtshan la sgra snyan mngon brjod sdeb sbyor sogs/ grub chen rdo rje rgyal por khong rang gis rnal 'byor ma la dngos su gsan pa'i
'pho ba zab mo/ gong dkar tshul khrims pa la

zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang dang bran bdud kyi rjes gnang thun mong min pa/ des mtshon chos 'brel gsan pa 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ gong dkar ba rgya ston byang chub
dbang rgyal/ rgyal yum tshul khrims bzang mo/ lam yig tu ku su lu'i bla ma gsung pa'i lcags sgog lung pa bkra shis dpal 'byor/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge /sgra pa sku skye
shes rab rin cen/ sngags 'chang sangs rgyas 'phel/ sngags 'chang sangs rgyas grags pa/ sngags 'chang rdo rje legs ldan/ bla ma sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ stag lung rin cen
rnam rgyal grags pa/ lo ba spyan snga ngag dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / bdag chen a tshes pa/ rnal 'byor ma dkon mchog ldan/ nub ra ba
blo bzang brtan pa/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgyal mtshan/ chos rje chos skyong rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bkra shis rnam rgyal/ 'brug pa ngag dbang
chos rgyal/ rje btsun dam pa kun dga' grol mchog /ngor chen dkon cog lhun grub/ chos rje dbus smyon pa/ gre chen nam mkha' 'od zer/ snye thang lung zin pa/ grub chen nam
mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bla ma blo gros seng ge /bdag chen kun dga' don grub rnams kyi steng du tshigs snga phyi bar gsum gyi mkhan slob rnams bsnan pas yongs 'dzin drug cu
rtsa gsum legs par bsten nas thos bsam rgya cher mdzad pas kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses/ drug cu rtsa gsum dam pa'i yongs 'dzin bsten/ mdo sngags gsar

rnying dam chos mtha' dag la/ /thos bsam sgom pas 'khrul med thugs su chud/ /rtsod dus kun mkhyen gnyis par gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes byung la/ tsa ri rdor 'dzin pa chos kyi mgon
po'am mthu mkhan rgya bor grags pa la chos skyong gi skor gsan pa kho rang gi rnam thar du 'dug pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtshor chos 'brel gsan pa gnyis
gsol 'debs su 'tshems pa zhig yin par mngon/ bla mar rlom pa la la dag ni rigs rus skye brgyud stobs 'byor gos sogs kyi khengs pas chos 'tshol ba la bag tsha ba'i gnas
su byed cing cung zad don du gnyer ba'ang / sdom gsum las/ rta dang nor bu la sogs pa/ /cung zad tsam gyi nyo tshong la/ /kun la 'dri zhing brtags nas spyod/ /tshe 'di'i
bya ba cung zad la'ang / /de 'dra'i 'bad pa byed pa mthong / /skye ba gtan gyi legs nyes ni/ /dam pa'i chos la rag las kyang / /chos 'di khyi yi zas bzhin du/ /bzang ngan
gang du'ang mi dpyod par/ /gang phrad de la gus par 'dzin/ /nyin gcig gi ni skyel ma 'am/ /tshe gcig gi ni gnyen 'brel la'ang / /'bad de brtags nas len pa mthong / /deng
nas brtsams te rdzogs pa yi/ /sangs rgyas ma thob bar gyi don/ /bla ma mchog la rag las mod/ /'on kyang rtogs dpyod mi byed par/ /tshong 'dus ngan pa'i zong bzhin du/ /su
phrad rnams las len pa mthong / /kye ma snyigs ma'i dus 'di mtshar/ /zhes chos khungs btsun mi btsun sogs la mi blta bar bla chen du ming btags pa zhig 'gangs che'o snyam
pa'i blun dad

kyis 'jug pa tsho dang mi 'dra bar rje btsun 'di nyid khungs dang 'brel ba'i tshigs bcad re'i ched du'ang dka' spyad rtag tu ngu ltar mdzad pas gong du ma 'dus pa'i rigs med
pa'i mtha' ma bkag mod/ bshes gnyen de dag la thos pa ji ltar mdzad na lung sde bzhi/ mdo rtsa/ sum brgya pa/ me tog 'phreng rgyud/ las rnam 'byed sogs 'dul mngon dang
'brel ba'i rgya bod kyi gzhung / brgyad stong pa/ ngor lugs su grags pa'i mdo chung bco brgyad mdo phran gyi rigs sna tshogs/ byams chos lde lnga/ rigs tshogs drug /bka'
gdams gzhung drug /blo sbyong gi 'khrid sogs theg chen thun mong ba dang 'brel ba'i rgya bod kyi yig sna/ gsar ma rgyud 'bum/ gdugs dkar zhe gnyis ma/ tshe dpag med lha dgu/
'chi med rnga sgra/ don yod zhags pa/ bcu gcig zhal/ mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang / rnam rgyal 'joms/ rigs gsum spyi sogs bya rgyud kyi dbang rjes gnang
/ rig gtad/ rnam snang mngon byang / phyag rdor 'byung 'dul sogs spyod rgyud kyi skor/ rdor dbyings/ dpal mchog /rdor sems/ sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis sogs rnal
'byor rgyud/ gsang 'dus lugs gsum/ rim lnga dmar khrid/ sems nyid ngal gso'i 'khrid/ dgra gdong 'jigs gsum/ dus 'khor/ lo nag dril gsum gyi dbang 'khrid/ phag mo'i skor/
mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ sdom 'byung / bong zhal can/ sampu Ti/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur sogs bla med dang 'brel

pa'i dbang lung 'khrid mtha' yas pa/ rje btsun gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum sogs rgya bod kyi mkhas grub mang po'i gsung gis mtshon gsan pa mtha' dag brir ma lang pas gsan yig
sogs gzhan du shes par bya'o/ /de ltar yongs 'dzin mang du bsten nas gsan pa'i chos rnams kyang dag dang ma dag pa'i shan legs par phye bas tshig gi cha la lung dang rigs
pas sgro 'dogs rnam par bcad/ don gyi cha theg dman byang sems gsang sngags sogs theg pa so so'i ched du bya ba'i gdul bya rnams so so'i khams dang dbang por 'tsham pa'i
nad thog tu sman bzhin gang la gang 'dul gyi sgo nas thar pa'i lam la bkri ba'i gnad 'gag ma 'dres pa thugs su chud par mdzad pas/ 'jam dbyangs sa paN gyis/ bsregs bcad
brdar ba'i cho gas gser gyi khams/ /sbyong pa'i rim bzhin dgag gzhag spang gsum gyis/ /gzhung lugs 'bum sde'i lhad kun 'byin pa la/ /kun dga'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin khyod bskos
pa snyam/ /zhes pa'i don dang mtshungs shing rtog ge dang tha snyad sogs gtsug lag mang por mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs pas/ mkhas pa'i gsung las/ snyan ngag mngon brjod
sdeb sbyor zlos gar dang / /rtsis bzo gso ba sgra tshad nang don rig /skye bar 'grogs pas de dag sred pa bzhin/ /mthong ba'i mod la de yi blo dang 'thams/ /zhes pa'i don
thog tu babs par ma zad gtso bor gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i smin grol man ngag gi gnad la byang chub pas/ tha snyad bslab pa chu 'dod smig rgyu'i rjes/ /snyegs ltar mthong

nas snying po'i don btsal bas/ /sbas don rlung gi zab gnad 'tshol ba la/ /gnad du che bas rtsis tshul bzhin du bslabs/ /gcig shes kun la mkhas na rtog ge pa'i/ /yun ring ngal
byas rnams kyi khengs pa bstungs/ /zhes pa ltar yin zhing / de yang sdom gsum du/ /lha chen skad ngan shor ba la/ /sdug bsngal bden pa mthong zhes grags/ /zhes pa ltar/
log pa'i bshes kyi rdzun tshig dang chos ma yin pa smra ba lta bu'i 'chad nyan gyi gzugs brnyan tsam la mtha' ci bkag /drag shul can gyis zhus pa'i mdo las/ gal te byang
chub sems dpa' lung nod pa'am sbyin pa dang ldan pa'am tshul khrims dang ldan pa'am bzod pa dang ldan pa'am brtson 'grus dang ldan pa'am bsam gtan dang ldan pa'am shes
rab dang ldan pa'am byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi tshogs gsog pa dang ldan pa'i tshig bzhi pa'i tshigs su bcad pa su las nyan tam lung nos sam blangs pa'i slob dpon de la
des chos kyi gus par bya'o/ /ming dang tshig dang yi ge ji snyed pa de snyed kyis bskal par gal te slob dpon de la g.yo med par rnyed pa dang bkur stis rim gro byas kyang
da dung slob dpon de la gus par bya ba yongs su rdzogs par bya ba ma yin na chos ma yin pas gus par byas pa lta ci smos zhes gsungs pa dang mthun par bshes gnyen de dag
rnams la mnyes pa gsum gyi sgo nas gus pa lhur mdzad pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'brom stod chos kyi rgyal pos bla ma se btsun dang / se ston kun rig gis rje btsun 'brog mi'i
zhabs bsten pa'i

ngang tshul dang mtshungs so/ /bcu phrag drug lhag yongs 'dzin chu gter klong / /mkhyen dpyod brtson pa'i ri bo bsgril ba las/ /legs bshad nyin byed thon pa'i 'od stong gis/
/gangs can bstan pa'i snang ba ches cher dkar/ /thub gsung dgongs 'grel mes po'i ral klung las/ /lnga rig shes bya'i yan lag brgyad ldan rgyun/ /blo gros lto bar 'dzin
pa'i drang srong khyod/ /sngon med dzahnu yi mched po bzhin/ /bshes gnyen bsten la mi ngal kun dga' bo/ /bgrang yas bka' rnams sdud por 'od srungs che/ /rnam par 'byed pa'i
shes rab shA ri'i bu'i/ /ngang tshul zla gzugs gangs can chu mtshor shar/ /drang nges gnad gsang dbye ba 'od gzi'i mdangs/ /mkhas rloms nai ru ka dpal bzod min yang /
/mtha' klas chos kyi dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis char/ /brdar nus bi shwa karma deng 'dir 'grub/ /de yang sngar dbus nas bo dong du phebs pa'i sngon du bsnyen rdzogs lo rtsis kyi
yong dgos rgyur 'dug rung thog ma nas lo zla sogs dus tshigs nges sbyar gyi sa bon zhig med 'dug gshis/ mdzad pa 'gangs che ba rnams phyogs su bsdoms pa'i gsol 'debs kyi
go rim ltar byas pa 'gal med du rtogs pas/ gsol 'debs las/ grub pa'i gnas mchog kha'u brag rdzong dang / /mang mkhar cha lung rdo rje'i brag rdzong sogs/ /dben pa'i ri
khrod rnams su zab mo'i lam/ /rtse gcig nyams su bzhes la gsol ba 'debs/ /mtshungs bral bshes gnyen sdom brtson dbang po mchog /yongs rdzogs mkhan po grags pa rgyal mtshan
zhabs/ /

gus bsten bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa bzhes/ /dge slong rdo rje 'dzin la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gong du smos pa'i gsan bsam mthar phyin par mdzad pa de dag go yul tsam du
ma lus par thugs nyams su bstar bas/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtses gsol 'debs las/ brjod bral bde chen gnas lugs mngon gyur kyang / /rim gnyis bzlas par bcas pa'i rnal
'byor la/ /nam yang g.yel med sgrub pa lhur len pa'i/ /grub pa'i gtsug rgyan mchog la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa'i don ltar bsnyen sgrub kyi rim pa mdzad pa aShta'i bsnyen
chen nA lendra gsung ngag gnang ba'i snga rol nas song zin pa dang snga phyir bde mchog yab bka' yum bka'/ 'jigs byed/ gshed dmar/ phur pa/ mgon po che chung sogs yi dam
chos skyong mang po'i ljags bsnyen dus rtags grangs tshad du thon par ma zad rgyun du'ang nyin mtshan khor yug tu thugs dam gyi rim pa gnyis kyi rnal 'byor zab mos dus 'da'
zhing sngags kyi bzlas pa'ang nyin zhag re'i khongs su aShta/ oM gsum ma/ ya ma rA dzA/ shA sa na/ sa phur gyi snying po rnams so sor stong phrag re chag med du mdzad
cing / bka' las/ ngas gsang sngags gsar rnying gi sngags phal cher bsnyen tshad bzhin ma bzlas pa ye med/ de rnams kyi nang nas mgon po'i sngags shA sa na 'di nus pa che
shos la 'dug ste/ 'di bgrangs pas 'phreng ba la dngos su me 'bar ba yong gin 'dug /ces gsungs/ skabs shig zhal gyi bsnyen pa gnang

ba'i tshe thog mar cung zad 'tshub pa'i rnam pa dang rjes su gzigs snang la bar snang nas gos chen lcags nag gi phod ka chen po gyon pa zhig gis phu thung gi sbugs nas lag
pa chen po yang yang ston pa sogs byung ba'ang chos skyong gis dngos su rjes su bzung ba'i cho 'phrul du snang / gzhan yang grum stod kha'u'i brag rdzong du bzhugs pa'i dus
thugs rgyud la nyams dang rtogs pa ting nge 'dzin gyi 'char sgo bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'khrungs shing dbang las byung ba'i ye shes khyad par can lam gyi dus su gong nas
gong du 'phel ba dri ma dang bral ba phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes la dbang 'byor bar mdzad/ 'phan yul bya bzang du bzhugs pa'i tshe/ bka' las/ nyi ma dgongs phyogs skyo
bsangs byas pa'i tshe mdun gyi spang gshong la gong mo mang po rtse zhing / rgyab kyi thang la phyug rji gzhon nu mang po shing 'thu zhing rtsed mo byed pa mthong bas 'di
dag kyang bsams na dge sbyong gi bskul mar 'dug snyam nas rang sems la gsal 'debs su smras gsung ba'i nyams glu gnang ba'i skabs yun ring du bzhugs shing thugs dam gyi bogs
shin tu che bar byung / chu bo rir phebs pa'i tshe brag phug tu sgrub pa mdzad pas dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro mas tshogs kyi 'khor los mchod cing thugs nyams kyi ngang nas
rdo rje'i lus kyi rtsa 'khor gyi lha rnams gsal bar gzigs pas/ gsung mgur las/ gnas spyi bo bde chen gyi ri bo'i spor/ /rje sku yi rdo rje yab yum bzhugs/ /ma mkha' 'gro
so gnyis kyi 'khor gyis bskor/ /sku zla shel gsar pa'i mdangs 'od can/ /pha

gsol ba 'debs so rdor ring pa/ /bu mi mngon dbyings nas thugs rjes skyongs/ /tshogs mchod par 'bul lo drin can rje / /lus snang stong sprul skur byin gyis rlobs/ /zhes sogs
tshig don ngo mtshar ba yod/ chu bo ri'i dur khrod du tshogs 'khor mdzad nas bzhugs pa'i mtho phyir shab shub kyi sgra dang bcas skor ba byed pa'i skad thams cad kyis thos
par byung / dur khrod de'i gong tsam du thugs dam la cung zad bzhugs pa'i gnas der zhabs 'bring ba rnams kyis mngon sum du rlung 'tshub chen po'i dkyil nas thag sgra chen
po yang yang byung skabs/ dpal ldan lha mo dud pa'i sol ba can sku stod ja bsus pa'i rlangs pa lta bu sngo skya nam mkha' khengs pa gsal bar gzigs shing shog dril zhig
phyag tu phul/ de nas bzung dus rgyun du bde chen gyi nyams bzung du med pa rdol/ de la brten dus lan cig ma yin par bde stong lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes khor yug tu g.yo
ba med pa'i rgyu mtshan/ thugs dam gyi rim pa stod phyogs su 'phel bar dgongs te rmu bla brang du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig zhabs cung zad bsnyun pa'i tshul bstan tshe 'khrul
zhig dkon cog bzang por zhu shog phul ba'i nang du bdag kyang lus bsam gtan gyi khang bu'i sgor mi thon kyang sems la bde chen gyi ye shes mnan pas mi non pa khor yug
tu yod ces pa'ang byung / de yang rje btsun chen pos/ lta ba spros bral du blo cham 'gro na 'da' kha ma mi thebs pa mi srid tshe 'di dang mthong lam gyi bar na dar tsam
las med/ ces pa'i tshad der phebs nges pas dam pa 'di

nyid bzang po bzang po zhes pa'i ming tsam gyi stong 'ur mkhan rnams dang mi 'dra bar slu med gtan gyi skyabs mchog tu lung dang rigs pas bsgrub nus pas dran pa'i mod la srid
zhi'i gdung ba mtha' dag sel bar snang / bcom ldan 'das dgyes mdzad rdo rje dang ma he'i zhal can sogs yi dam gyi lha mang po nang rang byung lus kyi pho brang du rlung
sems dag pa'i gar mkhan me long las gzugs brnyan ltar phyi rol tu shar te zhal gzigs/ gur zhal/ beg tse/ stag zhon sogs dam can srung ma rnams rgyal gyis 'bangs la bsgo
ba bzhin ji ltar bzhed pa'i 'phrin las bsgrub pa la mi g.yel lo/ /ring por ma lon par mang mkhar du byon te sa skya'i mi 'gyur ba'i gzer bzhi zhes pa shar du bya 'gyur rdo
rje'i brag /lhor phul byung bdud po brag /nub tu cha lung rdo rje brag /byang du ga ra g.ya' yi brag ste bzhi'i nang nas cha lung rdo rje brag rdzong gi rje btsun grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyi gzims spyil shing sgo ma zer ba'i phug par sgrub pa mdzad kyin bzhugs pa'i re zhig na nye ba'i sri zhu ba des snga dro drung du phyin pas gzims zhwa
sbubs thibs se byas sku dngos ni mi snang / ci yin sgo bca' sogs ni mdang nub kyi de ga 'dug skar khung ni shin tu chung gang yin snyam nas slar log ste sgo'i phyi nas bltas
pas lho'i mchod rten gyi drung na chos gos rnam gsum dang bcas sku zil pa phrom me 'od mer re bzhugs 'dug pa na bdag cag gi bla ma dam pa ni gang la'ang thogs pa med
par 'phur te byon to snyam dad pa zi bun pa'i ngang nas sku drung du phyin pa lta stangs kyi ngang na had de bzhugs

pa mthong / slar gzims spyil du phebs/ brag gi phug nas lcags kyi rdo rje rtse dgu pa zhig byung ba thub bstan dge 'phel gyi mgon po'i thugs kar bzhugs/ bka' las/ 'phur ba
yin zer ched du theb theb rang dgos dogs med sems cer bltas pas gang dgos sa ru slebs yong ba yin gsungs/ de dus bde stong lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes mngon du gyur pa'i
nyams 'ur chen pos 'khrul snang a 'thas rdzun phugs rdib pa'i kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa grub pa'i sa dang lam gyi rtogs pa mthar phyin pa mdzad pa yin te/ yang gsang brgyud
'debs las/ mang mkhar cha lung rdo rje'i brag rdzong du/ /blo gsal bung ba 'du ba'i padmo'i tshal/ /rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i bcud phyung gdams pa'i gter/ /drin can tshar
pa smyon par gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes byung la/ gnas 'di dang thub bstan dge 'phel gnyis su chos nyid skye ba med pa'i don mngon du mdzad pa'i tshul bstan pa yin te/ ji skad
du/ gzhi 'khrul snang gi rang zhal bltas tsa na/ /brjod med kyi dbyings su rjen ne ba/ /gser gling du bol dum ngas ma rnyed/ /ma sems can tsho mgo bo gang nas 'khor/ /zhes
dang / lam bskyed rdzogs gnad du bsnun tsa na/ /spyir snang 'di nyams kyi ban ma bun/ /snang grag rig gsum 'di rgyal ba'i ngang / /khong rnal 'byor tsho blang dor ga
la byed/ /lam sgom pa'i 'bras bu sgra bo che/ /gzhi mngon du gyur pa'i skad du gda'/ /'di rang bcas su yod pa rang ngo shes/ /da 'bras bu bya ba gzhan ma mchis/ /zhes gsungs/

de nas cho 'phrul chen po'i tshes bco lnga nas zla gcig tsam gyi bar sku mtshams bcad de dbang drag padma nye bar bsnyen pa'i tshe rgyal ba kun 'dus padma thod 'phreng rtsal
gyis zhal bstan zhing gsung gi gnang ba dang bcas dbugs dbyung / 'phags yul gyi slob dpon padmA ka ra dang bod kyi lo chen bai ro'i thugs kyi nying khu yang gsang khros
pa lha dgu'i gsung bsnyen dang de'i yig cha la brten nas myong grol bdud rtsi'i ril bu'i sgrub pa gnang ba'i tshe dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs dang gnod sbyin lcam dral rgyud
nas bshad pa'i srung ma rnams kyis rang rang gi sku dngos su bstan pa'i tshe ging lnga'i rta rmig kyang nam mkhar mi shong ba lta bu gzigs/ rmur skor tsam phebs pa'i
tshe yang gzigs snang de 'dra ba byung ba'i rkyen gyis chibs drag tu bskul nas phebs pas bu ri 'phrang gi mas snar chibs pa'i rmig rjes shin tu gsal ba da lta'ang kun gyi
spyod yul du mchis/ de yang cho 'phrul bstan pa'i mdo las/ rgyal srid mchil ma'i thal ba bzhin spangs nas/ /dben par dong ste dgon par gnas byed pa/ /nyon mongs spangs nas
bdud ni bcoms nas su/ /byang chub rdul med 'dus ma byas 'tshang rgya/ /zhes srid pa 'khor ba la yid 'byung ba'i rang byung gi bslab pa la brten nas myur du byang chub
rnyed par 'gyur pa'i gtso bo ni/ dge slong la rab tu gces pa'i mdo las/ dge slong zhes bya sdug bsngal spong ba yin/ /dge slong zhes bya rgyal ba'i sras po'o/ /zhes 'khor
los sgyur ba'i rgyal po la sras stong yod kyang thu bo la rgyal srid 'byung ba bzhin 'khor rnam pa bzhi'i nang nas mchog tu gyur pa

dge slong pha'i sdom pa yin la/ de yang bod 'dir sdom rgyun 'ga' zhig yod pa'i nang nas kha che'i paN chen bsod snyoms pa chen po'i sdom rgyun shin tu gtsang ba chos lung tshogs
su bzhugs par brten/ gsung las/ bdag gis tshe 'di'i ngo srung rgyab tu bor/ /phyi ma'i don chen 'ba' zhig snying nas bsams/ /yongs rdzogs kha che'i paN chen bsod snyoms
pa/ /shAkya shrI'i grar ni 'bad pas zhugs/ /zhes pa ltar dgung lo so gcig pa dga' ba zhes pa chu pho 'brug gi lo sa ga zla ba'i tshes bco lnga thub pa'i dbang pos bdud
btul byang chub brnyes shing mya ngan las 'das pa'i dus chen sum 'dzom gyi tshe nyes ltung gi cha phra mo'i 'dam gyis ma gos shing / tshul khrims kyi 'dab brgya yongs
su bzhad pa las mya ngan las 'das pa'i ze'u 'bru'i bcud kyis skal bzang ra yig gnyis pa'i dga' ston ches cher spel ba sa'i steng na 'gran pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba'i
don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mkhan po/ chos kyi rje bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis las slob/ rje
ngag dbang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis gsang ston/ g.yag sde lcang ra ba blo gros phun tshogs kyis dus bsgo ba/ spos khang pa 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan sogs nyi shus las
kyi kha bskang ste jo bo stan gcig pa'i bsti gnas nyang stod spos khang gi kun dga' ra bar bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i tshe sngar dge tshul gnang ba'i mtshan gyi steng du mkhan
po'i mtshan sgra grags pa rgyal

mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bsnan zhing bag yod pa kho na mdzad de tshul khrims rnam par dag pa ni/ ji skad du/ kha na ma tho phra rab la'ang / /thugs ni shin tu 'jigs par mdzad/
/dran dang shes bzhin ldan pa yis/ /tshul bzhin ma yin yid mi mdzad/ /bag yod dran dang g.yo sgyu med/ /ltung ba'i nyes pas khyod ma gos/ /zhes mnyam med jo bo chen
po'i rnam par thar pa dang mtshungs so/ /bzlas brjod nus pa'i glog zhags thod 'phreng la/ /'khyug tshe bdud snying sngags smyon thog gzer gyis/ /'bigs kyang lha rgyud bskul
ba'i dbyar gyi rnga/ /thos pas dngos grub rma bya'i mngal khur 'dzin/ /bde stong ye shes me lces gnyis 'dzin shing / /bsreg pa'i cho 'phrul la mtshar byis pa'i blo/ /skyon
med gnyug ma'i lam gyis 'dus mtha'i 'phrang / /brgal te bcu gsum sa la snyegs 'di ci/ /mtha' klas chos kyi rang mtshang rjen pa ru/ /shar tshe kun rdzob 'khrul pa dbyig
po ches/ /med kyang mngon sum snang ba'i sprul bsgyur gyis/ /sgyu ma'i glang seng 'jigs tshul bag la zha/ /bdag 'dra'i 'gro snying lcags khams 'khor ba la/ /nges par
mi 'byung tshe 'di'i grabs gshom na/ /mthon po'i sa la gshegs kyang tshangs spyod grus/ /srid mtshor sgrol brdzu'i rdzun gyis 'drid 'di ci/ /'on te chags bral tshul khrims
ngad 'thul yang / /dga' bzhi'i 'gros kyi bde stong smin legs mar/ /mnyam sbyor rtse dga' rgod pa'i theg gsum don/ /'gal med mdud pa'i gnad de lhod por grol/ /gsol 'debs
las/ grub dbang

bla ma 'khor lo sdom par gzigs/ /dge 'phel chos kyi khri la spyan 'dren pa'i/ /gzhi bdag gus pa'i rnam 'phrul pho nya'i tshul/ /zhabs kyi padmar son la gsol ba 'debs/ /ngag
dbang dbyangs can lha mo'i bzlas brjod tshe/ /mkha' la me tog dkar po'i char babs shing / /rgyud mangs sgra snyan rna ba'i bdud rtsi mchog /'od gsal ngang du gsan la gsol
ba 'debs/ /mnal lam ngang du dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs/ /sgron me bteg nas rje btsun rdo ring pa'i/ /'khor slob 'tshol ba'i zol gyi rnam thar mchog /rtsom par bskul ba
gzigs la gsol ba 'debs/ /grangs med mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i tshogs dbus kyi/ /gtso mo padma'i dra ba can zhes pas/ /glegs bam bstan cing cho 'phrul sna tshogs bcas/ /'dri ba'i
yo byad gtad la gsol ba 'debs/ /chos kyi khri la 'khor ba'i rab byung gis/ /rgyal ba'i rtogs brjod klog pa'i tshul can la/ /mkha' 'gro'i tshogs rnams dga' bas nyan pa
sogs/ /dge mtshan du ma gzigs la gsol ba 'debs/ /rje btsun bla mas zhal bzang yang yang bstan/ /rnam thar rtsom pa'i bya ba mthar phyin tshe/ /dpal ldan 'dod khams dbang
mos dgyes pa yi/ /srung mar zhal gyis bzhes la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes dngos shugs sna tshogs pa/ de ltar mkhas btsun bzang po'i bdag nyid can rnams ni 'khor ba'i mtha' ma
rdzogs pa de srid du rnam par dkar ba'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun chad pa med par 'jug pa chos nyid

yin pas mdo sngags kyi gra dang sde/ sa skyong ba'i che dgu/ rigs rus kyis mtho ba'i ya rabs/ rnam dpyod dang ldan pa'i mkhas pa/ nyams rtogs dang ldan pa'i sgom chen/ dpa'
mdzangs longs spyod dang ldan pa'i dpon skya sogs skye bo thams cad kyi bsam blo'i yul du dam pa 'di nyid bdag cag gi skyabs gnas su thob na ci ma rung snyam pa'i 'dun pa
rtse gcig tu gyur pas/ rje nyid kyis chos skyong rnams la bka' bsgo ba'i tshigs bcad las/ 'di na skye rgu'i phan bde ma lus pa/ /rgyal ba'i bstan pa mchog la rag las shing
/ /byang phyogs 'di na bstan pa'i snying po mchog /sa skya'i rje btsun zhabs las brgyud 'di yin/ /de yi yang snying gsang chen zab mo'i bcud/ /zhal dang snyan du brgyud
pa'i mdzod 'dzin pa/ /kho bo'i 'dren mchog rje btsun rdo ring zhabs/ /bka' drin mnyam med dam pa'i srol 'dir bas/ /de nyid mchod cing bkur ba'i sbyin pa'i bdag /stod lung
sa yi thig le'i stobs ldan ni/ /spa ra ba zhes grags pa'i ba dan can/ /zhes pa ltar stod lung nas sde pa spa ra ba rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa la mi phyed pa'i dad
pa dang ldan pas gsung ngag rin po che'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gser sku grwa tshar bzhengs pa'i rab gnas la gdan drangs te stod nas chibs kha bskyod/ dam tshig pa la ye shes
sems dpa' dngos su 'jug par mtshon 'dod chos rkyen sel gyi rim gro sogs re ba yongs su skong bar mdzad cing / rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams kyi rtag gtor 'dzugs pa sogs
mgon khang bzheng pa gnang tshe/ na mo gu ru de wa

maNDa la dharma pA la sa pa ri wA re bhyaH kun khyab kun gyi byed po gcig nyid srid zhi'i gzugs kyis kun la 'khyud/ /rgyal dang rgyal sras slob mar bcas pa'i tshogs kyi gtso
bo rgyal ba rje/ /mtha' yas mtha' med 'gro ba'i skyabs mchog rje btsun bla ma srid mtha' bar/ /gtsug rgyan gtsug gi nor bur gus mchod 'bral ba med par gtsug tu bzhugs/
/zhes sogs mkha' 'gro lnga bstod bskul dang / dam can srung ma dgyes pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sdes/ /gnas lugs bde ba chen po'i mkha' dbyings
su/ /rab zab thabs kyis bsgrubs pa'i mchod pa'i sprin/ /zhes rgyud dang man ngag las byung ba'i phyi nang gsang mchod rgyas par dbul mthar/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa spyi
dang bye brag tu/ /dpal ldan sa skya pa zhes grags pa yi/ /bstan pa'i nying khu rje btsun rdo ring pa'i/ /bstan pa sa yi phyogs 'dir dar rgyas mdzod/ /de nyid 'dzin dang
mchod pa'i sbyin pa'i bdag /mi nor 'khor bcas bsrung dang sba ba dang / /'du 'bral med par rtag tu skyong bar mdzod/ /ces dang / da lta'i gnod byed mi dang mi ma yin/ /skad
cig nyid la mngon sum 'dir khug la/ /rab rnon mtshon chas mgo lus dum bur gtubs/ /khrag zhag don snying dmar po hab kyis thob/ /ces phrin las rgyas par mdzad/ ring zhig
na 'gro ba'i las smin bdo ba rgyal po gzugs can snying po ltar tshad bzung dka' mod/ hor bya rig sogs rjes ma rnams la'ang srung ma'i za kha zug ste ming gi lhag mar
gyur/

dbus su zla ba drug tsam gyi ring bstan 'gro'i legs tshogs spel nas gtsang du byon/ chos sgo ba byams pa shes rab bzang po la sngar smos pa'i chos gsan rgyu'i sngon du rmu
gshong na bzhugs pa'i mnal lam du mi sngon po zhig na re phu na 'khor lo bde mchog byon yod pas chos zhus zer byung ba'ang rtsad gcod mi gnang ba dge 'phel mkhan chen byams
pa shes bzang bde mchog la mkhas zer ba las gzhan khungs ma chod zer bas de gar thugs nges pa rnyed de dge 'phel du phebs bde mchog lo nag dril gsum gyi dbang 'khrid zhal
gdams rdzogs par gsan tshe bla ma 'khor lo sdom pa dngos su gzigs pa dpon slob gnyis ka'i che bar mngon/ rang gi bsti gnas su bzhugs pa'i dus thub bstan dge 'phel gyi
zhal bdag mdzad dgos par gsol ba 'debs mkhan sang nyin yong ba'i do nub 'od gsal gyi ngang du bzhugs gnas kyi seng g.yabs nas mi dmar rta dmar can zhig babs byung nas gus
pa chen pos phyag btsal te thub bstan dge 'phel gyi gdan sa la spyan 'dren par yongs pa yin zer ba la khyed su yin gsungs pas/ bdag sho dmar gyi brag btsan lags/ mkhas
grub dam pa khyed phu dgon pa'i gdan sa la cis kyang 'byon dgos bdag gis kyang 'phrin las sgrub pa'i grogs byed/ khyed kyi dgon pa 'di zhal bdag mdzad na 'di phyogs kyi sems
can thams cad 'phral dang yun gyi phan bde la 'god nus shing dam pa khyed kyi chos rgyun yang bstan pa ji srid gnas kyi bar du phyogs 'dir gong nas gong du 'phel bar
'gyur ro/ /zhes zhus 'dug cing /

srung ma 'di ni/ bar chad lam sel ma las/ brag nag ha po'i mgon khang duH sho btsan dmar po dam la btags: zhes pa de yin zhing rje 'di nyid kyi bka' las cung zad tsam yang
mi 'da' la/ gzhan du drag shul dang gdug rtsub che bas thub bstan dge 'phel gyi 'og tsam byang ri'i ldebs la rten mkhar yod pa'i mdun der bla chen sde dpon sngags pa rtogs
ldan sogs lugs gnyis gang rung gis mngon par mtho rlom rnams kyis rta ma babs na nyin zhag gi khongs su rta 'chi ba yong ba'i grags pas/ sa skya nas bdag chen rin po che
phebs skabs kyang de gar gtor bsngo mdzad rjes chibs yob g.yas 'bud/ zhabs 'bring ba rnams rkang 'gros byed/ phyag rdzogs kyi rtogs pa klong du rdol ba'i sgom smyon sprul
sku dang / stobs 'byor gyi dregs ldan sde pa nor bu sogs kyi rta na shi mang du byung bar rnam rtog langs gsol mchod phul bas mtshon ches mang la/ tshar lugs la de ring
zhugs pa'i gsar bu ba zhig kyang rta 'bab mi dgos pa sogs mngon sum gyi spyod yul du gyur pas so/ /'od gsal gyi ltas ltar sang nyin thub bstan dge 'phel gyi chos grwa chen
po nas/ gdan sa mdzad dgos pa'i snyan zhus 'bul mkhan byung bas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don rgya chen por 'gyur bar dgongs te thugs dgyes ba chen pos/ bka' las/ de
ltar kho bo la rtse gcig tu gsol ba 'debs pa yin na cis kyang de bzhin du bya'o zhes zhal gyi 'ches pas gsol 'debs pa rnams yid bde

ba'i dpal la bkod/ de nas mi ring par kha che 'dus bzang mkhas mchog dbyig gnyen gyi phyogs su byon pa bzhin ngur smrig gos kyis nam mkha'i kha dog 'gyur pa lta bu'i 'dus tshogs
kyi ser sbreng 'phan gdugs rgyal mtshan rol cha sogs mchod tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa thogs pas mdun bdar chibs bsu'i bkod pa sngon du 'gro bas rgyal ba zhes pa shing
pho rta'i lo thub bstan dge 'phel gyi gdan seng ge'i khri la zhabs kyi chu skyes rnam par bkod/ de nas khams pa sangs rgyas rdo rje/ mi nyag mgon po 'od zer/ chos rje
brag chos pa/ phu pa dbu mdzad tshul khrims sogs rin po che lta bu'i gdul bya dbang po yang rab kyi skal ldan rnams la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa slob
ma mchog la bshad bya'i dbang byin rlabs 'khrid lung shin tu smin pa lo 'khor gyi bar du 'dzugs pa lam skor phyi ma brgyad dang / rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis par kun tu
dgos pa'i gzhung bdun gyis nye bar spras pa'i gsung bshad/ gzhan yang dbang rjes gnang sogs so so'i blo dang 'tsham pa'i chos kyi sgo 'phar phye nas re ba don ldan gyi sa
la bkod/ de'i tshe 'od gsal la bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan pa yin zer pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen khyad du 'phags pa zhig dang rin po che rdo ring pa dngos su byon nas
dgyes pa'i 'dzum zhal bstan pa ni rin chen sgang pa sgos kyi zab chos rnams ches cher spel ba la legs so mdzad par 'dug /mgon khang du rdzas 'khor lo gzungs sngags sogs
chos skyong gi rten bzheng pa'i man ngag ltar legs par bskrun

te sman 'dam las grub pa'i gur mgon mi tshad tsam/ lha mo/ las mgon yab yum/ pu tra ming sring / zhal bram gzugs/ beg tse lcam dral rnams khru phyed do tsam/ rtag gtor 'dzin
gtor spyan gzigs sogs rgyas shing ngo mtshar ba dang / de'i bzo phud du lam 'bras dang lam zab brgyud pa rkang gang tsam khyad par rje nyid kyi sku 'dra mi tshad chung
phyogs tsam byon gtsang zhing rab gnas kyi skabs shangs g.yon gyi sbub tu ring bsrel yungs 'bru tsam gnyis byung ba/ phyis mkhan chen rgyal rtse ba byams pa ngag dbang bsod
nams rgyal mtshan gyis khrus gsol dang mchod pa rgyas par mdzad skabs snyan g.yon gyi ltag tu ring bsrel che tsam gnyis gsar du 'khrungs shing da lta'i bar du sku grib
kyi rnam pa byung tshe spyan g.yas g.yon gyi 'gug nas khrag mda' 'dra ba'i dmar po zhig spyan 'bras kyi dkyil tsam sleb pa rgyugs yong zhing de la khrus gsol byas na sangs
'gro ba'i ngo mtshar can ye shes sems dpa' dngos su bzhugs pa'i byin rlabs che nges/ phyi'i chos khri/ lha g.yabs/ de nang du bzhugs rgyur mang mkhar chu tshan gyi phu'i
dol mtha'i gzhi bdag la rdo lha bzheng pa'i rdo thong zhes bka' shog mdzad pa bsgrags pas rdo gang 'dod ldang tshod tsam rnyed pa'i ngo mtshar can la lam 'bras dang lam
zab brgyud pa brkos pa rnams la/ dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dang 'brel ba'i rab gnas sogs bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad/ gang gi sku rgyu rin cen rdo/ /sbyin po
dol mtha'i gzhi bdag kyang / /

las nyon sgrib pa kun byang nas/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang myur 'grub shog /ces smon lam 'debs pa gnang zhing sa phyogs gang du phebs pa'am bzhugs kyang rung 'byung po mi ma yin
mthu bo che mtha' dag srog snying mdong gsol du phul nas bka' bzhin bsgrub/ dgon pa shar sbug tu ngag dbang lha mo dbyangs can ma'i ljags bsnyen mdzad pa'i tshe me tog
dkar po'i char 'bab pa dang nye skor du brdung mkhan med kyang pi wang gi sgra snyan po gsan zhing mthar zhal mngon sum du bstan nas lung bstan kyang thob/ spyir rig pa'i
gnas lnga dang bye brag snyan ngag la thogs pa med pa'i rnam dpyod ni slob dpon bsten nas yun du sbyangs kyang skam skam khrig chags shig las yod dka' bar thugs rtsom gang
mdzad snyan ngag tu 'gro ba'i blo gros kyi spobs pa nang nas rdol bar mngon/ thub bstan dge 'phel du bzhugs pa'i dus rdo rje 'chang kun spangs chos rje'i rnam thar thugs
rtsom gnang ba'i sbyar byang du spyir dam pa 'di'i rnam thar mtha' dag ni so so skye bo'i spyod yul ma yin par gong du brjod pa dag gis 'grub pa dang khyad par rje nyid
zhal bzhugs dus gsol ba btab pa'i gsung las kyang grub thob thang stong rgyal po dang nged dpon slob kyi rnam thar su byung gi blo yul du shong ba med gsung pas bdag lta
bu blo gros chung zhing sbyangs pa zhan la brjed nges pas ji lta ba bzhin brjod nus pa'i spobs pa ma mchis shing / zhal slob mkhas pa dang grub pa'i dbang phyug du ma bzhugs
pa rnams kyis mdzad pa 'os su 'dug pas mdzad grub pa zhig

'ong ngam snyam sgug sdod yun ring po'i ngang du gnas kyang grub par ma thos pa'i mtshams su ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro rnams kyis cung zad bskul ba'i mtshan ltas kyang 'dug cing
gsung ngag rin po che'i bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gyi kha skong dang / skal ba dang ldan pa'i gang zag dag gi rgyud la ye shes kyi byin rlabs 'jug pa'i mtshams sbyor
du zhes byung ba'i ngo mtshar ba'i ltas ni gsung rtsom phyag bris ma las/ zla ba dang po la skyes pho mo mang po tshogs te sgron me khur nas rdo ring kun spangs pa'i grwa
pa rnams gar song 'tshol ba yin zer nas kho bo'i mdun phyogs su yad yud mang po byed pa la/ lan du rje'i grwa pa 'di dang 'di zhes bya ba mang po yod nga yang yin byas
pas 'o na rnam thar bshad rgyu yod dam zer ba la med pa snyam byed cing shin tu ngo gnong ba zhig la gnyid sad byung nas sems mi bde ba snyam byed pa 'ga' byung / de rjes
kyi zla ba phyi ma'i nang du nub cig rmi lam du bud med snum bag can mang po brag steng zhig na tshogs khu dir dir 'dug pa la ltar phyin pas de rnams thams cad yi ge 'ba'
zhig 'dri zhing kha mi 'cham pa'i zi re ba byed pa la don gang yin labs pas/ bud med rgan mo byad dmar cham me ba so 'dzar ba zhig na re/ nged rnams khyed kyi bla ma'i
rnam thar rtsom pa yin zer/ khyed rnams la rgyus yod dam byas pas po ti chen po zhig 'dug pa la mdzub mo btsugs nas 'di phag mo gru pa'i rnam thar po ti yin 'di'i nang nas
'dri ba yin zer/ khyed rnams ga nas yin byas pas nga ni slob

dpon lwa ba pa'i dus kyi la ba'i dum bu za mkhan gyi mkha' 'gro'i gtso mo padma'i dra ba can yin/ gzhan gzhon nu zhig la mdzub mo bstad nas 'di seng ge'i dra ba can yin/ gzhan
'di rnams phyogs bcu nas 'dus par 'dug zer de rjes gnyid sad bsams par rje bla ma phag mo gru pa'i rnam sprul yin pa ni nges pa can du 'dug snyam pa byung / de nas zhag
'ga' song ba na nub gsum bstud nas rmi lam du 'dre mnan gyi rnam pa yang yang du 'ong ba zhig byung bas 'di 'dra'i rigs ne gu ba rnams rlung dbu mar 'jug kha ma'i 'od
gsal gyi rtags su byed/ mgon po'i rgyud dur khrod nag po nas grib gnon lta bur 'ong ba dang zhes chos skyong gi rtags su'ang bshad/ gang ltar dge sbyong du bsrangs pa drag
snyam pa byas pas nub bzhi pa'i rmi lam du sngar gyi bud med de byung nas lag tu snag tsha thod pa gang dang lcags smyug cig gtad byung nas nged rnams kyis gang labs kyang
mi go bar 'dug /mi gzhan gyi bla ma'i grwa pas bla ma'i rnam thar 'chos kyi 'dug zer ba'i 'phro la gnyid sad byung bas kha sang nas kyi ltas thams cad 'dir 'dug pas da
sang rang nas/ rje'i rnam thar rtsom dgos snyam pa byas nam langs dge sbyor grub nas gnyid zir tsam byung ba'i rmi lam du chos khri zhig gi steng nas bande gzhon nu zhig
gis skyes rabs dpag bsam 'khri shing sgrog gin 'dug pa nyan mkhan yin zer bud med gzhon nu mchor mo mang po glu len rkang bro byed kyin 'dug pa rmis/ sang de nas 'go btsugs
nas brtsams pas ma grub bar la rje bla ma lan gsum rmis/

gzhan yang dge ba'i ltas mang po byung / tshar khar 'dod khams lha mo yin zer ba'i bud med bong bu'i rna ba yod pa zhig gis gtso byas mang po byung nas 'di la bka' brgya zhig
kyang gyis bstan pa nged rang gis bsrung zer ba byung ngo / /zhes de ltar 'dod khams dbang mos rnam thar gyi mjug tu bka' rgyas thob ces gsol ba la brten nas/ de ka'i
mjug tu/ nyi gzhon 'od kyis pad tshal 'byed/ /ku mud me tog zum par byed/ /'o ma skyes bu'i 'tsho ba de/ /brang 'gro'i srog 'phrogs ha la'i bcud/ /de bzhin dam pa'i ngo mtshar
gtam/ /skal bzang rna ba'i utpal rgyan/ /skal dman log rtog can dag gi /snying la zug rngu'i bcud len 'gyur/ /de bas gsang chen gtam 'di yang / /dad dang dam tshig
ldan pa dang / /dpyod ldan skal bzang gzur gnas la/ /ston gyis skal dman dag la min/ /zhes bka' rgya mdzad cing dpal ldan lha mo dud pa'i sol ba can 'di ni rdo rje 'chang
blo gros rgyal mtshan yab sras rnams la dngos su zhal bstan cing gsung gi gnang ba stsol ba'i srung ma'i dbang mo khyad par can du snang / rtogs brjod 'di nyid grub nas
rje btsun a wa dhU tI pa chen po'i slob ma'i gtso bo spyod pa'i rdo rje'i rnam 'phrul rje btsun grol mchog la gzigs 'bul gnang ba'i lan du/ blo gsal mkhas pa'i rnam dpyod
gsar pa'i mdangs/ /mkhyen yangs rgya mtsho'i lcibs kyi drung phyung ste/ /ngo mtshar dad pa'i spu long cher g.yos pas/ /dam tshig rdo rje'i mched po gang gi

drung / /kun tu dang ba'i rtse dga'i yid gcugs kyis/ /rnam grol mchog gi go 'phang ma thob bar/ /gang la gus pa'i ting 'dzin yar ngo'i dpal/ /snying la ri mor bris te 'di skad
zhu/ /dpal ldan bla ma a wa dhU tI pa'i/ /rnam thar legs bshad bye ba'i rang bzhin can/ /mthong tshe mgon po nyid dang sras thu bo/ /gnyis min yid la bsam pa'i lhag bsam
rnyed/ /sangs rgyas ngo bor gzigs pa'i bden pa'i bka'/ /thog mtha' bar du snyan tshig spel legs kyis/ /smra mkhas 'jam mgon dpa' bo'i sgra dbyangs la/ /tshim par mi 'gyur
'di na blo ldan su/ /zhes tshigs su bcad pa'i 'phreng bar phul nas slar yang phul pa'i snying po bsdu ba rje btsun a wa dhU tI pa chen po 'di nyid la zhal slob gtso
bor dpal sa skya pa ngag gi dbang po sogs che dgu ji snyed cig mchis kyang dbyings la ye shes kyi rgyas thebs pa ni rdo rje'i mched po gong ma khyed nyid las gzhan du mi
sems pa'i dad gus snying la bcags pa'i cha rgya cher 'phel ba'i skabs nyid du gyur lags zhes bstod sngags bkur gsum gyi zhu lan 'phrod pa'i lan du/ legs bshad kun dga'i dpal
ster mkhas pa'i rje/ /rnam grol bdud rtsis myos pa grub pa'i dbang / /rje btsun bla ma'i thugs sras kun gyi mchog /gang de'i zhabs sen padmo bzhad pa'i drung / /dam pa'i
ngo mtshar ma la ya rlung gis/ /snying dbus bdud rtsi'i rlabs 'phreng stong g.yo ba'i/ /blo gsal yid bzhin rgya mtsho'i 'jing dbus nas/ /zhu mchid sprin dkar dga' ma
'di spros so/ /kA ye lhag bsam

zla shel bzhu ba'i 'od/ /snyan tshigs bdud rtsis khengs pa'i zil dngar can/ /dkar gsal chu 'dzin bu mo bzhad ldan ma/ /zhu 'phrin dbyar skyes rdza rnga 'di skad zhu/ /a ho
drin can bla ma'i thugs kyi sras/ /byang phyogs 'di na nag po spyod pa zhes/ /snyan pa'i grags dkar g.yo ba'i mkhas grub dbang / /dam tshig rdo rje'i mched de'i bka' yig
gi /'tshams sprin blo mtshor shar bas snying myos kyang / /zla zhal mjal ba'i dga' ston ma thob pas/ /snying la khyod sku'i snang brnyan 'dri byed cing / /bsam gtan zol gyi
bdag por ngal gso bgyi/ /nam zhig mkhas pa'i zla ris gzhon nu de/ /'dren byed ri bo'i spo la shar ba'i tshe/ /snying gi ku mud 'dzum dkar bzhad byed cing / /zab dbyangs
bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyis sim par smon/ /skabs kyi zhu mchid snying por gsol na ge re lha khang du gnas dus/ stod lung nas bka'i glegs bu skyes bcas rje bla ma'i rnam thar
rnams phyag rgyas mtshan pa phebs pas dngos su mjal ba lta bu'i spro dga'i bdud rtsi gsar pas yid kyi chu gter ci yang gang bar gyur lags/ phebs don gyi cha la bsams dus
rje btsun bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid la zhal slob sngar dag pa'i zhing du gshegs pa 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug rje btsun kun dga' legs pa'i zhabs la sogs
pa rgyal ba'i rnam par 'phrul pas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa kho na yin snyam pa yod cing / da lta'ang dam pa nyid lta bu mkhas pa dang grub pa'i bdag nyid ji snyed cig bzhugs
bzhin du bdag lta bu rnam thar rtsom pa sogs

kyi spros pa byed na rang gzhi med kyi rloms par 'dug lags na'ang / bka' drin bdag rang la che ba zhig lags te/ bdag blun po lug bong lta bu 'di dus da lta dam pa'i chos byed
'dod dang nyams su len tshul cha tsam shes pa/ ltar snang mi khyur chud tsam 'di rje'i bka' drin kho na ma gtogs med pas bka' drin dran pas byung rgyal du brtsams pa lags
na'ang legs 'dug gsung ba'i mdong gsol phebs pas dam pa nyid lta bus g.yo sgyu dang gcam bu'i zol zog gsung ba mi srid pas/ cung zad mgrin pa'i gzengs bteg nas rang gis
rang la the tshom du gyur lags/ slad kyi zhu ba skye rgu rnams kyi phan bde mtha' dag rgyal ba'i bstan pa kho na la rag las la de nyid 'dzin pa la deng sang gangs can
gyi ljongs 'di na mkhas shing dngos grub kyis kyang brgyan pa 'phrin las kyi tha gru yangs pa sogs dge mtshan du mas mngon par mtho ba dam pa khyed lta bur mchis pas sku'i
'tsho ba yun ring du brtan pa'i thabs rnams la ched du nan tan dang ris med pa'i 'gro ba rnams la thugs brtse ba chen pos zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun
mi chad par bskor du gsol/ bdag kyang skabs sbyar zhal gyi dkyil 'khor lta zhing gsung gi 'bel ba'i gtam gyi bdud rtsi myang bar snying nas smon lam zhu zhing / de bar
du dben pa'i ri sul bsten tshul sogs kyi snying gtam snyan ngag gi lam nas drangs pa snang bar shar na'ang dge sbyor gyi bogs 'don du che ba zhig 'ong snyam pa'i dad pa
dang dag snang gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig yong ba'i bka' drin zhu zhu/ zhes

chab shog tu byung ba'i rjod don gyis rtogs par nus/ de yang dus snga phyi gsol 'debs su phyogs bsdebs las rnam thar 'di rje sgo rum pa dag zhing du gshegs rjes mdzad par dngos
su bstan pas gzhan la'ang mtshon no/ /dgung lo so brgyad kyi bar du phal cher thub bstan dge 'phel du stan chags shing stod phyogs kyi sa'i cha nges med du zhabs kyis
bcags te skya ser 'gro ba mtha' klas pa'i re 'dod skong bzhin pa nas phal cher lha sngags ye shes kyi thugs dam zab mo'i ngang nas/ dbang 'khrid lung man ngag gis skal
ldan gyi slob ma rjes su 'dzin pa dang bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rnam thar yid 'phrog utpa la'i do shal sogs bstan bcos mdzad pas mtshon 'khor lo gsum gyi bstan
pa spyi dang bye brag kha'u pa'i ring lugs phyogs brgyar 'phel bar mdzad/ mang mkha' mu gu lung du skad gnyis smra ba lo chen 'brog mi'i sku 'dra rin po che mjal bar phebs
pa'i dus sku'i thugs ka nas 'od zer sngon po 'phros te thugs kar thim pas zag med kyi bde ba chen po la yun ring zhig gi bar cham gyis gnas par gyur to/ /ris med yid 'gugs
thugs rje mig gi dkyus/ /ring yang mos ldan gzhon nu'i sen rjes shul/ /lhag bsam nu mar 'dud pa'i zla bzhin mar/ /mngon 'dod rtse dga' gtong min dngos po'i gshis/ /slob
bshad bdud rtsir spyod 'khu'i lha min mgrin/ /lung rigs tshangs pa'i 'khor los rab phug kyang / /thar srog mi chad cha mthun zil mngar khong / /song 'bras a ho rdzogs
myang skal bzang dpyid/ /

mig gsum me yis log 'dren 'dod lha'i lus/ /rab bsreg legs ldan mgrin sngon ral pa'i rtser/ /dbang chu'i brgyud pa chad med tshes zhag tu/ /'char ba'i zla zer phan bde'i kunda
bzhad/ /lung rtogs rin cen mi 'dzad 'byung ba'i gter/ /zab rgya gnyis spangs zhabs kyi rnam par thar/ /rtsom par lha dang mkha' 'gros brda thabs kyis/ /bskul ba'i sgyu
'phrul ngo mtshar rmad po che/ /rjes 'brangs nyi zla'i 'od snang sgra skad kyis/ /ma phyes rtogs brjod ba ku la yi kha/ dad brtson mkhyen rab mdzes ma'i 'gram chang gis/
/phye tshe legs bshad ze'u 'bru g.yur du za/ /spyod pa'i rdo rje gzugs gzhan yongs bsgyur dang / /rnal 'byor dbang phyug bla gos mnabs pa gnyis/ /phan tshun dag pa 'byams
klas snang ba yis/ /tha mal 'dzin pa'i kun rtog ming du zad/ /gsol 'debs las/ shar phyogs nor 'dzin lam la zhabs bkod tshe/ /rnam dkar thog ma'i rten 'brel mtha' dag 'grig
/grub pa'i gnas mchog sag thang jo nang sogs/ /rim par zhabs kyis bcags la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes sgyur byed ces pa sa mo phag gi lo dgung lo so brgyad kyi dus yul dbus
sman ljongs dga' ba'i tshal gyi gzhi chen por zhabs zung 'khor los mtshan pa'i re khA bkod nas lo gnyis tsam gyi bar du bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad pa'i skor gyi mang
mkhar nas chibs kha bskyod de 'bras yul skyed mos tshal du phebs pa'i bar rang gi rtogs brjod lam glu dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i dga' ston zhes tshig don phun sum tshogs shing
byin

rlabs kyi gzi byin 'od du 'bar ba'i tshig sbyor ma nyams pa la bar skabs su gsol 'debs dang stong thun dgos nges 'dra sbyar ba ni 'di lta ste/ na maHsarba gu ru buddha bo dhi
sa twe bhyaH phyi ltar na phyogs med kyi bande/ nang ltar na gsang chen gyi sngags 'chang / gsang ba ltar na rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po rdo ring kun spangs pa zhes
yongs su grags pa de'i thugs gnyis su med pa'i ye shes dang / chos dbyings bde ba chen po'i ngang du ro gcig kyang / chos can gdangs 'gags med kyi rol rtsed tha dad du
shar ba/ rje de nyid kyi zhabs kyi padma gtsug gis bsten cing / bka' drin chen pos 'tsho ba'i 'phrin las kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i bka' 'bangs rig sngags 'chang ba'i bande
blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ da lta ming yongs su grags pa tshar pa chos rje/ don la ci med kyi bhu su ku/ yul phyogs med du rgyu ba'i sprang
po yin pa blo bde zhes bya ba des/ yul 'dar stod mang mkhar gyi pho brang du skye ba med pa la skye ba'i cho 'phrul bstan/ grum stod khu'u'i brag la sgom rgyu rdul tsam
med pa la sgom pa'i ro myangs/ rgyal khams phyogs med kyi bzhi mdor rang don gyi dgos pa ci yang med bzhin du nyin mtshan yad yud du 'gro ba'i dgos don mang po spyod cing
gnas pa las/ bye brag tu rang lo sum cu so brgyad yan la yul dbus kyi sman ljongs su lan gsum phyin pa'i dang po/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam par sprul pa rje
ngag dbang grags pa'i zhabs phyir 'brangs te phyin nas lo brgyad tsam bsdad/ bar pa la sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i

sbyin bdag spa ra bas gsung ngag bla ma brgyud pa'i gser sku bzhengs pa'i rab gnas la phyin nas zla ba drug tsam bsdad de mgyogs bskor byas/ de dag gi lo rgyus rnams bshad
na/ dga' ba la bsams na nam langs pa 'dra ba/ skyo ba la bsams na sa rub pa 'dra ba/ btang snyoms pa byang thang skya mo la gar byed pa 'dra ba ji snyed cig yod pa labs kyang
sprang po'i glu la nyan mkhan med pas dgos pa chung bas rgyab tu skyur la zhog /lan gsum pa rang lo so brgyad pa'i dus su phyin nas lo gnyis tsam bsdad dus kyi 'phros
gtam/ yas phyin gyi lam du ji ltar byung ba'i tshul gyi rtogs brjod lam glu dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i dga' ston/ ku mu da gsar pa kha bye ba 'dra ba 'di nyid smras pa la ched
du dgos pa chen po mi 'dug ste/ gsang dgos pa'i mtshang kyang med pas/ snang ba gdong 'ded gzhir bzhag la/ da lam lab pa ngos 'di snang ba la shar byung bas gsan pa zhu
zhig /de yang / de gong phyin dus gra rigs sbyin bdag so sor yong ba'i khas len kyang byas yod pa dang / rjes su rim par nan tan gyi 'bod mi 'phral du byung ba dang / 'dul
bar 'os pa'i snod ldan gyi gdul bya 'ga' zhig kyang 'dul ba'i dus la bab 'dug cing / rang nyid kyang yul phyogs med kyi bdud rtsi bsten na nang du sems nyid la 'gyur ba
chen po zhig 'ong shas che bas/ de snga phyin pa'i dus/ sbyin bdag gi rta drel gyis bskyel bsu byas pa'i tshe/ rta rdzi drel rdzi mi ngan bsam pa chung zhing ltogs 'dod
che ba rnams kyi ngo mi zin bzhin du 'dzin dgos pa de zhe sun la skabs su mi bab pa zhig 'ong gin 'dug pa dang

/ khyad par lam bar rnams su yang sngar chos 'brel yod pa dang / da chos zhu 'dod kyi bla ma mjal ba/ gnas bzang po dang rten khyad par can mjal ba sogs dgos don thams cad
blos btang nas/ bde gzar chen po 'khrug kha ma'i gser yig pa bzhin du nam langs sa rub drel khal gyi rjes la lam gzhung bsrangs nas thal mar rgyug dgos pa de ye yid la mi
'bab pa zhig byung bas/ bya bral 'gros kyi 'gro bar brtsams te phag gi lo hor zla lnga pa'i dus/ sa gzhi rnams ma rgad gsar pas byugs pa ltar rtswa sngon gyis sngo 'jam
du gyur cing / indra nI la'i rgya mtsho glo bur du rdol ba ltar chu bo dang chu phran mtha' dag rab tu rgyas shing rlabs 'phreng gis mdzes pa'i lbu ba'i 'dzum dkar phyogs
brgyar rgod pa/ skye bo rnams dpyid kyi dus ston bzang po la babs pas dga' zhing chags pa'i rnam 'gyur shas cher ston pa'i ri klungs kun khyab par glu dbyangs dang rgod
sgra 'brel mar rgyu ba'i tshe/ gdan 'dren gyi pho nya dang bcas pa'i nged dpon slob lnga phrag gsum tsam yod pa thams cad ha cang rgan pa dang gzhon pa ma yin par lang tsho
dar la bab pa/ dge sbyong la 'os pa'i cha lugs ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan zhe gcig pa/ ched du spong ba lhur len pa'i mtshon byed ras dkar gyi lcog pu gangs ri'i dum bu
tshal du chad pa 'dra ba re dang / rba dbyug dkar po dung gi tshugs shing lta buu re/ bsam gtan gyi 'bol chung kha gang ma grwa zur ma nyams pa re/ grwa chung dang grwa
phad zur gsum padma rA ga dang padma'i rtsa ba thags su btags pa lta bu re/ skal

ldan rjes su 'dzin pa'i slad du snyan brgyud zab mo'i be bum po ti re dang bcas pa khur/ kho bo cag rkang 'gros kyis bul bas/ rta sngon po brtan brling 'dzom pa sga srab la
sogs pa dkyus thub pa zhig la zhon/ thub pas dbyar gyi ras chen gnang ba dang mthun pa'i char skyob kyi ras nam thang yug po che mu men gyi mtha' 'jag btang ba lta bu zhig
gyon/ mang mkhar thub bstan dge 'phel gyi dgon pa nas chas te/ rang gi bsti gnas su cung zad ngal gsos/ 'dar stod rnam rgyal stag rtse'i pho brang gi 'dun sar mchod rten
gyi rab gnas dang dga' ston bsgrubs te rim par chas pa ni 'di ltar ro/ /yid 'ong mtsho chen ngogs su chas pa yi/ /dpal ldan ngang pa'i rgyal po 'dab bzang dbang / /ngur
pa bye bas bskor ba'i mdzes sdug ni/ /mkha' la li khri'i rdul dmar 'khrigs pa ltar/ /de bzhin bstan dang 'gro ba'i don chen la/ /rings bar chas pa'i rnal 'byor ku sA li/
/ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i slob 'khor dang bcas pa/ /yul dbus 'dzin ma'i sman ljongs yangs par chas/ /gang de mthong ba'i skal bzang gzhon nu rnams/ /bde skyid phyi ma bde
ba'i rnam thar can/ /'di 'dra'i rjes su nga yang khrid na snyam/ /yid kyis re smon ci yang 'debs par byed/ /de'i nub ha cang mi ring ba'i grong khyer don grub gling zhes
bya bar skyed tshal ljon shing gi do ra 'khrigs pa zhig 'dug pa der lcog grwa rnams sprin dkar gyi 'phreng ba tshar du dngar ba ltar brgyab/ chos spyod kyi rim pa 'brug gi
sgra ltar du ldir/ rgya ja bzang po ngar ngad 'dzom pa'i

btung ba dbyar gyi chu mtsho ltar chal chil du longs spyod cing gnas pa'i tshe/ de'i dgon par chos rje'i drung gis nged dpon slob 'ga' gdan drangs gzhis len shangs len bzabs
ma mdzad/ nang so dang sngar 'dris kyi grwa pa rnams kyis kyang ja 'dren sogs legs tshogs kyi rten 'brel thog mar 'grig pa byung / de snga yan char dkon tsam yod pa la/
de rjes nged dpon slob rnams so sor dgongs thun gyi rim gnyis kyi rnal 'byor la 'jug par rtsom pa na/ phyogs tha gru nas char sprin dal bu gtibs/ 'brug sgra zab mo'i sgra
dbyangs dang bcas pa'i char gyi rgyun chen po babs pas/ 'bru bcud rnams rab tu sos shing skye bo rnams yid dga' bdes 'tsho bar gyur to/ /bhu su ku de lam du chas pa'i tshe/
/de yi gtsug rgyan rje btsun kha'u pa'i/ /thugs rje'i dge mtshan 'od zer stong 'phros pas/ /rgya mtsho'i klu rnams dga' ba'i zlos gar las/ /phyogs kun char sprin gsar
pas ched du gtibs/ /sprin rum nang nas 'brug sgra dal gyis rgod/ /glog 'bring gzhon nu'i go skabs dbye ba yi/ /yid bzhin spos chu'i char chen deng 'dir babs/ /lo tog rtsi
shing nyi gzhon gyis phye ba'i/ /padmo ji bzhin phyogs bcur 'dzum dkar g.yo/ /mi rnams sbrang rtsis myos pa'i bung ba bzhin/ /rab tu dga' ba'i dar dir glu dbyangs len/
/zhes bka' stsal pas char rgyun gyis 'dzin ma rnams brlan te myu gu'i 'tsho ba skyed bsring ba'i sngon 'gro'i rten 'brel 'grig pa'ang spyir dam pa 'di gang du byon pa'i
sar yul khams bde zhing bkra shis par 'byung ba chos nyid yin

la/ khyad par rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos rig byed ma'i chos skor na char dbab pa'i man ngag ches zab pa dngos su phyag len ma mdzad na'ang / rje btsun bcom ldan 'das
mas rjes su bzung ba'i byin rlabs kyi mthu dang nges pa'i don du rlung sems la dbang 'byor pa'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po rnams phyi nang rdo rje'i lus la gnad du bsnun
pas/ /ji ltar phyi rol de bzhin nang / zhes pa ltar nang gi ting nge 'dzin gyis phyi rol gyi chos rnams bsgyur du btub pa'i gnad gsang chen por mngon/ lam yig las/ sang
nyin snga bar chas nas lcags la zhes bya'i la brgal nas rim par brgyud/ lcags thang gi mda' phyug po shar ba zer ba'i khyim bdag dad pa can zhig gi lcang ra klu sdings
zhig 'dug par bsdad/ der zla ba yar ngo'i tshes bco lnga rje bla ma'i tshes mchod kyi skabs su bab byung bas/ bla ma mchod chog rgyas par byas sbyin bdag des kyang bsnyen
bkur 'bul ba sogs yang dag byung / sang tsha ba'i steng du bla ma zhang dgon pa ba'i sgrub gnas/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po'i gsung ngag rin po che gsan pa'i yul sag thang
ding zhes bya bar sleb/ de'i gtsug lag khang mchod rten chos khri dang bcas pa mjal/ phyag mchod smon lam gsol gdab byas te/ dpal jo mo nang gi ri khrod chen por sleb/
de'i nub sku 'bum thang du lcog gra byas bsdad pas/ der gnas mjal la 'ongs ba'i phyogs kyi skya ser pho mo mang po 'dug pa rnams kyis/ nged dpon slob la ston mo dag snang
skor ba chos 'brel zhu ba sogs mang po byung / sang snga dro sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo/ sbyor drug brgyud pa'i lha khang

sogs mjal/ ri khrod la rgyang bltas byas pas blo 'gro zhing yid 'phrog pa/ sngon gyi dam pa rnams kyis 'di lta bu'i gnas su sgrub grwa'i rgyun btsugs/ skye bo mang po thar
pa'i lam la 'god par mdzad pa ches cher ngo mtshar zhing rmad du byung ba'i rnam thar du 'dug /kho bo cag kyang 'di lta bu'i dben gnas zhig tu byang chub sgrub pa zhig nam
'ong snyam pa snying gi dkyil du lhang lhang ba'i dag snang byung ngo / /e ma nags rgyal sman btsun dbang mo'i ri/ /ri ngos tshang tshing 'khrigs pa'i nags kyi khrod/ /khrod
yangs rdo ba'i spyil chung skyid pa'i nang / /nang der byang chub sgrub pa'i skal bzang tsho/ /mthong ba'i mod la yid ni za zir gyur/ /bdag kyang nam zhig 'di 'dra'i
skal bzang zhig /cis kyang sgrub snyam snying gi gseb dbrag tu/ /'gyur med dam bca'i phur pa brtan por thebs/ /de nas mda' skor byas zhes byung / /gsol 'debs las/ gnod
sbyin dbang po'i gnas su mchod gtor phul/ /bla lung ri bor 'khrul zhig bla ma mjal/ /mkhas grub dbang po kun dga' legs pa la/ /zab mo'i dbang mchog gsan la gsol ba 'debs/
/zhes pa'i don lam yig las/ brag ram chos sde'i mgon khang mjal/ gnod sbyin chen po la snyan dar gsol mchod 'phrin bcol dang bcas pa rgyas par byas/ brag ram slob dpon pas
gdan drangs/ ja 'dren ras dkar gyi phyag rten dang bcas pa phul/ gnod sbyin gyi chos skor zhu ba'i snyan gsan phab/ rjes su de ltar byed pa khas blangs/ de dang khad nye
ba'i chu mo lung gi dgon pa na grub pa mchog gi dbang

po 'khrul zhig ratna bha dra bzhugs pa'i drung du mjal/ de nub tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang bcas pa'i sgo nas bcom ldan 'das padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa khrag 'thung lha
dgu'i dbang / de'i tshe dbang / bka' sdod ging lnga gza' gdong gi srog dbang bka' gtad dang bcas pa zhus/ sang 'gro khar nged dpon slob thams cad kyis lhan cig tu slob
dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas kyi sgo nas bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhus/ de'i tshe rje bla ma 'khrul zhig gi spyod pas hU~M ring hU~M thung gi gdangs dbyangs gar stabs nged
kyi grwa pa rnams la bka' bkyon dang thugs 'dogs spel ba'i hur spyod mang po mdzad kyi 'dug pas khong tsho thams cad dad pa skyes/ 'jig rten chos brgyad med pa'i bla ma zer
na 'di 'dra zhig 'ong ba yin zer zhing gda'/ bla lung ri bo'i spo la 'khrul zhig rje/ /kun bzang dgongs pa'i bcud kyis myos pa des/ /gar dgu'i rol rtsed hU~M sgra sgrog
pa'i tshe/ /skal ldan snying la 'dod 'jo'i bka' drin sbyin/ /zhes grub pa'i dbang phyug 'dar phya ru pa rin chen bzang pos byin gyis brlabs pa'i mgon khang brag ram du
gnod sbyin chen pos zhal dngos su bstan par bka' bsgo dam bzhag mdzad pa'i tshan du 'dug /dam pa 'di nyid kyi yongs 'dzin rnams kyi nang nas drang srong bka' bzhi pa 'khrul
zhig dkon cog bzang po 'di nyid bka' drin che ba'i bla ma gcig tu mdzad cing / yang gsang khros pa'i rnal 'byor mthar phyin pas gnod sbyin beg tse dang ging lnga gza'
gdong bran du 'khol/ rig 'dzin chen po rgod kyi ldem phru can gyi zab gter lhun grub dgongs pa zang thal la brten nas

gzhon nu bum skur rang rig gdod ma'i kun bzang mngon sum du rang ngo 'phrod pas phyi rol kun rdzob kyi rdzun phugs rdib nas gang shar thams cad longs sku'i zhing du 'byams
klas pas rje 'di nyid kyi nyams rtogs me long la gzugs brnyan bzhin bla nas blar 'phel bar snang / lam yig las/ de nas bo dong phun tshogs rab brtan gyi pho brang na/ rje
btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang po kun dga'i mtshan can bzhugs pa'i zhabs drung du mjal/ ngos kyi dpal kye rdo rje'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du
dbang bzhi rdzogs par zhus/ nged dpon slob thams cad thun mong du gser g.yabs zer ba'i 'khyams grwa zhig 'dug pa der phebs/ gdan khri shin tu mtho ba la bzhugs nas sku'i
