gzi brjid nyi zla zil gyis gnon nus pa tsam/ gsung gi gdangs 'brug ltar ldir bzhin pas rol mo bzang po 'khrol ba dang bcas tshe dpag med grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang bka'
drin bskyangs/ /kho bo rang gis sngar phul ba'i dbang dril shing khul mas gtso byas/ zang zing gi gnang sbyin bzang po'ang gnang / nged rang ni rje btsun rdo ring pa chen
po chos dbyings su gshegs rjes rje 'di nyid bla ma'i gtso bo yin zhing / rdo rje 'chang dngos kyi 'du shes yod pas dad pa dang spro ba cig car byung / grwa pa rnams ni
ha cang mjal dka' zhing gzi brjid che ba tsam 'dug /nged rang grwa pa rnams kyi bla ma chos rje bka' bzhi pa de 'dra ba zhig yong ba yin zer ba la/ nged kyis de 'dra ma
zer rje 'di pa deng sang gzur gnas kyis bltas na sa skya pa'i sngags 'chang kun gyi gtso bo/

nged rang bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i brgyud 'dzin rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu/ khyad par nged rang gi bla ma'i gtso bo rdo rje 'chang dngos dang zhal mi gnyis pa zhig
yin thag chod pas/ so sor snying nas gsol ba thob/ byin rlabs khyad par can 'jug nges pa'i khag khur ba yin/ 'phral che khyad che ba tsam rje la chos brgyad kyi rtog pa
ci mnga'/ sbyin bdag stobs ldan gyi zhabs tog la dmigs pa yin mod byas/ de mthun gnas gsar nas nang so zhal ngo rnams kyis kyang bsnyen bkur shangs len yang dag mdzad do/
/rnam rgyal rab brtan rgyal po'i pho brang na/ /chos kyi rgyal po rje btsun kun dga'i mtshan/ /'jigs med seng ge'i khri la 'gying bzhin du/ /nges don zab mo'i ngang nas
ma g.yos pa'i/ /zhal bzang ston gyi zla shel lta bu mthong / /zhabs kyi padma gtsug gi rgyan du blangs/ /gsang chen bdud rtsis snying la bde ba thob/ /kwa ye grogs dag chu
gter kha dog la/ /ma 'jigs dad pa'i gzings su zhugs shig dang / /bshes gnyen dam pa'i ded dpon bka' drin gyis/ /dngos grub nor bu thob par the tshom med/ /sa steng 'di
na rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /bstan 'dzin yongs kyi ral pa'i zur phud la/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i zhabs sen ngal gso ba'i/ /kho bo'i gtsug rgyan sngags 'chang 'di 'dra dkon/
/zhes pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhal slob kyi khrod kyi rdo rje 'chang kun spangs chen po'i 'og nas mkhas grub kyi dbang po rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po 'di nyid
'gran zla dang bral ba yin zhing / rje 'di nyid kyis kyang thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi rtsa ba'i

bla ma gcig tu mdzad/ 'di'i skabs lha rigs 'a zha'i sa skyong bar byang gtsang gi phugs su bdag po sngags 'chang pa'i mi srun sgyu 'phrul gyi 'khor lo ma 'khor ba'i mnga' thang
sgang la rgyab pa nas rje sgo rum par zhabs tog shin tu che ba'i gzi brjid kyi nyi 'od blo chung me khyer rnams kyis ma bzod pa'i rigs su snang / lam yig las/ de nas
rdzi lung du zhag gcig bsdad/ sang nyid dge sdings na dpal sa skya'i chos kyis mngon par mtho ba'i khri la bzhugs pa/ bdag chen rin po che khri thog pa'i drung bzhugs pa
dang mjal/ de snga nas dpon slob 'dris pa lta bu'i nang gtsang zhing thugs 'gol bas bka' lung bag phebs par gnang / nged rnams la bdag chen thams cad mkhyen pa chen pos
mdzad pa'i bla ma mchod chog rgyas bsdus kyi lung / de dang rjes su 'brel ba'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'dod zhus ltar bka' drin bskyangs/ sku na phra mo de lta bu la 'di 'dra'i
lugs kyi gnang skyong dang ngo mtshar ba 'ong ba nges par 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul yin pa la the tshom mi za ba 'dug snyam pa'i dad mos dang / sa skya pa'i rmongs
zhen gyis blo bde ba tshad med pa byung / byin rlabs kyi rten gnang sbyin sogs yang dag thugs rjes bzung zhes byung / gsol 'debs las/ khro phu dga' ldan byams pa'i bsti
gnas su/ /rdo rje btsun mo'i sprul pas lung bstan zhing / /DA ka'i sku la shel dkar myu gu ltar/ /gsal ba'i 'od snang gzigs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa ltar lam yig las/
de'i nub khro phur phyin 'du khang chen po zhig 'dug pa der sdod sa byas/ nged

rang gcig pur zhal ras lha khang gi phyi skor byed cing yod tsa na/ skor lam de na bud med gzhon nu nad pa yin zer ba zhig khyel byas nas 'dug /skor ba 'ga' song tsa na de
la mche ba je ring je ring yong gi 'dug /mig 'khrul pa'am/ krung krum lta bu la bcos nas 'jigs pa ston pa yin nam snyam pa'i tshe/ mthar kha thams cad mche ba skya zang nge
ba mtho re lhag pa tsam gyis khengs pa/ dpral ba'i dkyil na khrag gi mig sman tshe lung thang gi rdog po 'dra ba zhig byas har te langs byung bas/ 'di srin mo'am 'bal
mo lta bu zhig yin pa 'dug snyam yi dam gyi nga rgyal dang bcas pas lag tu 'phreng ba khur nas ded pas skor lam la bros song / rjes la bcug phyin pas lho phyogs kyi khyim
tshang gi nang zhig tu bros nas sgo de nang nas bcad song / de 'phral 'og tu log gam snyam pa la/ sems theng nge ba 'dra ba zhig byung nas skor ba gsum tsam byas pas/ khang
pa de'i steng nas bud med de'i mgo 'dra ba zhig skra zing nge ba mthong tsam byas/ skad gdangs ngar che ba'i gdangs ma dbyangs la/ dad mos kyi snang ba mi 'dug kyang
/ /tshe sngon gyi las 'brel gcod thabs med/ /khrag 'dzag srin po'i ri la phrad/ /'phan dkar gyi ljongs su rjes su 'dzin/ /'jigs snang log lta ma byed ang / /bde chen longs
spyod rnal 'byor pa/ /zer ba zhig labs byung ba'i mod la sngar gyi 'jigs snang de zhig pa 'dra ba'i rig pa had de chod de ba/ lus ljid med pa 'dra ba'i za zi ban bun/ /rdog
pa gar rgyab mi shes pa/ snang ba 'di gsal la bstad so med pa skad bton la

/ rgyug gam snyam pa zhig byung bas 'di bar chad dam dngos grub gang yin mi shes pa 'dug /da res nas brda zhig ston pa ma byung / da mngon du ma gyur ba la gsang dgos snyam
zla 'o rnams la bgros ye ma btang / de'i nub 'og gi 'du khang nang gi lcog bur bsdad pa'i tshe/ gtor bsngo sogs spros bcas kyi dge sbyor rnams kyang de ga'i ngang du 'gro
ba zhig byung / ci yin nam cha med ya mtshan ni che snyam dge sbyor gyi ngang du sral/ der byams chen/ sku 'bum chen mo/ rnam sras rang byon sogs mjal/ phyag mchod smon
lam yid ches pa btab/ sang tsha thon la dge sdings nas bdag chen rin po che'i phyag phyi drung 'khor gzhon pa kha cig kyang gnas mjal la byung / nged tshos ja bzang po bskol
nas drangs/ dag snang byas thams cad bsdongs nas zhal ras lha khang mjal/ de na phag mo zhal gnyis ma'i sku li ma zhig 'dug pa de'i phag zhal ngang thog gi bar la shel
gyi 'khar ba btsugs pa lta bu zhig 'dug pas/ 'di gang yin byas lag pa reg pas 'od ma gtogs reg rgyu mi 'dug /dkon gnyer de na re/ de phag zhal yin pa gda' zer/ de khong
rnams kyi ma mthong ba 'dug pas kha rog bsdad/ sku de la mgo gtugs de dbang bzhi blangs smon lam btab bo/ /lar rje btsun mkha' spyod dbang mo 'di nged rang la thog ma nas
dgyes pa zhig yin 'dug pas/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po'i gsung nas kyang / chos rje la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs byas res kyi nged la ltas khyad par can re yong gi
'dug /'bad rtsol mdzad na 'dis mkha' spyod la 'khrid

nyen gda'o gsung ba yod cing / 'di skor gyi gtam mang po zhig yod de/ snod mi 'dug pas nam mkha'i dbyings su phaT/ /sprang rgyal khams phyogs med rgyu ba'i tshe/ /yul ya mtshan
gyi ltad mo 'di ltar mthong / /sha ba dge sdings rdo rje'i pho brang na/ /rje sa skya lo tsA'i sku yi dbon/ /thugs gcig tu 'dres pa sras kyi mchog /khong 'jam dbyangs
gzhon nu dngos dang mjal/ /gsung bag phebs kyi bdud rtsi snying la sim/ /chos zab lam gyi rnal 'byor bka' drin zhus/ /khong skyon bral gyi mdzad 'phrin mthong ba'i tshe/
/nged sa skya pa'i mdun ma grub 'dug snyam/ /sems dga' spro ngang dad pas mchi ma 'khrug /zhabs spyi gtsug tu blangs nas smon lam btab/ /der shab stod kyi chu klung brgal
nas phyin/ /yul ya mtshan can khro phu'i gtsug lag sleb/ lha byams mgon gyi sku brnyan zhal bzang mthong / /rten khyad par can kun la byin rlabs zhus/ /ma mi min mkha'
'gros 'jigs gzugs bstan/ /nga khro rgyal gyi nga rgyal dbyings nas rgyas/ /mtshon 'phreng lcag gi 'ded drag btang ba'i tshe/ /khong lung bstan gyi sgra dbyangs sgrog pa
skad/ /khyod ye shes kyi DA ki'i lung bstan dang / /mo sha zan gyi mkha' 'gro'i rgyang 'bod gnyis/ /nga rnal 'byor gyi sems la bde sdug med/ /gang yin kyang rang ngo dbyings
su snyam/ /a la la rgyal khams bskor ba'i tshe/ /sngon men kyi ltad mo a re 'jigs/ /sems nyid kyi rang gdangs yin par go /drin can gyi bla ma de sku drin che/ /dpal mkha'
spyod kyi dga' ma yid 'ong ma/ /dus ring nas bskyangs pa'i ma ma des/ /da rig 'dzin gyi grub pa ster ba'i

brda/ /yongs ngo mtshar gyi zlos gar ci yang rtse/ /zhes 'byung ba khyab bdag bla ma 'di nyid 'das ma 'ongs pa'i gnas lugs mtha' dag gsal bar gzigs pa'i mngon mkhyen thag thogs
mi mnga' na'ang kun tu rgyus 'phags pa maunggal gyi bu bcom pa'i lo rgyus ltar chos gos 'og gi dug mdar ma dgongs pa'i bsngags brjod che na'ang rgyu mtshan 'og tu rim
gyis gsal/ khro phur rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i ngo mtshar cho 'phrul gyi bkod pa dang phag zhal gyi steng nas 'ja' tal le zug pa slar thugs kar thim pas zhag mang
po zag med kyi bde chen kho nar 'byams pa sogs drang srong srin po ri dang 'phan dkar gyi ljongs su rjes su 'dzin/ zhes pa'i don ltar rjes sor 'phan yul du phebs pa'i
lam zhig tu nam mkha' nas me dpung 'ur sgra dang bcas byung ba ci yin snyam gzigs pas chibs sga'i snga ru'i steng bab ma thag rnal 'byor mar gyur nas sku la 'khril bas zhag
bdun gyi bar zag med kyi bde chen kho na'i ngang du song ba sogs rjes su 'dzin pa'i lung bstan du nges/ lam yig las/ de nas gnas kyi mda' na dam pa dmar po'i rus yin zer
ba zhig gi lag na gdung rus las grub pa'i spyan ras gzigs kyi sku dang sras kyi thugs rang byon yin zer ba sogs 'dug pa mjal/ de'i nub gangs can chos 'phel gyi dgon pa'i
'khris/ lha mo dmag zor ma'i bla mtsho yin zer ba/ mtha' ljon pa'i tshal gyis bskor ba'i dbus na ne'u gsing gi dkyil na mtsho chung khor ba zhig 'dug pa'i kha stod skyid
skyid 'dra ba zhig 'dug pa der lcog grwa byas bsdad/ ja bzang skol zhing chos

spyod byas pas grwa pa rnams byon byung nas/ /'di pa cha lugs sogs rtogs ldan du mi 'dug /gra mthun la skying mdog rnam pa sgo yangs pa zhig 'dug pas/ sde pa zil gnon pa lta
bu zhig brdzus pa yin nam zer/ gcig na re nga dang zhal 'dris yod/ sde pa zil gnon pa yin thag chod 'dug zer bas/ phal cher de la yid ches song / su yin zer ba la/ nga
ci med kyi sprang po yin pa blo bde bya ba yin no ang byas pas/ khyod rang su yin kyang nyams dga' la snang ba bde ba zhig 'dug zer ro/ /thag khra sbrul du 'khrul pa'i snang
ngo na/ /'jigs skrag 'bros la thug pa don byed nus/ /yid ches mos gus ldan pa'i gang zag la/ /khyi so ring bsrel phung por song ngo skad/ /ming tsam brda tsam btags pa
kho na la'ang / /rang rang ngo bos grub pa rdul tsam med/ /ci med cir yang 'char ba'i ngo mtshar can/ /rten 'brel zab mo'i rang mtshang de ru rig /skye bos bzhi mdor smra
ba'i khungs med gtam/ /gang zer bden par 'dzin pa'i blo chung tshos/ /gzhi med ri bong cal gyi sgra dbyangs kyis/ /rang gzhan mang po'i rang mtshang ston nyen gda'/ /zhes
byung / gsol 'debs las/ chu mig nang gi rten mchog mtha' dag mjal/ /zab lam rdo rje'i pho brang e waM du/ /skal bzang rang rang blo dang 'tsham pa yi/ /chos kyi dga'
ston spel la gsol ba 'debs/ /zha lu gser bkang chos grwa chen po ru/ /bstan srung lha mo'i rnam sprul bud med gzigs/ /mtshan nyid kun ldan yongs 'dzin ku sA lis/ /dbang dang
rjes gnang stsal la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes

pa lam yig las/ stag la skya mo dung gi sgo brgal te/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rim pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i gnas gtsang chu mig ring mor sleb/ de nub gnas 'brel
byas/ sngon zangs dkar lo tsA bas bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang / gnyan sgrol/ 'phags pa rin po che'i sku 'dra sogs bzhugs pa'i lha khang / bdag chen rin po che grags blo
bas bzhengs pa'i mgon khang sogs mjal/ gsol gdab smon lam yid ches par byas/ /de dag la ngo mtshar zhing byin rlabs kyi zil gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig 'dug pas dad mos tshad
med pa skyes/ deng sang zhabs tog bdag rkyen cher med pa'i gogs nyams chen po 'dug pa la sems kyis mi bzod pa'i skyo snang yang yod pa zhig byung / sang nyin nyi ma
phyed yol tsam na ngor e waM chos ldan du sleb/ mdzo mo ra ba yod pa'i spang steng der lcog sgar byas bsdad/ lam zab lha khang du bla ma'i rnal 'byor rgyas pa zhig blangs/
spyi sgos kyi bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam btab gzhan yang lam 'bras lha khang gis gtso byas pa'i rten gsum rnams kyang mjal/ dbon po rin cen seng ge bas gzhis len skabs
bab byas/ khrom thog dpon po sogs 'dod chos dgos zer ba mang dag byung bas/ thog cig la gur mgon gyi rjes gnang byas/ 'phral mkho'i ja gos dar sogs 'bul ba'ang 'ga' byung
/ de nas zha lu la chas te phyin pa'i lam bar nas lcags stod mthong byung bas/ nged tsho sa skya pa'i yus po che'i mi gsum gyi nang nas/ shar smad btsong kha'i

dge bshes rin cen brtson 'grus kyi brgyud pa/ dpon chen dben shrI rgyal ba bzang po dang / hu shrI rgod po rin cen sogs rim par brgyud pa'i pha tshan shin tu nye ba zhig yin
pas/ khong tsho dar rgud dang bde dog gang 'dra zhig yod dam snyam dgos med 'jig rten gyi rmongs zhen zhig skyes/ zhu rag gi bsam pa med kyang bya bral gyi gnas skabs sems
la gang shar lag tu blangs chog snyam pas der phyin/ khong tsho'i gzhis ka'i stod der lcog gra byas/ ngas lcog bur bsdad/ khong grwa pa rnams nyams dga' ngang sbrags
pas bsngo ba smon lam rgyab pas mang ja nyung ja gdan gnon dang bcas pa bskyal song / su yin zer ba la nged rnams la stod mthon po nas yin zer ba byas na'ang / rjes su ngor
pa'i grwa pa 'ga' sogs rim par brgyud nas cha tsam ngo shes 'dug pas/ dpon 'og ma 'dra ba'i mi gzhon zhig nga'i rtsar byung / 'di 'dra yin pa 'dra zer ba'i rtsad gcod
zhib po byed kyin 'dug pas da ci nas nged bya bral du song bas skyug bro byas dogs spam me bsdad pa yin/ ngo bo de ltar yin pas mjal phrad tsam mdzad 'dod yod na de ga bgyis
pas chog byas pas kho log song / re zhig nas sleb nas/ deng sang sku mtsham me ba zhig yod pas mjal ma bde byung / sang nyin cis kyang bzhugs pa gnang dgos zer ba la/
mjal bzhed med pa thugs dang bstun pas chog pa 'dug /nged tsho rgyal khams la ring po yod sdod pa'i long med byas/ don la rang gi rigs rus dang pha tshan sogs gang yin gyi
blang dor med pa'am/ yang na mi sngun du ngo 'degs mi thub pa zhig

yod pa yin yod/ nga la shAkya thub pa'i bka' drin gyis phyogs gang la phyin kyang bsnyen bkur byed mkhan ni thogs med 'ong gi 'dug /'di skor gyi zhen thag de chod pas blo bde/
lar btsun pa gnyen sred ches pa la de 'dra mang po 'byon/ khyod snying tshim tshim snyam pa byas/ nam zi la langs phyin/ nged tsho'i rjes la chas ka phran bu dang bcas
lam sna ba yin zer ba zhig btang byung / mi dgos log rgyug byas kyang mi nyan par zha lu bar phyin/ de nub rgyan gong gi gtsug lag khang gi mgon khang mjal bas der gtor
ma'i 'khris su bud med gos dkar khra gyon pa zhig byung ba de mthar phyi nang gang du song cha med pa la yal ba lta bu zhig byung / zha lu gnas kyi gser bkang gi thugs rje
chen pos gtso byas steng shod kyi lha khang mgon khang rnams zhib par mjal/ gzhal yas khang gi mdo der drung chen bya ba yin zer ba'i gyong rgan bka' brgyud pa la rgyab
rten bcol ba/ dom ra dang slel bem gyi sgrib shing gyon pa zhig dang / drung rgyal ba zer ba'i ban gzhon mig ltag pa na yod pa 'dra ba zhig 'dug pas/ khong tshos ja 'dren
gzhis len byas/ khong rang tsho dang blo bstun pa'i cha le cho le mang po labs btang bas shin tu dga' song / de na je las pa bya ba 'grul pa thams cad la za 'dod byed
pa zhig 'dug pas/ slong mo dgos zer byung bas/ nged rang rnams sprang po ni mnyam por 'dug /khyed tsho zha lu ba yin snyam pa yod na'ang / nged tsho 'dar ba yin sprad chog
byas pas thams cad bzhad gad theg ge byung nas za 'dod cher ma byas/ de nub ri phug tu phyin/ bu ston thams cad

mkhyen pa'i chos khri'i mdun der lcog gra byas bsdad/ nA lendra'i bco brgyad pa'i 'tsho byed cig yod pa des gzhis len bsnyen bkur zur chas sogs zhabs tog yang dag byas/ sang
de ri phug bla brang na bzhugs pa'i bu ston rin po che'i sku 'dra phyag nas mas gtso byas pa'i rten gsum shar chen gyi rten sogs zhib par mjal/ mkhyen rab rin po che'i
zhal slob bgres po zhig 'dug pa la phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi dbang / rnam sras zhi drag gi rjes gnang / rdo rje rab brtan ma'i bka' gtad yig lung dang bcas pa zhus/ de nub
rdzing phur brag sgo ba zer ba'i khams pa phyug po zhig gis gdan drangs der phyin/ tshe dbang / rta mgrin gyi rjes gnang sogs byas/ ja bzang po zhig phul byung bas lam ja
la shin tu mkho ba byung / zhen med kyi nye du'i sgo bsnyegs pas/ /dgos med kyi lam stabs de ru bcag /don med kyi lung sbug bskor ba'i 'bras/ /'brel med kyi sa mtshams
de ru bris/ /spyir sems can kun drin can pha mar 'dug /sgos su byams gnyen la gang skyid yul/ /nga bya bral gyi mdun ma yang rtser yod/ /khyed pha tshan sku khams ci bder
bzhugs/ /dpal zha lu gser bkang gi dgon pa na/ /ban smyon kun gri rings la shal 'dzugs byed/ /mi bsad la ya 'ud mi gda' bas/ /sprang po ngas ri phug dgon par bros/ /sngar
'dris kyi slob mas zhabs tog bzang / /ku su lu'i bla ma lam du mjal/ /gang zhus kyi chos 'brel lhug par gnang / /khod bka' drin mi chung che bar 'khums/ /lar da lta gangs
ri'i ljongs 'di na/ /dgon spyi chos kyi rang tshugs

'dzin pa la/ /khong 'gran zla bral ba'i zha lu pa/ /bod chos sde'i tsho'i srog shing dam pa lags/ /zhes gsung pa bstan pa phyi dar gyi lo tsA ba brgya phrag tu longs pa byung
na'ang rgya mtsho mtha'i skad shes pa kho bo las ma byung zhes bsnyems pa'i tshul 'dzin pa 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyis rgya gar nas gdan
drangs pa'i rje btsun sgrol ma 'gangs can de mjal ba gnang ba'i mnal lam du bud med gzhon nu gos sngon po gyon pa zhig byung nas 'di gnyan lo sbrul gyi 'jigs pa las bskyabs
pa'i paNDi ta sangs rgyas gsang ba'i thugs dam gyi lha de yin zer ba sad tshe rje btsun ma sgrol ma dngos su mos pa'i thugs dad 'khrungs/ rting res snar thang byang
chen du phebs skabs dkon gnyer gyis mgon po zhal shing gi mchod rten 'di la gnas pa yin zer de nub der gzims pas A tsarYa zhig byung nas me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang bzhi'i
ngos 'dzin dang bcas pa smra zhing khyed rang gi gnas khyed rang gis ngo los shes zer dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur sna tshogs ston pa byung ba zhal gyi rnam 'phrul yin gsung /
lcags stod kyi lo rgyus ni lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med du gzigs pa'i rnal 'byor pa bzang ngan gnyis 'dzin gyi mtha' las 'das pa gnyen sred ci la mnga' na'ang / rang cag snyigs
mar spyod pa'i dge sbyong sa'i snying po 'khor lo bcu pa'i mdo nas bshad pa'i tha ma'i rigs rnams la bag yod byed dgos zhes gdams par snang / /lcags sgog lung pa bkra
shis dpal 'byor de skabs grags chung yang ku su lu'i mkhas grub chen por dgongs te chos 'brel gsan cing

rgyan gong du lha mos rnam 'gyur zur tsam byung ba sogs ni dus phyis chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i khrir phebs nas bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal ba'i rten 'brel du mngon/ gsol
'debs las/ gus ldan sbyin pa'i bdag po'i bar chad bsal/ nye bar mkho ba'i rnyed dang bkur sti bsgrubs/ /thar dgon sman lung gnas kyi lha khang mjal/ /rigs brgyud srung
ma mchod la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa lam yig las/ khong brag sgo ba bya ba'i phyug po de/ /mig rgya khab las phra ba zhig yin zer na'ang / /nga bya bral la lam ja bzang po
phul/ /dus gzhan gyi ja sigs gcig las dga'/ /khos khengs dregs kyi brnyas pa yin las che/ /yul rgyan gong gi lha mo de gnod kyi 'dug /ngas gtor ma dang bka' bsgo drag po
byas/ /de re zhig log nas bde bar byung / /de nas thar pa dgon par sleb/ /de nub bsdad nas de'i steng shod kyi lha khang mgon khang rnams zhib par mjal/ sang tsha thog tu
sman lung du phyin/ bla brang bde ba dang nye tshan rnying pa zhig tu 'gro bas ngo shes byas/ gzhis len yang dag byung / nA ro'i rgyan drug kha che paN chen gyi sku chos
sogs kyi byin rlabs zhus/ gtsang khang gi rten gsum/ smr-i ti'i gdung 'bum sogs mjal/ stag zhon mgon khang du gtor gsos snyan dar 'phrin bcol yid ches par byas/ de nas
pa rnam gzhung la phyin/ grong stod du zhag sdod byas/ sang nyin snga bar phyin lhun grub rtser sleb/ ngas gnas tshang zhig tu bsdad/ zla'o rnams gzims khang sogs kyi ltad
mo dang / zhar la bsod snyoms kyang byed/ sde

dpon chos la dkar po zhig yod pa 'dug zer nas song / khong rnams kyis nyi phyed bar bsgugs pas lan tsam yang ma khugs/ nged rang rnams kyi tsha thebs kyang chag pa zhig byung
nas log byung / lar gnangs chung la blo rigs rgod pa'i sde dpon dpon skya'i rigs 'di/ lug thug gi sgro bas wa mo'i nyin thebs gcig pa ma gtogs dgos pa mi 'dug pas de 'dra'i
rigs la bya bral rnams lam gzhung srong ba rang gnad du gda'/ de nas bsam sdings dgon par slebs nas de nub gnas 'brel byas bsdad/ sang nyin de'i ne gu brgyud pa'i pho
khrom mgon khang / yang dgon gyi lha khang mgon khang sogs mjal/ chos rje'i drung du nged dpon slob rnams kyis bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi chos 'brel zhus/ sger gyi mgon dkar
gyi rjes gnang zhus pas ma gnang bar/ rtsis kyi mgon po lha chen dpal 'bar gyi rjes gnang bka' drin bskyangs/ de nas rtsis gnas gsar gyi lha khang mgon khang rnams mjal/
sde pa bsod nams rab brtan pas gzhis len shangs len sogs yang dag mdzad/ der 'dol chung na tsha mo zhig yod pa des 'bod du rta pa gnyis rkang tshugs btang byung nas cis
kyang yong dgos pa'i nan tan byed kyi 'dug pas khong byings po der bzhag /nged dpon slob 'gas skor tsam phyin pas gnas tshul nges par byung ba lags so/ /thar dgon sman
lung 'phrul gyi lha khang mjal/ /pha mes brgyud pas bsten pa'i mgon gnyan de/ /snyan dar ba ling rgya mtshos mchod byas te/ /bstan pa bsrung ba'i 'phrin las bka' bsgo byas/
/

de nas pa rnam rdzong gi gzhung du phyin/ /'khor rnams gtor tshogs med pa'i rnga gshang gi /sgra dbyangs snyeg pa'i bya rog bzhin du 'gyod/ /kho bo pho tshod che ba'i khrom
thog chod/ /phyin chad phyogs 'dir 'ongs pa'i rnal 'byor rnams/ /'di 'dra'i rigs la rim pa ltar 'dzem mdzod/ /zer ba'i rgyang glu len zhing bsam sdings kyi/ /ri la 'dzegs
pas lugs gnyis 'dod pa tshim/ /yang smras pa/ nyang stod kyi a mo 'dol chung na/ /tsha mo zhig yod pas nan gyis bos/ /rngan chen dang gzhis len bsres se ba/ /khram dus
kyi kha rgyan bcas pa byung / /gter sbyin 'dra yod snyam yod tshod gda'/ /nga rgyal khams kyi longs spyod char ltar babs/ /chos ldan gyi 'gro sa tshags las mang / /dpon ngan
gyi khral 'bab yong don med/ /tshom po la snum bskus ma re mdzod/ /ces gsungs/ gsol 'debs las/ bsam sdings grub pa'i gnas sogs rim brgyud de/ /yul ljongs rnams su dad
ldan bkur stis mchod/ /shambhar gnas su 'dren mchog bla ma la/ /bstan srung rjes gnang gsan la gsol ba 'debs/ /dus der ye shes chen po gzigs snang du/ /zhun chen dud sprin
me rlung 'tshub pa'i dbus/ /'jigs rung stag smyon zhon pa'i mon pa che/ /'khor bcas gsal bar shar la gsol ba 'debs pa/ /zhes lam yig las/ de nas bod kyi lha btsan po'i
gdung brgyud dri ma med pa skya bo byang chub sems dpa'i mdzad pa lhur len pa/ 'brong rtse nas khri nam mkha' bsod nams kyi drung bzhugs pa'i gzhis ka rnam sras mthong smon
dang khad nye ba zhig

tu sleb/ su yin rtsad gcod mi gnang byung bas/ dpal ldan sa skya skor nas yin zer ba'i brdzus se ba zhus kyang dgongs nas cis kyang shog gsungs nas phyin/ zhabs tog gzhis len
yang dag thugs dkar bas kun nas bslangs pa mdzad/ sde ba'i drung du padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ bka' sdod rnams kyi srog dbang
sogs phul/ gzhan yang 'dod chos kyi thugs bzhed mang po 'dug pa yar lam 'bul ba'i khas len zhus nas rgyal mkhar rtser phyin rdzong rgyab tu lcog gra byas bsdad pas/ gnas
chen pas cis kyang yong dgos gsungs/ dpal 'khor bde chen gyi shag tu bos gzhis len mdzad/ nang ses sne sbyor mdzad nas chos sde'i lha khang steng shod/ mchod rten chen
po/ rgyal rtse'i li ma lha khang / gzims chung steng shod 'ga'i rten rnams zhib par mjal/ rgyal rtse nas sde pa chen po de nyin re bzhin chos sde la zhabs skor la sgrigs
bcug phebs pa mthong bas/ deng sang gi a po hor 'dra'i don spyi yod pa zhig mi 'dug na'ang / chos rgyal gyi mdzad spyod skyo sun med par bsgrigs su bcug pa 'di tsam rang
thog tu babs na'ang nus pa dka' bas nges par chos rgyal du 'dug snyam pa'i dag snang chen po byung / de rjes 'brug pa ngag dbang chos rgyal dang de gong nas gsung chos kyi
'brel pa yod pas mjal ba dang ra lung bskor ba sbrags mkha' ro nas yar 'brog gi nang la zhugs/ do ri sogs gnas mjal rim par byed 'dod yod na'ang gra pa rnams kyang mgyogs
skor la dga' ba tsam 'dug cing /

nged rang gi rkang tshab kyi rta de yang babs kyi rnam pa yod pa zhig byung ba sogs phyogs du ma nas mdor bstan pas 'phred la bcad de rong chung la 'gro ba'i gros thag bcad
do/ /bod rgyal po gzhon nus gtsug gis mchod/ /shar rgyal po'i mdzad pas yid rab phrogs/ /rta mdo phrug gi bar 'gros de ru zad/ /khong grwa pa kun za thag nye la dga'/ /dpal
ra lung gi ri khrod lta ba dang / /pha ngag dbang chos rgyal mjal snyam tshe/ /lus 'khos med kyi rkang pas rang mtshang bstan/ /nga lugs gnyis kyi blang dor mi zhan kyang
/ lus rkang pa'i 'khrul 'khor 'dor len bral/ /khong dud 'gro la 'gro 'dug gi skyabs gnas 'chol/ /nga mi phyed du 'dug snyam snying khong grang / /nga yang cig bsams
pa 'di ltar shar/ /gnas lugs la lta ba'i mig yod na/ /chu bur gyi khra hrig med kyang chog /ci bsam kun 'grub pa'i blo yod na/ /sha rus kyi rkang pa med kyang chog /sems
nyid kyi yang dgon mthong tsa na/ ra lung gi ri ltas de gar gda'/ /dad mos kyi rang zhal mjal tsam na/ /mtshan ldan gyi bla ma de gar gda'/ /gang byung gi chog na ci byas
bde/ /bya btang gi blo sna gang shar yin/ /'gyur med kyi bden grub med pas 'tshengs/ /rong chung la sprang po'i lam sna zug /dpal 'khor bde chen du bsdad pa'i dgongs de/
nged ni gnas chen pa'i mkhar las byed sgang gi nang 'u lag pa dang thug chom gyi khengs pa der nan med byas sgor bas zhe sun la tshig pa za/ zla bo rnams ni de'i nub char
lhags 'dres pa zhig gis lcog bu rnams bsgyel/ 'dam bag gi dkyil du nyal dgos

byung 'dug /nged rnams chos sde'i sgor 'dzom tsa na thams cad phar yus tshur yus su 'dug pas/ ngas kha ma blangs par sngon la thal le phyin/ nyang stod gu la'i phu de na pho
rog mdo sde mgon po bya ba'i grub thob cig gi sku 'dra snyan grags can/ mgon khang dang bcas pa 'dug pa mjal/ de nub dpon slob thams cad rnam sras mthong smon du 'dzom/
sang mkhar kha'i mdun man lung dgon pa'i 'khris la byas/ thu ru stag tshal zer ba'i lung nang du zhag gcig bsdad/ sang de snga bar la shin tu che ba zhig brgal phyin pas/
rong sham bhar gyi dgon par tsha ba phyi ba la sleb/ sham bhar chos rje'i drung du mjal/ mgon po stag zhon 'khor bcas kyi dbang rjes gnang / rong pa'i stag zhon gyi phur
dbang du grags pa'i rten mjal bka' bsgo dang bcas pa zhus/ chos skyong de'i chos skor tshang ma dang / zhal bzhi pa'i las mkhan pu tra nag po rnams zhu ba'i rjes su sleb
pa'i rgyu mtshan phul/ zhal bzhes kyang phebs so/ /lha snyan sham bhar mgul gyi dgon par slebs/ /'khrul zhig bla ma'i zhal bzang mngon du byas/ /pha mes brgyud kyi srung
ma nag po de'i/ /sku brnyan mthong zhing dbang dang rjes gnang thob/ /de nub gnas der nyal ba'i 'char sgo la/ /gnyid 'chag thog 'tsheg ba spu zing nge ba/ /mngon sum rmi
lam gang yang ma yin pa'i/ /'og 'gyu'i tshul gyi za zi'i 'char tshul ni/ /gsur dud me dmar 'tshub ma'i lung stong na/ /stag chen smyon pa zhon pa'i mon nag cig /bstan dgra
dam nyams 'tshol zer rgyug cing 'dral/ /

stong gsum khu sgras 'gengs shing yod do snyam/ /res 'ga' ling pa khyi khrid mang po yis/ /ri dwags 'ded cing bsha' ba'i dmar myog dang / /gzhan yang stag gzigs dom dred bya
'ug sogs/ /rgyug 'bral 'phur lding ban bun za zi yis/ /nam langs bar du thub pa'i 'khrul snang byung / /de dag legs par bsams tshe pha rgod rje'i/ /bstan srung mchog 'di
mngon sum zhal gzigs nas/ /sgos dgra kha khyer khur nas za ba sogs/ /'jigs su rung ba'i las rjes mngon du bstan/ /de yi rig 'dzin rnal 'byor bdag yin pas/ /da dung 'di
yis dam nyams mang po la/ /drag po'i las sbyor 'grub pa'i ltas su go /de nas sha ra'i gru lcags thon pas/ de'i gru shan gyi rta mgo'i ngos la rin spungs nas sde pa'i bka'
shog lcags leb la gzong ris bris pa gser chus byugs pa la/ gru lcags 'di dge rgyun la btsugs pa dang / mnyan pa la gzhis zur na byin yod pas/ za 'dod kyi gtser ba byung
na ngo bsrungs med pa'i zhu bas sleb pa gyis/ phyis 'doms pa'i khrims lugs byed zer ba gzer gyis bsdams nas brgyab 'dug cing / mnyan pa de rnams kyang snga gong dang mi 'dra
ba'i ngo gnong pa byas/ ltogs 'dod cung zad byed 'dod pa'ang gnang sbyin zhu ba yin zer ba las mi 'dug pas/ gzhis ka rin spungs pa khrims dam zer ba'i snyan grags bden
par 'dug /rgyal po khrims lugs yod pa'i sa phyogs 'di 'dra ba zhig yong ba yin/ snyoms chung lam bde ba/ rdzas ldan blo bde ba sogs bsod nams dpag med 'ong ba 'dug /ngo
mtshar snyam pas sde pa

la'ang dag snang ci yang skyes/ zhes 'byung bas bsam sdings nas rim gyis 'chi med kyi grong khyer la co 'dri ba nyang stod kyi yul gru rnams zhabs kyis bcags nas shambhar du
yab mes kyi chos skyong dpal mgon stag zhon nag po'i chos skor rnams gsan pas bstan dgra tshar gcod pa'i ltas mngon sum du bstan cing / rje 'di nyid la rgya zhang phrom/
drang nga kun grags/ chos dbang / ayon gling pa sogs kyi gter nas byon pa dang / jo bo chen po/ dpyal pa sogs las 'ongs pa'i stag zhon mtha' dag gi bka' babs pa'i be'u
bum kyang dbang lung man ngag thams cad khungs btsun brgyud pa las nye bar 'ongs te yid brtan du gyur pa ma gtogs khungs med dang lung med kyi dpe hrul sdud pa'i zog spyod
mkhan po rnams dang 'dra ba ni ma yin no/ /gsol 'debs las/ skyed tshal dgon par chos kyi sbyin pa mdzad/ smyug ri'i yang rtser rje btsun 'phrin las pas/ /'dzum zhal bstan
zhing dgyes pas byin gyis brlabs/ /gsung gis rtses su bsngags la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa lam yig las/ /de nub 'bras yul skyed tshal du sleb/ gra pa rnams shol rag chen
po der lcog gra byas/ sger gyis mkhyen rab chos rje'i dbon/ nged kha'u brag rdzong pa'i gra rigs kun gyi gtsug rgyan rje brag dkar rab 'byams pa bzhugs pa'i gzims spyil
du phyin nas mjal/ dad pa dang dag snang bsam gyis mi khyab pas zhal 'phros 'bel gtam 'ar ma 'ur ma byas skyed tshal ba'i gra pa sngags chos kyi 'dod zhen che ba mang dag
la'ang rjes gnang rig

gtad lung sogs mang po byas/ de'i tshe karma pa mi bskyod rdo rje gzhu lung par phebs/ sde pa rin spungs pas gdan 'dren zhu rtsis dang / mnga' zhabs kyi skya ser thams cad
la zhabs tog dang bsu ba sogs kyi khral rgyab/ thams cad dga' ba dang skyo ba spel ma'i 'ur ding ba 'dug /'bras yul ba dpon slob kyang de ga'i grabs yul khur che ba spro
seg ge ba yod 'dug pas/ nged kyi bsam pa la 'bras yul ba'i tshan 'di dpon slob sbyin bdag la bsten pa'i khral 'bab tsam ni mi byed kha med du 'dug /de tsam gyi dang dod rang
byed pa'i 'brel med dam snyam pa shar/ ngo shes phrad pa rnams khyed karma pa mjal las che zer/ 'phral de tsam byed zer ba tsam byas/ don la karma pa rang skyes bu dam
pa yin nyen yod mod/ nged rang gi thos tshod la dpags pa'i lhan skyes kyi shar tshod karma pa'i rtsa ba dang dwags po rin po che'i slob ma'i gtso bo khams pa mi gsum du
grags pa'i nang tshan/ dus gsum mkhyen pa khams pa dbu se zer ba de yin pas/ khong rnams la babs thob byed na/ rgya gar gyi nA ro mai tri sogs kyi gdams pa bod yul gyi mar
pa mi la sogs nas brgyud pa'i sgrub brgyud bka' babs chu bo'i gzhung lta bu zhig yod pas/ de gtso bor skyong dgos rgyu yin pa la/ dgos pa'i mchod rten nag por bzhag mi
dgos brag la dbu dkar gsol ba'i dpe'i rnam pas sa skya pa dang / dga' ldan pa sogs gang byed la mi bsdo bzhin du 'gran pa'i rnam pas mtshan nyid dang / sgra snyan ngag /rgyud
'chad nyan 'di nas 'chad rang cher med pa'i rnam grangs

mang la dngos ma gtsang ba myog pa zhig dang / 'jig rten gyi dpon chen dang / dpon chung dang / yang chung sogs chos brgyad gong 'phel gyi bya ba lhur len pa 'dra ba/ khong
rang gi brgyud pa'i bla ma dang de dag gi gsung rab rnams la chas chos ras su bor re ba/ deng sang karma pa rang gi bshad sgrub kyi bstan 'dzin cung drag pa rnams la'ang
smod cing / de dag gi gra rigs drag pa tshun chad khong rang gi phyag phyir gang khugs byed pa sogs 'dug zer bas/ snying nas dad pa ldang ba ni ma skyes byung / de phyin
nged rang sa skya pa'i bza' rkang ma gtogs/ karma pa'i khral 'bab kyi khur ni ci yang med/ deng sang gi mi phal cher gyi byed pa ltar/ sde dpon dpon skya zhig gi bla ma
bcol 'dug na cis kyang chos zhu snyam pa dang / mtha' mi mang gis skor 'dug na sangs rgyas yin snyam rgyug pa'i blun po ni nged rang min/ rang gi dgon chung la mang ja 'gyed
bcas yod dam snyam pa dang / gzhan dgon chung ngam grwa rigs re re tsam 'byor re ba'i ched du chos 'brel zhu ba'i ltogs la me 'bar gyi bla ma slob dpon ni min/ legs legs
kyi khral 'jal ni byed don mi 'dug /lar rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po dang mjal nas gsung ngag rin po che 'di thob man chad/ gzhan bla ma dang gdams ngag gang la'ang
byang chub sgrub pa'i ched du mi smon zhing / 'gram chu mi ldang ba'i nges shes gting tshugs shig yod pas lam gzhung bsrangs phyin/ 'on kyang rje thams cad mkhyen pa karma
'phrin las pa'i zhabs 'bring du karma pa'i zab chos mang po thob pas/ karma pa sngon ma rnams kyi sku skye yin

thag chod na mi btub snyam/ ma dad ma gus pa ye ma byung ba byas/ de yang spyir theg chen gyi gang zag gis sems can thams cad drin can gyi pha mar shes nas dag snang sbyong
ba dang / bye brag tu gsang sngags bla med kyi sgor zhugs pa rnams kyis cir snang thams cad lha dang ye shes kyi rnam rol du shes par byas nas de dag la dad pa dag snang
tshad du bskyal nas so so'i rang zhal rjen par mthong ba'i mod la lhug par skyong ba 'di gnad du yod pas de ga'i ngang du mnyam par bzhag pa lags so/ /rje yongs grags kyi
sangs rgyas karma pa/ /bod skye bo kun 'dus pa'i gnas gcig pu/ /khyed bslu med kyi skyes bu los kyang yin/ /khong dad can kun 'khor ba'i mtsho las sgrol/ /sems log rtog
gi sprin gyis ma bsgribs kyang / /khyed mdzad spyod kyi rnam thar 'od dkar gyis/ /nga snying dbus kyi padma bzhad ma nus/ /dus da res rgya lam srong ba zhu/ /khong phal
cher gyis mjal ba stong 'ur yin/ /khong la la dag mjal ba de che 'dod yin/ /khong 'ga' zhig mjal ba ltogs 'dod yin/ /khong de 'dra tsho snying nas dad pa min/ /nga skad stong
la rgyug pa'i khyi rgan min/ /nga lto phyir du rgyug pa'i sprang rgan min/ /nga zol zog gis 'khor ba'i blun rgan min/ /nga dgon chung gis phongs pa'i bla rgan min/ /gnas
dpal ldan sa skya'i dben gnas mchog /dpal kha'u'i brag gi pho brang na/ /rje rnal 'byor dbang phyug rdo ring pa'i/ /thugs gcig tu 'dres pa'i gces phrug yin/ /ma bdag
med mkha' 'gro'i thugs kyi bcud/ /rje rnal 'byor dbang phyug zhal gyi rgyun/ /

dpal sa skya'i bla chen gdams pa des/ /rgyud yongs su tshim pas gzhan mi smod/ /dus da lta'i sa brdzus kyi bande tsho/ /chos 'di 'dra'i skal bzang ma thos pas/ /sems chos brgyad
ltogs 'dod kyi rgyug 'bral gyis/ /yul gar 'gro dang 'dir 'gro med snying re rje/ /rje drin can gyi bla ma rdo ring pa/ /khyed bsams bzhin du bka' drin 'khor thabs med/
/sprang rang mgo thon pa bla ma'i drin/ /de dran pa'i mod la mchi ma bku/ /nga phyogs med kyi dad pa mkha' ltar yangs/ /sgos karma pa la snying nas dad / /khyed chos
brgyad ltogs 'dod don gnyer tsho'i/ /gnas tshul nas smras pa bzod par gsol/ /zhes pa sde srid rin spungs pa dang mchod yon gyi dbang gis skyed tshal ba rnams mi chos kyi
mthun 'jug 'os 'tshams las dang dod lugs gang sa nas dgos don med pa'i pher rgya la thugs khrel ba med par snang / rje 'di nyid dpon slob lnga tsam dbu zhwa dmar po dang
nyid kyis sku gzan ser po bzhes te skyed tshal seng g.yabs nas gzigs rtog mdzad pa rje btsun bod mkhar ba dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam 'gro ba'i tshogs su bzhugs pa des
gzigs ma thag thugs dad shin tu che bar 'khrungs te de nyin brang khang du gdan drangs rnyed bkur cher bstab/ chos 'brel gyi thog mar zhal gdong brnyan can gyi rjes gnang
gsan zhal slob kyi khrod nas mngon spyod kyi las sbyor yongs su rdzogs pa la brten te khra ma nas rtsa brlag tu btang ba sogs drag las la bka' babs shin tu che ba yong
ba'i

rten 'brel 'grig gam snyam/ rje mi bskyod rdo rjes res gsang sngags rnying ma chos log dang skabs 'gar gter kha 'og ma'i tshes bcu 'dzugs pa/ 'bri gung zur ba rin po che dang
mjal dus bsnyen phur sogs sngags chas rnams dbu thog tu bzhag nas nga yang 'di 'dra ba zhig 'dod ces gus par mdzad/ sne'u sdong gong ma chen por phul ba'i chab shog tu/
deng sang dbu ru byang phyogs brgyud 'di na/ /gter ston lcang lo can zhes bdud sprul de/ /zhes dang / bla ma gter gro bar zlo bzhes thugs rnal du mi gnas pa'i gsung rigs
dang mdzad pa sna tshogs la dang ba mi skye ba ni thugs bden par ma zad/ sgar chen 'dzam gling rgyan zer ba'i stong 'ur la sku'i ba spu'i cha shas tsam yang mi ldang ba
rje btsun kha'u pa'i spyan sngar phebs pa nas bzung bla ma dang chos gzhan la brten nas byang chub mi sgrub pa'i dbang rnon chos rjes 'brang ba'i thugs mos la lhag par nges
rnyed kyis lag pad snying gar zum mo/ /rim gyis lha mthong ba'i rdzong lhun grub rab brtan du phebs/ zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta sbrags ma'i dbang sogs bka' drin du stsal/
smyug la rdzong du rje karma 'phrin las phyogs las rnam rgyal du grags pa mjal du phebs/ der bdud mgon zhing skyong seng gdon can dang dam can mgar nag sogs kyi chos
bka' ci rigs gsan/ spyir ris med pa'i bstan rgyun la dgongs pa'i 'chad nyan dang khyad par rje 'phrin las pa nyid kun mkhyen bkras rnam pa'i dbon por song ba'i thugs zhen
gyis nA lendrar phan thogs mdzad dgos pa'i bslab bya/ gong dkar chos sder phebs rtsis kyis rgyu mtshan

gsal bar thugs shin tu mnyes pa'i sgo nas phyag thugs kar thal mo sbyar te rjes su yi rang dang bsngags pa rgya chen po mdzad/ bla ma dam pa 'di nyid kyang thugs dad shugs
drag po'i rkyen gyis spyan chab 'khrug pa sogs phan tshun 'bral mi phod pa lta bu'i thugs yid gcig 'dres su gyur/ de nas mi 'gyangs par dpal 'dam bu byin gyi chos grwa dang
sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms kyi rnam sprul thu btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal gyi gdan sa gong dkar rdo rje gdan du phebs te/ smin grol lung man ngag sogs zab rgyas chos kyi
sgo 'phar phye nas gdul bya rnams bzang po'i skal ba can du bkri bar mdzad/ thub bstan dge tshogs 'phel nas thos bsam 'bras/ /yul ljongs skyed tshal bar gyi zlos gar gtam/
/bcad lhug spel legs nyams 'gyur dbyangs can ma/ /mgrin par byon nas gsungs kyang de las ci/ /sa skya'i ring lugs mthor brtsegs kha ba'i rir/ /kar mtshan na bun 'khrigs
pa'i bshes gnyen dang / /thugs yid 'dres pa'i mdza' bcings zhags pa de/ /'brom ston nag tsho'i rnam thar gnyis pa bzhin/ /'phags bod gzhung brgya smra ba'i chos grags dang
/ /nges gsang theg pa mchog gi sde chen por/ /skal bzang skye rgu'i bung ba tshim byed pa'i/ /bshes gnyen pad dkar 'dab stong deng 'dir 'dzum/ /gsol 'debs las/ bde ba
mchog gi pho brang srin po rir/ /slar yang rdo rje btsun mo'i rnam sprul gzigs/ /mkha' spyod dga' ma'i mdzes sku snyan grags can/ /rtsol med thugs rjes mjal la gsol ba 'debs/
/chu

'dzin dkar po'i gur khang la gnas pa'i/ /'chi med gzhon nu'i dris lan dbyangs kyi skad/ /rab dkar lha yi bdud rtsi gsar ba'i rgyun/ /ljags kyi padmar sim la gsol ba 'debs/
grub mchog dbang po bsod nams bstan 'dzin gyis/ /dud sol lha mo bka' yi bran du gtad/ /dpal ldan bla ma'i sku dgra dngos su bsgral/ /mngon spyod 'phrin las sgrub la gsol
ba 'debs/ /zhes rje btsun mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug gnyis spangs zhabs sogs dam pa bcu phrag tsam bsten nas me 'bar mas thog drangs mgon po lcam dral gyi chos skor rnams
gsan pa'i dus/ bye brag 'dod khams ma'i skor la tshogs bdag ltar sgrub pa/ bka' sdod ltar sgrub pa/ phyi pa ltar sgrub pa/ nang pa ltar sgrub pa rdzogs par gsan kyang sa
lugs la rjes gnang zur bka' dang dam pa'i yi ger yum 'khor dang bcas pa sgrub pa la ngos 'dzin mi gsal ba sogs nas de dag la zhib mor spyod bzhed pas bod du grags pa'i lha
mo'i rigs kyi chos skor phal cher gsan cing zhib mor mdzad pa na/ dmag zor ma dang lcags phur ma sogs khol mo'i rigs dang / rje mo'i rigs dud sol ma 'di la'ang sgrub lugs
mi 'dra ba mang ba'i sa rngog gi sgrub yig ming mi 'dra ba las don gcig pa dang / rngog lugs la rjes gnang sgrub skor shin tu rgyas pa sogs gdams pa zab gnad che bar
dgongs te rtsad gcod gnang kyang sa skya pa dang dwags brgyud pa'i phyogs su rjes gnang gzhan ma'i rgyas bkab 'dra dang man ngag kyang tshang bar ma byung bar thugs ka ma
khengs te/ thugs 'dun ngur re ba yod pa

'di res gong dkar nas gzhung rngog tshang 'og ma thar pa gling du phebs par gnas de gar phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang dang sgrub skor yongs su rdzogs pa gnang ba'i rjes gnang gi
dus ltas khyad par can zhig kyang gzigs pas bla ma dang lha la mi ldog pa'i thugs dad chen po 'khrungs/ phyogs der bla ma'i sku dgra gdug pa can zhig 'dug par 'di lta bu'i
chos skyong yod bzhin du bstan dgra yal bar 'dor mi rung tshul zhu ba mdzad pa'i lan du/ khong tsho'ang lha 'di mchod pa dang mgon khang gi sku rgyab bstan pa sogs kyis
yin nam sngar phan rtags mtshan gang yang ma byung / lan chags 'ded pa lta bur mchis pas da dung ci 'dra yong zhes thugs chad de ba mdzad par/ des na kho bo la chos kyi
bka' drin stsal ba'i yon du dam nyams 'di sgrol ba lags zhes gsol bar shin tu dgyes pa'i legs so gnang ba na/ khyab bdag bla ma 'di nyid kyis lha mo'i ljags bsnyen 'bum
lnga bcu tsam sngar gnang zin pa'i mgon po'i yum 'dod khams ma dang dud sol ma gnyis thugs rgyud gcig par bzhed gshis lha nye bar zur du bsnyen pa gnang ma dgos pa nas/
gnas de ga'i mgon khang rngog ston gong mas bzhengs pa'i sku byin can gzi byin bskyed pa dang dgra bo zhal du 'debs pa'i bcas legs par bsgrigs nas bstan srung gi zhal du
dmar stob mdzad tshul/ /dud sol ma'i chos skor gyi dkar chag las/ sa rngog bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan nas brjod de bka' bsgo drag po lan gsum byas pas rang nyid kyang skyi
bun pa dang lha mo'i sku 'dra de'ang zhal khro zhing zhal ras nag ngam byas

pa 'dra pa zhig byung gsungs/ de nas drang srong srin po rir phebs pa gong gi dkar chag 'phros las/ de nub nas lha mo 'di la gtor ma zur pa re bcos ched du 'phrin las drag
tu bcol bas zhag bdun song ba'i nub drang srong srin po rir gnas tshang zhig gi khang steng du lcog bu phub nas bsdad/ srod dus gtor bsngos kyi mthar mchod g.yog gis khang
pa'i bad steng du thun gtor phul ba'i gtor ma'i gseb nas me stag mtheb rdog tsam zhig chad song ba kho bo rang gis mthong / de je cher song nas rdza ma tsam dang mthar
khang pa tsam du song ba mchod g.yog gis mthong ba la gzhung gi thad du babs song zer/ de nas ring por ma lon par mi tshang de pal shi chad thon bud sogs mi 'dod pa du ma
byung nas rjes stongs pa zhig byung / brgyud pa 'di las 'ongs pa'i lha mo 'di la drag shul nus mthu 'di lta bu yod pas rjes 'brang rnams yid ches par gyis la nan tan du
sgrub par gyis shig /ces bka' stsal pa ltar rtags mtshan mngon du gyur/ de gar bzhugs mur sngar byung ba'i/ khrag 'dzag srin po'i ri la phrad/ /ces pa'i lung bstan thog tu
babs te khro phur mjal ba'i bud med 'jigs su rung ba de ji lta ba zhig zhal gzigs/ de nas sngar gyi lung bstan thugs ngo 'phrod de mos gus chen pos rtse gcig tu gsol ba
btab pas rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rnam par gyur te dngos su zhal bstan/ gsung gi gnang ba stsal ba sogs rje btsun rdo rje btsun mos mngon sum du rjes su bzung /
rim gyis stod lung brgyud ra tshag tu rje btsun nA ro ta pa'i thugs dam rten mthong bas don ldan mjal tshe gzigs snang khyad par can byung bar

gor ma chag cing de nas 'phan yul bya bzang gi ri khrod du phebs/ thugs dam zab mo'i ting nge 'dzin khor yug tu gnang ba'i skabs shig nam mkha' bai DUrYa mthing ga'i mdog ltar
dngas pa'i dbus na sprin dkar lang long du 'khrigs pa'i khrod nas lha'i bu mdzes shing yid du 'ong ba gnyis byung nas dri ba dang / de la lan mdzad pa'i skor gsung mgul
las byung ba 'di lta ste/ e ma ho/ kha bas bskor ba'i sman ljongs kyi/ /yul dbus sa yi thig le'i ngos/ /dben pa'i ri sul yang steng na/ /bla ma sgom pa'i ku su lu/ /khyod
kyi thog ma'i skye yul gang / /dam pa'i yongs 'dzin su yis bzung / /da lta nyams len gdams ngag gang / /phyi ma'i bstad so ji ltar yod/ /ces gleng ba la kho bo'i sems
la 'di lta bu'i ngo mtshar ba bar chad dam dngos grub gang yin kyang rung lan drang por btab snyam nas 'di ltar smras so/ /ston dus bdud rtsi'i 'byung gnas ltar/ /dkar zhing
yid 'phrog chu 'dzin gseb/ /gnas pa'i 'chi med gzhon nu gnyis/ /rna ba'i bdud rtsi sgra dbyangs snyan/ /shAkya'i bstan la rab byung zhing / /dam pa'i ded dpon gyis bzung
yang / /snyom las dbang gis bcings pa yi/ /ser gzugs bdag gi skyes pa'i yul/ /gangs ri'i khrod kyi gtsang stod cha/ /chu bo pakShu'i lho yi ngos/ /grum stod sa skya'i
bya 'dabs ljongs/ /'brog mi lo tsA'i gnas kyi mda'/ /'phrang gsum nang nas srin 'phrang gdong / /rmu rje btsad pos bzung ba'i sa/ /der ni sngon gyi las dbang gis/ /dal
'byor rin cen rnyed

pa yin/ /thub bstan rin chen sgor zhugs nas/ /dam chos bdud rtsi nos pa yi/ /spyir ni yongs 'dzin bcu phrag bzhi/ /zung gnyis dag gis lhag par bzhugs/ /khyad par tshe rabs
dpag med nas/ /rjes su bzung ba'i 'dren pa mchog /tshe 'dir rang sems lhan skyes 'di/ /skye med chos skur ngo sprod cing / /zab mo dbang bzhi'i chu bo'i rgyun/ /bum pa gang
byor gnang ba yi/ /bka' drin mnyam med rdo ring pa/ /'gran zla kun dang bral ba yin/ /nyams len gdams pa'i gtso bo ni/ /rgyal yum bdag med mkha' 'gro la/ /paN grub dbang
po bi rlu pas/ /nos pa nas bzung da lta'i bar/ /rtsa ba'i bla ma yan chod du/ /dbang bzhi'i chu bo ma nub pa'i/ /bla ma'i gsung ngag bdud rtsi'i rgyun/ /tshad ma bzhi
ldan dbang bzhi'i lam/ /rdo rje theg pa'i snying po yin/ /yang snying zab mo bla ma'i lam/ /rang sems bla ma phyag rgya che/ /yengs pa med par sgom pa yin/ /phyi ma'i gang
'gro da lta med/ /sgyu ma'i skyas chen 'degs pa'i tshe/ /kho bo'i bla ma slu med de/ /mdun gyi nam mkhar 'byon snyam yod/ /bde chen thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / /rang sems
stong pa spros bral gnyis/ /dbyer med bsres nas lhug par 'jog /gang ltar song yang 'gyod pa med/ /ces gsungs pa'i lha'i bu gnyis kyang rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po'i
rnam sprul du nges/ yang skabs shin tu lha'i bu gzugs dang lang tsho kha dog phun sum tshogs pa zhig gis rin po che'i bum pa bdud rtsis gang ba phyag tu phul ba ljags thog
tu gsol bas ro brgya phrag bro ba byung zhing / klu'i rgyal pos yid bzhin gyi nor bu phul ba'i

gtam zur tsam las zhib pa yig rgyun dang gsung bgros tshor mi gsal/ zla ba brgyad dgu tsam nas slar yang rngog thar pa gling du phebs sku dgra de la'ang rtags mtshan yod pa'i
'go tshugs pa sogs nas rngog ston chen po thugs lhag par dgyes nas rngog dkyil bdun la sogs pa'i rngog lugs kyi chos skor rnams gnang ba'i rjes su/ brgyud pa 'di pa rang
gi srol la lha mo gsang sgrub rjes gnang 'di rngog pa'i bstan pa zin nges shig la byed pa'i lugs yin gsungs nas gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang cho ga shig tu rgyas pa'i sgo
nas bka' drin chen pos gnang / de dus kyang lha mo dngos su gtad pa tsam gyi nges shes dang yid ches pa byung / gong gi mngon spyod kyi ltas byung ba'i rjes nub mang po'i
bar du sdig pa dag pa'i rmis ltas ches che ba ji snyed cig byung bas lam thams cad kyi nang nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'di ga zab pa la nges shes khyad par me
'bar ba la shing bsnan pa lta bur gyur to/ /zhes gsungs pa spang rtogs mthon por slebs pa'i rigs tshor bla mar sri zhu dang byin rlabs 'jug pa gnyis ka shugs kyis 'byung
na'ang phyi rabs kyi rjes 'jug rnams la rdo rje slob dpon gyi zhabs tog la 'bad na phan yon chen po 'byung ba rtogs pa'i ched du dgongs te gsungs par snang ngo / /snga phyi
mang por bla ma yi dam chos srung gi zhal gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ ayon padma dus dgra ma he'i zhal/ /rdo rje btsun mo yang gsang khros
pa sogs/ /lha mchog du ma dngos su zhal gzigs nas/ /lung bstan gnang ba thob la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes

gsungs so/ /gang thugs dag pa'i btsun mo lte 'og nang / /a shad gtum mo yongs 'bar phyi rol tu/ /chu dang rlabs bzhin so sor gzigs pa'i tshe/ /nyer bzhi'i yul nas 'tshol rnams
smin rgyur snyeg /khyab bdag bla ma'i rnam 'phrul legs bris bu/ /yid 'phrog ri bong 'dzin ltar dkar ba gnyis/ /chu 'khur dbus na nyer gleng byang chen bar/ /thang lhod
med pa'i thugs rje'i brda thabs tsam/ /dwags brgyud me lha'i mngal du ma bzod pa/ /mar lo'i thugs bcud lha chen dngas ma'i khams/ /rngog ston ganggA las skyugs mgon khyod
kyi/ /blo gros smin tshal skyed bsrings gdong drug lha/ /'dod khams dbang mo bran bkol mthu stobs mdas/ /log 'dren snying ga phug pa'i khrag dron skom/ /ma rgyud dregs
tshogs kyis btungs rkan sgra yis/ /gnam lcags 'bar ba'i thog kyang ming du zad/ /gsol 'debs las/ dri med mkha' dbyings 'ja' gur bzhad pa'i dbus/ /ayon mkhan pos mdzes sku
gsal bar bstan/ /'khrul zhig bla ma'i dbu gtsug mkha' ngos su/ /dpa' bo rta mgrin gzigs la gsol ba 'debs/ /'dar stod dgon pa chos 'khor yang rtse yi/ khri la zhabs bkod
slob bshad bstan pa spel/ /rnam par rgyal ba'i yang rtser chos skyong sku/ /bzhengs shing dge legs mdzad la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes dbus phyogs su lo gnyis la nye bar bzhugs
nas lcags byi'i mjug gtsang la chibs kha bsgyur/ stag gru kha'i khad nyer phebs pa na nam mkha' la spyan hur gyis gzigs nas chibs sna 'khrid mkhan la khyod kyis ci mthong
gsungs par bltas tsa na

'ja' tshon bun bun 'dug pa mthong nas 'di ltar 'dug zhus pas cang mi gsung na'ang rjes su thugs nang gtsang ba 'drar de dus 'ja'i khrod na ayon chen po padma 'byung gnas bzhugs
'dug pa gzigs zhes bka' stsal/ phebs lam tshor 'phrin las rgya cher skyong mu nas lcags mo glang gi lor bo dong phun tshogs rab brtan du rje btsun rdo rje 'dzin pa mkhan
chen sgo rum pa mjal bar phebs skabs thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje 'di la chos gsan bzhed kyis zhal ngo rnams dang bka' 'gros mdzad par/ thugs dang
bstun chog pa thugs rtse mthun pa'i khrol cha mdzad cing / 'on kyang nged rang tsho'i byed srol bzhin brtag pa zhus gsung ba ltar khyab bdag sgo rum pa chen por zhus
pa shin tu bzang ba babs/ thams cad mkhyen pas nan zhus mdzad par bla ma'i slob ma slob mar min gsungs nas zhal gyis ma bzhes pa'i tshe/ rje btsun sgo rum pas bla ma'i slob
ma slob mar min zer ba bdog ste bla ma mnyes byed gang yin bya'ang mi gda' lags sam/ cis kyang gnang mdzod ces nan chags gsung bar gnas gsar pa mi min zer ba bden par
'dug /bla ma la thel 'bebs sogs sngar med kyi srol btsugs gsung sku rtsed dang bcas zhal gyis bzhes/ thog mar sgrol dkar gyi tshe 'khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun 'od zer drug sbrags
kyi rjes gnang / chag lugs tshe dpag med dkar po/ /dbyangs can ma dkar mo ste dkar lha gsum gyis sgo phye nas zhag drug gi ring la byin rlabs rjes gnang nyer drug lung
du ma dang bcas pa stsal/ gsung gleng zhig gi 'phros la

nged la chos nyan par brtag pa byas pa e yin gsung bar nged rang yab sras min pa gzhan la rgyus ni med dgongs pa'i thugs 'jigs zhum pa'i ngang nas de 'dra'i srol yod pas byas
lags zhus par/ legs po e byung gnang bar shin tu bzang gsol ba la bzhad cing nged kyi rmi lam du pha rgan yin rgyu ba zhig gis gnas gsar ba brtag pa 'di bzhin grabs 'dug
pa ji ltar byed 'dri bar/ bstan pa la phan na chug pa dang mi phan na mi chug pa mdzod zhus pas chug 'dug pa bstan par phan pa yin nam gsung ba na/ thugs dgyes pa dang
'jigs pa cig car du byung / bka' las/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum par bzhugs pa rnams zhabs drung du gang thob dang de phyin gyi sa stong ngas 'geng gsung chos grol gdong dpal
mgon dkar po tshe 'phel gyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa gnang / bla lung du 'khrul zhig dka' bzhi pa chen po mjal bar dpon slob nyung bsdus kyis phebs/ /dmangs ma thugs
'gros chung khyad nas bal mdar gtong ba gnang / zla bo rnams do nub jo nang du slebs pa yong ba yod pas bdag thogs gzhi med par thon pa dgos snyan du gsol bar dka' bzhi
nas kyis mngon par mkhyen pas khong rnams bal mda' rang du sdod pa 'dug do nub 'dir cis kyang bzhugs dgos gnang ba bzhin bka' dang bstun te padma yang gsang gi dbang gsan
pa'i tshe 'khrul zhig chen po'i dbu'i thad du dpal rta mgrin bzhugs pa dngos su gzigs phan tshun thugs nang dag pas bde chen gyi ye shes chen po'i ngang du gsung sgros
dang nyams bsdur sogs

shin tu 'phel bar mdzad/ dpon slob gnyis ka phyir mjal 'dzom byung res kyi dka' bzhi pas/ de ring tshar pa chos rje khong 'byon gyi yod pa 'dug dpal mgon zhal sngon mgyogs
su byung tshul dang / res chos rje tshar pa la bya ba khag can zhig yod par mchis dpal mgon zhal brel gyin 'dug gsung ba ni mgon po 'di nyid dpal 'khor lo sdom pa drag po'i
skur bstan pa yin pas de 'dra'i rigs gzigs pa thag shin tu ring bas dpon slob gnyis ka'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam thar ro/ /sang nyin jo nang du phebs lam dngos gzhi
dang mi gcig pa'i brag skras zer ba rta bong bgrod mi thub pa'i gzar po der dre'u la chibs te byon/ snga 'gros sogs med na'ang rje btsun grol mchog gi thugs mkhyen gyis
bcad de/ de ring mgron chen zhig 'ong bar 'dug pas bu ram sgor ba sogs gzhis len dang ser sbreng gi sta gon gyis gsung ba ltar brag skras la rkang thang ma gtogs mi thar
gshis gzhung lam phyogs su ser spreng bsgrigs pa na/ brag lam la dpon slob 'ga' zhig phebs pa mthong ste de phyogs su mgyogs par phyin/ skya ser mtha' dag sngar bzhon pa
dang bcas thar pa'i dpe med pa la da lam chos rje tshar pas rdzu 'phrul bstan pa yin zhes ngo mtshar gyi gnas su gyur/ phebs pa'i bgros med par bsu ba'i bkod pa la dpon
slob rnams thugs rangs pa dang ches pa phan tshun 'gran pa bzhin song / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' grol mchog gi phebs bsur byon dpon slob gnyis kas mnyam phyag mjal dar rtse
sprod

gzims chung ngu bzhugs khri mnyam pa gnang chos kyi 'bel gtam sogs khams pa gsar rnying gi dpe bzhin gsung gleng zhib par mdzad/ jo nang chos gra'i dbus su bal po shing kun
gyi mchod rten la 'dra dpe blangs pa bzhengs skabs dang 'grig /rje 'di nyid kyi phyag rdor gyi li sku khyid gang ba zhig yod pa de 'bul ba mdzad pa rje btsun dam pa shin
tu mnyes nas rten 'brel 'grig ces gzungs bzhugs la 'bul bar mdzad/ dpon slob gnyis ka rdor ring rin po che'i zhal slob rdo rje'i mched po bla na med pa'i dad dung phun sum
tshogs par de phyogs kyi skye rgu rnams mgrin pa gcig tu gleng / rim gyis rmuu gshong dang thub bstan dge 'phel sogs su zhabs zung bkod de 'chad nyan sgom sgrub kyis mtshon
pa'i rnam dkar gyi 'phrin las dbyar mtsho ltar 'phel bzhin pa'i mur/ se ston chen po mthu chen nyi ma bzang po dang mkhas grub chen po rin chen rgyal mtshan sogs sngags
rnying ma'i rig pa 'dzin pa mang du byon pa dang gdung gcig pa se dkar rigs kyi thig les skyong ba 'dar pa dang / grangs chen 'dus tshogs rnams mgrin gcig dbyangs gcig
pa'i sgo nas gsol ba btab pa bzhin mdzes byed ces pa chu mo yos kyi lo 'gor dge 'dun rnams kyis chos gos zlum por bgo zhing mchod rdzas sna tshogs thogs pa'i ser sbreng
/ sde pa dpon g.yog gis rin cen rgyan cha'i skya hrags dang bcas pas mdun bsus te 'dar stod chos 'khor yang rtse'i seng ge'i khri chen por zhabs zung 'khor lo'i ri mo rnam
par bkod/ phyogs de'i skya ser che dgu mtha' dag

gis gtong ba'i snyim pa ring por brkyang ste zang zing gi bdog pa'i mchod sprin rgya cher spros/ phyogs 'dus gnyug mar gnas pa'i don gnyer can rnams la pha rgyud 'dus pa dang
ma rgyud 'khor lo sdom pas thog drangs rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang rig gtad 'khrid lung man ngag mang du gsungs/ khyad par gnyis su med
pa dpal kye rdo rje'i man ngag lugs dang 'brel ba'i lam 'bras slob bshad kyi dbang 'khrid kyi byin rlabs lung sogs 'jigs pa med pa seng ge'i rgyud kyi nga ro'i sgra dbyangs
phyogs brgyar bsgrags pas/ mus pa dkon grags pa sogs phyogs lhung smyo chus zin pa'i glang po rnams kyi dregs pa'i mgo bo bkas par gyur/ 'jam dpal dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug bsnyen rdzogs gnang ba'i sgo dod pa'i tshe rje btsun sgo rum pa chen pos las slob chos rje tshar pa 'gab gsung ba bzhin bo dong du lha rigs 'a zhwa rgyal pos
gdan drangs pa bzhin phebs/ 'dul ba'i gzhung nas ji ltar bshad pa bzhin gyi las slob kyi bya ba gsol ba dang bzhi'i las kyi bsgrub bya la bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa byin
pas thams cad mkhyen pa dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa chen por mnga' gsol/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis thog drangs pa'i snod ldan 'ga' zhig la rdo rje nag po chen
po gur mgon gyi dkyil 'khor lnga'i dbang rdul tshon la brten pa/ phyi 'khrid rdo rje brag rdzong du grags pa la nang gses kyis phyi nang gsang gsum yod ba'i nyams 'khrid
zab mo smin rgyas su stsal/ rje mkhyen brtse'i thugs rab

dang thugs 'dun la mnyes pa'i gsung 'phros kyang gnang / rdo rje 'chang sgo rum chos rje'i drung du dbang lung man ngag du ma gsan te gzhung skor mdzad nas 'khrul zhig dka'
bzhi pa chen po mjal bar phebs pa na 'khrul zhig chen po'i gsung las rje rin po ches bo dong du mgon po'i zab chos shig mi mang rab cig la bshad yod pa 'dra pu tra 'di cung
zad mi dgyes pa'i rtags tsam byed kyi 'dug pas 'tshub kyi rnam pa cung zad byung dogs 'dug gsungs/ de nas lam bar du chibs g.yang la 'dred pas rje nyid kha 'gram du bzhugs
chibs grog po'i nang du lhungs kyang skyon med par rdo la rmig rjes bzhag pa sogs ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i rdzu 'phrul bstan/ rmu gshong du bskang bshags tshogs
mchod rgya cher mdzad pas dam can dgyes pa'i 'dzum zhal lhug par bstan/ dpal ldan grang mo cher re zhig gi bar stan chags nas chos kyi 'khor lo ji snyed cig bskor/ shing
pho 'brug lo rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po dpa' bo'i tshogs dpon du mkha' la spyod pa'i gnas su gshegs pa gsan pas rings stabs su phebs/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i gdung
yid bzhin gyi nor bu he ru kaHzhal brgyad pa'i ngo bor gyur par phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid kyi mchod pa rgya cher mdzad cing rjes sor me mchod kyi phyag phyi yang
mdzad par snang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zhabs la da nga yang ci 'dra byed mi shes gser chos dmar po skor gsum dang mgon po che chung sogs yongs rdzogs thob pa dang
tshul ldan shes pa ye mi bdog pas ma 'gyangs par gsan pa 'gab ces bslab bya mdzad par brten rje sgo rum

pa gshegs pa'i thugs ngal kyang sangs pa lta bu'i ngal gsos/ zhabs drung rig 'dzin chen po dang rje mkhyen brtse lhan du dkar bdud lcam dral gyi rjes gnang stsal nas grang
mo cher phebs te skor cig bzhugs nas rmu gshong du stan chags pa'i dus sngar skyed tshal du chos 'brel gsan pa dang / phra ma nas kyis rin spungs su snyan phra phul ba'i
rkyen gyis bod mkhar nas tshang ming gi lhag mar gyur pa'i rkyen ngan grogs shar lta bus bskul te rje btsun bod mkhar ba mai tri byams pa don grub rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
pos zhabs pad bsnyen par phebs/ zang zing gi dngos po yod dgu lta bu 'khor gsum yongs dag gi 'bul ba rgya cher mdzad/ zhal gyi bdud rtsi rdzogs par myangs rjes bstan pa
spel ba dang sgom sgrub rtse gcig tu mdzad dgongs pas sku la bcar nas bzhugs/ ma chen rdor bkras pa phyogs 'byon dang thug pa'i re zhig gnyer gyis gsung pa bzhin mdzad pa'i
tshe de snga gong nas gsol ja cung zad dkon pa yod par mi nyag dpon po mgon po 'od zer gyis gsol ja phon shin tu che ba'i 'bul skyel slebs pas rje drung gi gnyer kha 'phrod
ces thugs dgyes/ rin po che bod mkhar ba gtso bor gyur pa'i don gnyer can 'ga' la gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi snang gsum nas bzung dbang bzhi pa'i bar gyi
nyams 'khrid zla brgyad lhag tsam smin rgyas de'i cha lag tu dgos pa'i dbang byin rlabs lung man ngag /dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi dbang bzhi mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud/
rnal 'byor bzhi/ rnam par 'byed pa/ rwa rtse sems 'dzin/ mtshan ma gyen sgreng /

mtshan mo rgyu ba rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs nas dbang bzhi'i lam rdzogs pa'i 'khrid/ rwa pod/ dpal 'dzin pod chung rnams kyi lung phyag 'khrid/ shin tu zab pa gshed dmar
bir lugs kyi dbang bzhi/ byin rlabs gsum/ spros med kyi 'khrid yig sna/ rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa'i dbang bzhi dang tshe dbang / rta pod/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i bdag po
chen po'i bar gyi dbang / rgyud 'grel/ shin tu zab pa nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs dang nyams 'khrid chos skor/ indra mkha' spyod/ mai tri mkha' spyod/ gzhan ma phag
dkar shes rab gsal byed/ dpyal pa'i bden gnyis ma/ dbu bcad ma/ zhal gnyis ma rnams kyi skor/ seng ge sgra/ 'jam dkar/ seng gdong ma sogs rjes gnang gi rigs mang ba/ bstan
srung gi gtso bo gur gyi mgon po gtso rkyang / sbags sgrub lha brgyad/ bcu gnyis ma/ phyi nang gsang ba ru mtshon gyi las mkhan dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang / dkyil 'khor
la brten pa'i dbang lnga/ rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga ldan dang brag rdzong ma gnyis kyi nyams 'khrid/ me 'bar kha skong / gyi ljang / dud sol/ snyan brgyud rnams kyi glegs bam/
ngor rdzong gong dkar gsum nas brgyud pa'i be'u bum/ sbas pa'i mgon po'am mnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa'i bka' mi 'dra ba bcu bzhi/ tshe sgrub srung 'khor dang gsang ba'i 'khrid
man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa/ gnod sbyin beg tse/ dur khrod bdag po/ dpal ldan dmag zor ma/ rdo rje rab brtan ma rnams kyi skor/ tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes
gnang dang 'khrid/ gser chos dmar chen

skor gsum gyi thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / gnyan lo'i dmar chung skor gsum/ gser chos dang grwa pa mngon shes gnyis kyi dzam dmar/ kun rig gi dbang / phyag
rdor u tsa ya/ rnam rgyal 'joms/ sme brtsegs dud kha sogs kyi rjes gnang / snying po don gsum dang tshem bu lugs kyi dmar 'khrid/ rnam sras bka' mi 'dra ba bco lnga'i
rjes gnang / be'u bum yongs rdzogs/ 'ba' ra ba nas brgyud pa'i tshe 'khrid kyis mtshon zab chos shin tu mang ba gnang zhing 'dir bsdoms pa rnams kyang rje bod mkhar ba'i
rnam thar spyan snga rin po ches mdzad pa nas btus pa yin la/ lo mang sbrel nas dpon slob chabs cig par bzhugs pa la brten rim gyis stsal ba'i dus la snga phyi khyad che
ba 'ga' yod par snang / khyad par chos skyong che chung gi skor rnams bla ma dang slob ma gnyis kar gnyan cha che bas dus gcig tu rdzogs par mi mdzad pas kyang shes nus/
rdo ring rin po ches tshar pa chen por khyed la bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa'i slob ma mchog tu gyur pa gsum yod pas de gsum po la ring bsrel 'di 'dra re re byin gsungs
pa'i ya gyal gcig rin po che bod mkhar bar gnang ste zhal slob kyi gtso bor ngos 'dzin mdzad pa dang mthun par phyis su lo dgon pa sogs kyi zhal 'dzin mdzad/ spyan
snga rin po che mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ chos rje bstan pa rgya mtsho sogs la snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa rdzogs par stsal/ spyan snga rin po che/ mkhan chen thar pa rgyal
mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ lo pa spyan snga

kun dga' don grub/ rab 'byams chos rje chos sku rdo rje sogs gsung las skyes pa'i dam pa du mas kha'u pa'i ring lugs rgya cher spel/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtshor
gser chos bcu gsum dang mgon po che chung gi chos skor rnams 'bul ba gnang / chos 'khor rgyal lhun grub dga' ba'i tshal gyi bsil ba tshal du mgon po che chung gi sku dang
/ chos 'byung shod du gnod sbyin beg tse rnams bzheng ba'i zhal bkod snyan brgyud dang 'brel ba'i gzungs bzhugs rab gnas sogs gnang / mnga' ris drung pa rin po che lha'i
btsun pa bsod nams dpal bzang / dga' ldan shar chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ sgrom mda' mkhan chen sogs mnyam med ri bo dga' ldan pa'i bstan 'dzin mang por chos kyi bka'
drin stsal/ sa skyong dga' ldan pa a khu bkra shis zhes ngag gi dbang phyug dbyangs can bsnyems pa'i sder grags pa khu dbon gyi bla mchod du gyur pas mtshon dbu ru stod
kyi rgyal khams su kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bstan pa'i sgron me ches cher sbar/ lha sa brag sgor star sdong chos mdzad kyis bdag po kun rin pa'i sku la gri ltag phul ba sogs
'o brgyal byung bar brten 'phan yul mkhar rtser bdag chen mjal bar phebs dus/ rnam thar las spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa 'di mar 'grib la song ba dang khyad par du
sa skya pa'i bstan pa 'di da lta gang na'ang dar rgyas che rgyu rang mi 'dug rung chos rje'i drung gis dbus phyogs 'dir bstan pa la phan zhing sa skya pa'i rkang zin pa zhig
byung 'dug /nged tsho sa skya pa'i zhal ngo chibs rags bsgrigs nas yong dus lha

sa brag sgo'i thad du star sdong dbon po dang phrad tshe rbud shar re 'gro yang chos rje'i drung las dga' ldan thams cad mthun grub pa 'dug gsungs pas mtshon thams cad mkhyen
pa mkhyen brtse'i 'og nas rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje'i zhal slob kyi dang mar mngon/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis bka' chos gnang dgos tshul gyi zhu yig
phul bar/ sa dbus gtsang khams gsum gyi sman ljongs na/ zhes sogs kyi lan dang bcas zhal gyis 'ches pa bzhin zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bzhi la bla ma dam pa rdo rje 'chang
bo dong du phebs/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug dpon slob nyung bsdus la zab chos ji ltar stsal na/ khyab bdag gur gyi mgon po'i chos skor ni/ /'phags
pa'i yul du paN grub rnams kyis phye/ /rgyud rgyal ma dros chu gter las byung ba'i/ /bka' babs rnam bzhi'i gdams pa'i chu rgyun ni/ /lo tsA rnam bzhi'i gsung gi 'bab
stegs las/ /legs 'ongs sa skya'i bla chen thugs mtshor 'khyil/ /gang de'i gsung gi bdud rtsi'i gzegs ma ni/ /phyogs brgyar 'phros pas kha ba'i sman ljongs 'dir/ /zab don
lbu 'phreng bye bas phyug pa yi/ /rjes 'brangs chu klung rnam bzhi ring du 'bab/ /ces pa ltar bka' babs bzhi ldan du bzhugs pa'i rdo rje nag po chen po gtso rkyang / lha
bcu gsum ma/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma/ las mkhan rnams kyi rjes gnang / dkyil 'khor dang 'brel ba'i dbang / brag rdzong dang gsang 'khrid dang thun mong min pa'i nyams
'khrid/ me

'bar kha skong dang bcas pa/ snyan brgyud/ gyi ljang / dud sol/ ngor pa'i pod ser/ rdzong lugs dkar chag ma/ rdo rje gdan pa'i thugs dam mgon pod rnams kyi lung / gsang ba
yid bzhin nor bu'i yi ge dang zhal shes la brten nas phyag len dmar 'khrid/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje'i gsung las/ de ltar rgyal ba'i dri med rgyud sde las/ /gsungs
pa'i bstan srung kun gyi mchog gyur pa/ /drag shul mthu ldan stobs 'phrog nag po zhes/ /rgya bod mkhas grub kun la rlung ltar grags/ /zhes pa ltar/ lo chen gnyan gyi chos
skyong brgya rtsa'i nang nas gtso bo mchog tu gyur pa mnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa'i bka' mi 'dra ba'i rjes gnang bcu bzhi/ tshe sgrub srung 'khor dang spu gri'i so sdeb/ rtsa
gsum 'khor lo bzhi'i nyams 'khrid/ phyi bram ze nang zhing skyong gsang ba stobs 'phrog nag po ltar sgrub pa'i las tshogs man ngag phyag len dmar 'khrid dang bcas pa
legs par gsan pa 'dir phyogs mtshungs su bsdus pa ma gtogs chos skyong bka' gnyan pas dus snga phyi 'ga' zhig tu rim gyis gnang bar mngon zhing / rje mkhyen brtse thugs sras
kyi gtso bo bzung ste zab chos kun bum pa gang byor gnang bas/ gsung las/ bdag chen chos rje'i sku yi dbon skyes shing / /grub mchog rdor ring chos rje'i bstan la dad/
/sgo rum chos rje'i thugs kyi sras su gyur/ /shes rab snying rje rnam dpyod phun tshogs shing / /dad dang sgrub pas bla ma mnyes pa ste/ /rgyu drug 'dzom pas zab mo'i gdams
pa rnyed/ /grogs dag 'di 'dra'i skal bzang

kho bo tsam/ /zhes pa'i don thog tu babs shing rin cen gser gyi maNDal sogs rin po che'i rigs dang ja gos dar go khrab kyis gtsos pa'i bdog pa gya nom pa/ mkha' 'gro lnga mnyes
par byed pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgya chen pos snyan brgyud dang po'i rten 'brel kun nas sgrig par mdzad pa sogs kyang / bsam 'phel nor 'phreng las/ phyi nang gsang
ba'i man ngag zhu ba'i tshe/ /tshogs dang gtor mas mkha' 'gro mnyes par byas/ /rin cen gser gyi maNDal lan gsum phul/ /gsang chen grub mtha' 'dzin pa'i dam bca' byas/ /zhes
pas mtshon nus/ dkar chags dbang sdud padma rA ga'i za ma tog las/ bstan pa'i bdag po sa skya pa'i/ /gsang las yang gsang gser gyi chos/ /dmar po skor gsum zhes grags
pa/ /zhes rje btsun sa skya par gdams pa rgya mtsho lta bur bzhugs pa'i nang nas thun mong bsgrubs pas mchog zhar la 'byung ba dmar po skor gsum yang / ji skad du/ kho bos
dam pa'i zhabs pad ring du ba~Xsten/ /snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i zhal 'ong snying la shar/ /'khrul med gdams pa'i gnad la nges pa thob/ /grogs dag 'di 'dra'i skal bzang
kho bo tsam/ /zhes rdo rje 'chang 'di nyid la mnga' ba'i rje btsun rig byed ma/ tshogs bdag bgegs kyi rgyal po/ khro bo 'dod pa'i rgyal po gsum gyi thun mong dang thun mong
ma yin pa'i rjes gnang lung man ngag phyag len/ zhar byung dmar chung skor gsum dang bcas pa gnang /

de yang nyin re chos thun gnyis dang 'chams dbyangs kyi phyag len rnams kyang dpyis phyin par thugs la btags par slob ma snod kyi skyon dang cung zad tsam yang mi ldan pas
mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyi rnam thar las/ mtshan phyed tsam dbyangs bslabs/ de nas dgongs thun yod tsam dang gtor bsngo sogs byas/ de nas mar me'i 'od la mgon po'i phyag dpe
khag che ba sogs yi ger bris pas zla ba gcig la shog bu bcu gras sum brgya tsam tshar byung zhing / nged kyi mgon po'i dpe drag shos rnams la skyer thig gar po byas pa
kho na yod pa'i rgyu mtshan de yin/ zhes byung ba mnga' ris paN chen rin po ches po sti drug cu tsam phyag bris gnang zer ba dang dbyibs 'dra ba'i rdzu 'phrul gyi bkod pa
las tha mal pa'i ngang tshal du mi sems shing / chos bdag por gnang ba'i nyams kyis dpon slob gnyis ka la ngo mtshar ba'i gzigs snang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / zhal
ngo rim par dge ba'i bshes gnyen zla med pa byon par ma zad zhal slob mkhan chen bslab gsum pa dang sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis snyan brgyud mi nyams pa'i srog
shing du song zhing / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi gsung las skyes pa/ bdag chen rin po che ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/
/'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes gnyen/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ rje bka' 'gyur ba/ mkhan chen zha lu ba/ glang bu chos rje/ rgyal rtse bdag po byams pa ngag dbang bsod
nams rgyal mtshan/ bya gshong mkhan chen mang thos grags pa rnam rgyal/ yangs can mkhan

po byams pa bsod nams mtha' yas/ rje btsun bka' 'gyur bas zur thams cad mkhyen par stsal bas mtshon te zhal slob de dag las kyang yal slob nying slob sogs srid mtha'i bar du
'phel nas rang bstan kha'u pa'i ring lugs 'dzin par zla med pa'o/ /de nas bya rgod gshong gi rten mjal la phebs de nub rgyal blon lha khang du bzhugs pa'i srod kyi dus
rta rgyugs pa'i rmig pa'i khrab sgra chen po dang bcas 'od dmar po ches gsal ba zhig dmar 'ur 'ur byung ba'i khrod na rta dmar rgyan khrab khrab mang po btags par mi dmar
zhig gis zhon nas skor phyogs la yud kyi song zhes pa tsam las gsal bar mi 'dug kyang / chos rgyal gyi dus byang gi so kha bsrung bar lha sras mu rub btsan po dang zhang
blon lha bzang klu dpal gnyis kyis gtsos pa'i g.yul bshams dus ayon chen pos rnam sras bkug nas bstim pa'i 'phyar dar dang phyag mtshan bzhi pa'i chos skor rnams bya rgod
gshong du gter du sbas pa gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab kyis spyan drangs pas gnas 'dir rgyal po chen po dngos su bzhugs gshis mdung dmar can phyag mtshan bzhi pa'i zhal mngon
sum du gzigs par snang / sang tho rengs thegs rtsis kyis sgo drung na khal 'gel ba'i bar la rdo kyong de la khyel mdzad bzhugs pas mdang gi rta'i rmig sgra de byung zhing
'od dmar po ches gsal bas sa'i rtsi sbur yan nyin mo ltar gsal ba drung na 'khod pa thams cad kyis mthong ba byung / de nas rmuu gshong du phebs yol nas shangs chos rdo
rje'i rgyas btab kyi brgyud pa drug

pa gnyan ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor gyi rnam sprul mkhan rin po che gzhon nu blo gros ched bstad kyis phebs/ bla ma 'di nyid bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu chen por dgongs te gsung
ngag rin po che mkha' spyod skor gsum/ dmar po skor gsum sogs gser chos mgon po che chung / gnod sbyin beg tse sogs kyi dbang rjes gnang 'khrid lung man ngag rnams 'di
nas bzung snga phyir mjal ba tshor rim gyis stsal zhing gzhan yang bstan pa spyi sgos kyi gsung chos ji snyed cig gnang / mkhan chen nyid kyi gsung las kyang deng rang 'gro
don khyongs chung bas 'chad 'chad nyung gsung ba ltar chos bka' dog pa tsam yod tshod du 'dug cing / dpon yol ba bla chen du grags pas rags rim gsan tshod du 'dug rung
khong pa rjes sor rtags brtan sprul skur ha cang mos drag pa'i skyon gyis rang bstan zin pa'i rjes che ba ma byung zhing / zhal slob 'di thon gyi grags mi che'ang dbus g.yo
ru'i phyogs su bkra shis chos kyi sde gsar du bskrun pas bstan pa'i me btsa' lta bur song / bdag chen rin po che 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po thugs blo gzu bor gnas
pas yar klungs bkra shis rtser phebs nas brag rdzong ma'i 'khrid kyis gtsos snyan brgyud kyi chos skor mang du gsan/ gsang 'khrid skor re zhig phul ba mi 'gab 'dra dgongs
te ma gsan gsungs pa mkhan rin po che'i gsan yig btsems ma bya rog gis khyer te bdag chen rin po che'i sku pang du bskyur bas chos skyong gis gdams pa rnams gtod cig ces
skabs dbye ba lta bus dpon slob gnyis ka'i che bar song zhing / thugs yid

ches te tshang bar phul bas mi thog gnyis tsam gyi ring bzhi thog bla brang pha nor dang bral ba'i khang stong 'dra ba slar rang nor ga~Xtong len lta bu'i dbu tshugs shing
/ rim gyis sngags 'chang sems dpa' chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams yab sras nas gong ma'i ring lugs kyi nyi ma phyogs brgyar 'char ba'i rten 'brel gyi sgo yang brgyud
pa 'di nas phye bas rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho'i bstan 'dzin gyi gtso bo zhig tu mngon/ 'dar ba chos rje chos dbang rin chen dpal gyi rgya mtsho rje btsun kun
spangs chen pos mgon po phur zhabs ma gnang ba'i chos gling drung pa sogs gzhi byes kyi 'dus pa du ma dang / bstan pa'i sbyin bdag sde pa 'dar ba rin cen dpal bzang sogs
zhal ngo rnams dang / mdor na skya ser mchog dman mang por so so'i blo dang 'tsham pa'i dbang 'khrid lung man ngag sogs sbyin pa rnam pa bzhi'i sgo nas 'dod pa'i re ba bskang
/ shing sbrul lo bo dong du thams can mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i ljags bsnyen gyi sku mtshams shin tu dam par bar du gcod pa'i mtshan
ma chen po zhig 'jug nye ba thugs kyis mkhyen nas gdan 'dren zhus pa la ma ltos par phebs/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gzigs snang la rje bla ma sku mdog byu ru ltar dmar zhing
zhal rgyan sogs ye med pa zhig 'dug par sngar phan ni zhal rgyan gzhor ba gnang gin med da lam ci yin nam dgongs shing / mjal ma thag thugs la dga' spro dang mos gus chen
po 'khrungs/ bgegs kyi rnam pa byung ba la'ang dogs gcod zhu ma dgos par lhug par gsungs shing

cho 'phrul sna tshogs bstan pa'i sgo nas yid srubs kyi g.yul las rgyal bar mdzad pas de nub nas bzung thugs bde nyams shin tu che bar gyur/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang du thams
cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug 'dar du phebs zhag nyer drug bzhugs thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i lugs kyi dpal mgon stobs 'phrog dbang po'i gtor ma/
drag po'i 'chams dbyangs phyag len thams cad mkhas par sbyong bdar mdzad/ zhar byung du gur mgon gyi man ngag mang po chig brgyud dang dud sol ma'i skor du ma gnang / tshar
chen chos kyi rgyal pos rdo rje slob dpon dang mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis las kyi rdo rje mdzad nas dpon slob rnams kyis nyer dgu la gtor chen gnang bas bstan la log par
'khu ba'i gzugs can gzugs med kyi dpung tshogs mtha' dag thal ba'i rdul phran bzhin du song / de nub mnal lam du rje bla ma rtse gdong yin snyam pa'i lung pa zhig na yar
phebs pa'i mthar khang pa zhig 'dug pa der byon pa'i nang du shing khris bteg pa'i 'bol gdan nar mor bting ba'i g.yas su khyab bdag kun spangs chen po dang / g.yon du kun
mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa gnyis bzhugs 'dug par dpon slob gnyis la phyag 'bul dang byin rlabs zhu ba mdzad tshe/ thu chen 'jigs med dpa' bos phyag len sogs bkur gzos mdzad
byung bar kun spangs rin po ches kyang 'di 'dra zhig mdzad thang ngam dgongs pa shar bar rdo ring rin po ches kha sa nga tsho chos rje gar byon gsung bar bdag gis jo nang
pa'i grwa pa 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa zer ba gzugs chung nge ba jo zhwa gyon pa de la chos

'chad kyin bsdad zhus par rje rdo rje gdan pas khyed rdzun ma zer/ 'jam sgeg dang gnas gsar rje drung mi gcig gsung ba na kun spangs rjes sngon dang da lta'i khyad par tsam
las gnyis ka'i gsung la 'gal ba med/ khong yar klungs par gyur skabs 'jam sgeg dang deng sang gnas gsar chos rje yin pas rgyud cig /der ma zad chos rjes bsnyel yod pa 'dra/
khyed ayon gyi yul du stha bi rar 'khrungs nas rdo rje rnal 'byor mar dbang zhu dus rnam 'byor pa sbrul gyi ga sha can de nga yin/ de dus stha bi ra pas gdug pa mang
po bsgral gsung pa sogs bla ma rnam gnyis dri ba dri lan gyi tshul mdzad pas 'od gsal des khyongs shing mnal sad pa na thugs rgyud la bde chen gyi ye shes khyad par can dang
/ sku tshe sngon ma'i gnas tshul la thugs nges 'drongs pas nged rang dpon slob rnams kyis zhal gyi gtor chen byas par kun spangs rje dang rdo rje gdan pa gnyis dgyes
yod pa 'dra/ mdang rmi lam 'di 'dra byung zhes rje mkhyen brtse la gsungs par thugs la dgyes tshor dang spyan chab 'khrug pa sogs byung bas/ /kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i rnam
thar du/ mnal lam ming du btags pa'i 'od gsal ngang / /rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang gnyis mngon sum gzigs/ /lkog gyur sngon gyi gnas 'ga' lung bzhin thob/ /ngo mtshar 'di dang
'di 'dra gsung ba thos/ /a ho srid par 'khyams pas ches dub pa/ /bdag la nyid kyis ring mo zhig nas bskyangs/ /mngon gyi zhal bzhes slu med bden pa'i mthus/ /'dir yang
slob bshad snyan brgyud lhug par stsal/ /da dung khyed dang mtshungs

par ma gyur pa/ /de srid mgon skyabs dpung gnyen gzhan med pas/ /yid ches dad dang gus pas gsol ba 'debs/ /slu med thugs rjes sngar bzhin gzung du gsol/ /zhes byung zhing /
rje mkhyen brtse dpon slob phyir phebs gdong bla ma dam pas 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims kyi gter ma'i phur pa/ rje nyid kyi dbang bum yun ring gnang ba'i phyag dril
shing 'khul ma shubs bcas/ seng ldeng gi kha TwAM ga /bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi TIkka mu tig 'phreng ba/ 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam gur mgon hor sku zhig sogs gnang
sbyin phun sum tshogs pa stsal/ yang khams pa a kro zer bas kha'ur rdo ring rin po che la mgon po zhal gyi chos skor dgos tshul zhus tshe rje 'di la spyan cer gzigs nas cis
kyang byed gsungs zhal gyis bzhes kyang gnang ma thub pa phyis rje bla mas gnang dgos byung ba lung bstan du 'dug /mi ring ba'i skabs shig rje bla ma 'di nyid bo dong
du spyan 'dren ma zhus par phebs nas gzhan don gcod kyi rigs med khyed la chos shig gshod du yongs ba yin phebs pa gang yin dri ba zhus par 'jigs byed yin tshul byung ba
bzhin 'o yug sding mar spyan drangs/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang bzhi rwa pod sogs yig sna'i lung dang man ngag /shin tu zab pa rwa 'khrid mkha'
'gro snyan brgyud kyi nyams 'khrid gnang bas rdo rje theg pa'i lam gyi gnad gsang thams cad thugs kyi klong du gyur pas bka' drin dran te mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ dran
pas gdung sel khyab bdag ma he'i zhal/ /ngur smrig zol gyis rol pa'i pha rgod des/ /'khrul med gnad kyi lam bzang

'di bstan tshe/ /mtha' yas chos kyi rang zhal rjen par mthong / /zhes gsungs/ gzhan yang padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang dang rta pod kyi lung rdzogs par gnang
/ rim gyis shangs mda'i rdo rje sgrub phug tu gnas 'brel zhag gsum mdzad pa'i nub cig gzugs med pa'i skad cig la zab bur song ayon rin po che bzhugs yod zer ba zhig byung
bas rkyen byas/ rje bla ma zab bu phyogs la phebs pa'i me tshor du zhag gnyis bzhugs pa'i nub khye'u gzhon nu sngags chas can zhig gis sngar gsan pa dang ma gsan pa'i chos
kyi rnam grangs so sor dbye zhing / ma thob pa rnams brag phug 'di'i ltag na yod gsung de ayon rin po che'i sprul par snang / rim gyis zab bu'i gzims phug gi sku brnyan
bde gshegs 'dus pa'i drung du gcig pur thugs dam mdzad pa'i tshe dkon gnyer gyi bsam par bla ma 'di tshos gter 'don zer nas gzungs bzhugs mi blug pa'i nges pa med snyam
sgo drung nas rdzi gsang bltas pas skad gdangs yid du 'ong ba shin tu snyan pa zhig gis thog mar gsung 'phros dang de'i rjes su chos lhang lhang gsung ba thos pas mi 'ga'
re yod dam snyam thal gyis yongs pa na gcig pur bzhugs 'dug pas dad pa lhag par skyes shing de dus ayon chen po dngos su zhal gzigs nas zab chos mang po gsungs par gda'/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sogs la drag po rtsal gyi byin rlabs thugs dbang dang nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs sogs stsal/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis drung
yig mdzad nas bde chen dag

zhing mar grags pa'i ayon rin po che'i gsol 'debs tshig don phun sum tshogs pa de yang mdzad/ myug rgyal khang du zhag lnga tsam bzhugs nas 'dar du phebs/ rnam rgyal chos rdzong
du mgon khang gsar du mdzad nas rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i sku byis pa lo bcu drug 'gro ba'i tshad/ yum chen/ lha mo/ zhal bram gzugs gsum khru phyed
do/ /rtag gtor mgon po che chung las mkhan bcas mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i 'dzin gtor spyan gzigs/ thog tu man ngag las byung ba'i ru mtshon btsugs/ sku brnyan rnams dam
pa'i shog dril zhal shes mas brgyan pa'i rab gnas zhag bdun mas 'og min gyi gnas nas mgon po dngos su byon pa'i gzi byin gyi 'phrin las rnam bzhi thogs pa med par sgrub pa'i
sku rnams dus phyis sde srid gtsang pas rdzong bshigs nas gzhis kar spos/ de nas kyang 'phos te deng sang sa skya'i khyad 'phags mgon khang du bzhugs par snang / rnga
yab gling gi mgon sogs 'dren pa dang / /yi dam srung ma'i zlos gar gang thugs shel/ /dag pa'i tshon ris dbang gzhu ltar bkra ba/ /bur shing dngar ba'i ro bzhin dbye nus
min/ /skye mang rjes bzung thugs sras gnas gsar bar/ /gnyis spangs bla ma'i gdams pa yongs gtod pa'i/ /rten 'brel zhing skyong dbang pos te se nas/ /dmar zlum spyan gyis
gzigs te nye bar bsgrigs/ /g.yang sar 'jigs bral brtul zhugs gshog rlabs kyis/ /brgya phrag cho 'phrul bstan tshe gos ser mig /mkha' lding zhon pa'i khengs pa yongs bor nas/
/rus sbal gzugs kyis sa chen

'degs par brdzu/ /rab dkar chos 'khor gangs ri'i yang rtse nas/ /tshad ma bzhi ldan 'jigs med seng ge'i glus/ /shes rlom ri dgas spyod med thun mong gi /gdams pa'i rtswa chur
mgo bo bstad de nyol/ /'khor los sgyur ba'i rigs brgyud lha yi sras/ /stong phrag byung la mang por 'dzin blo chungs/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i slob bu gser ri'i sbubs/ /shar
ba'i grangs med zla ba 'di la ltos/ /legs ldan dpa' bo lha min dpung tshogs las/ /rnam par rgyal ba'i gad brgyangs sgrog pa'i gnas/ /ha har bzhad pa'i dur khrod rgyu
ba'i stag /mche ba'i rtse mor dgra bo'i don snying 'khrig /gsol 'debs las/ bstan srung mchog rnams las la bskul ba'i tshe/ /ru mtshon rtse la gri gug 'bar ba gzigs/ /bka'
yi springs yig bi hAr gtsug gis mchod/ /dam can bran du 'khol la gsol ba 'debs/ /mu stegs 'dul bar rje btsun bkas bskul zhing / /rnal 'byor dbang mos spyan 'dren tshul bstan
