kyang / /bstan la rjes dgongs sku tshe'i 'du byed mchog /slar yang byin gyis brlabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /dad ldan bka' 'bangs mchog gi skye ba gang / /lcang lo can nas
yongs pa'i gnod sbyin gyis/ /dri med nor bu'i 'od zer 'phreng mdzes pa/ /drin bsab mchod pa phul la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes par tshig gis zin mi zin sna tshogs pa'i lo 'di
nang du dbyangs can lha mos rjes su bzung ba'i rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho zhes shes bya thams cad la mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs pa de nyid zhabs kyi padma la gtsug gi nor bus
reg par byon te sku gsung thugs kyi yon tan

zla ba'i zer gyis rnam par phye ste mi 'phrogs pa'i dad pa mchog gi kunda yongs su bzhad pa la brten lcags mo phag gi lo dpyid kyi dpal mo'i dga' ston dar ba'i tshe gsang chen
slob bshad kyi sngags gra 'dar stod chos 'khor yang rtser mkhan rin po che 'jam pa'i dbyangs blo gros rnam rgyal/ thugs kyi sras gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po klu
sgrub rgya mtsho/ rje rab brtan pa sogs skal ldan gyi gdul bya kha shas la tshe gcig la 'dus pa rnam gsum gyi 'phrang brgal te bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sa chen por
bgrod pa'i nges lam zab mo snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi dang 'brel ba'i gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi dbang byin rlabs 'khrid lung man ngag mtha' dag rdzogs par gnang
/ gsung rgyun nyams pa med pa'i lam 'bras kyi 'khrid yig chen mo'ang zin bris mdzad nas spyan lam du phab pas nga'i gsung ngag slob bshad kyi bka' khyed la babs slob ma'i
tshil bu lta bu yin zhes dgyes rtser son/ zhal slob kyi nang nas kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse gong du phud pa'i rje btsun bod mkhar ba/ mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros/ rje 'di
gsum 'gran gyi zla med du mngon zhing / khyad par kun mkhyen klu sgrub pa'i gsung las skyes pa'i bshes gnyen paN chen ngag dbang chos grags/ /'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes
gnyen sogs mkhas grub mang du byon zhing / mkhan ngag dbang chos grags nas rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ sa skya khri rin po che/ rgyal rtse bdag
po byams pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan khu dbon/ bya gshong mkhan chen mang thos grags

pa rnam rgyal/ yangs can mkhan po byams pa bsod nams mtha' yas/ gzims shag chos rje ngag dbang rnam rgyal sogs mtha' klas pa byon te ru lag stod kyi 'dzin mar kha'u brag rdzong
pa'i ring lugs gdugs dkar po gcig gis mngon par khyab pa'i 'phrin las kyi 'jug pa mchog tu yangs/ rje 'di nyid kyi bslab ston ltar klu sgrub rjes gzhi bsnyen mdzad par
gegs kyi rnam pa cung zad byung ba'i tshe zhu yig phul ba'i lan 'di lta ste/ oM swa sti/ dpal brgyud pa kun 'dus rigs brgya'i mgon/ /pha dngos grub 'byung gnas yid bzhin
nor/ /rje dran pas gdung sel rdo ring pa/ /bu snod ldan gyi rgyud la byin gyis rlobs/ /khyed dal 'byor rten mchog legs par thob/ /phyi thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs rgya cher
bcad/ /yongs las 'phro dang brtson 'grus gnyis su 'dzom/ /lam rdo rje theg pa'i yang bcud thob/ /dus deng sang bsam gtan gyi khang bu na/ /lus zab gsal lha ru lam me bsgom/
/ngag rdo rje'i sngags su dir ri sgrog /sems bde chen gyi ngang du cham me ba/ /chos 'di 'dra'i nyams len shes tsa na/ /rten dal 'byor la snying po longs pa yin/ /ma
'gro ba'i drin lan lon pa yin/ /bu mkhas pa'i thugs la de ltar zhog /sems dga' ba spro ba rgya cher skyed/ /yang dar cig thugs la 'di ltar zhog /rje bla ma spyi gtsug na
'du 'bral med/ /chos ci gnang rang sems dag pa'i 'khrul/ /de rim gnyis lam du 'khyer tshul shes/ /da gang ltar byas kyang bde ba yin/ /ces tshigs su bcad pas mdor bsdus
te gdams nas

bgegs kyi rnam pas khams 'dus pa sgyid lug pa ting nge 'dzin mi gsal ba snyam byed pa sogs skabs 'gar 'byung ba ni rdo rje theg pa'i lam gyi bogs yin pas lta ba gsal stong
zung 'jug las ma g.yos par gnang ba zhu/ zhes pa gnang ba la brten nas bgegs kyi 'ching ba mtha' dag nam mkha' la sbrul mdud bzhin grol/ mkhas grub chen po 'di nyid la mkha'
spyod skor gsum/ dmar chen skor gsum sogs klu pa'i gser chos bcu bzhi/ rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po/ dpal mgon stobs 'phrog dbang po sogs kyi chos skor thun
mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ gshed dmar spros med/ bka' gdams sogs bstan pa spyi bye brag gi zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsis thugs kyi bum bzang yongs su gang bar mdzad
do/ /lan cig shar phyogs su dgag dgos che ba zhig la phebs pa'i sta gon gyi tshe grang mo che'i mgon khang gi ru mtshon rnams la bka' bsgo 'phrin bcol mdzad pa'i dus gzigs
snang la de'i thad kyi nam mkha' rdo rje srin po sku shin tu che ba zhig gis phyag g.yas kyis gri gug sgo tshad tsam 'char stabs su bzung bar me lce tsha zhing rtsub pa'i
tsha tsha phyogs bcur 'phro ba gsal bar gzigs shing / der ma zad gnyan mgon chen po dang pho nya las mkhan rnams kyis log par 'khu ba'i dpung tshogs rnams phye ma leb
dang me lce'i tshul bzhin rdul du brlag pa'i gzigs snang ci yang byung bar mngon/ gtsug lag khang bsrung ba'i rgyal po li byin ha ra sogs snang srid kyi dregs pa can mang
por bka' rtags kyi springs yig stsal ba dag kyang gtsug tor gyi rtse mor 'god cing dam las mi 'da' bas

'phrin las tshul bzhin du sgrub pa mang la/ de bas ches lhag pa rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams kyang bran du 'khol te ji ltar bsgo ba lhur len pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen
brtse'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i bstod par/ gur gyi mgon po dpa' bo bram ze'i gzugs/ /'chi bdag dbang phyug ging lnga gza' gdong sogs/ /dam can rgya mtsho mngon sum bran du
'khol/ /mthu stobs nus pa'i gter la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes byung bas kyang shes nus/ de yang kun spangs rin po ches khyed la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs byas res kyis ltas
ya mtshan pa re yong gin 'dug pas mkha' spyod du myur bar 'khrid nyen yod tshul tshe sgrub la nan tan skyed mdzod sku tshe ring ba byung na bstan pa dang sems can la phan
zhing mthu stobs chen po yong ba'i lung bstan ltar snga gong zhig gzigs snang la skas ring po btsugs pa la bud med mda' dar khyer ba gsum babs byung nas khyed gdan 'dren
la yongs zer bar da lta nga la pha ma'ang yod pas mi 'gro gsungs par bud med de rnams log song / grang mo cher bzhugs skabs shig 'od gsal gyi ngang du rje btsun rdo ring
pa chen po byon te da lta rgya gar lho phyogs na mu stegs kyi rgyal po stobs che ba zhig yod pas de 'dul du khyed 'gro dgos pa 'dug gsungs par brten zhag 'ga'i bar bla ma
la gsol ba 'debs pa mdzad pa na 'jam dbyangs mkhyen rtse'i dbang phyug sku drung du bzhugs pa'i nub cig dag snang du nam mkha' nas mthongs khung lta bu skya shar re ba
nas rus pa'i skas btsugs par bu mo dmar mo lo brgyad tsam lon pa rus rgyan chab be ba btags pa zhig rgyab 'bab

tu byung nas rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos khyod 'bod du btang ba yin 'gro'am mi 'gro zer ba la thugs mi spro ba'i rnam pas lam 'bras bshad 'phro yang yod gsungs pas skas
de la rgyab 'dzegs kyis log song rjes skas bsdus shing mthongs khung mi snang ba gyur na yang ltas de dag dang rdo rje btsun mos mkha' spyod du gshegs par bskul bas zhing
khams 'pho'am dgongs pa'i thugs som nyir gyur pa'i tshe/ re zhig lon pa na kun spangs rin po che 'od gsal gyi ngang du phebs nas mu stegs pa'i rgyal po rgan pa de shi bas
gzhon pa dang khyed las 'brel mi 'dug da lam gzhan zhig btang yod skor cig 'byon mi dgos 'dugs gsungs par snang zhing / skal ldan gyi slob ma mang pos yun ring por bzhugs
pa'i rten 'brel gyi sgo sgrig pa'i gsol btab dang / rje btsun a ba dhU tI pa'i bslab bya'i gsung rnams thugs kyis dran te kha ba ri pa rnams kyi bstan 'gro'i ched du sku
tshe byin gyis brlabs pa ni/ 'phags pa yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i mdo las/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku ni rdo rje'i sku yin te/ deng phyin chad khyod kyis don 'di rtse
gcig pa'i sems kyis yid la bya yis/ zag bcas kyi skur ni mi bsam mo/ /zhes 'ja' lus rdo rje'i sku 'grub pa thams cad kyi ngang tshul yin zhing gdul bya so so'i las snang
gi dbang gis mthong tshul sna tshogs 'byung ba ni/ myang 'das rgya gar 'gyur las/ res 'ga' ni sems can rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa grongs so snyam du yang dag par shes
mod kyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa ni dus thams cad du rtag pa dang brtan pa dang ther zug pa yin te/ zhes 'byung ba ltar ro/

/gsang ba'i bdag pos rjes su bzung ba'i 'a zha nam mkha'i mtshan can sbyin bdag gi gtso bo thugs dad shin tu che ba'i khar gshegs par sngon du phyogs tshe skyabs 'jug gi gsol
'debs nan tan du mdzad pas thugs rje'i rgyud bskul ba'i mthus mtshan bcas mtshan med kyi skyabs 'jug ched du bstad pa rgyun mar gnang zhing / rje btsun rdo ring pa chen
pos rje nyid la ltos pa thams cad rjes su 'dzin pa'i zhal bzhes yod pa bzhin thugs yus pa'i rnam pas gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab pa na/ thugs dam 'od gsal zhig la rje btsun
gnyis spangs zhabs byon nas gnas gsar pa'i sde pa khong bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyi bstan pa stobs kyis 'dzin pa'i sbyin bdag khyad par can yin gshis chos skyong
srung ma rnams kyis kyang lus dang grib ma bzhin 'grogs nas grogs byed kyin 'dug /'on kyang sngon gyi las shugs shig gis rgya nag gi mtha' 'khob tu ru dra mo zhig gi
mngal du zla ba bdun tsam gnas rjes ma de chos skyong rnams kyis bsgral nas phyag na rdo rje'i drung du skye ba blangs te don 'grub par mchis mod/ khyed kyis 'bad rtsol
mdzad na yun thung ngu zhig gis chog pa 'dra gang ltar do nub mjal bar 'ong gsungs pa bzhin ched du thugs 'dun bstad pas tshes bco lnga'i nub A tsarYa 'dras brten nas sde
pa sngon dus kyi srid pa'i cha byad bzhin byung ste/ kho bo tshe 'phos rung bla ma rnams kyi thugs rje dang grogs A tsarYa 'di rnams kyis byas pas rgyal kha byung / da lta
lha'i sgom bzlas dang gtor bsngos kyang ma chag phyag rdor gyi gsal 'debs shig dgos zhu ba ltar phyag 'khrid mdzad

de nas zhag gsum gyi ring gsang bdag gi dkyil 'khor du bcug ste mtshan byang la dbang bskur lam ston mdzad pas zhag 'ga' zhig song ba na 'brug gi sgra snyan po byung ba'i rkyen
gyis gzigs pa'i tshe nor bu mig gsum pa 'od zer 'phro bas gzims chung gi nang gang ba byung bas sde pa de gnod sbyin bde ldan 'od zer zhes 'brug gi gzhon pa can gyi
rnam par lcang lo can du skyes te/ dpal gsang ba'i bdag pos rjes su bzung bas rje 'di nyid la drin lan bsab pa'i ched du nor bu phul bar snang / sde pa gshegs rjes rje bla
ma bo dong nas myur du phebs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gtso bor gyur pa'i zhal ngo rnams dang don gnyer can nyi shu skor la nA ro ta pa'i slob bshad kyi byin
rlabs/ rtsa dbu ma'i nyams 'khrid zab mo dang chos skor rnams stsal/ sems nyid gsal stong gsang ba'i rje btsun ma gcer mthong du ngo sprad par brten/ mkhyen brtse'i gsung
las/ a ho rgyal yum dbang mos mngon sum du/ /du ma'i skye bar rjes bzung bla ma mchog /mchog 'dis zab mo'i nye lam 'di bstan tshe/ /tshe 'dir mkha' spyod sgrub la the
tshom bral/ /zhes gsungs/ rim gyis shangs sreg shing rin cen sgang gi dgon par sde pa gnas gsar bas spyan drangs pa bzhin phebs/ dpal ldan chos skyong gi thugs bcud 'jam
dpal dmar po'i dbang byin rlabs/ zab lam spros pa med pa'i nyams 'khrid zab mo shin tu smin par gnang bas/ mkhyen brtse'i gsung las/ dpe nag bltas pa'i bshad yams tsam
ma yin par thugs nyams su ji ltar myong ba bzhin bstan pas sems kyi sgro 'dogs thams cad der chod

/ slar grub thob tu btags pa'i blun po 'ga' re'i rkang pa la gtug dgos bsams pa'i blo rtsa ba nas bud lam dang lam min pa'i shan chod pa zhig byung ste/ 'jam dpal khros pa
dus dgra'i dbang po des/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis thugs bcud 'di bstan tshe/ /'jam dbyangs bzhed pa'i don de kho bos rtogs/ /'jam dbyangs dngos su byon kyang zhu rgyu med/
/ces gsungs/ rim bzhin bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po'i thugs ngo dang bstun 'o yug sdings mar phebs thugs sras mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug la rje btsun yab dang thun mong
ba'i rtsa dbu ma'i 'khrid sogs stsal/ de nas rje bla mas kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse la da lo zha lur gnas skor dang sbrags nas byon bu lugs kyi dbang rnams thob na ma thob
na mdzod/ chos lung du bzhugs mkhan khri khang rje btsun ma rang khungs dag pas der zhu ba dang rnam sras kyi dbyangs rol 'dra yang rtsad gcod dgos pa'i bslab ston gnang
ba ni yab sras gnyis ka zha lu'i mkhan thog tu phebs pa'i mngon mkhyen du mchis/ rje 'di nyid dbus nas mgyogs 'khor zhig mdzad nas khri khang du phebs dus rje mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug la bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang dang zhal bzhi pa'i gsang 'khrid gnang / rje'i drung nas kyang gser dngul sogs 'bul ba stobs che ba bstar ro/ /mang thos nor
bu'i gdengs can klu yi dbang / /rig pa srid sgrub mda' bzhin rab drang bas/ /rgya chen gzhung brgya smra la mtsho byung ma/ /snying zhugs mkhas des khyod zhabs gtsug tu
bsten/ /slob bshad khyab 'jug rkang tog snod ldan gyi/ /rgyal mtshan

rtser bkod dga' ston la rol kyang / /thun mong rjes 'brangs lha min dogs bral ba/ /skal ldan shing rta gnyis pa sa 'dir snang / /khrag 'thung gar la bzhengs pa'i zhal sen rdul/
/ma mgon mkha' 'gro'i thor tshugs rtser 'dzegs nas/ /bka' rtags ri mo sde brgyad gtsug 'char ba/ /rgyal phran 'khor sgyur lung gi rjes 'gro bzhin/ /'chi med tshe byin
brlabs pa gzhom bral skus/ /gsang bdag rig pa 'dzin pa nam mkha'i mtshan/ /mkha' la mkha' yi sbyor ba ji bzhin du/ /lag na rdo rje'i 'khor lor smin cing grol/ /gsol 'debs
las/ 'dren pa mchog gis sngon nas lung bstan cing / /chos skyong lha mos gus pas spyan drangs te/ /dpal ldan zha lu'i chos kyi gdan khri la/ /zhabs pad mdzes par bkod
la gsol ba 'debs/ /dpal phug rnam par grol ba'i pho brang du/ /slob bshad zab mo'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ /mkhas grub slob mas sa gsum kun khyab ste/ /bstan pa nyin mor
mdzad la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes sngar mkhyen rab rin po ches rje btsun rdo ring pa chen por zha lu'i gdan sa mdzad pa 'char shas kha bas nged kyi tsha bo 'di la'ang mgo 'don
legs po mdzod gsung par bdag de 'dra mi byed zhus pas khyed mi mdzad na nyid kyi grwa pa zhig la nges par 'ong gsungs par brten/ rdo ring rin po ches sngar gyi lo rgyus
dang bcas brag dkar sems dpa' chen por khyod mkhan po mdzad dgos pa yong shas che gsungs pa'i lan du bdag gis yong yang mi yong byed kyang mi byed zhus pas des na chos
rje tshar pas mdzad 'gro nyen che gsungs pa dang /

de mtshungs rje nyid kyis rgyal yum tshul khrims bzang mo mjal bar phebs dus khyed la 'di mkho ba'i dus shig 'ong cis kyang gsan mdzod ces lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma'i rjes
gnang lung rnams rdzogs par stsal ba'i bla ma gnyis kyi lung bstan dus babs dang / bu ston rin po che slar yang rang bstan la bsams bzhin skye ba bzhes pa'i smon lam gyi
mthu brtas te zha lu'i chen slob thams cad mgrin gcig dbyangs gcig pa'i tshul gyis mkhan po'i gsol 'debs la yong ba'i sngon du nub cig mnal du song tshul bstan pa'i srod
'khor la bud med smug nag 'jigs su rung ba mche ba gtsigs shing ral pa dmar ser rting par sleb pa zhig byung nas khyed kyis zha lu'i gdan sa mdzad dgos zer ba zhig byung
ba dpal ldan ma'i cho 'phrul du 'dug ces zhabs 'bring pa 'dra la gsungs/ tho rengs thog kha nas rje nyid kyis zhal shar du gzigs te dung dkar po zhig bus pa skad shin tu
che ba byung / sang nyin phyag phyi rnams la de ring su byung yang gtam kha ma len so ma sod pa las med phebs par cung zad song ba na khang rnying slob dpon rnam sras/
rin spungs byams pa ba sogs zha lu'i mkhan por phebs dgos pa'i snyan gsan 'bul mi rnams slebs/ rgyu mtshan gsol bar zhal gyis ma bzhes pa'i de nub mnal lam du kun spangs
rje bzhugs gdan dma' ba la na bza' hrul zhing zhal mdangs ngan pa zhig byas bzhugs nas khyed la zha lu'i gdan sa'i snyan gsan byung ngam gsung bar byung yang khas ma blangs
gsol bar skyag re la a ngas na ning nas khyed la byas pa min pa e yin gsung ba

lung bstan du dgongs nas mkhan po'i zhal bzhes mdzad pa'i mtshan lam du/ rdo ring rin po che sku mdangs dang na bza' legs shing shin tu dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur ston pa zhig byung
/ de nas srin po zhes pa shing yos sos kyi dga' ston la babs pa 'phrod sbyor dge ba'i dus skya rags kyis chibs bsu dang 'dus tshogs rnams kyis 'phan gdugs rol mo sogs
mchod pa'i yo byad thogs pa'i ser sbreng / mchod gar gyis sna drangs pas mdun bsus dpal zha lu gser bkang gi chos gra chen po snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa bu ston rin
po che'i seng ge'i khrir phebs/ de'i tshe nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa la me tog gi char 'dab ma lnga pas mtshon lha rnams kyis mchod pa'i ched du phab cing / gan spos kyi dri
'dra rung ba la zhib tu brtags na sngar tshor ma myong ba'i dri bsung gis khyab pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas phun sum tshogs pa byung / sngon mthu chen gangs pa shAka
'bum gyi slob ma sngags rnying ma bka' gter thams cad la mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i g.yung ston rdo rje dpal zhes gos dkar lcang lo'i 'phreng ba 'dzin pa'i sngags 'chang
chen po des phung po ri bo che nas gtum mo dug hrul ma'am/ gsar ma ba rnams tsa munTi 'bod pa'i zhal brnyan ma he'i gdong can zhig gter nas bzhes pa dang cha 'dra ba'i
yab kyi zhal 'bag cig kyang bzos pa'i rwa nang du thams can mkhyen pa bu ston chos rjes gsol zan gyi lhag la gshin rje pho brgyad mo brgyad kyi gzugs brnyan phyag bzo
mdzad pa bcug pas byin rlabs shin tu che bar byung ba/ yos lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i dmar cha la bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel ba dang

bsam sbyor ngan pa 'chang ba'i gzugs can gzugs med rnams tshar gcod pa'i ched du ma he mchod pa'i srol btsugs/ thog mar dam bzhag gnang mkhan chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa/
zhal brnyan bzhes pa po sngags 'chang g.yung gis mdzad de 'phrin las rnam bzhi thogs med du sgrub pa'i dbu gtsugs/ /de nas mkhan thog mang po'i bar lo skor rer 'cham pa'i
srol rgyun nyams med du byung na'ang bar skabs su 'tshub kyi rnam pas shangs mtshal shor ba phyag zhabs rengs pa re gnyis byung bar brten la las dmod nas 'thor ba tsam las
bka' bsgo ma mdzad pas nub par nye ba'i lo skor gcig gnyis ma he 'cham gra'ang chag pas 'cham dgos pa'i ltas sna tshogs byung ba nas spyir rje 'di nyid mkhas grub kyi
snyan pa che bar ma zad bye brag mthu stobs kyi grags pa phyogs kun tu khyab pa'i mthun snang grub gshis de dus bu lugs kyi chos rgyun sgrub mchod sogs bstan pa nyams che
ba gso ba dang lhag par ma he'i bka' bsgo mdzad du re ba'i sngar gyi rgyun rnams dang bcas bstan pa spyi bye brag gi 'phel rgyas dang skye rgu'i bde thabs la dgongs te/
chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsang ba'i chos skyong las kyi gshin rje'i bka' bsgo ba gnang dgos zhes zhus pa bzhin zhal gyis 'ches/ dbus gtsang gi sde brgyad gnas sa gnyen
po mtha' dag tu dus tshes 'di la shog cig pa'i brda 'grems su rlung sems la nang byan chud pa'i rtogs ldan skad gtong rdzong bda' mdzad/ dam pa 'di nyid las shugs dbang
thang rim gro sogs la re ba dang / 'phral du zla sbrel gyi bsnyen pa tsam

gyis phan du re ba'i rigs ma yin par dus dgra'i dbang po ma he'i zhal can gyi bskyed rim la brtan pa thob/ rdzogs rim klong du gyur/ bsnyen sgrub pha mthar son pas 'jigs pa
dang bral na'ang gsang sngags phyag len gyi che ba mi nub pa'i slad du bdun gnyis kyi bar ljags bsnyen kha gso mdzad pa'i tshe 'od gsal du 'chi bdag yab yum la gshin rje
pho brgyad mo brgyad/ lha srin dregs pa'i tshogs kyis bskor nas zha lu'i rdo gcal du stang stabs byed pa shar/ spyi sgos so so nas gra sgrig dgos pa'i rigs sngar srol 'phyugs
med yong ba'i zhal ta gnang / dus der sgo yig gnang pa 'di lta ste/ shrI manggu ru badzra bhai ra wA ya na maH rgyal ba khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid nas bzung
bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa yab sras kyis gtso mdzad bdag gi bla ma rje btsun gnyis spangs zhabs kyi bar du byon pa'i rtsa ba dang brgyud par bcas pa'i dpal ldan bla
ma dam pa rnams kyi bka'/ khro bo'i dbang po dpal gshin rje'i gshed kyi lung / dpal zha lu gser bkang gi gdan sa bcu gsum pa shAkya'i dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa dpal dus
dgra nag po ma he'i zhal gyi brtul zhugs grub pa'i yi ge /srid pa gsum na gnas shing rgyu ba'i 'byung po mi dang mi ma yin pa rnams la zlo ba/ zla ba 'di'i nyer gsum gyi
nyin lho phyogs rim pa bdun gyi sa 'og 'jigs rung gshin rje'i grong khyer chen po nas dpal gshin rje'i gshed kyi bka' sdod chen po 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje yab yum dang
'khor las kyi ma gshin pho mo snang srid lha srin sde brgyad dang bcas pa spyan drangs/ mchod pa dang gtor

ma dang bstod pas mnyes par byas/ dmar chen gyi arghaM dang rdo rje bdud rtsi'i mna' chu blud/ dam tshig rdo rje 'bar bas dam la bzhag cing bka' bsgos te rgyal ba'i bstan pa
rin po che dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas pa dang / skye rgu sems can yongs kyi bde skyid 'phel bar bya ba'i ched dang khyad par chos grwa chen po 'di nyid kyis gtso
byas dge 'dun gyi sde dang rnal 'byor 'khor bcas bde zhing dam pa'i chos spyod pa'i 'phrin las 'chol ba dang / de dag la gnod cing bar du gcod pa'i mi dang mi ma yin pa
rnams srung ma dam tshig can rnams kyis rang rang gi khas blangs dang dam tshig rjes su dran pas mchod gtor gyis tshim par gyis la mthu dang nus pa stobs dang rdzu 'phrul
gang yod kyis bcol ba'i 'phrin las sgrubs/ /'dir 'dus shing tshogs pa'i mi rnams kyang bsam sbyor dge zhing zhi ba'i sgo nas ngo mtshar gyi ltad mos yid tshim pa dang
ma rungs pa'i las byas na 'di lta bu'i 'phrin las kyi sgo nas tshar bcad 'ong snyam pa'i skrag shes par gyis/ gal srid kha drag shed khyer mi sha kha mchu gsar rnying 'brel
bu lon/ /gtes gting 'dzin/ spyod ngan gshis ngan gyi sgo nas rgya 'dre 'thab rtsod/ gzings rkyen byas pa byung na chos sde chen po'i spyi sa nas lugs gnyis dang mthun
pa'i tshar gcod phyis lam khegs pa gtong ba dang 'jam dpal gshin rje'i gshed kyi rnal 'byor pa rab tu khros pas bka' bsgos te gtes po su yin pa de 'chi bdag gshin rje nag
po'i zas skal du ster bas nges pa gyis/ so so tha dad nas dran 'dzin dang bag yod la gnas pa dge

zhing zhi ba gal che/ me pho 'brug lo hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bcu la dpal zha lu gser bkang gi bla brang chos dbyings bde ba chen po'i pho brang nas bris/ zhes zla ba
bcu gnyis pa'i nyer gsum gyi nyin thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i bzhugs khri'i steng du phebs pa'i mtha' skor gyi khyon kun skya ser gyi khrom khri phrag tu brgal
bas bskor/ zha lu chos sde ba rnams kyis rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgo nas dbyu gu drug cu rtsa bzhi'i cho ga /las kyi gshin rjer mchod bshags bskang mdos rgyas par bstar/
lho phyogs na sa 'og rim pa bdun gyi rnam pa'i khang pa nas 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje yab yum la 'khor lha srin sde brgyad kyi 'bag chas gos kyi kha dog rnam pa sna tshogs
pa 'gros kyi rkang grangs kyi nges bzung med pa'i yid la gang shar gyi 'chams stabs dang / ngag nas sku sgra bso sgra sogs sgra sna tshogs pas phal cher rnam rtog dang
ya nga ba'i gnas su 'god pa'i gtso 'khor de rnams sbug sil rnga dung chen gyis gtsos pa'i rol mo gnam sa 'gas pa lta bus yar spyan drangs te khyams rar 'khor lugs sngar
srol ji lta ba la/ rje bla ma'i drung du khad nyer slebs pa'i tshe shes pa rang bzhin du gnas pa'i mis 'bag phod gyon par khu 'khris yong don mi 'dug rung zhal brnyan
gyi ye shes pa'i nus pa 'jug gi yod pa zhig yin nam rje'i drung du 'gro ba la 'jigs pa lta bu'i 'gro ma nus par tsho 'then byas pa'i ngang nas rim gyis 'ong te mgo bos btud
pa na/ 'jam dpal drag por khros pa'i nga rgyal gyi dpa' gdengs nang du shar ba'i phyi rol tu sku mdangs dmar smug tu gyur/ gdung shugs drag

pos rtsa brgyud bla ma'i mtshan nas brjod pa sogs bka' bsgo ba'i tshig rnams khrom pa kun gyi rna ba'i yul du thos pa dang chabs cig par gtsug tu rdo rje dang lce thog tu bdud
rtsi bzhag nas bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel zhing / gzugs can dgra dang gzugs med kyi bgegs dpung thams cad tshar gcod pa sogs 'phrin las rnam bzhi sgrub pa'i dam bsgrag
mdzad pa'i tshe ye shes kyi khro bo'i gzi byin dang sde brgyad kyi 'tshub lhongs kyis der 'khod thams cad 'jigs shing skyi g.ya' bar gyur/ bka' bsgo grub mtshams nang du
'khod pa'i dad ldan rnams ni gangs ri la zla ba shar bas dkar ba bzhin sngar bas kyang gus pa ches cher 'phel/ kun mkhyen bu ston zhabs dang rje btsun kha'u pa'i ring lugs
la snying nas smod cing 'tshe ba dag 'chi bdag gshin rje'i dmar zas su bstab song snyam pa'i yid khong du chud/ bzang ngan dang bral ba'i btang snyoms can rnams dang
tshod bgam par byed pa rnams ni tshar pa chos rje khong las shugs kyi dbang thang dang rdzas bsod can min 'dug kyang yi dam gyi lha'i gnang ba thob cing sngags smyon bgrangs
pa'i nus can zhig go zhes ca co'i sgra dir dir du glengs/ las kyi gshin rje'i gtor ma bstan dgra gang yod kyi phyogs su 'phangs shing sde brgyad rnams kyang dngos bshams
yid kyis sprul pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor los tshim nas bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i yi dam brtan pos so so'i gnas su dengs dngos gzhi khrom mi 'jam pa sogs ma byung na'ang zhag
khongs der zha lu bar shin tu gnag pa'i bstan dgra zhig khrag skyugs pa'i

rkyen gyis dus kyi pho nya'i dbang du song / rnam sras mchod pa sogs rgyas par mdzad/ me 'brug lo nag pa zla bar kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs/ khyab bdag bod mkhar ba chen
po/ mkhyen rab chos rje'i dbon po sogs grwa pa nyis brgya lhag pa la 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i dbang cha dgu tsam dang / spros med kyi 'khrid sogs so
so'i blo dang 'tsham pa'i dbang rjes gnang lung man ngag rgya cher stsal/ sgrub mchod chen mo'i tshogs dbur phebs pa'i gung gseng zhig la chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i
sku 'dra'i drung du gcig pur bzhugs te gdung shugs drag po'i gsol 'debs mdzad pas sku de gzi mdangs je cher rgyas shing sku'i cha shas thams cad las 'od zer sna lnga 'phros
nas bar snang khyab pa dang slar tshur 'dus la la rje nyid kyi sku la thim/ la la sku 'dra rang la thim pa'i thugs nyams shar/ mi ring bar sprul sku bde bsam pas gzigs
snang ji ltar byung ba'i sku zhig kyang thugs dam rten la bzheng du bcug /ri mthil gyi sgrigs kun spyod sgrub mchod che chung sogs chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i dus kyi
srol rgyun nyams pa rnams gsos te bstan pa rin po che nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad/ re zhig stod phyogs su phebs grang mo che dang rmu gshong du rgyang tsam stan chags nas
zha lur phebs skabs shig lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma'i gtor ma zhal bsgyur ba sogs dpal ldan ma 'dis 'phrin las thams cad sgrub pa'i dgyes mtshan gsal bar bstan/ me sbrul
zla ba dang po'i nang du thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis gtsos phyogs 'dus kyi slob ma mang du byon/ ri phug chos kyi pho

brang chen por gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad yongs rdzogs gnang bar kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bzhed pa ma nor ba gsang chen bstan pa rgyas byed ces
bya ba bum dbang gi rmi lam yan chad kyi zin bris yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu zhig mdzad/ zla ba bzhi pa nas don gnyer can du ma la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i
rim lnga'i 'khrid sogs bu lugs kyi 'khrid chen bzhi dang 'khrid chung bzhi rnams kyi nyams 'khrid rim bzhin chos thun gsum du bcad de so so'i rgyab rten gyi lung bcas
smin rgyas dang / gzhan yang mdo sngags kyi zab chos ji snyed cig stsal/ de yang rim lnga gnang gdong dbang ma thob pa kha yar byung bar smin byed med kha med nas rje bla
ma bka' chos gzhan gnang ba'i thugs brel gyis g.yengs nas gnang long ma byung bar kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse la khyed kyis gzhan ma'i rgyas bkab sogs 'dres bslad med pa'i
bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i yig cha sor bzhag gi dbang zhig bskur mdzod bka' phebs pa bzhin thun 'tshams kyi dgongs mo bzhi tsam zhig mar me la gzigs 'jug mdzad de rdul
tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang cha gnyis gsung bzhin bsgrubs/ zha lu pa'i pha chos bde chen ral gcig gi smin grol gnyis bar zhig nas ya bral te rje bla mas grol byed ma
gtogs smin byed ma gsan pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis mchog sprul legs ldan rdo rjer gsan zhing / 'di gnyan cha che grags kyis mang por spel ba ma mdzad rung 'di dus rje
nyid kyis da lam ngas bka' rgya bkrol ba yin pas 'tshub mi yong bstan rgyun la

dgongs nas cis kyang mdzod ces gsung ba ltar dbang cha gsum la bde chen ral gcig lha nyer lnga'i dbang bzhi/ gzhan don nus pa kha shas la byin rlabs gnyis dang bdag po chen
po'i dbang yang gnang bar brten chos 'di snum zad kyi mar me lta bu'i srog mthud pa'ang tshar chen bla ma nyid kyis bka' drin kho nar sems shing / rjes su gal chung chos
la byas pa'i rgyun nub par nye na'ang mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis gsan skabs rigs 'dzin chen po'i mchod dpon bla ma ayon rgyal po yod 'dug pa nas dbang lung gnyis ka gang
dkar phyogs su me stag tsam zhig byung mod/ la lar spang gi sha mo rdol ba lta bu ni gang yin ma shes/ rje bla mas yos lo nas bzung lo gsum gyi bar gdan sa mdzad nas kun
spangs kyi dgongs pa bstod pa'ang thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che sku na bgres song ba'i skabs zha lu'i gdan sa mi mdzad gsung ba'i bka' phebs pas zha lu ba rnams
kyis nan cher zhus pa'i tshe 'o na lo drug tsam bya yi zhes zhal gyis bzhes nas gsum song mtshams su 'jog pa gnang ba'i tshe zhal bzhes kyi lo ma thengs tshul zhus pa'i lan
du slar lo gsum byed gnang ba sku tshe rting ma zhig la dgongs pa'i zhal bzhes grub pa dang / sngar mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' las/ gnas gsar chos rje nyid
bu lugs kyi chos skor gsan pa dang cho ga phyag len gdangs dbyangs tshun la bslab sbyang zhib mo dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan phebs pa'ang mkhan thog tu 'byon dgos par dgongs pa'i
ye shes kyi gzigs pa gsal 'grib med pa'i thog tu babs pas zha lu'i chen slob sogs grwa rigs sbyin bdag kun mkhan chen

thams cad mkhyen pas zur bzhugs gnang phyin chos rje gnas gsar ba las 'os pa gzhan med do zhes mgrin gcig dbyangs gcig tu glengs te/ sde srid rin chen spungs pa la snyan 'bul
phul ba la'ang shin tu legs pa'i dgongs bstad bzang po'i bde khrol dang / gtso bor rje nyid kyi thugs rje'i gzigs pa lhod pa med pa sogs rgyu rkyen rnams 'dzom par brten
zha lu spyi sos mkhan po'i snyan gsan phul bar/ rje bla ma'i dgongs bstad dang bcas bzlog ma bde bar lo gcig gi zhal len gnang ba na rje nyid kyis ngas lo gsum khyed kyis
lo gcig mdzad na sde dgon tshos phyag rten kyang mi 'byor bas gsum nges par mdzod/ de nas mdzad bde mi bde'i babs la gzigs chog /dgon spag sbug gzhan gyi bla ma'i dod
min chos 'jig rten ga nas kyang rnam gzhag rgya chen po'i sleb thebs yod tshul phebs pa ltar chu stod zla ba'i tshes gcig rgyal phur gyi 'grub sbyor dus ma pham mgon po
rin chen grub kyi gdan sar bsko ba gnang bar/ sde srid rin spungs pa'i bsko 'ja' khri ston zha lu'i chen slob dge 'dun yon bdag gzhan yang phyogs kyi sde phran gyis mtshon
pa'i bdog pa rgya chen po spel/ khyad par mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pas ber zlam dbu zhwa sogs kyi gnang sbyin/ dpon slob tshang mar 'phral yun du dge ba'i bslab bya/
bkra shis me tog gi char chen po phab/ chos rje gdan sa bas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang cha gnyis dang sbyor drug gi 'khrid cig mdzad/ yab sras lhan rgyas sde pa gnas
gsar bas myug tu bro bzhas rtsed sna bsu ba ser sbreng gi bkod

pa dang bcas gdan drangs rnyed bkur gya nom pa bstabs/ dpal phug rnam par grol ba'i ri khrod du zla ba bdun tsam gyi ring rje 'di nyid kyis kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs/
mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel sogs dpon slob bco brgyad tsam la gsung ngag slob bshad shin tu smin pa gnang / sngar mkhyen brtse'i
mnal ltas la dpal phug tu pha bla mas gsung ngag bskyar nas gnang rgyu'i skor kyang 'di'i lung bstan du mchis/ lam 'bras kyi mjug tu dmar po skor gsum mgon po che chung
sogs kyi rjes gnang lung 'khrid yang bskyar dang shangs pa du gu pa'i gser chos kyi phyed tsam gnang / chos rnams gegs med du grub pa'i gtang rag yang steng du mdzad pa'i
tshe mdun gyi nam mkha' sprin du ma chad cig gi steng na mgon po thog tshad tsam gyi zhal nas ha ha dang hU~M hU~M gi sgra la chos 'di'i bdag po sngar yang nga rang gis
byas da dung yang nga rang gis byed zer ba gsal bar gsan/ rje nyid zab bur phebs pa'i lam zhor du rje mkhyen brtses 'o yug tu gdan drangs nas sri zhu rgya cher mdzad/ myug
tu shangs chos kyi 'phro dang sgrub thabs rgya mtsho rgyal khang du sgrol dkar gyi tshe 'khrid sogs thugs sras mkhyen brtse'i bzhed pa bkang nas stod du phebs/ sa rta'i
dbyar yab tshan 'phan yul ayon gzhis ka bas gdan drangs te phebs/ lam zhor ngur smrig gi gtsug lag khang du rje btsun sgrol ma mjal ba gnang ste der bzhugs skabs dag snang
la bud med mang po rten mjal gyin 'dug pa'i khrod na mig gsum yod pa'i bud med cig gzigs gsung pa

rdzu bag tsam las 'phags mas dngos su byin gyis brlabs par gdon mi za/ rim gyis phebs pa'i bzhugs mtsher rgyal sa shin tu che ba zhig tu gnas mal mdzad pa'i nam phyed tsam
la 'byung po des glags lta bar rtsom pa na gtum drag 'bar ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mes mtha'i rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu bskrad pa na phyis mi tshad de la 'gong po'i 'tshe ba
ye ma byung ba gda'/ 'phan yul ayon gzhis kar bzhugs skabs thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho hor bar ta karma dpal gyis rong po 'dam du gdan 'dren zhus pa'i phebs
lam du sde pa ayon gzhis ka bas gdan drangs pa dang 'grig rje nyid kyis nged thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i zhal slob yin pas rten 'brel legs gsungs nas thams
cad mkhyen pa la bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi chos 'brel gsan/ thams cad mkhyen pas gur mgon gyi rjes gnang zhu ba mdzad pas kha'u brag rdzong pa'i zab chos thugs nyams su bstar
ba'i rten 'brel gyi sgo thog mar 'grig /slar rin po che bod mkhar nas la gsung ngag tsam ma gtogs snyan brgyud phal cher gsan cing nA ro mkha' spyod dang rig byed ma
mgon po che chung sogs la nyams bzhes shin tu smin par gnang / nA lendra'i khams pa bla ma sdor dkar ba sogs don gnyer can nyi shu skor la bde mchog lo nag dril gsum gyi
dbang / dpyid thig nag po rim bzhi rim lnga rnams kyi nyams 'khrid/ rtsa rgyud kyi bshad pa/ ne gu chos drug gi dbang 'khrid byin rlabs lung sogs zab chos mang du gsungs/
phyogs der 'gro don 'phrin las kyi 'ur cher langs pa'i ngang nas gtsang du phebs pa'i lam g.yung mda' mkhar gyi

g.yabs steng du bzhugs/ mchod dpon gyis thugs dam gtor ma bshams phyag dril sogs phul kyang spyan mkha' reg shar gyi ri rtse la zim me bzhugs pa las gtor bsngos mi gnang 'dug
pa skabs mtshams shig nas zhabs bskul zhus par bsdus pa zhig mdzad/ gsol ba zhus pas kyang cung zad tsam las mi bzhes par sngar ltar bzhugs/ de bar phyag g.yog byings
khal bkal nas sngon la song gsol dpon blo gsal can la da dung ja skol gsungs gsol ja sbyor gnyis tsam gyi bar bzhugs nas phebs/ de'i tshe jo mo mkha' reg gi gangs ri'i rtser
sprin dkar po chen po zhig lho phyogs su skyes byung ba'i steng nas ayon rin po che sku mi tshad las cung che ba za hor gyi sku chas sprad pa na bza'i gong len la stag
lpags gsar pa'i mu 'gril yod pa/ phyag g.yas na gser gyi rdo rje dang g.yon na ka pA la bdud rtsis gang ba bsnams pa zhabs rdo rje skyil krung du bzhugs pa gsal bar gzigs
nas rim bzhin bsti gnas su phebs so/ /gnyis spangs bla ma'i lung bzhin bu ston rje'i/ /seng khrir phebs la 'dod khams dbang mo yis/ /nyer bskul srid mthar bstan pa 'phel
ba'i sgra/ /rab dkar bkra shis g.yas 'khyil dung las sgrog /'jig rten gsum dbang lha chen nyi ma'i bus/ /rdo rje'i rwa rtse spu gri ltar rno ba/ /khyod drung pad 'dab
rjes 'gro'i 'jam mnyen gyi/ /reg byar lta la mkha' ngos rgyu skar 'khrigs/ /mkhan gzugs lha gral sgrig pa'i las dbang bcud/ /myangs pas srog ldan sbyin skyes mched min pa/
/lha sngags ye shes gser sgong mngal 'dzin pa'i/ /mes po blo gsal rgya mtsho yab sras tsam/ /

bu ston bzhed srol padma'i skud pa la/ /rdo rje'i khams su rlobs zhes gnas gsar pa/ /gdung 'tshob dam par gsol tshe phyogs bcu'i rgyal/ /sras bcas yongs kyis bsngags pa'i me
tog gtor/ /kha bshad chu bor snyan brgyud gser ldan ma/ /bying las gyen 'degs bstan 'dzin mig sngon can/ /thos bsam sgom pa'i rus sbal 'phrul gyi stobs/ /tshangs pa'i blo
gros des kyang gzhal nus min/ /ris med 'gro ba'i bsod nams rlabs po ches/ /zhing gyur rgya mtsho'i gos can 'phrin las kyi/ /dbang phyug dam pa'i gnag snum ral pa'i rtser/
/zhabs sen zla ba tshes te gcig tu dkar/ /gsol 'debs las/ khyab bdag bla ma'i thugs rjes bskul ba bzhin/ /rang gi bsti gnas dam par zhabs bkod de/ /skal bzang sbyin pa'i
bdag po 'khor bcas rnams/ /'bral med thugs rjes bskyangs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pas zin so yod med sna tshogs las sa lug 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis
gdan 'dren gnang skabs myug tu rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan sku 'khrungs pa'i byin rlabs la spyan drangs pa bzhin phebs nas 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du
smin par mdzad pa sogs rjes su bzung zhing dgung lo lnga tsam gyi dus dmar po skor gsum chos skyong che chung tshe dpag med sogs kyi byin rlabs rjes gnang gi rigs kyang
mang du stsal/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gyi rnam thar las/ bdag gi spyil bu na de snga gong chos rje rab brtan pa'i bzhugs yul yin pas khong gnas rnying rgyal po
de la gsol mchod gnang gin yod 'dug pas de'i nang na

rgyal po de 'khor re 'gro ba zhig gzigs pa dang / lhag par bdag thugs rje'i gzigs pa mi lhod par gnang gin yod gda' bas zla ba de ga'i nang du rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po bka'
drin mtshungs med tshar pa rjes myug nas phyag dam bdud rtsi ril bu'i thums gsol ras dang bcas phebs byung ba'i nang na khyod kyi sgrub khang der gnas rnying rgyal po
'di 'phral 'phral 'gro ba zhig 'dug pas bar chad dam 'tshub kyi rnam pa bzhin mi 'ong 'dug gam/ ngas kyang dmigs pa sogs gang yong byed kyin yod lar rdo ring rin po cher
rang re'i brgyud 'dzin kun la gnod pa mi byed pa'i srog snying phul nas dam bca' 'o skol rnams la 'di gcig pu'i bka' drin yang bsam pa'i ra ba las 'das/ gang ltar de la
dmigs pa'i gtor ma 'dra dang dge sbyor 'bungs skyed de byed pa dang lhag par lam zab mo nyid la nan tan gyis rtag tu gsol ba thob/ gegs sel bogs 'don gyi skyel so 'di gcig
pu yin no gsung pa zhig phebs byung zhes bslab ston rgyas par stsal/ zha lu'i gdan sa kun spangs mdzad pa nas bzung rgyal khams phyogs med kyi gdul bya'i re ba skong ba
tsam ma gtogs 'jig rten za zi'i mthun 'jug la thugs sun pa'i tshul gyis spong ba bsam gtan la bzhol ba'i rnam pas rmu gshong du lo gsum phyogs gsum mdzad pa'i skabs 'jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i rnam thar du lcags sprel zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes gcig nas gzhi bsnyen gyi sngon 'gro bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshugs pa'i tshes bzhi'i nub rmi lam du
rje btsun rdo rje 'chang pha tshar pa rje dang mjal rta 'grin yang gsang gi dbang rdzogs par gnang / dkyil 'khor gtor ma dbang tshig sogs kyang shin tu

gsal ba dang / phyag len la dogs gcod 'dra zhu rgyu yod pa'ang zhus shing lan gnang ba zhig byung / yang nub cig pha bla ma bzhugs khri thog rtsar snyogs pa zhig gi steng na
ber thul ne tso kha gsar pa zhig bzhes nas bzhugs pa'i sku zhabs g.yon na bdag 'dug pa la a skyabs kyis gsol ja zhus rjes gsol kha zhu yi 'dug pas nga'i de khong la drongs
gsungs gsol kha de bdag la drangs pa zhig rmis/ yang nub cig dbu rtse 'og 'dra ba zhig na khri sngar gyi de las mtho ba 'dra ba zhig la bzhugs tshe 'khrid kyi tshar chos
de gsung rgyu yin snyam pa byas bdag sku mdun na 'dug pa la gsung chos ha cang gsal ba ni ma byung rlung bum can bzung spyan lta stangs mdzad har re bzhugs pa gsal po
zhig rmis/ yang nub cig bo dong rdzong gi bde ba can yin snyam pa zhig na bzhugs gdan mthon po zhig la rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa chen po bzhugs de'i sku gzhogs g.yon na
bdag /bdag gi g.yon na rje btsun dbon bzhugs pa rje rin po ches gzhis len mdzad rgyu ba'i ston gshom bzang po byas pa zhig rmis zhes byung / zha lur bzhugs skabs 'od gsal
du rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po na bza' sogs shin tu legs pa'i ngos ma chen rdo rje bkra shis phyags phyir khrid pa'i 'dar gyi phyogs su thal ler phebs pa zhig byung ba
phugs de phyogs su sdod dgos pa yod pa 'dug ces rje nyid kyi gsung 'phros las byung ba bzhin bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po 'dar pas 'di phyi bar gsum gyi skyabs gcig mgon
gcig zhus par brten phal cher grang mo che phyogs su stan chags/ sde pa'i sku rim la 'jigs byed drug

cu pa gnang skabs lingga skad ngan rtser re re bton pa tho phyin yod pa kun gyis tshor/ de bzhin gshegs pas lus las chad pa'i sgra gcan zin dang dgra ltar lta ba'i lhas byin
la nye ring med pa'i bden tshig bka' stsal ba'i mthus lhas byin ma 'ju ba'i nad las grol ba'i lo rgyus bzhin dam pa 'di nyid kyang ris med kyi 'gro ba la ma 'dris pa'i
mdza' bshes lta bur mdzad pa las 'dzin rtog gi phyogs lhung dri ma can mi mnga' na'ang / nyi mas ched du byas pa min par rten 'brel gyi dbang las zer 'phreng gis padma kha
'byed cing / brag phug byang bstan du nyi 'od mi 'char ba dngos po'i gshis lugs su grub pa ma go bar rje nyid la re bar bca' ba'i skye bo mchog dman rnams thugs rje chen
pos rjes su bzung bar brten se dkar rigs kyi thig le 'dar nas kyi mnga' thang je 'phel du gyur pa gdong dga' phyogs kyis ma bzod pa'i bdag po kun rin par chos rje tshar
pa 'di sa skya pa'i chos la mkhas drags/ gdung brgyud rnams chad na kho rang la bstan pa'i bdag po yong du re ba'i rmu gshong gi mgon po'i zhabs 'og tu mnan pa sogs ngan
byed byas zhes phra ma bcug pa dang btsun mo gnyis kyang gdong dga' ba'i lcam la song ba'i rgyus sa skya dang gdong dga' brtse bstun gyi dmag shing byi mang mkhar phyogs
su btang ba'i skabs dmag mi rnams kyis rmu'i mgon khang la lag rgyag byas sku rnams bshig pa'i bzungs bzhugs bdag chen pa'i spyan lam du phab pas/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa
dang gdung brgyud 'phel ba'i spel tshig gzigs pa na thugs 'gyod byung yang zer/ ma chen rdo rje bkra shis kyis dgon pa ni dmag gi bcom zin 'dug mthu yod na rtags thon

pa zhig gnang dgos zhus pa'i lan du bdag chen khong rang ci mdzad kyang kho bo sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i sgor zhugs nas gdung brgyud la mthu mi byed khyod kyis yod na gyis zhes
bka' bkyon pa'i rnam pa'ang mdzad/ bya gshong du gtor bzlog la phebs skabs gnas khang de thog ma las yangs shing gru bzhi lam pa gyang logs la rdul sogs med pa'i snum
zhag che ba de'i 'khor kun gyis gsal bar mthong / yol rin chen gling du chos rje blo gros brtan pa mi ma yin du skyes nas smyug la ba yas mas gnod tshabs che ba'i gtam byung
ba na mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros kyis brtag pa dang yin na sbyin sreg dgos tshul zhu ba mdzad pa'i lan du de dngos bstan min rgya 'dres brdzus pas dgon pa la cher mi
gnod gtor bzlog 'ur chil ba zhig mdzad na sku nye tshor 'gyur 'gro/ ma nas smyug la ba tshang la gang stongs shig yong ba 'dug tshul gsungs pa'i lung bstan gyi thog kho
nar song / yang lo phyi ma zhig sa skya ngam ring gdong dga' ba gsum rtse bstun pa'i gsang dmag btang ba'i tshe rje nyid rnam rgyal stag rtser bzhugs skabs yin gshis/ 'dar
ba rin cen dpal bzang pas dmag bsdu gsog kyang ma grub gshis rdzong sprod dgos pa yong 'dra zhes rtab rtab por gsol ba na bka' las/ rdzong rtsig pa dka' ba ma gtogs sprod
pa la gnangs med lar lte phrag pho sa ru snying khrag 'thor ba legs pas tshab tshab ma mdzad gsungs nas cung zad song ba na bskyar zhu zhus pas/ da dmag ga tsam na slebs
gsung bar rdzong ri'i rked sgrol tsam mchod rten rtse ring rtsar 'byor 'dug zhus par/ mchod dpon la khyod rang thog khar song la dmod nas 'di

thor/ mi rkang 'di lan gsum bus gsung pa bzhin byas pas dgun stod yin kyang glog 'brug gi sgra drag po dang bcas ser ba cog mo'i sgo nga tsam babs pas dmag rnams skad cig la
byer/ sgar thog tu srin bya dang 'ug pa babs pa'i 'khrul gyis nad rims kyis btab nas stong log tu song ste g.yul las rnam par rgyal/ de dus gzigs snang la mdun gyi nam
mkha' sprin sngon 'khrigs pa'i steng du rje btsun rdo ring pa de nyid sku la chos gos rnam pa gsum gyis brgyan pa'i phyag g.yas gser gyi rdo rje nam mkha' la 'phyar zhing
/ g.yon pa dngul dkar gyi dril bu 'khrol ba yid tsam khros pa'i nyams dang bcas seng ge dkar mo rgyan gyis spras pa'i steng na rgyal po rol pa'i 'dug stangs kyis bzhugs
pa/ de'i dbu gtsug gi thad du bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yan gyi gsung ngag bla ma brgyud pa yongs rdzogs/ de'i g.yas g.yon du sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug /ku
ku ri pa/ lo hi pa/ g.yung po khrag 'thung / dril bu pa/ nA ro ta pa brgyad po zhi drag gi rnam 'gyur du ma ston pa/ gzhan yang tshe dpag med/ dzambha la/ gur zhal/ las
mkhan dang bcas pa zhal gzigs/ de'i tshe/ dpal ldan rgyal ba kun gyi mthu stobs ni/ /gcig tu bsdus pa drin can chos kyi rje/ /khyod zhabs dran pa'i mod la bdud dpung rnams/
/phye mar 'thag mdzad de la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes sogs gsol 'debs bdud dpung phyer 'thag mar grags pa zhal gzigs ji ltar byung ba dang mthun pa thugs rtsom gnas/ gsung
'phros kyi lhongs su bdag chen kun dga' rin chen 'di ma byon na sa skya pa'i bstan pa 'di grum tse gung med 'dra ba'i mtha' yod kyang

dbus med pa zhig yong nges su 'dug kyang bdag chen 'dis bstan pa'i khur bzhes pa sa skya pa'i 'phrin las mtha' dbus med par rgyas pa 'di rang re rnams blo bag bro ba'i tshad
yin gsung zhes bgros la lar snang ba bar skabs su lha khang bla brang pa'i nye gnas kyi brgyud pa dang shar pa sogs gdan sa nang du dbang chen mangs bas/ 'jam dbyangs chos
rje yab sras dang sa lo rnams kyi dus gnang re dka' tsho bdag po kun rin pas tshar bcad nas sde ma lag dang bcas pa 'jam dar la song ba 'jig rten phyogs nas mdzad go
chod gras la dgongs snang ba bdag nyid chen po'i mdzad pa ji ltar yang dpon chen gyi gras la chud nges su 'dug /chos rgyun gyi phyag rjes ni shin tu chung / rdor dbyings
kyi blos slong dang mgon sku bshig pa sogs gnang sgo ji ltar yang bla ma khyi dang khyi mjug mgo'i dpe bzhin rje bla mas thugs gting nas ma gus pa ni ma mdzad/ gus po rang
gis gnang thebs kyang mi 'dug /gong gi 'phros las/ phyogs 'dir sa chen bde skyid 'od chags pa/ /thal ba ji bzhin skya bor sgyur byed cing / /dkon cog rten dang bstan 'dzin
skyes bu'i tshogs/ /'joms byed bdud dpung tshogs rnams bzlog tu gsol/ /zhes rang bzhin brjod pa'i rgyan kho nar mchis/ bdag po kun rin pa'i phur zor skyer mda' 'ug sgro
ma bo dong gi 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gzims chung gi gdung ma la thebs nas ring por ma lon par gshegs pa'i mthu skad ni tshag mgo bum nang du btsos pa'i gtam rgyus
kho nar 'dug cing / khong gi mthu de rdog gi gze ma rnon po phyogs kun tu 'dzug pa'i dpe bzhin sa lo

'jam rdor yang sku tshe ring po ma byung bas brgyab pa 'dra/ gter chen chos kyi rgyal po ratna gling pa'i lung bstan chen mor/ sa yi phyogs su bla mas slob ma bslu: zhes dang
/ byang chub gling pa dpal rgyan gyi thugs gter 'khor 'das rang grol gyi zhus lan gsal ba'i sgron me las/ mnga' ris gdug pa'i dmag 'go g.yo: 'khon rigs kun zhes bya bas
'khrugaH khol bur sdug bsngal cung zad bskyed: ces sogs dogs pa'i gnas mang tsam yod kyang gnas lugs shes na zog po'i mtshang gi dpe ltar spros par dgongs pa chung zh-ing
gang shar thams cad lha dang lha mo'i rnam par 'char ba'i dag snang gi bden kha phul nas rtsod pa chos thog tu zhi bar byed do/ /de yang tshoms las/ thub rnams sdig pa
chu yis mi bkru zhing / /'gro ba'i sdug bsngal phyag gis mi sel la/ /nyid kyi rtogs pa gzhan la spo min te/ /chos nyid bden pa bstan pas grol bar 'gyur/ /zhes 'o skol gyi
ston pa bu ram shing pas kyang chos kyi 'khor lo rim pa gsum du bskor nas 'gro ba rnams phan bde'i lam la 'god par mdzad pa bzhin/ dam pa 'di nyid kyis mdo sngags kyi chos
tshul gdul bya so so'i blo dang 'tsham par bstan pas mchog rnams kyis ni bstan pa phyogs bzhir skyong ba'i dar chen btsugs/ la la dag klog pa thos bsam gyi sgo nas 'chad
nyan/ 'ga' zhig spong ba bsam gtan gyi rim pa lhur len pa'i bshad sgrub kyi chu rgyun rje bla ma'i 'phrin las ma dros mtsho las phyogs brgyar 'bab/ sa skyong ba'i bstan
pa'i sbyin bdag sogs skye rgu grangs yas pa dkon mchog gsum la bla mar 'dzin cing 'di phyi'i legs tshogs sgrub pa la sbyar ba'i

grangs kyi mtha' ni brjod pa'i yul lta ga la zhig /'on te che long rags rim tsam brjod na/ rang bstan kha'u brag rdzong pa'i lugs srol 'dzin nges kyi skyes bu ni/ mkhyen brtse
nus gsum thams cad la 'jam dpal rdo rje mi'i zlos gar can sras kyi thu bo zha lu mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang
phyug chen po spyan snga rje btsun bod mkhar ba mai tri byams pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ nyams dang rtogs pas bdag rgyud yongs su grol bas thugs rjes gzhan rjes su 'dzin
pa la 'gran pa'i zla dang bral ba rtse tshogs mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros/ rgyan drug mchog gnyis kyi gzhung lugs la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa rnam par dge ba ngam ring mkhan
chen byams pa blo gros rnam rgyal/ dbyangs can lha mos rjes su bzung bas gnas lnga rig pa smra ba la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i mkhyen rab kyi mkhas pa kun gyi gtsug gi
nor bur gyur pa mnyan yod bya gshong mkhan chen mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ lung dang rtogs pa'i yon tan gyi nor bus thugs rgyud yongs su gtams shing snyan brgyud tshad
ma bzhi ldan gyi bstan pa'i srog shing bo dong mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ mthu stobs nus pa rwa lo gnyis pa lta bu sngags 'chang yongs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba
chos 'khor yang rtse'i mkhan chen bsod nams chos 'phel/ zab don snyan brgyud bdud rtsis thugs kyi bum bzang yongs su gtams shing mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i dngos kyi
gdan sa pa chos dbang rin chen dpal gyi rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i chos kyi khri la mngon par mdzegs pa mkhan byams pa rab brtan/ zab

don chos kyi mnga' bdag smyug la mkhan po bsod nams dbang po/ mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i gzhung la blo gros kyi snang ba gcig tu dkar ba skyed tshal mkhan po rab brtan dpal 'bar/
mang thos mkhyen pa'i spyan ldan mkha' ri mkhan po blo gros chos 'phags/ rab 'byams rgyud sde rgya mtshor mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs pa 'jam dbyangs byang gling rje bkra
shis rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig bla ma'i rigs sras zab don rtogs pa'i nyi ma rje gzhon nu stobs ldan/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin pa mchod dpon drung
kun dga' legs pa/ bla ma'i zhabs tog lhur blangs pas byin rlabs thugs la zhugs shing snyan brgyud zab mo'i mdzod 'dzin pa ma chen rdo rje bkra shis/ nges don zab mos
rtogs pa'i klong rdol ba 'phags mchog byams pa bskal bzang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyi bstan pa'i shing rta chen po dbon rin po che khyab bdag dbang phyug rab
brtan/ mnyan mgon gdams pa'i srog shing mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug drung yig byams pa don grub/ mdo khams gdung ba'i mun sel chos gling drung pa/ mi phyed dad pa'i dbang
phyug rje mgon po 'od zer/ thos bsam sgom la gzhol ba rje mgon po rdo rje/ spar phu'i gdan sa pu tra ming sring bran du 'khol ba'i brag chos pa sogs dang / ris med pa'i
bstan par phyogs bcur spel ba/ rgya hor bod kyi skye rgu mtha' dag gi gtsug tor rtse mor zhabs zung 'khor lo'i ri mo 'god pa thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho dpal
bzang po/ karma pa'i bstan 'dzin chen po rgyal tshab rin po che grags pa don grub/ mchog gi sprul sku mnga' ris gter chen nyi zla 'od zer/ byang pa rigs ldan

rim par byon pa'i ti shrI rdo ring dbon po kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ ngor e waM chos ldan gyi mkhan po thar pa rtse ba paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkha' ri chos sde'i mkhan
po kun dga' lung rigs/ rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po'i dbon po ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ mnga' ris ru thog pa bla chen nam mkha' gzi brjid/ kun mkhyen tshe dbang bkra
shis kyi dbon po chos kyi rje rnam rgyal bkra shis/ chos rje smon lam pa/ dga' gdong slob dpon shes rab rdo rje/ bsdu dngos bzhi'i sgo nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa rje bsam
gtan rin chen/ stobs ldan mang po'i bla mar gyur cing snang sems la dbang 'byor ba dpal sdings rab 'byams pa chos dpal bzang po/ grub pa tshad du 'khyol bas don gnyis
lhun gyis grub pa cha lung grub chen ma bde legs dpal 'dzom/ nges don zab mos thugs rgyud grol ba rje rdzogs chen pa byams pa rin chen rdo rje/ mkhas pa'i dbang po ma ma
pa byams pa rab dga'/ myug chos lung pa chos rje nam mkha' mtha' yas/ khro phu gdung brgyud shangs 'ba' ra ba bya btang chos grags/ myug pa chos rje bsod nams dpal 'byor/
rin po che drung rams chos rje bsod nams tshul khrims/ rje byams pa rab dkar/ lo chen rnam rgyal grags pa sku mched/ brag ram slob dpon pa/ chos rje rin cen rgyal mtshan
gtsang pa rdor rgyan sogs dang / bstan pa'i sbyin bdag lha rigs 'a zha'i sa skyong nam mkha' sogs sde pa gnas gsar ba'i zhal ngo / se dkar rigs kyi thig le mi rje rin chen
dpal bzang sogs sde pa 'dar pa'i zhal ngo/ lugs gnyis kyi rnam dpyod yangs

pa'i sde pa khri khang nas nyin byed dbang po dang dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po'i rigs brgyud ayon gzhis ka ba mi dbang rin chen rdo rje/ sde ba spar nas/ sde pa snang rtse
ba nam mkha' tshe brtan rdo rje sogs sde dpon dpon skya'i rigs mchog dman du mas 'di phyi'i skyabs mgon gling dang dpung gnyen du gsol ba mtha' dag 'di phyi bar gsum du dge
ba'i lam chen po la sbyor ba mdzad/ thugs rtsom gyi rim pa che long tsam ni/ ayon chos kyi rgyal pos gtso mdzad 'dren pa 'ga' la bstod pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ so thar
sdom rgyun/ gsung ngag slob bshad/ rwa 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud/ lam zab rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i 'khrid/ rta mgrin yang gsang / skyer sgang lugs kyi rta mgrin gsang
sgrub/ ne gu chos drug /grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe 'khrid/ tshe sgrub zhag bdun ma/ dmar 'khrid/ sgrol dkar tshe 'khrid/ ku ru kulle phyi sgrub/ 'dod rgyal thun mong ba
dang dpal gur gyi mgon po'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi 'khrid/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i gsang 'khrid rnams kyi brgyud 'debs dang sham bur rang rang gi lam rim dang sbyar ba'i
smon lam rdo rje'i tshig rkang lta bu shin tu ngo mtshar ba dang bcas pa/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs zhi drag gsum/ bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa/ dpal rdo rje nag po gur
gyi mgon po/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa/ rje btsun ma ku ru kulle/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub/ rnam sras ser chen/ mgon po ber chen/ zha lu'i dpal ldan ma la sogs te yi dam dang
chos skyong so so la bstod pa/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa dngos grub rin cenasgo 'byed/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje

btsun rdo ring pa gsum gyi rnam thar/ rje nyid kyis dbus la phebs pa'i lam yig sogs lo rgyus kyi skor/ kye rdor man ngag lugs dang 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi sgrub mchod kyi lhan
thabs/ kye rdo rje phy-i nang gi bskyed rim rnam bshad ngo mtshar ba/ mgon po'i khog phug snyan brgyud rin cen lde mig /phyi nang gi 'khrid kha'u brag rdzong pa'i rgyun
gyi nyams len zhal shes kyi skor/ gtor chog chen mo/ gtor bzlog dgra bgegs kyi stobs 'phrog rol pa/ gtor ma gsum gyi zhal shes/ zungs 'dzugs/ thug chog la sogs pa med
du mi rung ba'i chos skor/ snying chu bsre ba/ dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar/ mgon po khro bcu dang / zhal bzhi pa/ phyag drug pa/ mgon dkar bzhi'i rjes gnang / zhal sgrub dus
kyi rjes gnang lhan thabs zhal gyi gsang 'khrid/ tshe sgrub srung 'khor/ gur mgon gyi bskang gso'i lhan thabs/ pu tra'i sgos bskang / beg rtse'i las byang / me 'bar kha
skong / snyan brgyud/ gyi ljang / dud sol/ zhal bzhi pa/ dmar po skor gsum sogs kyi dkar chag /mgon po che chung las mkhan dang bcas pa'i skor la chos sna bzhi bcu lhag
tsam yod/ ja mchod/ gsung mgur/ chab shog /sgrol dkar tshe 'khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun sogs yod la/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen pos gsung 'bum pod gsum ma zhig bzheng pa
gnang 'dug pa da dung ma 'dus pa kha shas yod par mngon/ de dag kyang legs par bshad pa kho na ma gtogs rtsom rnying brkus pa/ don med don log sogs snag shog gi gron du 'gro
ba ci yang ma mchis/ zhal slob mkhas pa rnams kyis gsung rgyun zin bris su bkod pa'i rigs don gyis rje bla ma'i

gsung yin mod/ de tsam rgyu mtshan du byas na thug med du thal bas 'dir ma bkod do/ /gnyis spangs bla ma'i brda thabs lung bstan bzhin/ /so dkar rigs kyi sa la spyod pa'i thar/
/zhabs sen atpal chun po nyer bcings nas/ /'di phyi'i mdun ma bu bzhin ngang gis mdzad/ /mthu stobs brgya byin yan lag rnam bzhi'i dpung / /bso sgrar bcas te mtshon
char phab pa'i mod/ /mi srun lha min sde rigs bsgral ba'i g.yul/ /rngom pas gdong smad mya ngan khang bur brgyal/ /kun nas yid dbang dga' mas 'khrid pa'i glang / /dad bstan
pad dkar rdzing bu 'dam bzhin du/ /brdzi yang bzang rdzu'i gser sbyangs rgyan mdzes pa/ /bshes gnyen rin chen bdun gyi bgrang byar min/ /ra gan gser chus byugs dang sa
le sbram/ /so sor spyod la 'khrul med mkhas pa'i tshogs/ /khyod zhal bdud rtsi btungs pa'i ring lugs mtha'/ /nam mkha'i ska rags ma des gzhal nus min/ /rnam dag brjod pa
pi'u wang yangs pa'i khog /don gyi rgyud mang 'khrol ba'i pusta kaH /shes ldan yid dbang 'gugs byed snyan pa'i sgra/ /skal bzang skye rgu'i rna bar gcig tu 'jebs/ /gsol
'debs las/ zhing 'dir ma lus gdul bya'i don grub nas/ /rje btsun bka' yi pho nyas spyan drangs te/ /zab yangs mkha' spyod dag pa'i zhing khams su/ /dge mtshan dang bcas gshegs
la gsol ba 'debs/ /'od gsal nam mkha'i dbyings las bzhengs pa'i sku/ /skal bzang mchog gi thugs mtshor gsal bar bstan/ /gzhan yang rtse gcig dad ldan bka' 'bangs rnams/
/slu med dbyings nas bskyangs la gsol ba 'debs/ /

rgyal ba kun gyi thugs rje gcig bsdus pa/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'dzin/ /'gran zla kun bral drin can tshar pa rje/ /rnam thar dran zhing snying nas gsol
ba 'debs/ /zhes me tog 'thor bar nye ba'i sngon rol tu rin po che bod mkhar ba'i rnam thar las rang la yod pa'i zang zing gi dngos po rnams kyang phul bka' chos 'dra yang
zhus/ rje'i zhal nas nga la yang dgra 'dra yod pas 'dul dgos pa yod gsung yang na so rgas pas mi yong 'dug pas nga'i dgra khyed slob ma rnams kyis 'dul dgos gsung / ha cang
dgra tshan che shos 'khor bar sgyur mkhan dug lnga yin pas 'di 'dul ba yin mod gsung / yang dug lnga med pa byas na ye shes lnga'i rgyu mi yong 'dug de yang mi yong 'dug
gsungs/ bdag la da chos rje'i drung dbus la byon dbus su dgon pa che chung gang byung yang zhal bdag mdzod gsungs/ dam tshig dril bu yang 'di 'khrol bar mdzod gdul bya
mang po yong sun pa tsam yong gsungs te rjes su ji ltar gsung pa bzhin byung / zhes gsung gi tha ma lta bu'i lung bstan stsal/ shing bya'i lo bo dong phun tshogs rab brtan
du bzhugs pa'i tshe gzibs chung gi sbug cig nas rje btsun rdo ring pa'i gsung 'dra rung ba'i gdangs las lan cig khur bskyed la sdod de nas ngas 'bod mi btang gis gsung
ba dngos su gsal bar byung ba nas lo gnyis song ba me pho stag gi lo thugs dam 'od gsal la khyab bdag kun spangs chen po phebs nas chos rje yar byon gsung brda yang yang
mdzad pa na thugs nges par byung ba'i rtags phyir rol sogs su dus ma yin par rlung ldang ba/ sa g.yo ba/ 'khrug long sogs mi dge ba'i ltas mang du shar/ de'i tshe thams
cad

mkhyen pa klu sgrub rgya mtsho la grang mo che'i spe'u ser por chos du ma stsal zhing gsung 'phros kyi lhongs la da lo drug cu rtsa lnga'i thog dog cha che ba yod zer yang
ma shi tsam yong ngam gsung pa sogs kyis mtshon zhabs 'bring ba dang drung du byung ba du mar zhing khams 'pho ba'i mdangs kyi gsung mang du byon yang / bdud kyi mthus kun
dga' bos de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan las mi 'da' bar gsol ba ma btab pa bzhin bu slob dang nye 'khor ba rnams kyang gzhan 'phrul dbang byed nas rmongs byed kyi mda' bsnun
pa lta bus brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs kyi rigs ma byung ba dang / gtso bor zhing 'di'i gdul bya phal cher rdzogs shing bla ma dam pa'i bka' ltar dag pa dang ma dag pa'i zhing
khams rgya mtsho'i lus can 'dren pa la thugs lhag par spro ba'i tshul gyis zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bdun brgyad skor la grib zas shig gis bslang ba'i sku khams mi bde
ba'i tshul bstan par gsos sman dang sku rim sogs zhabs tog pa rnams kyi 'bad nas bsgrubs kyang dngas skyed med pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin gzugs sku mtshan dpe'i dkyil 'khor
chos dbyings dag pa'i klong du sdud par gzhol ba'i 'da' kha ma'i thugs dam zab mo'i ting nge 'dzin gyi tshe/ 'dar bla brang gi tshoms chen du dge 'dun rags rim gyis rje
btsun rdo ring pa chen po'i sku bstod gsung ba'i tshe sdengs tshabs kyis shlo ka gcig dkyus nas chad pa rje bla mas thugs dam gyi ngang nas mkhyen te ting nge 'dzin las
bzhengs nas shlo ka 'di chad song bas bskyar nas thon gsung ba dpal mar me mdzad kyis sbrul gyi shun pa brjes kyang sbrul mi 'chi gsungs pa bzhin skye 'chi la rang dbang
thob pa'i gang zag gnas khang gcig nas

gcig tu 'pho ba tsam gyi nyams las med pas blos gzhal bar dka' ba yin no/ /kha sang phan chad dkar phyogs kyi lha rnams mya ngan gyis gdungs pa'i shugs kyi gnam sa bar gsum
gyi ltas mi legs pa mang ba 'di nas bzung nam mkha' baiDArYa mthing kha'i mdog lta bu la 'ja' tshon pir gyis bris pa ji lta bar 'khrigs shing me tog gi char chal chil du
'bab pa sngar tshor ma myong ba'i dri ngad bzang pos khyab pa sogs lha rnams kyis mchod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa spros/ ting nge 'dzin de'i ngang nas lam gyi 'phro rdzogs
par mdzad de bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sa mngon du gyur pas/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ zhing 'di'i mdzad pa legs par mthar phyin tshe/ /kun spangs chen pos byon zhes
bskul ba'i mthus/ /bgrang yas ngo mtshar ltas dang lhan cig tu/ /mkha' spyod gnas su gshegs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so/ /de'i tshe rje mar pa lo tsA la nA ro ta pas puShpa
ha rir mdzad pa bzhin thugs kyi sras du ma la dag pa ye shes kyi sku dngos su 'di dang lo mang song nas kyang bstan te chos 'chad lung bstan dbugs dbyung rgya cher mdzad
pa dper na 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi gzigs snang la mdun gyi nam mkha'i dbus su rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/ g.yas su sprul sku shAkya thub pa/
g.yon du ayon chos kyi rgyal po gsal bar gzigs/ rin po che bod mkhar bas go yab kyi gdan sa bzhag nas dben pa bsten bzhed pa'i dus tshes bcu'i tho rengs shig rje bla ma
phebs nas spyan nan cher gzigs te gsungs pa rnam thar du/ nged rang la slob ma a re mang yod kyang chos rje'i drung dam tshig dang sdom

pa la gnas shing byang chub kyi sems dang ldan pas bla ma dang bstan pa la bsams/ brtson 'grus drag pos skyo ngal spangs nas gzhan don byed dgos pa yin/ da lta bshad sgrub
kyi bstan pa'i rjes su 'jug pa yod tsam gyi dus 'dir 'chad nyan thos bsam byas na phan yon gzhan las che ba yin/ gzhan don mi yong ba zhig yin na sgrub pa kho na byed pa
khe che mod de 'dra ni ma yin/ yang 'di yin gyi mdzub mo 'dzugs rgyu med par dpe nyog mang po bltas pa'i 'chad nyan la snying po ci yang med/ bla ma gong ma tshad ldan gyi
dgongs pa dang mthun zhing rang gi bla ma tshad ldan gyi zhal nas brgyud pa'i chos thos bsam sgom gsum gyi sgro 'dogs bcad pa'i nges nges de rang gzhan la phan thogs pa
yin/ zhes byung zhing / rin po che yol pa gshegs khar steng mthongs su rje bla ma phebs pa'i sku rdo rje 'chang dngul chu lta bu song tshul/ mkhan chen bslab gsum pas rje
dbang phyug rab brtan la lam dbang gnang dus rnam thar du/ rje nyid kyi bzhugs sa'i mdun gyi nam mkhar tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po dang thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug yab sras gnyis dbang ma grol bar bzhugs nas dbang bskur gyi cho ga mdzad kyin 'dug pa la khong yab sras kyi dbang bskur ji lta ba bzhin khyed rnams la bshad
pa yin ang / de 'dra'i dga' ba la ang zhes byung / sngags 'chang rin po che'i rnam thar las/ rmi lam na rje bla ma tshar chen nyid sngon du gsung ngag rin po che gnang
ba'i dus su lam zab gnang ba'i skabs kyi sku'i gzi byin dang zhal 'dzum na bza' sogs ji lta ba mdzad nas khyod kyis bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba lhur blangs nas snyan brgyud
thun mong ma yin pa'i bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi zab chos 'di nyid

rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i gnas su 'chad par gyis shig gsungs byung ba dang gnyid sad byung bas de lta bu'i bla ma dang mjal gsung gi bdud rtsi zab mo thos pa'i dus kyang byas
snyam mchi ma mang du shor tshe rabs kun tu gdul bya'i zhing khams su skye ba/ de nas kyang rjes su 'dzin pa zhig snyam pa'i gsol ba phur tshugs su btab ces dang / de
nyid las/ 'dar du gsung ngag bshad skabs de dus zla ba gsum tsam song ba'i bskyed rim gyis mngal 'byin pa'i dmigs pa gal gnang shin tu che ba zhig gi dus su the tshom cung
zad yod pa zhig byung ba de de nub tho rangs kha'i dus su rmi lam na zhabs drung rjes zhu sna mdzad rje btsun tshar chen dang sngon gyi gzhi bsnyen skabs su phebs pa'i
bla ma yab sras rnams zhal 'dzum lta bar mi bzod pa lta bu'i dges pa'i rnam 'gyur ji snyed gnang / de nas sngon gyi bla ma nyid kyis skad cig la spyan nam mkha' gzigs pa
dang dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro yin zhu bas char sprin lhags pa ltar byas 'ja' tshon lham me ba zhig byas so/ /de nas bdag gi dogs pa phran bu 'di sel ba zhig zhu snyam pa na/
e ma legs pa'i lam la legs so zhes/ /de ga yin pas bka' stsal mi dgos te/ /logs su yod pa'i 'bras bu til tsam med/ /blo gros ldan pa khyod la ci zhig dgos/ /gsung ba zh-ig
gnyid khongs su zin/ de nas me long la has btab pa ltar yal ba dang gnyid sad/ e ma ngas 'di lta bu'i lam tshang la ma nor ba thos nas lan bskyal ba lta bu la'ang thugs
dgyes dgyes gnang ba ni bstan pa nyams dma' bar 'dug snyam pa'i blo la 'khu 'phrig chen po dang dad pa'i dpa' 'bar ba'i dga' spro dang / snying chu mig

sngar 'bab pa lhan cig byung / bsams tsa na nga rang skal ba bzang snyam pa'i blo bde phugs su chud ltos bcas kun kyang lugs gnyis bya ba phra rags gang la'ang gegs kyi mtshan
ma mi 'byung ba zhig lags zhes dang / de nyid las/ 'dar du skye bdun ril sgrub skabs zhag lnga song ba'i snga thun gyi bar la gnyid kyi rnam pa thung tsam byung ba'i
rmi lam na rje btsun sprul sku chen po padma rgyal po'i sku nyid myug rgyal khang du skyes bdun sgrub pa'i skabs kyi sku'i mdangs ji lta ba dang g.yas na 'khrul zhig chos
skyong bsod nams yin zer ba'i sku gzi brjid che ba zhig dang / g.yon na tshar chen yab sras dang bcas dgyes pa'i zhal 'dzum gyi mdangs gsal le ba byas pa zhig rmis pa/ gnyid
dngas pa na e ma ho nga yang bsod nams che/ de lta bu'i slu med kyi bla ma rnams dang mjal snyam pa dang / da snying po bdag dang bdag la ltos pa thams cad ayon bla
ma'i drung du skye nges kyi smon pa yid ches nges shig btab/ ces dang / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan dpal sphug tu bzhugs skabs dag snang du gsung ngag gnang ba'i
thugs nyams shar/ yar klungs bkra shis rtse chos sder lam 'bras 'dzugs pa mdzad skabs 'od gsal du yang yang zhal gzigs/ 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtser mnal lam du rje bla ma'i
zhabs gnyis dbu gtsug tu bzhag phyag gnyis kyis zhal 'gram skyor nas byin rlabs gnang dus ayon dngos yin dgongs pa'i tshe de'i skur gyur/ rnam pa de ltar shar yang ngo
bo pha bla mar thag chod pa'i mos gus kyi ngang nas mnal sad tshe dbu gtsug tu zhabs drod kyis tsha chil li ba byung bas mtshon te dngos slob yang slob mang por zhal ston
chos gsung byin rlabs gegs sel bogs

'don lung bstan gnang ba sogs mang / rje bod mkhar ba'i rnam thar du/ rmi lam la tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid na bza' sogs shin tu bzang ba sku la 'od 'phro ba
dang bcas phyogs shig la thegs song ba dang rje'i drung la ltos pa rnams ngas rjes su 'dzin no gsungs spyan cer ba zhig gzigs pa rmis/ de nas ring por ma lon par pha bla
ma rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su thim zer ba'i skad ca byung ba yug cig 'di bya dang 'di byed med pa'i ngang la 'di rmi lam yin las che bsam
pa dang / de las sad de kye ma kye hud shin tu 'jigs su rung ba'i 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho las sgrol bar byed pa'i ded dpon chen po lan cig rnyed pa de nyid/ rmi lam sgyu
ma bzhin du yal nas thal da mgon med pa'i bdag sogs 'gro ba rnams ji ltar byed bsams pa dang / mig mchi mas gang sems la bzod glags med pa'i sdug bsngal dpag tu med pa byung
/ slar bsam blo la sngon yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nas bzung bla ma gong ma tshang mas mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshul bstan khong rnams bde ba nas bde ba'i
zhing du gshegs pas kham che/ snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa rnams ni thob rang re chos gsha' ma zhig byed dgos/ da dung gnas gsar nas rje drung rin po che lta bu yang bzhugs
bsams pa dang 'jig rten phyogs nas nged rang tsho'i byung tshul kyang dran sngon nas bsams pa'i gnas de lta bu zhig tu thugs dam byed pa las gzhan thabs med bsam pa shar
zhes byung ba/ rang sems bla ma'i ngo bor thag chod pa'i skyes bu de 'dra la'ang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon rol tu mchog zung nyid zhing khams

'phos pa bzhin thugs la mi bzod pa'i tshor ba drag po byung na tha mal pa dag lta ci smos pas phyogs de'i skye bo rnams cho nge 'don pa dang brgyal ba sogs nyam thag pa'i rnam
'gyur sna tshogs pa ston zhing / 'dar ba bsod nams lhun grub lo ngo bzhi tsam lon pa zhig kyang stod la 'tshangs pa byung ba na'ang rgyal ba nyi ma'i gnyen chos kyi dbyings
su gzugs sku'i bkod pa bsdus kyang 'od srung chen po sogs bstan pa'i gtad rabs rim byon ltar/ rje bla ma dam pa la re bltos 'cha' ba'i gdul bya rnams rjes su 'dzin
par zhal skyin lta bu'i zhal slob kyi 'dren mchog 'di lta bu yod do zhes dbugs dbyung ba la ched du bsngags pa ltar rim gyis phyogs nas 'dus shing sku gdung za ma tog tu
ma bzhugs pa'i gong du tshogs pa rnams la pur mjal gyi dus sku gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bur shing las thang chu bzhin sku rdul zhu ba shel dkar gyi 'khri shing lta bu gsal
la 'tsher ba kun gyi mthun snang du grub pa'i dge mtshan mtha' klas pa byung / zhal slob 'gangs che ba rnams dang / chos sde khag /bstan pa'i sbyin bdag gnas gsar pa dang
'dar ba sogs kyis thog drangs mdor na skya ser drag gzhan mtha' dag gis snyan dar mchod pa sna lnga sogs che 'byor chung 'byor dang / 'dar stod rnam rgyal stag rtse nas
sde pa yum sras kyis 'gan blangs/ bla brang gnyer tshang / bo dong phun tshogs rab brtan sogs nas dge 'dun mang por bsnyen bkur te kye rdor gtso bor gyur pa'i dkyil 'khor
du ma zhal 'byed kyi chog gra'i tshe rdo rje slob dpon rigs kun khyab bdag chen po'i skur bzhengs pa la phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid kyi mchod pa'i tshogs gsog rgya
cher bsgrubs skabs nyin zhag mang por me

tog gi char dang 'ja' 'od kyi gur sogs phyogs der 'dus pa mtha' dag ngo mtshar dang dad pa'i spu long g.yo bar gyur/ sku gdung rin po cher dar zab kyi na bza' dang dri bzang
gi phye ma'i sri zhu/ nyes pa'i skyon sel ba'i slad du tsha sogs kyi zhabs tog dang bcas rin po che'i sgrom bur bcug ste nyin re bzhin mchod pa sna tshogs pa'i bkur sti
chad pa med pa'i ngos lo bco lnga song ba lcags mo sbrul gyi lo sde pa rin chen dpal bzang ba mched sogs dad pa dang gtong ba phun sum tshogs pa'i sbyin pa'i bdag po chen
pos gser gdung thog tshad phyed gnyis tsam la sde pa rin chen dpal bzang mchad kyi g.yu pad/ yum a mdzes rgyal mo'i g.yu krel rna brgyangs kyis gtsos g.yu mu tig byu ru
spos shel sogs kyi phra rgyan phyug pa dang bcas bzhengs pa'i thog ma'i gegs sel nas gzungs bzhugs rab gnas kyi bar thugs sras dam pa mtshungs med sngags 'chang chen pos
mdzad pa ni rnam thar las/ de nas rje btsun rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho'i ring bsrel phung po gser gdung rin po che'i zhal bkod bdag la bar chad zhi phyir srung 'khor
dang lhag par rgyu dang zangs bzo ba rnams la bgegs skrod dang bskyed chog byed dgos tshul gsungs bla ma drag por langs nas byas pas bar chad mtshan mas glags blta bar
ga la nus/ rgyang grags tshun la bkra shis mnga' gsol ma grub par du nyes pa'i go skabs bral yang bla ma dam pa'i thugs rje las gnad du mi 'gro ba byung dogs med/ 'on
kyang srung 'khor ched bstad nan bskyed de bsgoms pa dang nyin mtshan dal med drag sngags rgyun chad med par bzlas/ zla ba drug gi khongs su yongs su rdzogs te rin po che'i
gdung nyid mchod rten

du spyan drangs pa'i ye shes phyir 'brang gi bgegs skrod 'jam dpal zhal dgu par langs te byas pas bdud rigs kyi tshogs thams cad byer zhing der tshogs pa kun kyang spu zing
byed pa mang dag byung 'dug /mchod stegs su phebs pa dang mchod pa dang sku khrus 'bul ba sogs rgyas par byas/ panytsa li ka snam sbyar gyi grwa sbubs nas gnyis med kyi
ye shes la kha dog med kyang bdud rtsi shel dkar gyi gong bu gcig tu byas pa tshul khrims kyi phung po gong 'phel dang dri bsung phyogs bcur 'phro ba'i spos dkar gyi rdog
ma bdag gi pang du gnang byung bas sgrib med ye shes kyi thugs rje rgyun chad mi mnga' lags so/ /de ltar rgyu rin po che gser las grub pa'i gnod sbyin pho mo'i 'khor lo
sgrub pa zla ba tsam byas rgyud nas ji skad bshad pa ltar bzhugs su gsol/ mthar rab tu gnas pa rgyud sde nas gsungs pa ltar mtshan nyid tshang ba'i sgo nas zhag gsum sbrel
zhig byas/ sgrub po sbyin bdag dang bcas pa'i tshe dang bsod nams dpal 'byor gyi rgyun thams cad gong 'phel du 'gro ba'i phyir rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg thun mong min pa'i
phyag len gyis brgyan nas byas/ zhes byung la/ gser gdung rin po che'i dbu thog tu gnam rgyan/ snyan dar/ ting kang bu maNDal me dam sogs mchod rdzas kyi rim pa rgya dpangs
mtho ba/ gdung rten gyi g.yas su rje bla mas bzheng pa mdzad pa'i lam zab dang g.yon du dgongs rdzogs la dmigs pa'i lam 'bras brgyud pa dang bcas pa bla ma so so'i sku
mdun du zhal dkar/ bzed zhal/ zhal bsil/ DA dril/ dbang bum/ 'bru phor/ nang mchod ka li sogs nyer spyad phun sum tshogs pa/ bstan pa'i sbyin bdag 'dar nas kyis zhing dang
nas rtsa sbyar ba'i gser gdung rin po che'i drung du

dkar me sdong rkang bco brgyad re'i rgyun btsugs pa deng sang yang nag me la brten pa'i phyogs 'dra tsam re yod snang / sngags 'chang rin po ches nga'i bur 'di gdong dga' ba
mi rtsa ma chad bar de phyogs la kha thod la zhog ces zhal chems ltar gdung rten dus bzhugs pa lcags stag lo dus babs kyis zhugs 'bul dgos pa 'gyangs pas me rang 'bar lta
bu'i rkyen gyis gtsug lag khang la me gshor byung du rje 'di nyid kyi gdung yang mes bzhes mod de yan chod phyogs de'i skye rgu mtha' dag gis shi gson gyi dge ba'i phud
gser gdung la 'bul zhing / 'dar ba'i bya ba gang gi tshe'ang zan ril bsgril pa la yid gtod par snang / ma 'gyangs par 'di gnas gser sga dngul sga cha 'grig legs pa re dang
gos yug lnga rta sogs kyi yon sbyar zhing gtso bor gdan sa nas 'jam mgon sa skya pa chen pos thugs khur bzhes te dngul gdung thog tshad ma phra rgyan dang bcas grub pa'i
nang du bdag chen rin po ches gdul tsha phyag dar ba mang du 'jug pa gnang bas byin rlabs kyi rgyun ma nyams par yod/ gzhan yang thub bstan dge 'phel dang grang mo che
gnyis kar zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes bco lnga la gzhi rten sbyar ba'i mang ja/ zla ba bdun pa'i dus chen thog tshes bcu gsum nas zhag bzhi'i bar kye rdor sgrub mchod/
de zhor du grang mo cher tshes bcu bzhi nas zhag gsum gyi bar dmar chen gtor bzlog gnod sbyin yab yum/ pu tra ming sring / beg rtse lcam dral/ sgo ma bzhi/ bran bdud/ nor
bdag yab yum rnams kyi 'chams sogs rgyas par tshugs pa deng sang gi bar du ma nub par gnas/ gzhan yang sde pa gnas gsar pa/ khri khang pa/ o gzhi ba sogs sbyin

pa'i bdag po rnams kyis sgrub mchod dus dran gyi thebs sogs gnas dgon mang por bsod nams rgya mtsho'i rlabs phreng dus las yol ba med par gyur to/ /mtha' yas zhing du grangs
med rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /'gro 'dren ngal khur bzung bzhin gangs ljongs 'di'i/ /gnyen gcig bsu mar 'ongs pa'i DA ka'i tshogs/ /phyogs 'di kho nar brtse bral kye ma hud/
/sems can kun don ring nas thugs bskyed mgon/ /rtsod ldan duHkhas ches mnar gdul dka' rnams/ /bor nas chos dbyings bde ba'i klong gzims na/ /zhal 'ches rdo ba'i ri mo ming
du zad/ /'og min zhing du ye shes them skas la/ /bshes gnyen mchog de 'byon par gsol btab nas/ /dbang gzhu'i gur khyim manda ra ba'i char/ /thabs kyis skal dman 'gro rnams
'bring 'di ci/ /tshur mthong skye bo mya ngan khang bu ru/ /brgyal mod gnas lugs rang ngo shes pa rnams/ /sems nyid dag pa'i ngo bo tshar pa rje/ /khyab bdag rdo rje
sems gzhan dmigs su med/ /'on te chos kyi rgyal tshab gnas gsar bas/ /nyer mtshon bstan 'dzin dpyid kyi gser ldan ma/ /rngul chu'i rgyun 'bab de bzhin snyan brgyud chos/
/srid mthar mi nub 'phel der spro dga' brtas/ /de ltar rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i ded dpon tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar
gsol 'debs sa skyong 'dar pa rin chen dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i chu gter rgod pa dang / de'i 'grel pa snyan ngag mkhan 'dar pa bsod nams lhun grub
kyis bsgrigs pa legs bshad zla ba'i snang ba/ rtsa 'grel de gnyis la gzhi bcol nas chos 'khor yang rtse dang mnyan yod bya gshong gi mkhan po 'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes
gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i

rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar nor bu'i mgul rgyan rnams la'ang rje bla ma zhal bzhugs dus zin bris nges sbyar med pa'i skyon gyis lo tshigs gal che ba rags pa tsam las zhib cha
ma mchis shing / mdzad pa 'gangs che ba rnams bsdebs mtshungs su 'dug pa zhal slob kyi rnam thar dang sgo bstun pa'i lo zla sogs cung zad gtan tshigs kyis gzhal nus kyang
mtha' dag rtogs par dka' bas gsol 'debs tshigs bcad ma rtsa bar bzung / 'grel pa dang 'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa gnyis la 'khrul skyong ngos zin
pa thor bu byung ba rnams la dag sbyor byas/ go rim phyogs tsam las nges sbyar ma thub rung don gyi cha la dpyad gang bzod kyi lugs bgyis par slad nas kyang mkhas pa rnams
kyis dag ther dang snon 'phri mdzad 'tshal lo/ /rgyal yum ye shes mkha' 'gros rjes bzung sa drug dka' ba med bgrod nas/ /brtul zhugs spyod pas log lam 'phyan kun mngon
mtho nges legs gnas bkod de/ /bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sar gshegs rnal 'byor dbang phyug chos skyong zhabs/ /a ho ngur smrig gos kyis nyer klubs rigs kun bdag po tshar
pa rje/ /'gro snang rdzing bu ganggA'i klung rdul snyed/ /sna tshogs sgyu dra'i zla gzugs 'char ba'i tshad/ /bskal brgyar 'tshol ba'i rtse gcig ting 'dzin mkhan/ /mkha'
mtha' ma rnyed ldog pa'i 'dab chags bzhin/ /bcu gsum rnam par sprul pa'i zlos gar gtam/ /gya tshom smra min lung rigs nges ster nor/ /grangs med skye bar bsgrubs pa'i legs
byas kyi/ /tshul zong des khugs tshul la gcig tu rangs/ /thos bsam cha bsags zla dkyil dman pa'i zol/ /gzhan nor 'phel dang 'grib pa ltar sbyor yang / /dpag

dka'i yon tan ri bong snang brnyan de/ /mngon sum gsal bar 'char la gang gis bsnyon/ /snyan brgyud ring lugs dpyid kyi dga' ston tshogs/ /chad med 'bod pa'i rtogs brjod gzhan
gsos glu/ /blo gsal rna ba'i bcud du srid mtha'i bar/ /ches dngar phang 'gro'i sgra bzhin snyan par shog /ched du sgo gsum 'bad rnams zung 'jug sku/ /mngon gyur de srid
tshad ma bzhi ldan chos/ /ston dang nyer mjal thos bsam sgom pa yi/ /bzang po'i skal ba can du 'gyur bar shog /gsung ngag gser chos rdo rje'i chos skyong gis/ /zab don
slob mar bshad bya gdams pa'i char/ /snod ldan gdul bya'i 'dzin mar rab brlan te/ /bshad sgrub snye ma srid mthar g.yur za shog /de yang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rtogs
brjod bya gshong mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa der 'khrul gzhi kha yar yod grags dang / sa spyod 'dar ba rin chen dpal bzang khu dbon gyis
sbyar ba'i gsol 'debs rtsa 'grel khungs btsun yang khyab che ba zhig mi snang bas bsgrig mdun yod ngos drin can bla ma dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' dngos bka' 'gyur ba
chen po dang 'dren mchog dam pa mkhan chen zha lu ba gnyis kyi bka'i khur lci ba'i steng / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras brgyud pa dang bcas pa la mi phyed pa'i dad pa
thob pa'i bstan pa'i sbyin bdag pA Ni/ ka tsan/ swa ra swasti bya ka ra Na sogs brda sprod pa'i gtsug lag rgya mtsho'i mthar son zhing / sdeb sbyor/ rtsis dkar nag gis
mtshon pa'i rig byed du ma la blo gros kyi snang ba rgyas pa 'dar ba ngag dbang phun tshogs lhun grub kyis lo rgyus kha 'thor rnams bsdu ba sogs 'bad pa chen pos bskul ba
dang / rab 'byams rgyud sde'i bang mdzod bco brgyad chos rje

byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ gnas gsar zhabs drung dbon rin po che nam mkha' bsod nams dbang gi rgyal po/ grub pa'i dbang phyug lcags zam pa chen po'i dbon ngag dbang bstan
'dzin phun tshogs gsum gyis gsung ngag brgyud pa'i kha skong du dgos pa'i mtshams sbyar bar brten rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya
mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa slob bshad bstan pa'i nyi 'od 'di ni kha'u brag rdzong pa'i ring lugs la rgyu mtshan shes nas dad pa thob pa'i
za hor gyi bande slob bshad 'dzin pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho 'jigs med go cha thub bstan lang tsho'i sdes A' na la zhes pa me 'brug gro bzhin zla ba'i yar tshes
bco lnga rje bla ma mkha' spyod du gshegs pa'i dus dran gyi nyin pho brang chen po dmar po rir sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni 'phyong rgyas spun bdun pa lhun grub rgya mtsho'i
bgyis te grub pa'i dge bas snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi ldan gyi bstan pa srid mtha'i bar du rgyas par gyur cig /sarba mangga laM// //
